// FILE: src/ai/agent.js

import { solidPaint } from '../lib/appearance.js';

export const AGENT_STATES = Object.freeze({
  IDLE: 'idle',
  UNDERSTANDING: 'understanding',
  AWAITING_CLARIFICATION: 'awaiting_clarification',
  PLANNING: 'planning',
  GENERATING_CONCEPTS: 'generating_concepts',
  AWAITING_CONCEPT_SELECTION: 'awaiting_concept_selection',
  REFINING_CONCEPT: 'refining_concept',
  AWAITING_CONCEPT_APPROVAL: 'awaiting_concept_approval',
  COMPILING_DESIGN: 'compiling_design',
  RESOLVING_ASSETS: 'resolving_assets',
  GENERATING_ASSETS: 'generating_assets',
  ASSEMBLING_DESIGN: 'assembling_design',
  RENDERING: 'rendering',
  CRITIQUING: 'critiquing',
  CORRECTING: 'correcting',
  AWAITING_FINAL_APPROVAL: 'awaiting_final_approval',
  COMPLETED: 'completed',
  PAUSED: 'paused',
  CANCELLED: 'cancelled',
  FAILED: 'failed'
});

export const AGENT_TASK_TYPES = Object.freeze({
  NEW_DESIGN: 'new_design',
  REVISE_DESIGN: 'revise_design',
  CREATE_ASSET: 'create_asset',
  REVISE_ASSET: 'revise_asset',
  RESIZE_OR_ADAPT: 'resize_or_adapt',
  CREATE_TEMPLATE: 'create_template',
  HYBRID: 'hybrid'
});

const id = prefix => `${prefix}-${globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID?.() || `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(16).slice(2)}`}`;
const lower = value => String(value || '').toLowerCase();
const has = (text, pattern) => pattern.test(lower(text));
const quoteMatches = text => [...String(text || '').matchAll(/[“"]([^”"]+)[”"]/g)].map(match => match[1].trim()).filter(Boolean);

export function createAgentTask(title, type, status = 'pending', details = '') {
  return { id: id('task'), title, type, status, details, progress: status === 'completed' ? 100 : 0, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
}

export function classifyAgentRequest(instruction, context = {}) {
  const text = lower(instruction);
  const selected = context.selection?.length || 0;
  const hasCurrentDesign = !!context.design?.id;
  const asksAsset = /(asset|illustration|icon|logo|sticker|background removal|cutout|texture|pattern|photo|image)/.test(text);
  const asksDesign = /(design|flyer|menu|poster|card|presentation|social post|page|layout|brochure|invitation|sign)/.test(text);
  const asksRevision = /(revise|revision|change|edit|improve|fix|update|replace|make this|current|selected|existing|keep|preserve)/.test(text) || selected > 0;
  const asksResize = /(resize|adapt|convert|reformat|different size|aspect ratio|letter size|a4|story size)/.test(text);
  const asksTemplate = /(template|reusable design)/.test(text);

  let intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.NEW_DESIGN;
  if (asksResize) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.RESIZE_OR_ADAPT;
  else if (asksTemplate) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.CREATE_TEMPLATE;
  else if (asksAsset && asksDesign) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.HYBRID;
  else if (asksAsset && asksRevision) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_ASSET;
  else if (asksAsset && !asksDesign) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.CREATE_ASSET;
  else if (asksRevision && hasCurrentDesign) intent = AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_DESIGN;

  const scope = selected ? 'selection' : intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.NEW_DESIGN || intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.CREATE_TEMPLATE ? 'document' : 'page';
  const confidence = text.length > 80 ? .94 : text.length > 30 ? .86 : text.length > 12 ? .72 : .55;
  const preserve = [];
  if (/(keep|preserve|do not change|same)/.test(text)) preserve.push('existing content explicitly protected by the user');
  if (intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_DESIGN) preserve.push('existing copy and user-locked objects unless explicitly replaced');
  const missingInformation = [];
  if (text.length < 14) missingInformation.push('What should the finished design communicate, and who is it for?');
  if ((intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.CREATE_ASSET || intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_ASSET) && !/(photo|3d|flat|vector|watercolor|painted|realistic|illustration|minimal|retro|vintage|modern)/.test(text)) missingInformation.push('What visual style should the asset use?');
  if (!context.brands?.length && /(brand|branded|on-brand)/.test(text)) missingInformation.push('Which colours, fonts, or logo should define the brand direction?');

  return {
    intent,
    confidence,
    scope,
    goal: String(instruction || '').trim(),
    preserve,
    missingInformation: missingInformation.slice(0, 3),
    recommendedNextStep: missingInformation.length ? 'clarify' : 'generate_concepts'
  };
}

export function createAgentBrief(instruction, context, classification, options = {}) {
  const quoted = quoteMatches(instruction);
  const requiredAssets = [...new Set(options.assetIds || [])];
  const existingText = (context.currentPage?.elements || [])
    .filter(element => element.type === 'text' && element.text)
    .map(element => ({ id: element.id, role: element.role || '', text: element.text }))
    .slice(0, 80);
  return {
    id: id('brief'),
    taskType: classification.intent,
    deliverable: classification.intent.replaceAll('_', ' '),
    goal: String(instruction || '').trim(),
    audience: options.audience || '',
    style: options.style ? [options.style] : [],
    exactCopy: quoted,
    existingText,
    contentPriority: existingText.slice(0, 6).map(item => item.role || item.text.slice(0, 40)),
    mustUseAssetIds: requiredAssets,
    optionalAssetIds: options.optionalAssetIds || [],
    brandKitId: options.brandId || context.brands?.[0]?.id || null,
    constraints: {
      width: context.design?.width,
      height: context.design?.height,
      preserveExactText: classification.intent === AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_DESIGN,
      preserveExisting: classification.intent !== AGENT_TASK_TYPES.NEW_DESIGN,
      useAssets: options.useAssets !== false,
      useBrand: options.useBrand !== false,
      draftQuality: 'low'
    },
    assumptions: [],
    answers: [],
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

export function appendBriefAnswer(brief, answer) {
  return {
    ...brief,
    answers: [...(brief.answers || []), String(answer || '').trim()].filter(Boolean),
    assumptions: [...(brief.assumptions || []), String(answer || '').trim()].filter(Boolean)
  };
}

const conceptStyles = [
  {
    key: 'editorial',
    title: 'Editorial Clarity',
    description: 'Structured typography, generous spacing, and a restrained professional palette.',
    palette: ['#fffaf0', '#172033', '#d97706', '#ffffff'],
    prompt: 'Editorial graphic design, refined typography, clear information hierarchy, generous negative space, premium print layout, subtle warm accent'
  },
  {
    key: 'campaign',
    title: 'Bold Campaign',
    description: 'High contrast, oversized type, and energetic colour blocking for immediate impact.',
    palette: ['#111827', '#ffffff', '#f97316', '#facc15'],
    prompt: 'Bold contemporary campaign design, oversized typography, high contrast color blocks, energetic composition, punchy modern advertising'
  },
  {
    key: 'commons',
    title: 'Illustrated Commons',
    description: 'Friendly organic shapes, layered imagery, and a collaborative handmade character.',
    palette: ['#eef6ee', '#173f35', '#e76f51', '#f4c95d'],
    prompt: 'Warm illustrated design system, organic shapes, friendly handmade details, layered collage, community-oriented visual identity, polished composition'
  }
];

function preferredAsset(context, brief) {
  const ids = [...(brief.mustUseAssetIds || []), ...(brief.optionalAssetIds || [])];
  return context.assets?.find(asset => ids.includes(asset.id)) || (brief.constraints?.useAssets ? context.assets?.[0] : null) || null;
}

function sourceCopy(context, brief) {
  const text = brief.exactCopy?.length ? brief.exactCopy : (brief.existingText || []).map(item => item.text);
  const headline = text[0] || brief.goal.split(/[.!?\n]/)[0].slice(0, 90) || 'Design Commons';
  const supporting = text.slice(1).join('\n').slice(0, 2400) || brief.goal.slice(0, 600);
  return { headline, supporting };
}

function conceptBatch(style, context, brief, index = 0, refinement = '') {
  const width = Number(context.design?.width || 1080);
  const height = Number(context.design?.height || 1080);
  const portrait = height >= width;
  const margin = Math.round(Math.min(width, height) * .075);
  const asset = preferredAsset(context, brief);
  const { headline, supporting } = sourceCopy(context, brief);
  const pageRef = `agent-concept-${style.key}-${index + 1}`;
  const commands = [
    { op: 'create_page', ref: pageRef, page: { name: `${style.title} concept` } },
    { op: 'set_page_background', pageRef, paint: solidPaint(style.palette[0]) }
  ];

  if (style.key === 'editorial') {
    commands.push(
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'rect', name: 'Editorial accent', role: 'decoration', x: margin, y: margin, width: Math.max(12, width * .018), height: height - margin * 2, fill: style.palette[2], radius: 8 } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept headline', role: 'headline', text: headline, x: margin * 1.55, y: margin, width: width - margin * 2.55, height: height * .22, fontFamily: 'Montserrat', fontSize: Math.max(38, Math.min(104, width * .085)), fontWeight: 700, fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: 1.02, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 30, maxLines: 3, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept supporting copy', role: 'body', text: supporting, x: margin * 1.55, y: height * .66, width: width - margin * 2.55, height: height * .23, fontFamily: 'Inter', fontSize: Math.max(16, width * .025), fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: 1.3, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 12, maxLines: 12, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } }
    );
    if (asset) commands.push({ op: 'create_image_frame', pageRef, assetId: asset.id, element: { name: 'Concept hero image', role: 'hero-image', x: margin * 1.55, y: height * .29, width: width - margin * 2.55, height: height * .31, radius: Math.round(width * .018) } });
    else commands.push({ op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'rect', name: 'Concept image area', role: 'hero-image', x: margin * 1.55, y: height * .29, width: width - margin * 2.55, height: height * .31, fill: '#eadfcf', radius: Math.round(width * .018) } });
  } else if (style.key === 'campaign') {
    commands.push(
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'rect', name: 'Campaign block', role: 'decoration', x: 0, y: height * .58, width, height: height * .42, fill: style.palette[2] } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'ellipse', name: 'Campaign badge', role: 'decoration', x: width * .68, y: margin * .55, width: width * .24, height: width * .24, fill: style.palette[3], rotation: 8 } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept headline', role: 'headline', text: headline.toUpperCase(), x: margin, y: margin, width: width - margin * 2, height: height * .39, fontFamily: 'Montserrat', fontSize: Math.max(44, Math.min(130, width * .105)), fontWeight: 800, fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: .94, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 34, maxLines: 4, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept supporting copy', role: 'body', text: supporting, x: margin, y: height * .68, width: width - margin * 2, height: height * .23, fontFamily: 'Inter', fontSize: Math.max(16, width * .026), fontWeight: 600, fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: 1.25, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 12, maxLines: 10, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } }
    );
    if (asset) commands.push({ op: 'create_image_frame', pageRef, assetId: asset.id, element: { name: 'Concept image', role: 'hero-image', x: width * .48, y: height * .35, width: width * .44, height: height * .29, radius: Math.round(width * .04), rotation: -4 } });
  } else {
    const heroWidth = portrait ? width * .72 : width * .45;
    commands.push(
      { op: 'create_svg', pageRef, svg: '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 240 240"><path fill="#e76f51" d="M34 127C17 88 45 39 90 32c43-7 87 18 107 57 18 35 4 83-26 108-31 26-83 25-112-4-17-17-18-43-25-66Z"/><path fill="#f4c95d" d="M151 48c25 12 45 39 42 67-4 35-39 63-73 56-31-7-50-41-41-71 9-32 42-67 72-52Z"/></svg>', element: { name: 'Organic motif', role: 'decoration', x: width * .59, y: margin * .35, width: width * .36, height: width * .36, opacity: .95 } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept headline', role: 'headline', text: headline, x: margin, y: margin, width: width * .67, height: height * .24, fontFamily: 'Playfair Display', fontSize: Math.max(42, Math.min(112, width * .09)), fontWeight: 700, fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: 1.02, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 30, maxLines: 3, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'rect', name: 'Copy card', role: 'container', x: margin, y: height * .62, width: width - margin * 2, height: height * .27, fill: '#ffffff', radius: Math.round(width * .028), opacity: .94 } },
      { op: 'create_element', pageRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Concept supporting copy', role: 'body', text: supporting, x: margin * 1.45, y: height * .665, width: width - margin * 2.9, height: height * .18, fontFamily: 'Inter', fontSize: Math.max(16, width * .025), fill: style.palette[1], lineHeight: 1.3, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 12, maxLines: 10, overflowBehavior: 'ellipsis' } }
    );
    if (asset) commands.push({ op: 'create_image_frame', pageRef, assetId: asset.id, element: { name: 'Concept hero image', role: 'hero-image', x: margin, y: height * .28, width: heroWidth, height: height * .29, radius: Math.round(width * .14), mask: 'rounded' } });
  }

  return {
    schemaVersion: 1,
    baseRevision: context.design?.revision || 0,
    instruction: `${style.title} low-quality concept for: ${brief.goal}${refinement ? `. Refinement: ${refinement}` : ''}`,
    commands,
    source: 'agent-local-concept'
  };
}

export function createLocalConceptVariants(context, brief, { refinement = '', parentConceptId = null } = {}) {
  return conceptStyles.map((style, index) => ({
    id: id('concept'),
    parentConceptId,
    title: style.title,
    description: style.description,
    prompt: `${style.prompt}. User request: ${brief.goal}${refinement ? `. Requested refinement: ${refinement}` : ''}. Generate a low-resolution design concept preview only; preserve exact supplied wording.`,
    negativePrompt: 'illegible text, overlapping typography, distorted logo, watermark, clipped content, random words',
    seed: Math.abs(hash(`${brief.goal}:${style.key}:${refinement}`)) % 2147483647,
    previewQuality: 'low',
    previewMode: 'structured-fallback',
    palette: style.palette,
    conceptSpec: {
      styleKey: style.key,
      palette: style.palette,
      hierarchy: ['headline', 'hero-image', 'supporting-copy'],
      assetManifest: createAssetManifest(context, brief),
      reconstruction: 'editable-command-bundle'
    },
    commandBatch: conceptBatch(style, context, brief, index, refinement),
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
  }));
}

export function createAssetManifest(context, brief) {
  const selected = (brief.mustUseAssetIds || []).map(assetId => context.assets?.find(asset => asset.id === assetId)).filter(Boolean);
  const result = selected.map(asset => ({ key: `user-${asset.id}`, type: asset.type || 'image', assetId: asset.id, description: asset.description || asset.name, sourcePreference: 'user-asset', required: true }));
  if (!result.length && brief.constraints?.useAssets) result.push({ key: 'hero-visual', type: 'image', description: 'A hero visual that supports the user request', sourcePreference: 'asset-library-first', required: false });
  if ([AGENT_TASK_TYPES.CREATE_ASSET, AGENT_TASK_TYPES.REVISE_ASSET, AGENT_TASK_TYPES.HYBRID].includes(brief.taskType)) result.push({ key: 'generated-primary-asset', type: 'image', description: brief.goal, sourcePreference: 'generate-draft-then-confirm', required: true });
  return result;
}

export function normalizeAgentConcepts(payload, context, brief) {
  const raw = Array.isArray(payload) ? payload : payload?.concepts;
  if (!Array.isArray(raw) || !raw.length) return [];
  return raw.slice(0, 3).map((concept, index) => ({
    id: concept.id || id('concept'),
    parentConceptId: concept.parentConceptId || null,
    title: concept.title || `Concept ${index + 1}`,
    description: concept.description || '',
    prompt: concept.prompt || '',
    negativePrompt: concept.negativePrompt || '',
    seed: concept.seed ?? Math.abs(hash(`${brief.goal}:${index}`)) % 2147483647,
    previewQuality: concept.previewQuality || 'low',
    previewMode: concept.previewUrl ? 'image' : 'structured',
    previewUrl: concept.previewUrl || concept.preview_url || null,
    palette: concept.palette || [],
    conceptSpec: concept.conceptSpec || concept.spec || { assetManifest: createAssetManifest(context, brief) },
    commandBatch: concept.commandBatch || concept.batch || null,
    createdAt: concept.createdAt || new Date().toISOString()
  }));
}

export function createAgentSession(instruction, context, options = {}) {
  const classification = classifyAgentRequest(instruction, context);
  const brief = createAgentBrief(instruction, context, classification, options);
  return {
    id: id('agent'),
    status: AGENT_STATES.UNDERSTANDING,
    previousStatus: null,
    instruction: String(instruction || '').trim(),
    classification,
    brief,
    questions: classification.missingInformation,
    messages: [{ id: id('message'), role: 'user', content: String(instruction || '').trim(), createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
    tasks: [
      createAgentTask('Understand the request', 'understand', 'completed'),
      createAgentTask('Inspect the design and selected assets', 'inspect', 'completed'),
      createAgentTask('Generate three low-quality concepts', 'concepts', 'pending'),
      createAgentTask('Wait for concept selection', 'selection', 'pending'),
      createAgentTask('Compile an editable design', 'compile', 'pending'),
      createAgentTask('Render and run design checks', 'quality', 'pending'),
      createAgentTask('Wait for final approval', 'approval', 'pending')
    ],
    concepts: [],
    selectedConceptId: null,
    steering: [],
    baseRevision: context.design?.revision || 0,
    options: { provider: options.provider || 'auto', useBrand: options.useBrand !== false, useAssets: options.useAssets !== false, brandId: options.brandId || null, assetIds: options.assetIds || [] },
    maxCorrectionLoops: Number(options.maxCorrectionLoops || 3),
    correctionLoop: 0,
    paused: false,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

export function updateAgentTask(tasks, type, patch) {
  return (tasks || []).map(task => task.type === type ? { ...task, ...patch } : task);
}

function hash(value) {
  let result = 2166136261;
  for (const char of String(value || '')) {
    result ^= char.charCodeAt(0);
    result = Math.imul(result, 16777619);
  }
  return result | 0;
}

// FILE: src/ai/assetPlanning.js
================================================================================
const clean = (value, max = 2000) => String(value ?? '').trim().slice(0, max);
const splitWords = value => clean(value, 2000).toLowerCase().split(/[^a-z0-9]+/).filter(word => word.length > 2);

export const AI_ASSET_KINDS = ['raster', 'svg'];
export const AI_ASSET_ASPECT_RATIOS = ['1:1', '4:3', '3:4', '16:9', '9:16', '2:1', '1:2'];

export function normalizeAITheme(input = {}) {
  return {
    name: clean(input.name || input.title || 'Page theme', 160),
    summary: clean(input.summary || input.description, 1000),
    keywords: Array.isArray(input.keywords) ? input.keywords.map(item => clean(item, 80)).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 24) : [],
    palette: Array.isArray(input.palette) ? input.palette.filter(value => /^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(String(value))).slice(0, 12) : [],
    visualStyle: clean(input.visualStyle || input.style, 300),
    illustrationStyle: clean(input.illustrationStyle, 300),
    photographyStyle: clean(input.photographyStyle, 300),
    consistencyKey: clean(input.consistencyKey || input.seedDescription, 300)
  };
}

export function normalizeAIAssetRequest(input = {}, index = 0) {
  const kind = AI_ASSET_KINDS.includes(input.kind) ? input.kind : 'raster';
  const aspectRatio = AI_ASSET_ASPECT_RATIOS.includes(input.aspectRatio) ? input.aspectRatio : '1:1';
  return {
    key: clean(input.key || `asset-${index + 1}`, 120),
    name: clean(input.name || input.title || `Asset ${index + 1}`, 180),
    purpose: clean(input.purpose || input.role, 500),
    role: clean(input.role || 'illustration', 100),
    prompt: clean(input.prompt, 6000),
    negativePrompt: clean(input.negativePrompt, 2000),
    kind,
    aspectRatio,
    transparent: kind === 'svg' ? true : input.transparent === true,
    reuseAssetId: clean(input.reuseAssetId, 160),
    reuseQuery: clean(input.reuseQuery || input.query, 500),
    placementHint: clean(input.placementHint, 500),
    required: input.required !== false,
    tags: Array.isArray(input.tags) ? input.tags.map(tag => clean(tag, 80)).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 30) : []
  };
}

export function normalizeAIAssetRequests(list = []) {
  return (Array.isArray(list) ? list : []).slice(0, 16).map(normalizeAIAssetRequest).filter(item => item.prompt || item.reuseAssetId || item.reuseQuery);
}

export function buildThemedAssetPrompt(requestInput, themeInput = {}) {
  const request = normalizeAIAssetRequest(requestInput);
  const theme = normalizeAITheme(themeInput);
  const sections = [request.prompt || `${request.name}. ${request.purpose}`];
  if (theme.summary) sections.push(`Page theme: ${theme.summary}`);
  if (theme.visualStyle) sections.push(`Visual style: ${theme.visualStyle}`);
  if (request.kind === 'svg' && theme.illustrationStyle) sections.push(`Illustration direction: ${theme.illustrationStyle}`);
  if (request.kind === 'raster' && theme.photographyStyle) sections.push(`Image direction: ${theme.photographyStyle}`);
  if (theme.palette.length) sections.push(`Use this palette where appropriate: ${theme.palette.join(', ')}.`);
  if (theme.consistencyKey) sections.push(`Keep all generated assets visually consistent with: ${theme.consistencyKey}.`);
  if (request.transparent) sections.push('Isolated subject on a transparent background. No border, frame, mockup, label, or text.');
  if (request.negativePrompt) sections.push(`Avoid: ${request.negativePrompt}.`);
  return sections.filter(Boolean).join('\n');
}

export function scoreAssetForRequest(asset = {}, requestInput = {}) {
  const request = normalizeAIAssetRequest(requestInput);
  if (request.reuseAssetId && asset.id === request.reuseAssetId) return 10000;
  const haystack = `${asset.original_name || asset.name || ''} ${asset.description || ''} ${(asset.tags || []).join(' ')}`.toLowerCase();
  const words = new Set(splitWords(`${request.name} ${request.purpose} ${request.reuseQuery} ${request.prompt} ${request.tags.join(' ')}`));
  let score = 0;
  for (const word of words) if (haystack.includes(word)) score += word.length >= 7 ? 4 : 2;
  if (request.kind === 'svg' && /svg|vector/.test(String(asset.asset_type || asset.type || '').toLowerCase())) score += 5;
  if (request.transparent && (asset.tags || []).some(tag => /transparent|cutout|isolated/i.test(String(tag)))) score += 3;
  return score;
}

export function findReusableAsset(assets = [], requestInput = {}, minimumScore = 6) {
  const ranked = (assets || []).map(asset => ({ asset, score: scoreAssetForRequest(asset, requestInput) })).sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
  return ranked[0]?.score >= minimumScore ? ranked[0] : null;
}

export function assetRequestPromptList(requests = [], theme = {}) {
  return normalizeAIAssetRequests(requests).map((request, index) => ({
    index: index + 1,
    key: request.key,
    name: request.name,
    kind: request.kind,
    aspectRatio: request.aspectRatio,
    transparent: request.transparent,
    prompt: buildThemedAssetPrompt(request, theme)
  }));
}

// FILE: src/ai/designIntelligence.js

import { normalizeAppearance, paintPrimaryColor } from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { normalizeDesignSystem, normalizePrintSettings } from '../lib/designSystem.js';

const round = value => Math.round(Number(value || 0) * 100) / 100;
const quantize = (value, step = 4) => Math.round(Number(value || 0) / step) * step;
const overlap = (a, b) => ({
  width: Math.max(0, Math.min(a.x + a.width, b.x + b.width) - Math.max(a.x, b.x)),
  height: Math.max(0, Math.min(a.y + a.height, b.y + b.height) - Math.max(a.y, b.y))
});

function visible(page) { return (page?.elements || []).filter(element => !element.hidden); }

function colorList(document, page) {
  const counts = new Map();
  const add = value => {
    if (typeof value !== 'string' || !/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(value)) return;
    const key = value.toLowerCase(); counts.set(key, (counts.get(key) || 0) + 1);
  };
  add(page.background);
  for (const element of visible(page)) {
    add(element.fill); add(element.stroke);
    const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
    for (const fill of appearance.fills || []) add(paintPrimaryColor(fill.paint, ''));
    for (const stroke of appearance.strokes || []) add(stroke.color);
    for (const shadow of appearance.shadows || []) add(shadow.color);
  }
  return [...counts.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, 16).map(([color, usage]) => ({ color, usage }));
}

function typography(page) {
  const groups = new Map();
  for (const element of visible(page).filter(item => item.type === 'text')) {
    const key = [element.role || 'unassigned', element.fontFamily, round(element.fontSize), element.fontWeight, round(element.lineHeight), round(element.charSpacing)].join('|');
    if (!groups.has(key)) groups.set(key, { role: element.role || '', fontFamily: element.fontFamily, fontSize: round(element.fontSize), fontWeight: element.fontWeight, lineHeight: round(element.lineHeight), charSpacing: round(element.charSpacing), count: 0, elementIds: [] });
    const group = groups.get(key); group.count++; group.elementIds.push(element.id);
  }
  return [...groups.values()].sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
}

function spacingScale(page) {
  const elements = visible(page);
  const values = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) for (let j = i + 1; j < elements.length; j++) {
    const a = elements[i], b = elements[j], ov = overlap(a, b);
    if (ov.height > Math.min(a.height, b.height) * .25) {
      const gap = a.x < b.x ? b.x - (a.x + a.width) : a.x - (b.x + b.width);
      if (gap >= 0 && gap <= 200) values.push(quantize(gap));
    }
    if (ov.width > Math.min(a.width, b.width) * .25) {
      const gap = a.y < b.y ? b.y - (a.y + a.height) : a.y - (b.y + b.height);
      if (gap >= 0 && gap <= 200) values.push(quantize(gap));
    }
  }
  const counts = new Map(); values.forEach(value => counts.set(value, (counts.get(value) || 0) + 1));
  return [...counts.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, 12).map(([value, count]) => ({ value, count }));
}

function alignmentLines(page) {
  const lines = { left: new Map(), centerX: new Map(), right: new Map(), top: new Map(), centerY: new Map(), bottom: new Map() };
  for (const element of visible(page)) {
    const values = { left: element.x, centerX: element.x + element.width / 2, right: element.x + element.width, top: element.y, centerY: element.y + element.height / 2, bottom: element.y + element.height };
    for (const [kind, value] of Object.entries(values)) {
      const key = quantize(value, 2); if (!lines[kind].has(key)) lines[kind].set(key, []); lines[kind].get(key).push(element.id);
    }
  }
  return Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(lines).map(([kind, map]) => [kind, [...map.entries()].filter(([, ids]) => ids.length >= 2).map(([value, elementIds]) => ({ value, elementIds })).sort((a, b) => b.elementIds.length - a.elementIds.length).slice(0, 20)]));
}

function repeatedPatterns(page) {
  const groups = new Map();
  for (const element of visible(page)) {
    const role = element.role || element.semanticName || element.name || element.type;
    const key = `${element.type}|${String(role).toLowerCase()}|${quantize(element.width, 8)}|${quantize(element.height, 8)}`;
    if (!groups.has(key)) groups.set(key, { key, type: element.type, role, elementIds: [], widths: [], heights: [] });
    const group = groups.get(key); group.elementIds.push(element.id); group.widths.push(round(element.width)); group.heights.push(round(element.height));
  }
  return [...groups.values()].filter(group => group.elementIds.length >= 2).sort((a, b) => b.elementIds.length - a.elementIds.length);
}

function hierarchy(page) {
  const children = new Map();
  for (const element of visible(page)) {
    const key = element.parentId || 'root';
    if (!children.has(key)) children.set(key, []);
    children.get(key).push(element.id);
  }
  return { roots: children.get('root') || [], children: Object.fromEntries([...children.entries()].filter(([key]) => key !== 'root')) };
}

export function analyzePage(document, page) {
  return {
    palette: colorList(document, page),
    typography: typography(page),
    spacingScale: spacingScale(page),
    alignmentLines: alignmentLines(page),
    repeatedPatterns: repeatedPatterns(page),
    hierarchy: hierarchy(page),
    designSystem: normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem),
    print: normalizePrintSettings(document.print, document.width, document.height)
  };
}

export function analyzeDocument(document) {
  return {
    pages: (document.pages || []).map((page, index) => ({ pageIndex: index, pageId: page.id, ...analyzePage(document, page) })),
    designSystem: normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem),
    print: normalizePrintSettings(document.print, document.width, document.height)
  };
}

function issuePenalty(issues, severity, weight) { return issues.filter(issue => issue.severity === severity).length * weight; }

export function scoreDesign(issues = [], analysis = null) {
  const categories = {
    layoutConsistency: 100,
    typographyHierarchy: 100,
    spacingRhythm: 100,
    contrastLegibility: 100,
    brandConsistency: 100,
    printReadiness: 100
  };
  for (const issue of issues) {
    const amount = issue.severity === 'critical' ? 18 : issue.severity === 'warning' ? 7 : 2;
    if (/align|overlap|out-of-bounds|stacked|size|grid|component/.test(issue.rule)) categories.layoutConsistency -= amount;
    if (/text|font|type|widow|orphan|line-break|hierarchy/.test(issue.rule)) categories.typographyHierarchy -= amount;
    if (/spacing|padding|gap|margin/.test(issue.rule)) categories.spacingRhythm -= amount;
    if (/contrast|small-text|low-resolution|overflow/.test(issue.rule)) categories.contrastLegibility -= amount;
    if (/style|radius|shadow|brand|colour|color|font/.test(issue.rule)) categories.brandConsistency -= amount;
    if (/print|bleed|safe-area|dpi|font-embedding|cmyk|trim/.test(issue.rule)) categories.printReadiness -= amount;
  }
  if (analysis?.typography?.length > 8) categories.typographyHierarchy -= Math.min(20, (analysis.typography.length - 8) * 2);
  if (analysis?.spacingScale?.length > 8) categories.spacingRhythm -= Math.min(18, analysis.spacingScale.length - 8);
  for (const key of Object.keys(categories)) categories[key] = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(categories[key])));
  const overall = Math.round(Object.values(categories).reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) / Object.keys(categories).length);
  return { overall, categories, criticalPenalty: issuePenalty(issues, 'critical', 18), warningPenalty: issuePenalty(issues, 'warning', 7) };
}

function esc(value) { return String(value ?? '').replace(/[&<>"']/g, char => ({ '&': '&amp;', '<': '&lt;', '>': '&gt;', '"': '&quot;', "'": '&apos;' }[char])); }

export function createInspectionSvg(document, pageIndex = 0, { includeGrid = true, includeLabels = true } = {}) {
  const page = document.pages?.[pageIndex];
  if (!page) return '';
  const width = document.width, height = document.height;
  const parts = [`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 ${width} ${height}">`, `<rect width="${width}" height="${height}" fill="#ffffff"/>`];
  if (includeGrid) {
    const grid = page.grid || {}; const step = Math.max(8, Number(grid.size || 20));
    for (let x = 0; x <= width; x += step) parts.push(`<path d="M${x} 0V${height}" stroke="#94a3b8" stroke-opacity=".12" stroke-width="1"/>`);
    for (let y = 0; y <= height; y += step) parts.push(`<path d="M0 ${y}H${width}" stroke="#94a3b8" stroke-opacity=".12" stroke-width="1"/>`);
  }
  const margins = page.margins || {};
  parts.push(`<rect x="${margins.left || 0}" y="${margins.top || 0}" width="${Math.max(1, width - (margins.left || 0) - (margins.right || 0))}" height="${Math.max(1, height - (margins.top || 0) - (margins.bottom || 0))}" fill="none" stroke="#22c55e" stroke-dasharray="8 6" stroke-width="2"/>`);
  (page.elements || []).filter(element => !element.hidden).forEach((element, index) => {
    const color = element.type === 'text' ? '#2563eb' : element.type === 'frame' ? '#7c3aed' : element.type === 'image' ? '#059669' : '#e11d48';
    parts.push(`<rect x="${round(element.x)}" y="${round(element.y)}" width="${round(element.width)}" height="${round(element.height)}" fill="${color}" fill-opacity=".035" stroke="${color}" stroke-width="1.5"/>`);
    if (includeLabels) {
      const label = `E${String(index + 1).padStart(2, '0')} ${element.role || element.semanticName || element.name || element.type}`;
      const labelY = Math.max(12, Number(element.y || 0) - 4);
      parts.push(`<text x="${round(element.x)}" y="${round(labelY)}" font-family="Arial" font-size="10" font-weight="700" fill="${color}">${esc(label.slice(0, 48))}</text>`);
    }
    if (element.parentId) {
      const parent = page.elements.find(item => item.id === element.parentId);
      if (parent) parts.push(`<path d="M${round(element.x + element.width / 2)} ${round(element.y + element.height / 2)}L${round(parent.x + parent.width / 2)} ${round(parent.y + parent.height / 2)}" stroke="#64748b" stroke-opacity=".35" stroke-dasharray="3 4"/>`);
    }
  });
  parts.push('</svg>');
  return parts.join('');
}

export function svgToDataUrl(svg) {
  return `data:image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8,${encodeURIComponent(svg)}`;
}

const pageFor = (document, command, currentPageIndex = 0, pageRefs = new Map()) => {
  if (command.pageRef) {
    const id = pageRefs.get(command.pageRef);
    return id ? document.pages.find(page => page.id === id) || null : null;
  }
  if (command.pageId) return document.pages.find(page => page.id === command.pageId) || null;
  const index = Number.isInteger(command.pageIndex) ? command.pageIndex : currentPageIndex;
  return document.pages[index] || null;
};

function flattenElementStyle(input = {}) {
  const source = clone(input || {});
  const style = source.style && typeof source.style === 'object' && !Array.isArray(source.style) ? source.style : null;
  if (style) {
    for (const key of STYLE_FIELDS) {
      if (!(key in style) || key in source) continue;
      if (key === 'color') source.fill = style[key];
      else source[key] = style[key];
    }
  }
  delete source.style;
  return source;
}

function sanitizePatch(patch = {}) {
  const source = flattenElementStyle(patch);
  const next = {};
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(source || {})) {
    if (!SAFE_PATCH_KEYS.has(key) || value === undefined) continue;
    next[key] = clone(value);
  }
  if ('text' in next) next.text = safeString(next.text, 50000);
  if ('svg' in next) next.svg = sanitizeSvgMarkup(next.svg);
  if ('name' in next) next.name = safeString(next.name, 160);
  if ('semanticName' in next) next.semanticName = safeString(next.semanticName, 500);
  if ('role' in next) next.role = safeString(next.role, 100);
  if ('contentKey' in next) next.contentKey = safeString(next.contentKey, 200);
  if ('fontFamily' in next) next.fontFamily = safeString(next.fontFamily, 120);
  if ('tags' in next) next.tags = Array.isArray(next.tags) ? next.tags.map(tag => safeString(tag, 100)).slice(0, 50) : [];
  // Migrate early professional-typography field names to the canonical document schema.
  if ('columnsCount' in next && !('columns' in next)) next.columns = next.columnsCount;
  if ('baselineGrid' in next && !('baselineGridStep' in next)) next.baselineGridStep = next.baselineGrid;
  if ('openTypeFeatures' in next && !('opentypeFeatures' in next)) next.opentypeFeatures = Array.isArray(next.openTypeFeatures) ? next.openTypeFeatures.join(', ') : String(next.openTypeFeatures || '');
  delete next.columnsCount; delete next.baselineGrid; delete next.openTypeFeatures;
  for (const key of ['x', 'y', 'rotation']) if (key in next) next[key] = Number(next[key]) || 0;
  for (const key of ['width', 'height']) if (key in next) next[key] = clamp(next[key] || 1, 1, 20000);
  if ('opacity' in next) next.opacity = clamp(next.opacity, 0, 1);
  if ('fontSize' in next) next.fontSize = clamp(next.fontSize, 4, 1000);
  if ('minFontSize' in next) next.minFontSize = clamp(next.minFontSize, 4, 1000);
  if ('maxLines' in next) next.maxLines = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(next.maxLines) || 0));
  if ('overflowBehavior' in next && !['visible', 'clip', 'ellipsis'].includes(next.overflowBehavior)) next.overflowBehavior = 'visible';
  return next;
}

function elementFactory(rawInput = {}) {
  const input = flattenElementStyle(rawInput);
  const type = ALLOWED_ELEMENT_TYPES.has(input.type) ? input.type : 'rect';
  const overrides = sanitizePatch({ ...input, id: undefined, zIndex: undefined });
  let element;
  if (type === 'text') element = textElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'rect') element = rectElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'frame') element = frameElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'ellipse') element = ellipseElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'shape') element = shapeElement(input.shapeKind || 'triangle', overrides);
  else if (type === 'line') element = baseElement('line', { width: 300, height: 0, stroke: '#111827', strokeWidth: 5, ...overrides });
  else if (type === 'path') element = pathElement(input.pathData || [], overrides);
  else if (type === 'svg') element = svgElement(input.svg, overrides);
  else if (type === 'chart') element = chartElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'table') element = tableElement(overrides);
  else if (type === 'qrcode') element = qrElement(overrides);
  else element = baseElement(type, overrides);
  element.createdBy = input.createdBy || 'ai';
  element.sourceId = input.sourceId || null;
  return element;
}

function resolveTargetRefs(target = {}, elementRefs = new Map()) {
  if (!target || typeof target !== 'object') return target;
  const ids = new Set(Array.isArray(target.ids) ? target.ids : []);
  if (target.ref && elementRefs.has(target.ref)) ids.add(elementRefs.get(target.ref));
  for (const ref of target.refs || []) if (elementRefs.has(ref)) ids.add(elementRefs.get(ref));
  return { ...target, ...(ids.size ? { ids: [...ids] } : {}) };
}

function matchesTarget(element, target = {}, selection = []) {
  if (!target || Object.keys(target).length === 0) return false;
  if (target.id && element.id !== target.id) return false;
  if (Array.isArray(target.ids) && !target.ids.includes(element.id)) return false;
  if (target.selected && !selection.includes(element.id)) return false;
  if (target.type && element.type !== target.type) return false;
  if (target.role && element.role !== target.role) return false;
  if (target.semanticName && String(element.semanticName || '').toLowerCase() !== String(target.semanticName).toLowerCase()) return false;
  if (target.name && String(element.name || '').toLowerCase() !== String(target.name).toLowerCase()) return false;
  if (target.tag && !(element.tags || []).includes(target.tag)) return false;
  if (target.contentKey && element.contentKey !== target.contentKey) return false;
  if (target.componentInstanceId && element.componentInstanceId !== target.componentInstanceId) return false;
  return true;
}

function targetElements(page, target, selection = [], { allowAll = false, elementRefs = new Map() } = {}) {
  if (!page) return [];
  const resolved = resolveTargetRefs(target, elementRefs);
  if (resolved?.all === true && !allowAll) return [];
  return page.elements.filter(element => matchesTarget(element, resolved, selection) && element.aiEditable !== false && !element.userLocked);
}

function firstTarget(page, target, selection, elementRefs) {
  return targetElements(page, target, selection, { elementRefs })[0] || null;
}

function resolveParent(page, command, selection, elementRefs) {
  if (command.parentRef) {
    const id = elementRefs.get(command.parentRef);
    return page?.elements?.find(element => element.id === id && element.type === 'frame') || null;
  }
  return command.parentTarget ? firstTarget(page, command.parentTarget, selection, elementRefs) : null;
}

function resolveRegion(document, page, regionName, fallback = {}) {
  const region = page?.regions?.[regionName] || page?.regions?.safe || defaultRegions(document.width, document.height).safe;
  return { ...region, ...fallback };
}

function fitInsidePage(document, geometry) {
  const width = clamp(geometry.width, 1, document.width);
  const height = clamp(geometry.height, 1, document.height);
  return {
    x: clamp(geometry.x, 0, Math.max(0, document.width - width)),
    y: clamp(geometry.y, 0, Math.max(0, document.height - height)),
    width,
    height
  };
}

function positionElement(document, page, element, layout = null, rawElement = {}) {
  const hasLayout = layout && typeof layout === 'object' && Object.keys(layout).length > 0;
  const explicitX = Number.isFinite(Number(rawElement.x));
  const explicitY = Number.isFinite(Number(rawElement.y));
  if (!hasLayout || explicitX || explicitY) {
    return { ...fitInsidePage(document, element), layoutRegion: element.layoutRegion || '' };
  }
  const region = resolveRegion(document, page, layout.region || element.layoutRegion || 'safe');
  const padding = Math.max(0, Number(layout.padding ?? 0));
  const width = clamp(layout.width ?? element.width, 1, Math.max(1, region.width - padding * 2));
  const height = clamp(layout.height ?? element.height, 1, Math.max(1, region.height - padding * 2));
  let x = region.x + padding;
  let y = region.y + padding;
  if (layout.align === 'center') x = region.x + (region.width - width) / 2;
  if (layout.align === 'right' || layout.align === 'end') x = region.x + region.width - width - padding;
  if (layout.verticalAlign === 'middle' || layout.justify === 'center') y = region.y + (region.height - height) / 2;
  if (layout.verticalAlign === 'bottom' || layout.justify === 'end') y = region.y + region.height - height - padding;
  return { ...fitInsidePage(document, { x, y, width, height }), layoutRegion: layout.region || element.layoutRegion || 'safe' };
}

function parseCsv(source) {
  const text = safeString(source, 200000);
  const rows = [];
  let row = [], cell = '', quoted = false;
  for (let index = 0; index < text.length; index++) {
    const char = text[index];
    if (char === '"') {
      if (quoted && text[index + 1] === '"') { cell += '"'; index++; }
      else quoted = !quoted;
    } else if (char === ',' && !quoted) { row.push(cell); cell = ''; }
    else if ((char === '\n' || char === '\r') && !quoted) {
      if (char === '\r' && text[index + 1] === '\n') index++;
      row.push(cell); cell = '';
      if (row.some(value => value.length)) rows.push(row);
      row = [];
    } else cell += char;
  }
  row.push(cell);
  if (row.some(value => value.length)) rows.push(row);
  return rows.slice(0, 1000).map(values => values.slice(0, 100));
}

function csvElement(command) {
  const cells = parseCsv(command.csv);
  if (!cells.length) throw new Error('CSV content did not contain any rows.');
  const mode = command.mode === 'chart' ? 'chart' : 'table';
  if (mode === 'chart') {
    const header = cells[0] || [];
    const body = cells.slice(1);
    const labels = body.map(row => row[0] || '');
    const series = header.slice(1).map((name, column) => ({
      name: name || `Series ${column + 1}`,
      values: body.map(row => Number(row[column + 1]) || 0)
    }));
    return chartElement({ chartType: command.chartType || 'bar', data: { labels, series: series.length ? series : [{ name: 'Series 1', values: labels.map(() => 0) }] }, ...sanitizePatch(command.element || {}) });
  }
  const columns = Math.max(1, ...cells.map(row => row.length));
  const normalized = cells.map(row => Array.from({ length: columns }, (_, index) => row[index] ?? ''));
  return tableElement({ cells: normalized, rows: normalized.length, columns, options: { headerRows: Math.max(0, Number(command.headerRows ?? 1)) }, ...sanitizePatch(command.element || {}) });
}

function normalizeZ(page) {
  page.elements = page.elements.map((element, index) => ({ ...element, zIndex: index }));
}

function alignElements(page, elements, kind, document) {
  if (!elements.length) return;
  const multi = elements.length > 1;
  const left = multi ? Math.min(...elements.map(item => item.x)) : 0;
  const right = multi ? Math.max(...elements.map(item => item.x + item.width)) : document.width;
  const top = multi ? Math.min(...elements.map(item => item.y)) : 0;
  const bottom = multi ? Math.max(...elements.map(item => item.y + item.height)) : document.height;
  for (const item of elements) {
    if (kind === 'left') item.x = left;
    if (kind === 'center') item.x = (left + right - item.width) / 2;
    if (kind === 'right') item.x = right - item.width;
    if (kind === 'top') item.y = top;
    if (kind === 'middle') item.y = (top + bottom - item.height) / 2;
    if (kind === 'bottom') item.y = bottom - item.height;
  }
}

function distributeElements(elements, axis) {
  if (elements.length < 3) return;
  const horizontal = axis !== 'vertical';
  const sorted = [...elements].sort((a, b) => horizontal ? a.x - b.x : a.y - b.y);
  const start = horizontal ? sorted[0].x : sorted[0].y;
  const end = horizontal ? sorted.at(-1).x + sorted.at(-1).width : sorted.at(-1).y + sorted.at(-1).height;
  const total = sorted.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (horizontal ? item.width : item.height), 0);
  const gap = (end - start - total) / (sorted.length - 1);
  let cursor = start;
  for (const item of sorted) {
    if (horizontal) item.x = cursor; else item.y = cursor;
    cursor += (horizontal ? item.width : item.height) + gap;
  }
}


function recipeCommands(recipe, command, context) {
  const input = command.inputs || {};
  const brand = context.brands?.find(item => item.id === input.brandKitId) || context.brands?.[0];
  const colors = input.colors || brand?.colors || ['#fff8ef', '#231f20', '#d5482f', '#f5c451'];
  const fonts = input.fonts || brand?.fonts || ['DM Serif Display', 'DM Sans'];
  const width = context.document.width, height = context.document.height;
  const pageIndex = command.pageIndex;
  const onPage = item => ({ ...item, ...(command.pageId ? { pageId: command.pageId } : command.pageRef ? { pageRef: command.pageRef } : Number.isInteger(pageIndex) ? { pageIndex } : {}) });

  if (['cocktail-menu', 'restaurant-menu', 'price-list'].includes(recipe)) {
    const items = Array.isArray(input.items) && input.items.length ? input.items : [
      { name: 'Menu item one', description: 'Ingredient or description', price: '$15' },
      { name: 'Menu item two', description: 'Ingredient or description', price: '$15' },
      { name: 'Menu item three', description: 'Ingredient or description', price: '$15' },
      { name: 'Menu item four', description: 'Ingredient or description', price: '$15' }
    ];
    const columns = Math.max(1, Math.min(4, Number(input.columns || 2)));
    const safeX = Math.round(width * .075), safeW = Math.round(width * .85);
    const headerH = Math.round(height * .22), contentY = Math.round(height * .29), contentH = Math.round(height * .58);
    const commands = [
      onPage({ op: 'set_page_background', paint: input.backgroundPaint || solidPaint(colors[0] || '#fff8ef') }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_element', ref: 'recipe-header', element: { type: 'frame', name: 'Menu header', role: 'header', x: safeX, y: Math.round(height * .055), width: safeW, height: headerH, fill: 'transparent', stroke: 'transparent', layout: { direction: 'vertical', gap: 10, padding: 0, align: 'center', justify: 'center' } } }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: 'recipe-header', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Menu title', role: 'headline', contentKey: 'title', text: safeString(input.title || 'Menu', 300), fontFamily: fonts[0] || 'DM Serif Display', fontSize: Math.round(width * .075), fontWeight: 700, fill: colors[1] || '#231f20', textAlign: 'center', width: safeW, height: Math.round(headerH * .46), autoFit: true, minFontSize: 28, maxLines: 2, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: 'recipe-header', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Menu subtitle', role: 'subheadline', contentKey: 'subtitle', text: safeString(input.subtitle || '', 500), fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .021), fontWeight: 700, fill: colors[2] || '#d5482f', textAlign: 'center', width: safeW, height: Math.round(headerH * .22), autoFit: true, minFontSize: 12, maxLines: 2, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_grid', ref: 'recipe-menu-grid', name: 'Menu card grid', bounds: { x: safeX, y: contentY, width: safeW, height: contentH }, columns, rows: Math.ceil(items.length / columns), columnGap: Math.round(width * .028), rowGap: Math.round(height * .024), padding: 0 })
    ];
    items.forEach((item, index) => {
      const cardRef = `recipe-card-${index + 1}`;
      commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', ref: cardRef, element: { type: 'frame', name: `Menu card ${index + 1}`, semanticName: 'Menu card', role: 'container', fill: item.fill || colors[(index % Math.max(1, colors.length - 1)) + 1] || '#ffffff', stroke: colors[1] || '#231f20', strokeWidth: 1.5, radius: Math.round(width * .018), layout: { direction: 'vertical', gap: 10, padding: Math.round(width * .025), align: 'start', justify: 'start', widthMode: 'fixed', heightMode: 'fixed' } } }));
      commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: cardRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Item name', semanticName: 'Menu item title', role: 'item-name', contentKey: 'name', text: safeString(item.name || 'Menu item', 300), fontFamily: fonts[0] || 'DM Serif Display', fontSize: Math.round(width * .035), fontWeight: 700, lineHeight: 1.04, fill: item.textColor || colors[1] || '#231f20', width: Math.round(safeW / columns * .68), height: Math.round(height * .07), autoFit: true, minFontSize: 18, maxLines: 2, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }));
      commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: cardRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Item description', semanticName: 'Menu item description', role: 'item-description', contentKey: 'description', text: Array.isArray(item.description) ? item.description.join('\n') : safeString(item.description || '', 1000), fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .018), fontWeight: 500, lineHeight: 1.35, fill: item.textColor || colors[1] || '#231f20', width: Math.round(safeW / columns * .75), height: Math.round(height * .115), autoFit: true, minFontSize: 11, maxLines: 6, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fill', grow: 1, alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }));
      commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: cardRef, element: { type: 'text', name: 'Item price', semanticName: 'Menu item price', role: 'item-price', contentKey: 'price', text: safeString(item.price || '', 80), fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .024), fontWeight: 800, fill: item.textColor || colors[1] || '#231f20', textAlign: 'right', width: Math.round(safeW / columns * .3), height: Math.round(height * .04), layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }));
    });
    commands.push(onPage({ op: 'place_in_grid', target: { semanticName: 'Menu card' }, gridRef: 'recipe-menu-grid' }));
    if (input.footer) commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Footer', role: 'footer', text: safeString(input.footer, 500), fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .014), fontWeight: 600, fill: colors[1] || '#231f20', textAlign: 'center', x: safeX, y: Math.round(height * .925), width: safeW, height: Math.round(height * .035), autoFit: true, minFontSize: 9, maxLines: 1, overflowBehavior: 'clip' } }));
    return commands;
  }

  if (['event-poster', 'invitation', 'report-cover', 'business-card', 'brochure', 'presentation', 'product-catalogue', 'infographic', 'social-promotion'].includes(recipe)) {
    const headline = safeString(input.headline || input.title || 'Your headline', 300);
    const offer = safeString(input.offer || input.subtitle || '', 500);
    const cta = safeString(input.cta || input.footer || '', 300);
    const commands = [
      onPage({ op: 'set_page_background', paint: input.backgroundPaint || solidPaint(colors[0] || '#111827') }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_element', ref: 'recipe-hero-copy', element: { type: 'frame', name: 'Hero copy', role: 'container', x: width * .09, y: height * .08, width: width * .82, height: height * .38, fill: 'transparent', stroke: 'transparent', layout: { direction: 'vertical', gap: Math.round(height * .02), padding: 0, align: 'center', justify: 'center' } } }),
      onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: 'recipe-hero-copy', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Headline', role: 'headline', text: headline, fontFamily: fonts[0] || 'Montserrat', fontSize: Math.round(width * .085), fontWeight: 800, fill: colors[1] || '#ffffff', textAlign: 'center', width: width * .82, height: height * .22, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 28, maxLines: 3, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', alignSelf: 'stretch' } } })
    ];
    if (offer) commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', parentRef: 'recipe-hero-copy', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Supporting copy', role: 'subheadline', text: offer, fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .032), fontWeight: 600, fill: colors[2] || colors[1] || '#ffffff', textAlign: 'center', width: width * .72, height: height * .10, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 14, maxLines: 3, overflowBehavior: 'clip', layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed', alignSelf: 'stretch' } } }));
    if (input.assetId) commands.push(onPage({ op: 'insert_asset', ref: 'recipe-hero-image', assetId: input.assetId, role: 'hero-image', semanticName: 'Hero image', layout: { region: 'hero', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'bottom', width: width * .78, height: height * .42 } }));
    if (cta) commands.push(onPage({ op: 'create_element', element: { type: 'text', name: 'Call to action', role: 'call-to-action', text: cta, fontFamily: fonts[1] || 'DM Sans', fontSize: Math.round(width * .026), fontWeight: 700, fill: colors[1] || '#ffffff', textAlign: 'center', x: width * .14, y: height * .88, width: width * .72, height: height * .07, autoFit: true, minFontSize: 12, maxLines: 2, overflowBehavior: 'clip' } }));
    return commands;
  }
  return [];
}

export function getAICapabilities() {
  const schemas = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(OPERATION_FIELDS).map(([op, fields]) => [op, { allowedFields: fields }]));
  Object.assign(schemas, {
    create_page: { ...schemas.create_page, required: [], notes: ['Use ref to target the new page from later commands. The page object may contain name, width, height, and regions.'] },
    create_element: { ...schemas.create_element, required: ['element'], notes: ['element.type is required. Explicit element x/y take precedence over automatic layout.'] },
    create_svg: { ...schemas.create_svg, required: ['svg'], notes: ['svg accepts a complete safe SVG document or a path beginning with M/m.'] },
    create_from_csv: { ...schemas.create_from_csv, required: ['csv'], notes: ['mode is table or chart. CSV supports quoted cells and escaped quotes.'] },
    set_reference_image: { ...schemas.set_reference_image, required: [], notes: ['Adds a non-exporting page reference overlay for visual matching. Use an assetId from context.assets.'] },
    create_image_frame: { ...schemas.create_image_frame, required: ['element'], notes: ['Creates a reusable masked image frame. assetId is optional.'] },
    set_image_frame_asset: { ...schemas.set_image_frame_asset, required: ['target'], notes: ['Provide assetId or query.'] },
    update_element: { ...schemas.update_element, required: ['target', 'patch'] },
    replace_text: { ...schemas.replace_text, required: ['target'] },
    insert_asset: { ...schemas.insert_asset, required: ['assetId'] }
  });
  return {
    schemaVersion: AI_COMMAND_SCHEMA_VERSION,
    documentSchemaVersion: 5,
    maxCommands: MAX_AI_COMMANDS,
    maxElements: MAX_AI_ELEMENTS,
    operations: [...AI_OPERATIONS],
    operationSchemas: schemas,
    elementTypes: [...ALLOWED_ELEMENT_TYPES],
    elementSchema: {
      allowedFields: [...ELEMENT_INPUT_FIELDS],
      styleFields: [...STYLE_FIELDS],
      geometry: 'Use element.x/y/width/height for absolute placement. If x or y is supplied, it takes precedence over layout placement.',
      svg: 'For type svg, provide sanitized SVG markup in element.svg.'
    },
    layoutFields: [...LAYOUT_FIELDS],
    targetFields: [...TARGET_FIELDS],
    pageTargetFields: PAGE_TARGET_FIELDS,
    fonts: FONT_FAMILIES,
    fontStatus: getFontLoadReport(FONT_FAMILIES),
    recipes: ['social-promotion', 'cocktail-menu', 'restaurant-menu', 'price-list', 'event-poster', 'business-card', 'presentation', 'brochure', 'invitation', 'product-catalogue', 'report-cover', 'infographic'],
    agentWorkflows: {
      taskTypes: ['new_design', 'revise_design', 'create_asset', 'revise_asset', 'resize_or_adapt', 'create_template', 'hybrid'],
      conceptCount: 3,
      conceptQuality: 'low',
      approvals: ['visual-direction', 'editable-reconstruction'],
      interruptible: true,
      maxDefaultCorrectionLoops: 3
    },
    semanticRoles: ['headline', 'subheadline', 'body', 'caption', 'price', 'call-to-action', 'logo', 'hero-image', 'background-image', 'decoration', 'legal', 'chart-title', 'chart-data', 'container', 'item-name', 'item-description', 'item-price', 'badge', 'divider', 'footer', 'header', 'illustration'],
    assetPlanning: {
      theme: { name: 'string', summary: 'string', keywords: 'string[]', palette: 'hex[]', visualStyle: 'string', illustrationStyle: 'string', photographyStyle: 'string', consistencyKey: 'string' },
      assetRequest: { key: 'stable string', name: 'string', purpose: 'string', role: 'semantic role', prompt: 'generation prompt', negativePrompt: 'string', kind: AI_ASSET_KINDS, aspectRatio: AI_ASSET_ASPECT_RATIOS, transparent: 'boolean', reuseAssetId: 'existing context asset id', reuseQuery: 'semantic search phrase', placementHint: 'string', required: 'boolean', tags: 'string[]' },
      strategy: 'Prefer reuseAssetId from context.assets. Request generation only for assets that are materially important and missing.'
    },
    nestedSchemas: {
      appearance: { fills: 'fill layers', strokes: 'stroke layers', shadows: 'drop/inner shadows', effects: 'layer/background blur', blendMode: 'Canvas composite mode' },
      frameLayout: { direction: 'horizontal|vertical', gap: 'number', rowGap: 'number', columnGap: 'number', padding: 'number or {top,right,bottom,left}', align: 'start|center|end|stretch', justify: 'start|center|end|space-between', wrap: 'boolean', widthMode: 'fixed|hug|fill', heightMode: 'fixed|hug|fill' },
      layoutSizing: { width: 'fixed|hug|fill', height: 'fixed|hug|fill', grow: 'number', alignSelf: 'auto|start|center|end|stretch' },
      typography: { fontFamily: 'available font', fontSize: 'number', fontWeight: 'number', lineHeight: 'number', charSpacing: 'number', autoFit: 'boolean', minFontSize: 'number', maxLines: 'number', overflowBehavior: 'visible|clip|ellipsis' },
      print: { trim: '{width,height}', bleed: '{top,right,bottom,left}', safeArea: '{top,right,bottom,left}', slug: '{top,right,bottom,left}', marks: '{crop,registration,colorBars,pageInformation}', colorSpace: 'rgb|cmyk|spot', pdfPreset: 'screen|print|pdf-x-1a|pdf-x-3|pdf-x-4' },
      designStyles: designStyleSchema()
    },
    examples: {
      createPage: { op: 'create_page', ref: 'menu-page', page: { name: 'Menu page' } },
      absoluteText: { op: 'create_element', pageRef: 'menu-page', element: { type: 'text', x: 80, y: 80, width: 650, height: 100, text: 'Headline', fontFamily: 'Montserrat', fontSize: 64, fill: '#111827' } },
      regionText: { op: 'create_element', element: { type: 'text', width: 650, height: 100, text: 'Headline', fontFamily: 'Montserrat', fontSize: 64, fill: '#111827' }, layout: { region: 'header', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'middle' } },
      customSvg: { op: 'create_svg', svg: '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path fill="#4f46e5" d="M50 5 95 95H5Z"/></svg>', element: { x: 100, y: 100, width: 300, height: 300, role: 'decoration' } },
      csvTable: { op: 'create_from_csv', mode: 'table', csv: 'Item,Qty,Price\nTacos,2,$12', element: { x: 80, y: 220, width: 620, height: 260 } },
      referenceImage: { op: 'set_reference_image', assetId: 'USE_AN_ASSET_ID_FROM_CONTEXT', opacity: .45, mode: 'overlay', fit: 'contain' },
      imageFrame: { op: 'create_image_frame', assetId: 'USE_AN_ASSET_ID_FROM_CONTEXT', element: { name: 'Circular photo', x: 60, y: 220, width: 150, height: 150, mask: 'circle' } },
      structuredCard: [{ op: 'create_element', ref: 'card', element: { type: 'frame', x: 60, y: 300, width: 330, height: 260, layout: { direction: 'vertical', gap: 12, padding: 24 } } }, { op: 'create_element', parentRef: 'card', element: { type: 'text', role: 'item-name', text: 'Item name', width: 280, height: 70, layoutSizing: { width: 'fill', height: 'fixed' } } }],
      grid: [{ op: 'create_grid', ref: 'grid', bounds: { x: 60, y: 300, width: 688, height: 560 }, columns: 2, rows: 2, columnGap: 28, rowGap: 28 }, { op: 'place_in_grid', target: { semanticName: 'Menu card' }, gridRef: 'grid' }]
    }
  };
}

function validateObjectKeys(value, allowed, label, errors) {
  if (!value || typeof value !== 'object' || Array.isArray(value)) { errors.push(`${label} must be an object.`); return; }
  for (const key of Object.keys(value)) if (!allowed.has(key)) errors.push(`${label} contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
}

function validateElementInput(element, label, errors, warnings) {
  if (!element || typeof element !== 'object' || Array.isArray(element)) { errors.push(`${label} must be an object.`); return; }
  for (const key of Object.keys(element)) if (!ELEMENT_INPUT_FIELDS.has(key)) errors.push(`${label} contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
  if (element.type != null && !ALLOWED_ELEMENT_TYPES.has(element.type)) errors.push(`${label}.type "${element.type}" is not supported.`);
  if (element.style != null) {
    if (!element.style || typeof element.style !== 'object' || Array.isArray(element.style)) errors.push(`${label}.style must be an object.`);
    else for (const key of Object.keys(element.style)) if (!STYLE_FIELDS.has(key)) errors.push(`${label}.style contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
  }
  if (element.fontFamily && !FONT_FAMILIES.includes(element.fontFamily)) warnings.push(`${label}.fontFamily "${element.fontFamily}" is not in the built-in font catalogue and may fall back on another font.`);
  if ((element.type === 'svg' || element.svg != null) && element.svg != null) {
    try { sanitizeSvgMarkup(element.svg); } catch (error) { errors.push(`${label}.svg: ${error.message}`); }
  }
}

export function validateCommandBatch(input, { revision = null } = {}) {
  const errors = [];
  const warnings = [];
  if (!input || typeof input !== 'object' || Array.isArray(input)) return { valid: false, errors: ['Command batch must be an object.'], warnings };
  const batchFields = new Set(['schemaVersion', 'baseRevision', 'instruction', 'commands', 'source', 'theme', 'assetRequests']);
  for (const key of Object.keys(input)) if (!batchFields.has(key)) errors.push(`Command batch contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
  if (input.schemaVersion !== AI_COMMAND_SCHEMA_VERSION) errors.push(`schemaVersion must be ${AI_COMMAND_SCHEMA_VERSION}.`);
  if (!Array.isArray(input.commands)) errors.push('commands must be an array.');
  if (input.commands?.length > MAX_AI_COMMANDS) errors.push(`A maximum of ${MAX_AI_COMMANDS} commands is allowed.`);
  if (input.theme != null && (!input.theme || typeof input.theme !== 'object' || Array.isArray(input.theme))) errors.push('theme must be an object.');
  if (input.assetRequests != null && !Array.isArray(input.assetRequests)) errors.push('assetRequests must be an array.');
  if (Array.isArray(input.assetRequests) && input.assetRequests.length > 16) errors.push('A maximum of 16 asset requests is allowed per planning pass.');
  for (const [assetIndex, request] of (input.assetRequests || []).entries()) {
    const assetLabel = `Asset request ${assetIndex + 1}`;
    if (!request || typeof request !== 'object' || Array.isArray(request)) { errors.push(`${assetLabel} must be an object.`); continue; }
    const allowed = new Set(['key', 'name', 'purpose', 'role', 'prompt', 'negativePrompt', 'kind', 'aspectRatio', 'transparent', 'reuseAssetId', 'reuseQuery', 'placementHint', 'required', 'tags']);
    for (const key of Object.keys(request)) if (!allowed.has(key)) errors.push(`${assetLabel} contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
    if (request.kind != null && !AI_ASSET_KINDS.includes(request.kind)) errors.push(`${assetLabel}.kind must be raster or svg.`);
    if (request.aspectRatio != null && !AI_ASSET_ASPECT_RATIOS.includes(request.aspectRatio)) errors.push(`${assetLabel}.aspectRatio is not supported.`);
    if (!request.prompt && !request.reuseAssetId && !request.reuseQuery) errors.push(`${assetLabel} requires prompt, reuseAssetId, or reuseQuery.`);
  }
  if (Number.isInteger(input.baseRevision) && Number.isInteger(revision) && input.baseRevision !== revision) errors.push(`The design changed after the AI inspected it. Expected revision ${input.baseRevision}, current revision ${revision}.`);

  const refs = { page: new Set(), element: new Set(), grid: new Set(), component: new Set(), style: new Set(), data: new Set() };
  const addRef = (kind, ref, label) => {
    if (ref == null) return;
    if (typeof ref !== 'string' || !ref.trim()) { errors.push(`${label}.ref must be a non-empty string.`); return; }
    if (refs[kind].has(ref)) errors.push(`${label}.ref "${ref}" is duplicated.`);
    else refs[kind].add(ref);
  };
  const requireRef = (kind, ref, label, field) => { if (ref && !refs[kind].has(ref)) errors.push(`${label} references unknown ${field} "${ref}". Create it earlier in the bundle.`); };
  const targetRefs = (target, label) => {
    if (!target) return;
    validateObjectKeys(target, TARGET_FIELDS, label, errors);
    requireRef('element', target.ref, label, 'element ref');
    for (const ref of target.refs || []) requireRef('element', ref, label, 'element ref');
  };

  for (const [index, command] of (input.commands || []).entries()) {
    const label = `Command ${index + 1}`;
    if (!command || typeof command !== 'object' || Array.isArray(command)) { errors.push(`${label} must be an object.`); continue; }
    if (!AI_OPERATIONS.includes(command.op)) { errors.push(`${label} uses unsupported operation "${command.op}".`); continue; }
    const allowed = new Set(OPERATION_FIELDS[command.op] || ['op']);
    for (const key of Object.keys(command)) if (!allowed.has(key)) errors.push(`${label} (${command.op}) contains unsupported field "${key}".`);
    requireRef('page', command.pageRef, label, 'pageRef');
    requireRef('element', command.parentRef, label, 'parentRef');
    requireRef('grid', command.gridRef, label, 'gridRef');
    requireRef('component', command.componentRef, label, 'componentRef');
    requireRef('style', command.styleRef, label, 'styleRef');
    requireRef('data', command.sourceRef, label, 'sourceRef');
    targetRefs(command.target, `${label}.target`);
    targetRefs(command.parentTarget, `${label}.parentTarget`);
    targetRefs(command.reference, `${label}.reference`);

    if (command.op === 'create_page' || command.op === 'duplicate_page') addRef('page', command.ref, label);
    if (['create_element', 'create_svg', 'create_from_csv', 'create_image_frame', 'insert_asset', 'duplicate_element', 'instantiate_component'].includes(command.op)) addRef('element', command.ref, label);
    if (command.op === 'create_grid') addRef('grid', command.ref, label);
    if (command.op === 'create_component') addRef('component', command.ref, label);
    if (command.op === 'create_design_style') addRef('style', command.ref, label);
    if (command.op === 'create_data_source') addRef('data', command.ref, label);

    if (command.op === 'create_page' && command.page != null) validateObjectKeys(command.page, PAGE_FIELDS, `${label}.page`, errors);
    if (command.layout != null) validateObjectKeys(command.layout, LAYOUT_FIELDS, `${label}.layout`, errors);
    if (command.op === 'create_element') {
      validateElementInput(command.element, `${label}.element`, errors, warnings);
      if (!command.element?.type) errors.push(`${label}.element.type is required.`);
      if (command.layout && (Number.isFinite(Number(command.element?.x)) || Number.isFinite(Number(command.element?.y)))) warnings.push(`${label}: explicit x/y take precedence over layout placement.`);
    }
    if (command.op === 'create_svg') {
      if (typeof command.svg !== 'string' && typeof command.element?.svg !== 'string') errors.push(`${label}.svg is required.`);
      else try { sanitizeSvgMarkup(command.svg ?? command.element.svg); } catch (error) { errors.push(`${label}.svg: ${error.message}`); }
      if (command.element != null) validateElementInput({ ...command.element, type: 'svg' }, `${label}.element`, errors, warnings);
    }
    if (command.op === 'create_from_csv') {
      if (typeof command.csv !== 'string' || !command.csv.trim()) errors.push(`${label}.csv is required.`);
      if (command.mode != null && !['table', 'chart'].includes(command.mode)) errors.push(`${label}.mode must be "table" or "chart".`);
      if (command.element != null) validateElementInput(command.element, `${label}.element`, errors, warnings);
    }
    if (command.op === 'set_reference_image') {
      if (!command.assetId && !command.query) errors.push(`${label} requires assetId or query.`);
      if (command.mode != null && !['overlay', 'difference', 'split'].includes(command.mode)) errors.push(`${label}.mode must be overlay, difference, or split.`);
      if (command.fit != null && !['contain', 'cover', 'stretch'].includes(command.fit)) errors.push(`${label}.fit must be contain, cover, or stretch.`);
    }
    if (command.op === 'create_image_frame') {
      if (!command.element || typeof command.element !== 'object' || Array.isArray(command.element)) errors.push(`${label}.element is required and must be an object.`);
      else validateElementInput({ ...command.element, type: 'image' }, `${label}.element`, errors, warnings);
    }
    if (command.op === 'set_image_frame_asset' && !command.assetId && !command.query) errors.push(`${label} requires assetId or query.`);
    const targetRequired = new Set([
      'update_element', 'delete_element', 'duplicate_element', 'replace_text', 'replace_image', 'apply_style', 'set_image_frame_asset',
      'place_in_grid', 'set_gap', 'set_padding', 'equalize_size', 'match_size', 'align_to', 'place_relative', 'tidy_up',
      'fit_content', 'fit_text', 'anchor_to', 'repeat_layout', 'create_component', 'update_component', 'detach_component',
      'set_component_property', 'swap_component', 'set_variant', 'attach_design_style', 'bind_data', 'create_repeater'
    ]);
    if (targetRequired.has(command.op) && !command.target) errors.push(`${label}.target is required.`);
    if (command.op === 'update_element') {
      if (!command.patch || typeof command.patch !== 'object' || Array.isArray(command.patch)) errors.push(`${label}.patch is required and must be an object.`);
      else validateElementInput(command.patch, `${label}.patch`, errors, warnings);
    }
    if (command.op === 'apply_style') {
      if (!command.style || typeof command.style !== 'object' || Array.isArray(command.style)) errors.push(`${label}.style is required and must be an object.`);
      else validateElementInput({ style: command.style }, `${label}`, errors, warnings);
    }
    if (command.op === 'insert_asset' && !command.assetId && !command.query) errors.push(`${label} requires assetId or query.`);
    if (command.op === 'resize_design' && !(Number(command.width) > 0 && Number(command.height) > 0)) errors.push(`${label} requires positive width and height.`);
    if (command.op === 'create_grid') {
      if (!command.bounds || !(Number(command.bounds.width) > 0 && Number(command.bounds.height) > 0)) errors.push(`${label}.bounds requires positive width and height.`);
      if (!(Number(command.columns || 1) > 0 && Number(command.rows || 1) > 0)) errors.push(`${label} requires positive rows and columns.`);
    }
    if (command.op === 'create_design_style' && (!command.kind || !command.style)) errors.push(`${label} requires kind and style.`);
    if (command.op === 'set_print_settings' && (!command.settings || typeof command.settings !== 'object')) errors.push(`${label}.settings must be an object.`);
    if (command.op === 'create_data_source' && (!command.source || typeof command.source !== 'object')) errors.push(`${label}.source must be an object.`);
  }
  return { valid: errors.length === 0, errors, warnings };
}

export function applyCommandBatch(source, input, context = {}) {
  const validation = validateCommandBatch(input, { revision: context.revision });
  if (!validation.valid) throw new Error(validation.errors.join(' '));
  let document = normalizeDocument(source);
  const createdIds = [];
  const deletedIds = [];
  const warnings = [...(validation.warnings || [])];
  const selection = context.selection || [];
  let activePageIndex = context.pageIndex || 0;
  const pageRefs = new Map();
  const elementRefs = new Map();
  const gridRefs = new Map();
  const componentRefs = new Map();
  const styleRefs = new Map();
  const dataRefs = new Map();
  document.localComponents ||= [];
  const assets = context.assets || [];
  const brands = context.brands || [];
  const components = context.components || [];
  const allComponents = () => [...(document.localComponents || []), ...components];
  const resolveComponent = command => {
    const id = command.componentId || componentRefs.get(command.componentRef);
    return allComponents().find(component => component.id === id) || null;
  };
  const resolveGrid = (page, ref) => (page?.designGrids || []).find(grid => grid.id === gridRefs.get(ref) || grid.ref === ref || grid.id === ref) || null;
  const resolveStyleId = command => command.styleId || styleRefs.get(command.styleRef) || null;
  const resolveDataSourceId = command => command.sourceId || dataRefs.get(command.sourceRef) || null;
  const ensurePageCollections = page => {
    page.designGrids ||= [];
    page.baselineGrids ||= [];
    return page;
  };
  const registerCreated = (command, elements) => {
    const list = Array.isArray(elements) ? elements : [elements];
    createdIds.push(...list.filter(Boolean).map(element => element.id));
    if (command.ref && list[0]) elementRefs.set(command.ref, list[0].id);
  };
  const componentValues = (component, variantName, overrides = {}) => {
    const variant = (component?.variants || []).find(item => item.id === variantName || item.name === variantName);
    return { ...(variant?.values || {}), ...(overrides || {}) };
  };
  const applyComponentValues = (page, instanceId, component, values) => {
    const properties = new Map((component?.properties || []).map(property => [property.id, property]));
    for (const element of page.elements.filter(item => item.componentInstanceId === instanceId)) {
      const property = properties.get(element.componentPropertyId);
      if (!property) continue;
      const value = values[property.id] ?? values[property.name];
      if (value == null) continue;
      if (property.type === 'text' && element.type === 'text') element.text = String(value);
      else if (property.type === 'image' && element.type === 'image') {
        const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === value);
        if (asset) Object.assign(element, { assetId: asset.id, src: asset.preview_url || asset.url, nativeWidth: asset.width || 1000, nativeHeight: asset.height || 1000 });
        else if (typeof value === 'string') element.src = value;
      } else if (property.type === 'boolean') element.hidden = !value;
      element.componentVariant = values.__variant || element.componentVariant;
    }
  };

  const execute = command => {
    let page = pageFor(document, command, activePageIndex, pageRefs);
    if (command.op === 'set_document_title') document.title = safeString(command.title || command.value || 'Untitled design', 500) || 'Untitled design';
    else if (command.op === 'create_page') {
      const pageInput = command.page || {};
      const template = command.fromPageId ? document.pages.find(item => item.id === command.fromPageId) : null;
      const next = template ? clone(template) : defaultDocument(document.width, document.height).pages[0];
      next.id = uuid();
      next.name = safeString(pageInput.name || command.name || `Page ${document.pages.length + 1}`, 500);
      next.elements = command.copyElements && template ? next.elements.map(element => ({ ...element, id: uuid(), createdBy: 'ai' })) : [];
      next.regions = { ...defaultRegions(document.width, document.height), ...(pageInput.regions || command.regions || next.regions || {}) };
      if (pageInput.backgroundPaint || pageInput.background) {
        next.backgroundPaint = normalizePaint(pageInput.backgroundPaint ?? pageInput.background, '#ffffff');
        next.background = paintPrimaryColor(next.backgroundPaint, '#ffffff');
      }
      next.transparentBackground = !!pageInput.transparentBackground;
      if ((pageInput.width && Number(pageInput.width) !== document.width) || (pageInput.height && Number(pageInput.height) !== document.height)) warnings.push(`Page "${next.name}" requested ${pageInput.width || document.width} × ${pageInput.height || document.height}; Design Commons pages share the document size ${document.width} × ${document.height}.`);
      document.pages.push(next);
      activePageIndex = document.pages.length - 1;
      if (command.ref) pageRefs.set(command.ref, next.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'duplicate_page') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const copy = clone(page); copy.id = uuid(); copy.name = safeString(command.name || `${page.name} copy`, 500);
      const maps = {};
      copy.elements = cloneElementTree(copy.elements, { maps }).map(element => ({ ...element, createdBy: 'ai' }));
      const copiedGroups = (document.layoutGroups || []).filter(group => group.pageId === page.id).map(group => ({
        ...clone(group), id: maps.layoutMap?.get(group.id) || uuid(), pageId: copy.id,
        elementIds: group.elementIds.map(id => maps.idMap?.get(id)).filter(Boolean)
      }));
