      document.layoutGroups.push(...copiedGroups);
      const insertIndex = document.pages.indexOf(page) + 1;
      document.pages.splice(insertIndex, 0, copy);
      activePageIndex = insertIndex;
      if (command.ref) pageRefs.set(command.ref, copy.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'delete_page') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      if (document.pages.length <= 1) throw new Error('A design must contain at least one page.');
      const removedIndex = document.pages.indexOf(page);
      document.pages.splice(removedIndex, 1);
      activePageIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(activePageIndex, document.pages.length - 1));
    } else if (command.op === 'set_page_background') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      page.backgroundPaint = normalizePaint(command.paint ?? command.background ?? command.value, page.background || '#ffffff');
      page.background = paintPrimaryColor(page.backgroundPaint, page.background || '#ffffff');
      page.transparentBackground = page.backgroundPaint.type === 'none' || !!command.transparent;
    } else if (command.op === 'set_reference_image') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === command.assetId) || assets.find(item => String(item.original_name || item.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(String(command.query || '').toLowerCase()));
      if (!asset) throw new Error(`Reference asset not found: ${command.assetId || command.query || 'unspecified'}.`);
      page.referenceImage = {
        assetId: asset.id,
        src: asset.preview_url || asset.url,
        name: asset.original_name || asset.name || 'Reference image',
        opacity: clamp(command.opacity ?? .45, 0, 1),
        visible: command.visible !== false,
        mode: ['overlay', 'difference', 'split'].includes(command.mode) ? command.mode : 'overlay',
        fit: ['contain', 'cover', 'stretch'].includes(command.fit) ? command.fit : 'contain',
        split: clamp(command.split ?? .5, 0, 1)
      };
    } else if (command.op === 'clear_reference_image') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      page.referenceImage = null;
    } else if (command.op === 'set_region') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const name = safeString(command.name, 100);
      if (!name) throw new Error('Region name is required.');
      page.regions[name] = { x: Number(command.region?.x || 0), y: Number(command.region?.y || 0), width: clamp(command.region?.width || 1, 1, document.width), height: clamp(command.region?.height || 1, 1, document.height) };
    } else if (command.op === 'create_image_frame') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      if (page.elements.length >= MAX_AI_ELEMENTS) throw new Error(`Page element limit of ${MAX_AI_ELEMENTS} reached.`);
      const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === command.assetId) || assets.find(item => String(item.original_name || item.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(String(command.query || '').toLowerCase()));
      const elementInput = command.element || {};
      const element = asset
        ? imageElement(asset, sanitizePatch({ ...elementInput, isImageFrame: true }))
        : imageFrameElement(sanitizePatch({ ...elementInput, isImageFrame: true }));
      element.createdBy = 'ai';
      Object.assign(element, positionElement(document, page, element, command.layout || null, elementInput));
      const parent = resolveParent(page, command, selection, elementRefs);
      if (parent?.type === 'frame') element.parentId = parent.id;
      element.zIndex = page.elements.length;
      page.elements.push(element); createdIds.push(element.id);
      if (command.ref) elementRefs.set(command.ref, element.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'create_element') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      if (page.elements.length >= MAX_AI_ELEMENTS) throw new Error(`Page element limit of ${MAX_AI_ELEMENTS} reached.`);
      const elementInput = command.element || {};
      const element = elementFactory(elementInput);
      Object.assign(element, positionElement(document, page, element, command.layout || null, elementInput));
      const parent = resolveParent(page, command, selection, elementRefs);
      if (parent?.type === 'frame') element.parentId = parent.id;
      element.zIndex = page.elements.length;
      page.elements.push(element); createdIds.push(element.id);
      if (command.ref) elementRefs.set(command.ref, element.id);
      if (element.parentId) applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, page.elements.find(item => item.id === element.parentId));
    } else if (command.op === 'create_svg' || command.op === 'create_from_csv') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      if (page.elements.length >= MAX_AI_ELEMENTS) throw new Error(`Page element limit of ${MAX_AI_ELEMENTS} reached.`);
      const elementInput = command.op === 'create_svg' ? { ...(command.element || {}), type: 'svg', svg: command.svg ?? command.element?.svg } : (command.element || {});
      const element = command.op === 'create_svg' ? elementFactory(elementInput) : csvElement(command);
      element.createdBy = 'ai';
      Object.assign(element, positionElement(document, page, element, command.layout || null, elementInput));
      const parent = resolveParent(page, command, selection, elementRefs);
      if (parent?.type === 'frame') element.parentId = parent.id;
      element.zIndex = page.elements.length;
      page.elements.push(element); createdIds.push(element.id);
      if (command.ref) elementRefs.set(command.ref, element.id);
      if (element.parentId) applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, page.elements.find(item => item.id === element.parentId));
    } else if (command.op === 'insert_asset') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === command.assetId) || assets.find(item => String(item.original_name || '').toLowerCase().includes(String(command.query || '').toLowerCase()));
      if (!asset) throw new Error(`Asset not found: ${command.assetId || command.query || 'unspecified'}.`);
      const element = imageElement(asset, sanitizePatch({ role: command.role || 'hero-image', semanticName: command.semanticName || asset.original_name, tags: command.tags || asset.tags || [], createdBy: 'ai' }));
      Object.assign(element, positionElement(document, page, element, command.layout || null, {}));
      const parent = resolveParent(page, command, selection, elementRefs);
      if (parent?.type === 'frame') element.parentId = parent.id;
      element.zIndex = page.elements.length; page.elements.push(element); createdIds.push(element.id);
      if (command.ref) elementRefs.set(command.ref, element.id);
      if (element.parentId) applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, element.parentId);
    } else if (command.op === 'create_from_recipe') {
      const nested = recipeCommands(command.recipe, command, { document, assets, brands, components });
      for (const nestedCommand of nested) execute({ ...nestedCommand, pageId: command.pageId, pageIndex: command.pageIndex, pageRef: command.pageRef });
    } else if (['update_element', 'replace_text', 'replace_image', 'apply_style', 'set_image_frame_asset'].includes(command.op)) {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (!targets.length) warnings.push(`No editable elements matched ${JSON.stringify(command.target || {})}.`);
      for (const element of targets) {
        if (command.op === 'replace_text') {
          if (element.type !== 'text') continue;
          if (command.find != null) element.text = safeString(element.text, 50000).split(String(command.find)).join(safeString(command.replaceWith ?? command.text, 50000));
          else element.text = safeString(command.text ?? command.value, 50000);
        } else if (command.op === 'replace_image' || command.op === 'set_image_frame_asset') {
          if (element.type !== 'image') continue;
          const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === command.assetId) || assets.find(item => String(item.original_name || item.name || '').toLowerCase().includes(String(command.query || '').toLowerCase()));
          if (!asset) throw new Error(`Replacement asset not found: ${command.assetId}.`);
          Object.assign(element, { src: asset.preview_url || asset.url, assetId: asset.id, nativeWidth: asset.width || 1000, nativeHeight: asset.height || 1000, cropX: null, cropY: null, cropZoom: 1, ...(command.op === 'set_image_frame_asset' ? { isImageFrame: true } : {}) });
        } else {
          const patch = sanitizePatch(command.patch || command.style || {});
          Object.assign(element, patch);
          if (['x', 'y', 'width', 'height'].some(key => key in patch)) Object.assign(element, fitInsidePage(document, element));
        }
        element.appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
        if (element.type === 'frame') applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, element);
        if (element.parentId) {
          const parent = page.elements.find(item => item.id === element.parentId && item.type === 'frame');
          if (parent) applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, parent);
        }
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'delete_element') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const roots = new Set(targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs }).map(item => item.id));
      const targets = collectDescendantIds(page, roots);
      roots.forEach(id => targets.add(id));
      for (const id of targets) deletedIds.push(id);
      page.elements = page.elements.filter(element => !targets.has(element.id));
      document.layoutGroups = document.layoutGroups.filter(group => !group.elementIds.some(id => targets.has(id)));
      normalizeZ(page);
    } else if (command.op === 'duplicate_element') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const roots = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { elementRefs });
      const rootIds = new Set(roots.map(item => item.id));
      const descendantIds = collectDescendantIds(page, rootIds);
      const sourceElements = page.elements.filter(item => rootIds.has(item.id) || descendantIds.has(item.id));
      const copies = cloneElementTree(sourceElements, { offsetX: Number(command.offsetX ?? 24), offsetY: Number(command.offsetY ?? 24), preserveExternalParents: false })
        .map((copy, index) => ({ ...copy, createdBy: 'ai', sourceId: sourceElements[index]?.id || null, zIndex: page.elements.length + index }));
      for (const copy of copies) Object.assign(copy, fitInsidePage(document, copy));
      page.elements.push(...copies); createdIds.push(...copies.map(item => item.id));
      if (command.ref && copies[0]) elementRefs.set(command.ref, copies[0].id);
    } else if (command.op === 'apply_brand') {
      const brand = brands.find(item => item.id === command.brandId) || brands.find(item => String(item.title || '').toLowerCase() === String(command.brandName || '').toLowerCase()) || brands[0];
      if (!brand) throw new Error('No matching brand kit was found.');
      if (command.colors !== false) document = replaceColors(document, brand.colors || Object.values(brand.tokens?.colours || brand.tokens?.colors || {}));
      if (command.fonts !== false) document = replaceFonts(document, brand.fonts || Object.values(brand.tokens?.typography || {}).map(item => item.fontFamily).filter(Boolean));
      if (command.tokens !== false && brand.tokens) {
        document.designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
        document.designSystem.tokens = { ...document.designSystem.tokens, ...clone(brand.tokens), colors: { ...document.designSystem.tokens.colors, ...(brand.tokens.colors || brand.tokens.colours || {}) }, typography: { ...document.designSystem.tokens.typography, ...(brand.tokens.typography || {}) } };
      }
      if (command.styles !== false && brand.textStyles?.length) for (const style of brand.textStyles) upsertDesignStyle(document, 'text', { id: style.id, name: style.name || style.title, semanticRole: style.role || '', value: style.value || style });
    } else if (command.op === 'align' || command.op === 'distribute' || command.op === 'reorder' || command.op === 'create_auto_layout' || command.op === 'group' || command.op === 'ungroup') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target || { selected: true }, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (command.op === 'align') alignElements(page, targets, command.kind || 'center', document);
      if (command.op === 'distribute') distributeElements(targets, command.axis || 'horizontal');
      if (command.op === 'reorder') {
        const ids = new Set(targets.map(item => item.id));
        const picked = page.elements.filter(item => ids.has(item.id));
        const rest = page.elements.filter(item => !ids.has(item.id));
        page.elements = ['back', 'backward'].includes(command.position) ? [...picked, ...rest] : [...rest, ...picked]; normalizeZ(page);
      }
      if (command.op === 'create_auto_layout') document = createLayoutGroup(document, page.id, targets.map(item => item.id), command.layout || command);
      if (command.op === 'group' && targets.length >= 2) {
        const groupId = uuid();
        targets.forEach(item => { item.groupId = groupId; });
      }
      if (command.op === 'ungroup') {
        const groupIds = new Set(targets.map(item => item.groupId).filter(Boolean));
        page.elements.forEach(item => { if (groupIds.has(item.groupId)) item.groupId = null; });
        for (const frame of targets.filter(item => item.type === 'frame')) {
          page.elements.forEach(item => { if (item.parentId === frame.id) item.parentId = null; });
        }
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'create_grid') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      ensurePageCollections(page);
      const bounds = command.bounds || {};
      const grid = {
        id: uuid(), ref: command.ref || '', name: safeString(command.name || 'Grid', 160),
        x: clamp(bounds.x || 0, 0, document.width), y: clamp(bounds.y || 0, 0, document.height),
        width: clamp(bounds.width || document.width, 1, document.width), height: clamp(bounds.height || document.height, 1, document.height),
        columns: Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(command.columns || 1))), rows: Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(command.rows || 1))),
        columnGap: Math.max(0, Number(command.columnGap || 0)), rowGap: Math.max(0, Number(command.rowGap || 0)), padding: Math.max(0, Number(command.padding || 0))
      };
      page.designGrids.push(grid);
      if (command.ref) gridRefs.set(command.ref, grid.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'place_in_grid') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const grid = resolveGrid(page, command.gridRef);
      if (!grid) throw new Error(`Grid not found: ${command.gridRef}.`);
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const order = Array.isArray(command.order) ? command.order : [];
      const sorted = order.length ? [...targets].sort((a, b) => order.indexOf(a.id) - order.indexOf(b.id)) : [...targets].sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
      const innerW = grid.width - grid.padding * 2, innerH = grid.height - grid.padding * 2;
      const cellW = Math.max(1, (innerW - grid.columnGap * Math.max(0, grid.columns - 1)) / grid.columns);
      const cellH = Math.max(1, (innerH - grid.rowGap * Math.max(0, grid.rows - 1)) / grid.rows);
      const start = Math.max(0, Number(command.start || 0));
      sorted.forEach((element, index) => {
        const cell = start + index, column = cell % grid.columns, row = Math.floor(cell / grid.columns);
        if (row >= grid.rows) return;
        const colSpan = Math.max(1, Math.min(grid.columns - column, Number(command.span?.columns || 1)));
        const rowSpan = Math.max(1, Math.min(grid.rows - row, Number(command.span?.rows || 1)));
        Object.assign(element, {
          x: grid.x + grid.padding + column * (cellW + grid.columnGap),
          y: grid.y + grid.padding + row * (cellH + grid.rowGap),
          width: cellW * colSpan + grid.columnGap * (colSpan - 1),
          height: cellH * rowSpan + grid.rowGap * (rowSpan - 1)
        });
        if (element.type === 'frame') applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, element);
      });
    } else if (command.op === 'set_gap' || command.op === 'set_padding') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      for (const element of targets.filter(item => item.type === 'frame')) {
        element.layout = { ...(element.layout || {}) };
        if (command.op === 'set_gap') Object.assign(element.layout, { gap: Math.max(0, Number(command.gap ?? element.layout.gap ?? 0)), rowGap: Math.max(0, Number(command.rowGap ?? command.gap ?? element.layout.rowGap ?? 0)), columnGap: Math.max(0, Number(command.columnGap ?? command.gap ?? element.layout.columnGap ?? 0)) });
        else element.layout.padding = typeof command.padding === 'object' ? { top: Math.max(0, Number(command.padding.top || 0)), right: Math.max(0, Number(command.padding.right || 0)), bottom: Math.max(0, Number(command.padding.bottom || 0)), left: Math.max(0, Number(command.padding.left || 0)) } : Math.max(0, Number(command.padding || 0));
        applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, element);
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'equalize_size') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (!targets.length) return;
      const strategy = command.strategy || 'max';
      const choose = values => strategy === 'min' ? Math.min(...values) : strategy === 'average' ? values.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) / values.length : strategy === 'first' ? values[0] : Math.max(...values);
      const width = choose(targets.map(item => item.width)), height = choose(targets.map(item => item.height));
      targets.forEach(item => { if (command.axis !== 'height') item.width = width; if (command.axis !== 'width') item.height = height; if (item.type === 'frame') applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, item); });
    } else if (command.op === 'match_size') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const reference = firstTarget(page, command.reference, selection, elementRefs);
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (!reference) throw new Error('Reference element not found.');
      targets.forEach(item => { if (command.axis !== 'height') item.width = reference.width; if (command.axis !== 'width') item.height = reference.height; if (item.type === 'frame') applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, item); });
    } else if (command.op === 'align_to') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const reference = firstTarget(page, command.reference, selection, elementRefs);
      const box = reference || resolveRegion(document, page, command.reference?.region || 'safe');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const gap = Number(command.gap || 0);
      for (const item of targets) {
        if (command.kind === 'left') item.x = box.x + gap;
        else if (command.kind === 'center') item.x = box.x + (box.width - item.width) / 2;
        else if (command.kind === 'right') item.x = box.x + box.width - item.width - gap;
        else if (command.kind === 'top') item.y = box.y + gap;
        else if (command.kind === 'middle') item.y = box.y + (box.height - item.height) / 2;
        else if (command.kind === 'bottom') item.y = box.y + box.height - item.height - gap;
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'place_relative') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const reference = firstTarget(page, command.reference, selection, elementRefs);
      if (!reference) throw new Error('Reference element not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const gap = Number(command.gap || 0);
      for (const item of targets) {
        if (command.side === 'left') item.x = reference.x - item.width - gap;
        else if (command.side === 'right') item.x = reference.x + reference.width + gap;
        else if (command.side === 'above') item.y = reference.y - item.height - gap;
        else item.y = reference.y + reference.height + gap;
        if (['left', 'right'].includes(command.side)) item.y = command.align === 'end' ? reference.y + reference.height - item.height : command.align === 'center' ? reference.y + (reference.height - item.height) / 2 : reference.y;
        else item.x = command.align === 'end' ? reference.x + reference.width - item.width : command.align === 'center' ? reference.x + (reference.width - item.width) / 2 : reference.x;
        Object.assign(item, fitInsidePage(document, item));
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'tidy_up') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (!targets.length) return;
      const columns = Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(command.columns || Math.ceil(Math.sqrt(targets.length)))));
      const rows = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(targets.length / columns));
      const left = Math.min(...targets.map(item => item.x)), top = Math.min(...targets.map(item => item.y));
      const width = Math.max(...targets.map(item => item.x + item.width)) - left, height = Math.max(...targets.map(item => item.y + item.height)) - top;
      const columnGap = Math.max(0, Number(command.columnGap ?? 24)), rowGap = Math.max(0, Number(command.rowGap ?? 24));
      const cellW = Math.max(...targets.map(item => item.width)), cellH = Math.max(...targets.map(item => item.height));
      targets.sort((a, b) => a.y - b.y || a.x - b.x).forEach((item, index) => { item.x = left + (index % columns) * (cellW + columnGap); item.y = top + Math.floor(index / columns) * (cellH + rowGap); });
      if (cellW * columns + columnGap * (columns - 1) > width || cellH * rows + rowGap * (rows - 1) > height) warnings.push('Tidy-up expanded the selection bounds to preserve the requested gaps.');
    } else if (command.op === 'fit_content') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      for (const element of targets) {
        if (element.type === 'frame') {
          element.layout = { ...(element.layout || {}), ...(command.axis !== 'height' ? { widthMode: 'hug' } : {}), ...(command.axis !== 'width' ? { heightMode: 'hug' } : {}) };
          applyDocumentFrameLayout(page, element);
        } else if (element.type === 'text') {
          const lines = String(element.text || '').split('\n').length;
          if (command.axis !== 'height') element.width = Math.min(document.width - element.x, Math.max(20, String(element.text || '').length * Number(element.fontSize || 48) * .55));
          if (command.axis !== 'width') element.height = Math.max(1, lines * Number(element.fontSize || 48) * Number(element.lineHeight || 1.16));
        }
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'fit_text') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs }).filter(item => item.type === 'text');
      for (const element of targets) {
        element.autoFit = true;
        element.minFontSize = Math.max(4, Number(command.minFontSize || element.minFontSize || 8));
        element.maxLines = Math.max(0, Number(command.maxLines ?? element.maxLines ?? 0));
        element.overflowBehavior = 'clip';
        const charsPerLine = Math.max(1, element.width / Math.max(4, Number(element.fontSize || 48) * .55));
        const estimatedLines = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(String(element.text || '').length / charsPerLine));
        const required = estimatedLines * Number(element.fontSize || 48) * Number(element.lineHeight || 1.16);
        if (required > element.height) element.fontSize = Math.max(element.minFontSize, Number(element.fontSize || 48) * element.height / required);
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'anchor_to') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      targets.forEach(element => { element.constraints = { ...(element.constraints || {}), horizontal: command.horizontal || element.constraints?.horizontal || 'scale', vertical: command.vertical || element.constraints?.vertical || 'scale', maintainAspectRatio: command.maintainAspectRatio ?? element.constraints?.maintainAspectRatio ?? false }; });
    } else if (command.op === 'repeat_layout') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const roots = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      if (!roots.length) return;
      const rootIds = new Set(roots.map(item => item.id)), descendantIds = collectDescendantIds(page, rootIds);
      const sourceElements = page.elements.filter(item => rootIds.has(item.id) || descendantIds.has(item.id));
      const count = Math.max(1, Math.min(1000, Number(command.count || command.data?.length || 1)));
      const direction = command.direction || 'vertical', gap = Math.max(0, Number(command.gap || 24)), columns = Math.max(1, Number(command.columns || 1));
      const bounds = { width: Math.max(...roots.map(item => item.x + item.width)) - Math.min(...roots.map(item => item.x)), height: Math.max(...roots.map(item => item.y + item.height)) - Math.min(...roots.map(item => item.y)) };
      for (let index = 1; index < count; index++) {
        const column = direction === 'grid' ? index % columns : direction === 'horizontal' ? index : 0;
        const row = direction === 'grid' ? Math.floor(index / columns) : direction === 'vertical' ? index : 0;
        const copies = cloneElementTree(sourceElements, { offsetX: column * (bounds.width + gap), offsetY: row * (bounds.height + gap), preserveExternalParents: false }).map((item, offset) => ({ ...item, createdBy: 'ai', zIndex: page.elements.length + offset }));
        const dataRow = command.data?.[index];
        if (dataRow) for (const element of copies.filter(item => item.type === 'text')) if (element.contentKey && dataRow[element.contentKey] != null) element.text = String(dataRow[element.contentKey]);
        page.elements.push(...copies); registerCreated({}, copies);
        if (command.refPrefix && copies[0]) elementRefs.set(`${command.refPrefix}-${index + 1}`, copies[0].id);
      }
    } else if (command.op === 'create_component') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const component = { id: uuid(), ...componentFromElements(targets, command.title || 'Component', { properties: command.properties, variants: command.variants, description: command.description }), linked: true };
      document.localComponents.push(component);
      if (command.ref) componentRefs.set(command.ref, component.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'instantiate_component') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const component = resolveComponent(command);
      if (!component) throw new Error(`Component not found: ${command.componentId || command.componentRef}.`);
      const elements = instantiateComponent(component, Number(command.x || 120), Number(command.y || 120), { linked: command.linked !== false, overrides: command.overrides || {}, variant: command.variant });
      elements.forEach((element, index) => { element.zIndex = page.elements.length + index; element.createdBy = 'ai'; });
      page.elements.push(...elements); registerCreated(command, elements);
      applyAllFrameLayouts(page);
    } else if (command.op === 'update_component') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const component = resolveComponent(command);
      if (!component || !document.localComponents.some(item => item.id === component.id)) throw new Error('Only document-local components can be updated by a command bundle.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      Object.assign(component, componentFromElements(targets, command.title || component.title, { properties: command.properties || component.properties, variants: command.variants || component.variants, description: component.description }));
    } else if (command.op === 'detach_component') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const instanceIds = new Set(targets.map(item => item.componentInstanceId).filter(Boolean));
      page.elements.forEach(element => { if (instanceIds.has(element.componentInstanceId)) { element.componentId = null; element.componentInstanceId = null; element.componentLinked = false; element.componentPropertyId = null; } });
    } else if (command.op === 'set_component_property' || command.op === 'set_variant') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const target = firstTarget(page, command.target, selection, elementRefs);
      if (!target?.componentInstanceId) throw new Error('Target is not a component instance.');
      const component = allComponents().find(item => item.id === target.componentId);
      if (!component) throw new Error('Component definition not found.');
      const values = command.op === 'set_variant' ? { ...componentValues(component, command.variant), __variant: command.variant } : { [command.property]: command.value };
      applyComponentValues(page, target.componentInstanceId, component, values);
    } else if (command.op === 'swap_component') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const target = firstTarget(page, command.target, selection, elementRefs);
      const component = resolveComponent(command);
      if (!target?.componentInstanceId || !component) throw new Error('A component instance and replacement component are required.');
      const instanceElements = page.elements.filter(item => item.componentInstanceId === target.componentInstanceId);
      const left = Math.min(...instanceElements.map(item => item.x)), top = Math.min(...instanceElements.map(item => item.y));
      const ids = new Set(instanceElements.map(item => item.id));
      page.elements = page.elements.filter(item => !ids.has(item.id));
      const elements = instantiateComponent(component, left, top, { linked: true, overrides: command.overrides || {}, variant: command.variant });
      elements.forEach((element, index) => { element.zIndex = page.elements.length + index; element.createdBy = 'ai'; });
      page.elements.push(...elements); registerCreated({}, elements);
    } else if (command.op === 'create_variant') {
      const component = resolveComponent(command);
      if (!component || !document.localComponents.some(item => item.id === component.id)) throw new Error('Only document-local components can receive variants.');
      component.variants ||= [];
      component.variants.push({ id: command.id || uuid(), name: command.name || `Variant ${component.variants.length + 1}`, values: clone(command.values || {}) });
    } else if (command.op === 'create_design_style') {
      const style = upsertDesignStyle(document, command.kind, command.style);
      if (command.ref) styleRefs.set(command.ref, style.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'update_design_style') {
      const styleId = resolveStyleId(command), system = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
      const current = system.styles?.[command.kind]?.find(style => style.id === styleId);
      if (!current) throw new Error(`Design style not found: ${styleId}.`);
      upsertDesignStyle(document, command.kind, { ...current, ...(command.patch || {}), value: { ...(current.value || {}), ...(command.patch?.value || {}) } });
    } else if (command.op === 'delete_design_style') {
      deleteDesignStyle(document, command.kind, resolveStyleId(command), { detach: command.detach !== false });
    } else if (command.op === 'attach_design_style') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      attachDesignStyle(document, targets, command.kind, resolveStyleId(command));
    } else if (command.op === 'deduplicate_styles') {
      const result = mergeDuplicateDesignStyles(document); document = result.document; warnings.push(`Merged ${result.groups.length} duplicate design-style group${result.groups.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}.`);
    } else if (command.op === 'set_print_settings') {
      document.print = normalizePrintSettings({ ...(document.print || {}), ...(command.settings || {}) }, document.width, document.height);
    } else if (command.op === 'create_data_source') {
      const source = createDataSource(document, command.source || {});
      if (command.ref) dataRefs.set(command.ref, source.id);
    } else if (command.op === 'bind_data') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const targets = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      const sourceId = resolveDataSourceId(command);
      targets.forEach(element => { element.dataBinding = { sourceId, row: Math.max(0, Number(command.row || 0)), key: command.key || '', template: command.template || '' }; });
      applyDataBindings(document);
    } else if (command.op === 'create_repeater') {
      if (!page) throw new Error('Page not found.');
      const sourceId = resolveDataSourceId(command), source = document.dataSources?.find(item => item.id === sourceId);
      if (!source) throw new Error('Data source not found.');
      const startRow = Math.max(0, Number(command.startRow || 0)), rows = source.rows.slice(startRow, startRow + Math.max(1, Number(command.count || source.rows.length)));
      execute({ op: 'repeat_layout', pageId: page.id, target: command.target, count: rows.length, direction: command.direction || 'vertical', gap: command.gap || 24, columns: command.columns || 1, data: rows, allowAll: command.allowAll });
      const roots = targetElements(page, command.target, selection, { allowAll: command.allowAll === true, elementRefs });
      roots.forEach(element => { if (element.type === 'text' && element.contentKey && rows[0]?.[element.contentKey] != null) element.text = String(rows[0][element.contentKey]); });
    } else if (command.op === 'detach_auto_layout') {
      document = detachLayoutGroup(document, command.groupId);
    } else if (command.op === 'resize_design') {
      document = resizeDocument(document, clamp(command.width, 1, 20000), clamp(command.height, 1, 20000));
      document.pages.forEach(item => { item.regions = { ...defaultRegions(document.width, document.height), ...(command.preserveRegions ? item.regions : {}) }; });
    }
  };

  for (const command of input.commands) execute(command);
  for (const page of document.pages || []) applyAllFrameLayouts(page);
  applyLinkedStyles(document);
  applyDataBindings(document);
  document = normalizeDocument(document);
  return { document, createdIds, deletedIds, warnings };
}

function estimatedTextMetrics(element) {
  if (element.type !== 'text') return undefined;
  const fontSize = Number(element.fontSize || 48), lineHeight = Number(element.lineHeight || 1.16);
  const charsPerLine = Math.max(1, Math.floor(Math.max(20, element.width) / Math.max(4, fontSize * .55)));
  const lines = String(element.text || '').split('\n').reduce((sum, line) => sum + Math.max(1, Math.ceil(line.length / charsPerLine)), 0);
  const estimatedHeight = lines * fontSize * lineHeight;
  return { charsPerLine, estimatedLines: lines, estimatedHeight: Math.round(estimatedHeight), overflow: estimatedHeight > element.height * 1.02, baselineStep: Math.round(fontSize * lineHeight * 100) / 100 };
}

function elementSnapshot(element, page = null) {
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  const children = page ? page.elements.filter(item => item.parentId === element.id).map(item => item.id) : [];
  return {
    id: element.id,
    type: element.type,
    name: element.name,
    role: element.role,
    semanticName: element.semanticName,
    contentKey: element.contentKey || undefined,
    tags: element.tags || [],
    text: element.type === 'text' ? safeString(element.text, 2000) : undefined,
    svg: element.type === 'svg' ? safeString(element.svg, 1000) : undefined,
    bounds: { x: Math.round(element.x), y: Math.round(element.y), width: Math.round(element.width), height: Math.round(element.height), rotation: Math.round(Number(element.rotation || 0) * 100) / 100 },
    typography: element.type === 'text' ? {
      textStyleId: element.textStyleId || null,
      fontFamily: element.fontFamily,
      fontSize: element.fontSize,
      fontWeight: element.fontWeight,
      fontStyle: element.fontStyle,
      lineHeight: element.lineHeight,
      charSpacing: element.charSpacing,
      textAlign: element.textAlign,
      verticalAlign: element.verticalAlign,
      autoFit: !!element.autoFit,
      minFontSize: element.minFontSize,
      maxLines: element.maxLines,
      overflowBehavior: element.overflowBehavior,
      columnsCount: element.columnsCount || 1,
      columnGap: element.columnGap || 0,
      hyphenation: !!element.hyphenation,
      widowLines: element.widowLines || 0,
      orphanLines: element.orphanLines || 0,
      metrics: estimatedTextMetrics(element)
    } : undefined,
    appearance: {
      fill: element.fill,
      stroke: element.stroke,
      strokeWidth: element.strokeWidth,
      radius: element.radius,
      opacity: element.opacity,
      fills: appearance.fills,
      strokes: appearance.strokes,
      shadows: appearance.shadows,
      effects: appearance.effects,
      blendMode: appearance.blendMode,
      styleRefs: { fillStyleId: element.fillStyleId || null, effectStyleId: element.effectStyleId || null, strokeStyleId: element.strokeStyleId || null, radiusStyleId: element.radiusStyleId || null, spacingStyleId: element.spacingStyleId || null }
    },
    layout: element.type === 'frame' ? element.layout : undefined,
    layoutSizing: element.layoutSizing,
    constraints: element.constraints,
    hierarchy: { parentId: element.parentId || null, childIds: children, groupId: element.groupId || null, zIndex: element.zIndex },
    component: element.componentId ? { componentId: element.componentId, componentInstanceId: element.componentInstanceId, linked: !!element.componentLinked, propertyId: element.componentPropertyId || null, variant: element.componentVariant || null } : null,
    dataBinding: element.dataBinding || null,
    image: element.type === 'image' ? { assetId: element.assetId || null, nativeWidth: element.nativeWidth, nativeHeight: element.nativeHeight, cropX: element.cropX, cropY: element.cropY, cropZoom: element.cropZoom, focalPoint: { x: element.cropAnchorX, y: element.cropAnchorY }, mask: element.mask, filters: element.filters, isImageFrame: !!element.isImageFrame } : undefined,
    hidden: !!element.hidden,
    locked: !!element.locked,
    aiEditable: element.aiEditable !== false,
    userLocked: !!element.userLocked
  };
}

export function createAIContext({ document, design, pageIndex = 0, selection = [], assets = [], brands = [], components = [], revision = 0, renderUrl = null, renders = [], annotation = null }) {
  const normalized = normalizeDocument(document);
  const page = normalized.pages[pageIndex] || normalized.pages[0];
  const visualRenders = (renders?.length ? renders : (renderUrl ? [{ url: renderUrl, pageIndex }] : []))
    .filter(item => item?.url)
    .map(item => ({ url: item.url, pageIndex: item.pageIndex ?? pageIndex, pageName: normalized.pages[item.pageIndex ?? pageIndex]?.name || `Page ${(item.pageIndex ?? pageIndex) + 1}`, createdAt: item.createdAt || null }));
  const analysis = analyzeDocument(normalized);
  const allComponents = [...(normalized.localComponents || []), ...(components || [])];
  return {
    schemaVersion: 2,
    design: { id: design?.id || null, title: normalized.title, revision, width: normalized.width, height: normalized.height, unit: normalized.unit, dpi: normalized.dpi, pageCount: normalized.pages.length, schemaVersion: normalized.schemaVersion },
    print: normalized.print,
    designSystem: normalized.designSystem,
    dataSources: (normalized.dataSources || []).map(source => ({ id: source.id, name: source.name, columns: source.columns, rowCount: source.rows.length, previewRows: source.rows.slice(0, 5) })),
    currentPage: { index: pageIndex, id: page.id, name: page.name, background: page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, referenceImage: page.referenceImage || null, regions: page.regions, grid: page.grid, designGrids: page.designGrids || [], margins: page.margins, elements: page.elements.map(element => elementSnapshot(element, page)), analysis: analyzePage(normalized, page) },
    pages: normalized.pages.map((item, index) => ({ index, id: item.id, name: item.name, background: item.backgroundPaint ?? item.background, regions: item.regions, grid: item.grid, designGrids: item.designGrids || [], margins: item.margins, elementCount: item.elements.length, elements: item.elements.map(element => elementSnapshot(element, item)), analysis: analysis.pages[index] })),
    selection: page.elements.filter(element => selection.includes(element.id)).map(element => elementSnapshot(element, page)),
    assets: assets.slice(0, 250).map(asset => ({ id: asset.id, name: asset.original_name, tags: asset.tags || [], width: asset.width, height: asset.height, url: asset.preview_url || asset.url, description: asset.description || '', type: asset.asset_type || asset.type || 'image', focalPoint: asset.focal_point || null, sourceType: asset.source_type || asset.sourceType || '' })),
    assetPlanning: { canGenerateRaster: true, canGenerateSvg: true, maxRequestsPerPass: 16, supportedAspectRatios: AI_ASSET_ASPECT_RATIOS, supportedKinds: AI_ASSET_KINDS },
    brands: brands.map(brand => ({ id: brand.id, title: brand.title, colors: brand.colors || [], fonts: brand.fonts || [], logos: brand.logos || [], textStyles: brand.textStyles || [], tokens: brand.tokens || null, designRules: brand.designRules || [] })),
    components: allComponents.slice(0, 100).map(component => ({ id: component.id, title: component.title, description: component.description || '', category: component.category, tags: component.tags || [], linked: !!component.linked, width: component.width, height: component.height, properties: component.properties || [], variants: component.variants || [], elementCount: component.elements?.length || 0, elements: (component.elements || []).slice(0, 80).map(element => elementSnapshot(element)) })),
    designAnalysis: analysis,
    fonts: FONT_FAMILIES,
    fontStatus: getFontLoadReport(FONT_FAMILIES),
    capabilities: getAICapabilities(),
    render: visualRenders[0] || null,
    renders: visualRenders,
    annotation: annotation ? { attached: true, pageIndex: annotation.pageIndex ?? pageIndex, sourceUrl: annotation.sourceUrl || null, width: annotation.width || null, height: annotation.height || null, strokeCount: annotation.actions?.length || 0 } : null
  };
}

export function diffDocuments(before, after) {
  const oldDoc = normalizeDocument(before); const newDoc = normalizeDocument(after);
  const oldElements = new Map(oldDoc.pages.flatMap(page => page.elements.map(element => [element.id, { pageId: page.id, element }])));
  const newElements = new Map(newDoc.pages.flatMap(page => page.elements.map(element => [element.id, { pageId: page.id, element }])));
  const added = [...newElements].filter(([id]) => !oldElements.has(id)).map(([, value]) => elementSnapshot(value.element));
  const removed = [...oldElements].filter(([id]) => !newElements.has(id)).map(([, value]) => elementSnapshot(value.element));
  const changed = [];
  for (const [id, next] of newElements) {
    const previous = oldElements.get(id); if (!previous) continue;
    const fields = [];
    for (const key of ['name', 'role', 'semanticName', 'text', 'svg', 'fontFamily', 'fontSize', 'x', 'y', 'width', 'height', 'rotation', 'opacity', 'fill', 'src', 'assetId', 'hidden', 'locked', 'parentId', 'groupId']) if (JSON.stringify(previous.element[key]) !== JSON.stringify(next.element[key])) fields.push(key);
    if (JSON.stringify(previous.element.appearance) !== JSON.stringify(next.element.appearance)) fields.push('appearance');
    if (fields.length) changed.push({ ...elementSnapshot(next.element), fields });
  }
  return { pagesBefore: oldDoc.pages.length, pagesAfter: newDoc.pages.length, added, removed, changed, summary: `${added.length} added, ${removed.length} removed, ${changed.length} changed` };
}

function luminance(hex) {
  const value = String(hex || '#000000').replace('#', '');
  if (!/^[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(value)) return null;
  const rgb = [0, 2, 4].map(index => parseInt(value.slice(index, index + 2), 16) / 255).map(channel => channel <= .03928 ? channel / 12.92 : ((channel + .055) / 1.055) ** 2.4);
  return .2126 * rgb[0] + .7152 * rgb[1] + .0722 * rgb[2];
}

export function lintDocument(source) {
  const document = normalizeDocument(source);
  const issues = [];
  const push = (severity, rule, message, pageId, elementId = null, suggestedFix = null, suggestedCommands = null, metadata = null) => issues.push({
    id: uuid(), severity, rule, message, pageId, elementId,
    suggestedFix: suggestedFix || suggestedCommands?.[0] || null,
    suggestedCommands: suggestedCommands || (suggestedFix ? [suggestedFix] : []),
    metadata: metadata || undefined
  });
  const pageScores = [];
  const print = normalizePrintSettings(document.print, document.width, document.height);

  for (const page of document.pages) {
    const pageIssueStart = issues.length;
    const visible = page.elements.filter(element => !element.hidden);
    for (const element of visible) {
      if (element.x < 0 || element.y < 0 || element.x + element.width > document.width || element.y + element.height > document.height) push('warning', 'out-of-bounds', `${element.name || element.type} extends outside the page.`, page.id, element.id, { op: 'update_element', pageId: page.id, target: { id: element.id }, patch: { x: clamp(element.x, 0, Math.max(0, document.width - element.width)), y: clamp(element.y, 0, Math.max(0, document.height - element.height)) } });
      const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
      const smallerSide = Math.max(1, Math.min(Number(element.width || 1), Number(element.height || 1)));
      const maximumReasonableStroke = Math.max(64, smallerSide * .75);
      const oversizedStroke = appearance.strokes.filter(stroke => stroke.enabled).find(stroke => Number(stroke.width || 0) > maximumReasonableStroke);
      if (oversizedStroke) push('critical', 'oversized-stroke', `${element.name || element.type} has a ${Math.round(oversizedStroke.width)}px stroke that can cover the page.`, page.id, element.id, { op: 'update_element', pageId: page.id, target: { id: element.id }, patch: { stroke: element.stroke || 'transparent', strokeWidth: Number(element.strokeWidth || 0) } });

      const safe = print.safeArea || {};
      const safeBounds = { x: Number(safe.left || page.margins?.left || 0), y: Number(safe.top || page.margins?.top || 0), width: document.width - Number(safe.left || page.margins?.left || 0) - Number(safe.right || page.margins?.right || 0), height: document.height - Number(safe.top || page.margins?.top || 0) - Number(safe.bottom || page.margins?.bottom || 0) };
      if (['text', 'qrcode', 'logo'].includes(element.type) || ['headline', 'body', 'caption', 'legal', 'footer', 'logo'].includes(element.role)) {
        if (element.x < safeBounds.x || element.y < safeBounds.y || element.x + element.width > safeBounds.x + safeBounds.width || element.y + element.height > safeBounds.y + safeBounds.height) push('warning', 'outside-safe-area', `${element.name || element.type} extends beyond the configured print-safe area.`, page.id, element.id, { op: 'align_to', pageId: page.id, target: { id: element.id }, reference: { region: 'safe' }, kind: element.y + element.height > safeBounds.y + safeBounds.height ? 'bottom' : element.y < safeBounds.y ? 'top' : element.x < safeBounds.x ? 'left' : 'right', gap: 0 });
      }

      if (element.type === 'text') {
        if (!String(element.text || '').trim()) push('warning', 'empty-text', `${element.name || 'Text'} is empty.`, page.id, element.id);
        if ((element.fontSize || 0) < 12) push('warning', 'small-text', `${element.name || 'Text'} may be too small to read.`, page.id, element.id);
        const fontReport = getFontLoadReport([element.fontFamily || 'Arial'])[0];
        if (fontReport && ['fallback', 'unavailable'].includes(fontReport.status)) push('warning', 'font-fallback', `${element.name || 'Text'} requests ${element.fontFamily}, but that font is not confirmed as loaded. Export may use a fallback.`, page.id, element.id);
        const metrics = estimatedTextMetrics(element);
        if (metrics.overflow && !element.autoFit) push('warning', 'text-overflow', `${element.name || 'Text'} may overflow its text box.`, page.id, element.id, { op: 'fit_text', pageId: page.id, target: { id: element.id }, minFontSize: Math.max(8, element.minFontSize || 8), maxLines: element.maxLines || 0 });
        const fg = luminance(typeof element.fill === 'string' ? element.fill : paintPrimaryColor(element.appearance?.fill, '#111827'));
        const parent = element.parentId ? page.elements.find(item => item.id === element.parentId) : null;
        const backgroundColor = parent?.fill || page.background || '#ffffff';
        const bg = luminance(backgroundColor);
        if (fg != null && bg != null) { const ratio = (Math.max(fg, bg) + .05) / (Math.min(fg, bg) + .05); if (ratio < 3) push('warning', 'low-contrast', `${element.name || 'Text'} has low contrast against its background.`, page.id, element.id, null, null, { contrastRatio: Math.round(ratio * 100) / 100 }); }
        const explicitLines = String(element.text || '').split('\n');
        const lastLine = explicitLines.at(-1)?.trim() || '';
        if (explicitLines.length > 1 && lastLine.split(/\s+/).length === 1 && lastLine.length < 12) push('info', 'orphan-line', `${element.name || 'Text'} ends with a short orphan line ("${lastLine}").`, page.id, element.id, { op: 'fit_content', pageId: page.id, target: { id: element.id }, axis: 'width' });
        if (/\b[A-Z]{2,}[a-z]+\b/.test(String(element.text || '')) && element.role === 'item-name') push('info', 'awkward-capitalization', `${element.name || 'Text'} contains unusual internal capitalization; verify that the line break and word treatment are intentional.`, page.id, element.id);
      }
      if (element.type === 'image' && element.isImageFrame && !element.assetId) push('warning', 'empty-image-frame', `${element.name || 'Image frame'} does not contain a managed asset yet.`, page.id, element.id);
      if (element.type === 'svg') {
        const inspection = inspectSvgMarkup(element.svg || '');
        for (const issue of inspection.issues.slice(0, 3)) push(inspection.valid ? 'info' : 'warning', 'svg-validation', `${element.name || 'SVG'}: ${issue}`, page.id, element.id);
      }
      if (element.type === 'image' && element.nativeWidth && element.nativeHeight) {
        const scale = Math.max(element.width / element.nativeWidth, element.height / element.nativeHeight);
        const effectiveDpi = Math.min(element.nativeWidth / Math.max(.01, element.width / document.dpi), element.nativeHeight / Math.max(.01, element.height / document.dpi));
        if (scale > 1.5 || effectiveDpi < print.minimumEffectiveDpi) push('warning', 'low-resolution-image', `${element.name || 'Image'} has an effective resolution of about ${Math.round(effectiveDpi)} DPI.`, page.id, element.id, null, null, { effectiveDpi: Math.round(effectiveDpi), minimumDpi: print.minimumEffectiveDpi });
        if (!element.assetId && /^https?:/i.test(element.src || '')) push('info', 'external-image', `${element.name || 'Image'} uses an external URL instead of a managed asset.`, page.id, element.id);
      }
    }

    const textElements = visible.filter(item => item.type === 'text').slice(0, 300);
    for (let firstIndex = 0; firstIndex < textElements.length; firstIndex++) for (let secondIndex = firstIndex + 1; secondIndex < textElements.length; secondIndex++) {
      const first = textElements[firstIndex], second = textElements[secondIndex];
      const overlapWidth = Math.max(0, Math.min(first.x + first.width, second.x + second.width) - Math.max(first.x, second.x));
      const overlapHeight = Math.max(0, Math.min(first.y + first.height, second.y + second.height) - Math.max(first.y, second.y));
      const overlapArea = overlapWidth * overlapHeight;
      const smallerArea = Math.max(1, Math.min(first.width * first.height, second.width * second.height));
      if (overlapArea / smallerArea > .58) push('critical', 'text-overlap', `${first.name || 'Text'} substantially overlaps ${second.name || 'another text element'}.`, page.id, first.id);
    }

    const stacks = new Map();
    for (const item of textElements) { const key = `${Math.round(item.x / 12)}:${Math.round(item.y / 12)}`; stacks.set(key, (stacks.get(key) || 0) + 1); }
    if ([...stacks.values()].some(count => count >= 4)) push('critical', 'stacked-text', 'Four or more text elements are stacked at nearly the same position. The command bundle likely lost its intended geometry.', page.id);

    const roleGroups = new Map();
    for (const item of textElements.filter(item => item.role)) {
      if (!roleGroups.has(item.role)) roleGroups.set(item.role, []);
      roleGroups.get(item.role).push(item);
    }
    for (const [role, items] of roleGroups) {
      if (items.length < 2) continue;
      const signatures = new Map();
      for (const item of items) {
        const signature = [item.fontFamily, Math.round(item.fontSize * 10) / 10, item.fontWeight, Math.round((item.lineHeight || 1.16) * 100) / 100, item.fill].join('|');
        if (!signatures.has(signature)) signatures.set(signature, []);
        signatures.get(signature).push(item);
      }
      if (signatures.size > 1) {
        const canonical = [...signatures.values()].sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length)[0][0];
        const inconsistent = items.filter(item => ![canonical.fontFamily, Math.round(canonical.fontSize * 10) / 10, canonical.fontWeight, Math.round((canonical.lineHeight || 1.16) * 100) / 100, canonical.fill].every((value, index) => value === [item.fontFamily, Math.round(item.fontSize * 10) / 10, item.fontWeight, Math.round((item.lineHeight || 1.16) * 100) / 100, item.fill][index]));
        push('warning', 'inconsistent-typography-role', `${items.length} "${role}" text elements use ${signatures.size} different typography treatments.`, page.id, canonical.id, null, inconsistent.map(item => ({ op: 'update_element', pageId: page.id, target: { id: item.id }, patch: { fontFamily: canonical.fontFamily, fontSize: canonical.fontSize, fontWeight: canonical.fontWeight, lineHeight: canonical.lineHeight, fill: canonical.fill } })), { role, elementIds: items.map(item => item.id) });
      }
    }

    const fonts = new Set(textElements.map(item => item.fontFamily).filter(Boolean));
    if (fonts.size > 4) push('info', 'too-many-fonts', `Page uses ${fonts.size} fonts; consider reducing the number for consistency.`, page.id);

    const candidates = visible.filter(item => item.type === 'frame' || (item.role === 'container' && ['rect', 'frame'].includes(item.type)));
    const repeated = new Map();
    for (const item of candidates) {
      const key = `${String(item.semanticName || item.role || item.name).toLowerCase()}|${Math.round(item.width / 12)}|${Math.round(item.height / 12)}`;
      if (!repeated.has(key)) repeated.set(key, []); repeated.get(key).push(item);
    }
    for (const items of repeated.values()) {
      if (items.length < 2) continue;
      const radii = new Set(items.map(item => Math.round(Number(item.radius || 0))));
      const paddings = new Set(items.map(item => JSON.stringify(item.layout?.padding || 0)));
      const shadowSignatures = new Set(items.map(item => JSON.stringify(normalizeAppearance(item).shadows.filter(shadow => shadow.enabled).map(shadow => ({ blur: shadow.blur, offsetX: shadow.offsetX, offsetY: shadow.offsetY, opacity: shadow.opacity })))));
      const canonical = items[0];
      const fixes = [];
      for (const item of items.slice(1)) fixes.push({ op: 'update_element', pageId: page.id, target: { id: item.id }, patch: { radius: canonical.radius, layout: item.type === 'frame' ? { ...(item.layout || {}), padding: canonical.layout?.padding || 0 } : item.layout, appearance: canonical.appearance } });
      if (radii.size > 1 || paddings.size > 1 || shadowSignatures.size > 1) push('warning', 'inconsistent-repeated-component', `${items.length} repeated card-like elements have inconsistent radius, padding, or shadow treatment.`, page.id, canonical.id, null, fixes, { elementIds: items.map(item => item.id) });
      const leftOffsets = items.map(frame => {
        const children = visible.filter(child => child.parentId === frame.id);
        return children.length ? Math.min(...children.map(child => child.x - frame.x)) : null;
      }).filter(Number.isFinite);
      if (leftOffsets.length > 1 && Math.max(...leftOffsets) - Math.min(...leftOffsets) > 4) push('warning', 'inconsistent-card-padding', `Repeated cards use inconsistent left padding (${Math.round(Math.min(...leftOffsets))}–${Math.round(Math.max(...leftOffsets))}px).`, page.id, canonical.id, { op: 'set_padding', pageId: page.id, target: { ids: items.map(item => item.id) }, padding: canonical.layout?.padding || Math.round(leftOffsets[0]) });
    }

    const edgeKinds = [
      ['left', item => item.x], ['right', item => item.x + item.width], ['top', item => item.y], ['bottom', item => item.y + item.height]
    ];
    for (const [kind, getter] of edgeKinds) {
      for (let i = 0; i < visible.length; i++) for (let j = i + 1; j < visible.length; j++) {
        const a = visible[i], b = visible[j], difference = Math.abs(getter(a) - getter(b));
        const crossOverlap = ['left', 'right'].includes(kind)
          ? Math.max(0, Math.min(a.y + a.height, b.y + b.height) - Math.max(a.y, b.y))
          : Math.max(0, Math.min(a.x + a.width, b.x + b.width) - Math.max(a.x, b.x));
        if (difference >= 3 && difference <= 10 && crossOverlap > 8) {
          push('info', 'near-misalignment', `${a.name || a.type} and ${b.name || b.type} are nearly, but not exactly, ${kind}-aligned (${Math.round(difference)}px difference).`, page.id, b.id, { op: 'align_to', pageId: page.id, target: { id: b.id }, reference: { id: a.id }, kind });
          if (issues.length - pageIssueStart > 120) break;
        }
      }
    }

    const duplicateStyles = findDuplicateDesignStyles(document);
    if (duplicateStyles.length) push('info', 'duplicate-design-styles', `${duplicateStyles.length} duplicate linked-style group${duplicateStyles.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} can be merged.`, page.id, null, { op: 'deduplicate_styles' });
    const analysis = analyzePage(document, page);
    pageScores.push({ pageId: page.id, pageName: page.name, ...scoreDesign(issues.slice(pageIssueStart), analysis) });
  }

  if (print.colorSpace === 'cmyk' && print.iccProfile.toLowerCase().includes('srgb')) push('warning', 'print-profile-mismatch', 'The document is set to CMYK but still uses an sRGB ICC profile.', document.pages[0]?.id || null);
  if (print.outlineFonts && print.embedFonts) push('info', 'font-output-options', 'Both font embedding and outlining are enabled; outlined text will no longer be searchable or editable in the exported PDF.', document.pages[0]?.id || null);

  const counts = issues.reduce((acc, issue) => ({ ...acc, [issue.severity]: (acc[issue.severity] || 0) + 1 }), {});
  const overall = pageScores.length ? Math.round(pageScores.reduce((sum, page) => sum + page.overall, 0) / pageScores.length) : 100;
  const categories = pageScores.length ? Object.fromEntries(Object.keys(pageScores[0].categories).map(key => [key, Math.round(pageScores.reduce((sum, page) => sum + page.categories[key], 0) / pageScores.length)])) : scoreDesign([], null).categories;
  return { issues, counts, score: { overall, categories, pages: pageScores }, safeFixCount: issues.filter(issue => issue.suggestedCommands?.length).length };
}

function quotedStrings(text) {
  return [...String(text).matchAll(/[“"]([^”"]+)[”"]/g)].map(match => match[1].trim()).filter(Boolean);
}

export function localPlan(instruction, context, options = {}) {
  const text = String(instruction || '').trim();
  try {
    const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
    const batch = Array.isArray(parsed) ? { schemaVersion: 1, commands: parsed } : parsed;
    if (Array.isArray(batch?.commands)) return { ...batch, schemaVersion: 1, baseRevision: context.design.revision, instruction: text, source: 'json' };
  } catch {}
  const lower = text.toLowerCase(); const commands = [];
  const svgMatch = text.match(/<svg\b[\s\S]*?<\/svg\s*>/i);
  const csvMatch = text.match(/```csv\s*([\s\S]*?)```/i) || text.match(/(?:^|\n)csv\s*:\s*\n([\s\S]+)/i);
  if (svgMatch) commands.push({ op: 'create_svg', svg: svgMatch[0], element: { name: 'AI custom SVG', role: 'decoration', width: Math.min(420, context.design.width * .45), height: Math.min(420, context.design.height * .45) }, layout: { region: 'safe', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'middle' } });
  if (csvMatch) commands.push({ op: 'create_from_csv', mode: /chart|graph/.test(lower) ? 'chart' : 'table', csv: csvMatch[1].trim(), element: { width: Math.min(720, context.design.width * .8), height: Math.min(420, context.design.height * .45) }, layout: { region: 'content', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'middle' } });
  if (options.useBrand !== false && context.brands.length && /brand|branded|brand kit|use my colours|use my colors/.test(lower)) commands.push({ op: 'apply_brand', brandId: options.brandId || context.brands[0].id });
  const size = lower.match(/(\d{2,5})\s*[x×]\s*(\d{2,5})/);
  if (size) commands.push({ op: 'resize_design', width: Number(size[1]), height: Number(size[2]) });
  const backgroundHex = lower.match(/background(?: color| colour)?\s*(?:to|is|:)?\s*(#[0-9a-f]{6})/i);
  if (backgroundHex) commands.push({ op: 'set_page_background', paint: solidPaint(backgroundHex[1]) });
  const replace = text.match(/replace\s+[“"]?(.+?)[”"]?\s+with\s+[“"]?(.+?)[”"]?(?:\.|$)/i);
  if (replace) commands.push({ op: 'replace_text', target: { type: 'text', all: true }, allowAll: true, find: replace[1].trim(), replaceWith: replace[2].trim() });
  if (/delete|remove/.test(lower) && options.scope === 'selection' && context.selection.length) commands.push({ op: 'delete_element', target: { selected: true } });
  if (/center|centre/.test(lower) && options.scope === 'selection' && context.selection.length) commands.push({ op: 'align', target: { selected: true }, kind: 'center' });
  if (/distribute/.test(lower) && options.scope === 'selection' && context.selection.length >= 3) commands.push({ op: 'distribute', target: { selected: true }, axis: /vertical/.test(lower) ? 'vertical' : 'horizontal' });
  if (!svgMatch && !csvMatch && /create|design|make|generate/.test(lower)) {
    const quoted = quotedStrings(text); const lines = text.split('\n').map(line => line.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    const headline = options.headline || quoted[0] || lines.find(line => line.length < 90) || 'New design';
    const offer = options.offer || quoted[1] || '';
    const cta = options.cta || quoted[2] || '';
    const matchingAsset = context.assets.find(asset => lower.includes(String(asset.name || '').toLowerCase())) || context.assets.find(asset => (asset.tags || []).some(tag => lower.includes(String(tag).toLowerCase()))) || context.assets[0];
    const recipe = /cocktail|drink menu/.test(lower) ? 'cocktail-menu' : /restaurant|food menu|menu/.test(lower) ? 'restaurant-menu' : /price list|pricing/.test(lower) ? 'price-list' : /invitation|invite/.test(lower) ? 'invitation' : /report cover|cover page/.test(lower) ? 'report-cover' : /business card/.test(lower) ? 'business-card' : /brochure/.test(lower) ? 'brochure' : /presentation|slide/.test(lower) ? 'presentation' : /catalog/.test(lower) ? 'product-catalogue' : /infographic/.test(lower) ? 'infographic' : /poster|event/.test(lower) ? 'event-poster' : 'social-promotion';
    commands.push({ op: 'create_from_recipe', recipe, inputs: { title: headline, headline, subtitle: offer, offer, cta, assetId: options.useAssets === false ? null : matchingAsset?.id, brandKitId: options.brandId || context.brands[0]?.id } });
  }
  if (!commands.length) commands.push({ op: 'update_element', target: options.scope === 'selection' ? { selected: true } : { role: 'headline' }, patch: { semanticName: 'AI reviewed element' } });
  return { schemaVersion: 1, baseRevision: context.design.revision, instruction: text, commands, source: 'local-fallback' };
}

// FILE: src/ai/handoff.js
