import { getAICapabilities, validateCommandBatch } from './engine.js';

const DEFAULT_SKILLS_PATH = 'SKILLS.md';
const safeJson = value => JSON.stringify(value, null, 2);

function findBalancedJsonCandidates(text) {
  const source = String(text || '');
  const candidates = [];
  for (let start = 0; start < source.length; start++) {
    const opener = source[start];
    if (opener !== '{' && opener !== '[') continue;
    const stack = [];
    let quoted = false;
    let escaped = false;
    for (let index = start; index < source.length; index++) {
      const char = source[index];
      if (quoted) {
        if (escaped) escaped = false;
        else if (char === '\\') escaped = true;
        else if (char === '"') quoted = false;
        continue;
      }
      if (char === '"') { quoted = true; continue; }
      if (char === '{' || char === '[') stack.push(char);
      if (char === '}' || char === ']') {
        const expected = char === '}' ? '{' : '[';
        if (stack.at(-1) !== expected) break;
        stack.pop();
        if (!stack.length) {
          candidates.push(source.slice(start, index + 1));
          start = index;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return candidates;
}

function commandEnvelope(value) {
  const envelope = value?.commandBatch || value?.batch || value?.result || value;
  return Array.isArray(envelope) || Array.isArray(envelope?.commands);
}

export function extractLLMJson(input) {
  if (input && typeof input === 'object') return input;
  const text = String(input || '').trim();
  if (!text) throw new Error('Paste the command response from the LLM first.');
  const candidates = [];
  for (const match of text.matchAll(/```(?:json|javascript|js)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/gi)) candidates.push(match[1].trim());
  candidates.push(text, ...findBalancedJsonCandidates(text));
  const parsed = [];
  for (const candidate of [...new Set(candidates.filter(Boolean))]) {
    try { parsed.push(JSON.parse(candidate)); } catch {}
  }
  const bundles = parsed.filter(commandEnvelope);
  if (bundles.length) {
    return bundles.map((value, index) => {
      const envelope = value?.commandBatch || value?.batch || value?.result || value;
      const commands = Array.isArray(envelope) ? envelope : envelope?.commands;
      return { value, index, score: (commands?.length || 0) * 1000 + (envelope?.schemaVersion ? 100 : 0) + index };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)[0].value;
  }
  if (parsed.length === 1) return parsed[0];
  throw new Error('No valid Design Commons command bundle was found. Paste the JSON object that contains a commands array. Design Commons ignored instruction text and unrelated JSON examples.');
}

export function normalizeLLMCommandBatch(input, { revision = null, instruction = '' } = {}) {
  const parsed = extractLLMJson(input);
  const envelope = parsed?.commandBatch || parsed?.batch || parsed?.result || parsed;
  const batch = Array.isArray(envelope) ? { commands: envelope } : { ...envelope };
  if (!Array.isArray(batch.commands)) throw new Error('The LLM response must contain a commands array.');
  batch.schemaVersion = Number(batch.schemaVersion || 1);
  if (!Number.isInteger(batch.baseRevision) && Number.isInteger(revision)) batch.baseRevision = revision;
  if (!batch.instruction && instruction) batch.instruction = String(instruction).slice(0, 5000);
  const validation = validateCommandBatch(batch, { revision });
  if (!validation.valid) throw new Error(validation.errors.join(' '));
  return batch;
}

export function commandExamples(revision = 0) {
  return [
    {
      title: 'Create a positioned headline',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [{
          op: 'create_element',
          element: { type: 'text', role: 'headline', semanticName: 'Main headline', text: 'Taco Tuesday', fontFamily: 'Montserrat', fontSize: 92, fontWeight: 700, fill: '#111827', x: 90, y: 80, width: 640, height: 140, textAlign: 'center', autoFit: true }
        }]
      }
    },
    {
      title: 'Create and target a new page',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [
          { op: 'create_page', ref: 'second-page', page: { name: 'Second page' } },
          { op: 'set_page_background', pageRef: 'second-page', paint: { type: 'solid', color: '#fffdf8', opacity: 1 } },
          { op: 'create_element', pageRef: 'second-page', element: { type: 'text', role: 'headline', text: 'Drink Menu', fontFamily: 'Allura', fontSize: 76, fill: '#4fa64f', width: 600, height: 120 }, layout: { region: 'header', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'middle' } }
        ]
      }
    },
    {
      title: 'Create a safe custom SVG',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [{
          op: 'create_svg',
          svg: '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path fill="#4f46e5" d="M50 5 95 95H5Z"/></svg>',
          element: { name: 'Triangle motif', role: 'decoration', x: 620, y: 60, width: 120, height: 120 }
        }]
      }
    },
    {
      title: 'Create a table from CSV',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [{ op: 'create_from_csv', mode: 'table', csv: 'Item,Qty,Price\nTacos,2,$12\nChurros,1,$6', headerRows: 1, element: { x: 90, y: 260, width: 620, height: 300 } }]
      }
    },
    {
      title: 'Update a semantic element',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [{ op: 'update_element', target: { role: 'headline' }, patch: { text: 'Three tacos for $15', fontSize: 84 } }]
      }
    },
    {
      title: 'Insert an asset and render',
      batch: {
        schemaVersion: 1,
        baseRevision: revision,
        commands: [{ op: 'insert_asset', assetId: 'USE_AN_ASSET_ID_FROM_CONTEXT', role: 'hero-image', layout: { region: 'hero', align: 'center', verticalAlign: 'middle', width: 860, height: 520 } }]
      }
    }
  ];
}

export function createLLMInstructions(context, options = {}) {
  const capabilities = context?.capabilities || getAICapabilities();
  const scope = options.scope || 'page';
  const pageRule = scope === 'selection'
    ? 'Modify only elements in context.selection.'
    : scope === 'page'
      ? 'Modify the current page unless the request explicitly requires another page.'
      : 'You may modify the whole design.';
  return `You are controlling Design Commons, a structured visual-design editor.

Your task is to translate the user's design request into a safe Design Commons command bundle.

OUTPUT REQUIREMENTS
1. Return exactly one JSON object. Do not return markdown, commentary, or code-fence markers.
2. Use this shape: {"schemaVersion":1,"baseRevision":${context?.design?.revision ?? 0},"instruction":"brief summary","theme":{...},"assetRequests":[...],"commands":[...]}. theme and assetRequests are optional.
3. Use only operations and fields shown in capabilities.operationSchemas. Unknown fields are rejected.
4. Use element IDs, asset IDs, semantic roles, regions, brands, components, and fonts from the supplied context. Never invent an existing ID.
5. Prefer semantic targets such as {"role":"headline"} or exact IDs over broad all-element changes.
6. Respect aiEditable:false and userLocked elements. Do not try to bypass protection.
7. Keep all objects inside the ${context?.design?.width || 1080} × ${context?.design?.height || 1080} page.
8. Preserve the user's existing work unless the request explicitly asks for a redesign.
9. For destructive operations, target exact IDs. Never delete all elements unless explicitly requested.
10. The active scope is ${scope}. ${pageRule}
11. When using an image, choose an assetId from context.assets.
12. Use only font families listed in context.fonts or capabilities.fonts.
13. For absolute placement, put x, y, width, and height directly on element. Do not also use layout alignment. Prefer frames, grids, components, linked styles, and relative placement over long lists of independent absolute coordinates.
14. For automatic placement, omit element.x and element.y and use layout.region/alignment.
15. When creating a page, assign create_page.ref and use pageRef on every later command for that page. Assign ref to important newly created elements, grids, components, design styles, and data sources; target them later with parentRef, target.ref, gridRef, componentRef, styleRef, or sourceRef.
16. Use create_svg for custom vector artwork. Supply a complete SVG root or a path beginning with M/m. Do not include scripts, event handlers, foreignObject, embedded HTML, external images, or external URLs.
17. Use create_from_csv to turn CSV data into an editable table or chart.
18. Break dense documents into separate heading, item-name, description, and price text elements. Set autoFit:true where text length may vary. Repeated cards must be frames or component instances with one shared structure, not separately improvised groups.
19. After commands are applied, CanvasForge can render a PNG. If context.render.url is present, use it as visual evidence for iterative improvement. Visual attachments may include both a clean render and a structural inspection image with labelled object bounds; use the inspection labels to connect screenshot geometry to context element IDs.
20. If context.currentPage.referenceImage exists, treat it as the visual target. Match its layout while keeping the reference non-exporting.
21. Use create_image_frame for circular or masked photos and set_image_frame_asset to fill an existing frame.
22. Check context.fontStatus before relying on a display font. Prefer fonts whose status is loaded; warn in instruction when a fallback may occur.
23. Use text autoFit with minFontSize, maxLines, and overflowBehavior for dense layouts instead of guessing text height.
24. One or more page screenshots may be attached after this prompt. Inspect them as visual evidence and reconcile them with context.pages and object bounds.
25. If an annotated screenshot is attached, treat the user's drawn arrows, boxes, and marks as spatial instructions. The marks are not design content and must not be recreated unless explicitly requested.
26. For document scope, inspect every supplied page screenshot and use pageRef/pageIndex deliberately. Do not accidentally apply page-one geometry to every page.
27. Use context.designAnalysis, page.analysis, linked design styles, spacing tokens, alignment lines, repeated-pattern detection, and print settings as constraints.
28. Use create_grid/place_in_grid, set_padding/set_gap, tidy_up, equalize_size, align_to, and place_relative for coherent geometry.
29. Use create_component/instantiate_component and named component properties for repeated content.
30. Use create_design_style/attach_design_style for repeated typography, colour, radius, spacing, stroke, and effect treatments.
31. Keep text, logos, QR codes, and essential content inside the configured print safe area and respect bleed/trim settings.
32. Aim to improve the design score without adding unnecessary decoration. Resolve critical checks first, then alignment, typography, spacing, repeated-component consistency, contrast, and print readiness.
33. Establish one coherent page theme before choosing assets. Put the theme in the optional top-level theme object using capabilities.assetPlanning.theme.
34. Inventory context.assets before requesting generation. Use reuseAssetId when an existing asset fits. Use assetRequests only for important missing illustrations, photos, textures, icons, or decorative motifs.
35. Every asset request must have a stable key, a production-ready prompt, kind, aspectRatio, transparency choice, purpose, role, placementHint, and consistency with the page theme. Do not request text baked into images.
36. When the workflow provides generated asset IDs in the user instruction, use those exact IDs with insert_asset, create_image_frame, or set_image_frame_asset. Do not request the same asset again.
37. A manual asset-planning response may return an empty commands array while still returning theme and assetRequests. A final design response should place the resolved assets and return the complete command bundle.

ASSET PLANNING CONTRACT
${safeJson(capabilities.assetPlanning || {})}

OPERATION CONTRACTS
${safeJson(capabilities.operationSchemas || {})}

ELEMENT CONTRACT
${safeJson(capabilities.elementSchema || {})}

ELEMENT TYPES
${(capabilities.elementTypes || []).join(', ')}

TARGET FIELDS
${(capabilities.targetFields || []).join(', ')}

PAGE TARGET FIELDS
${(capabilities.pageTargetFields || []).join(', ')}

SEMANTIC ROLES
${(capabilities.semanticRoles || []).join(', ')}

AVAILABLE FONTS
${(capabilities.fonts || []).join(', ')}

CANONICAL PATTERNS
- Absolute element: {"op":"create_element","element":{"type":"text","x":80,"y":80,"width":600,"height":120,"text":"Headline","fontFamily":"Montserrat","fontSize":64,"fill":"#111827"}}
- Region element: {"op":"create_element","element":{"type":"text","width":600,"height":120,"text":"Headline","fontFamily":"Montserrat","fontSize":64,"fill":"#111827"},"layout":{"region":"header","align":"center","verticalAlign":"middle"}}
- New page: {"op":"create_page","ref":"page-two","page":{"name":"Page two"}}
- Target new page: {"op":"set_page_background","pageRef":"page-two","paint":{"type":"solid","color":"#111827","opacity":1}}
- Update: {"op":"update_element","target":{"id":"..."},"patch":{"fontSize":72}}
- Custom SVG: {"op":"create_svg","svg":"<svg xmlns=\\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\\" viewBox=\\"0 0 100 100\\"><path d=\\"M...Z\\"/></svg>","element":{"x":100,"y":100,"width":300,"height":300}}
- CSV table: {"op":"create_from_csv","mode":"table","csv":"Item,Qty\\nTacos,2","element":{"x":80,"y":200,"width":620,"height":300}}
- Insert image: {"op":"insert_asset","assetId":"...","role":"hero-image","layout":{"region":"hero","align":"center","verticalAlign":"middle"}}
- Reference image: {"op":"set_reference_image","assetId":"...","opacity":0.45,"mode":"overlay","fit":"contain"}
- Image frame: {"op":"create_image_frame","assetId":"...","element":{"x":60,"y":220,"width":150,"height":150,"mask":"circle"}}
- Structured card: {"op":"create_element","ref":"card","element":{"type":"frame","x":60,"y":300,"width":330,"height":260,"layout":{"direction":"vertical","gap":12,"padding":24}}}
- Child by ref: {"op":"create_element","parentRef":"card","element":{"type":"text","role":"item-name","text":"Item name","width":280,"height":70,"layoutSizing":{"width":"fill","height":"fixed"}}}
- Grid: {"op":"create_grid","ref":"card-grid","bounds":{"x":60,"y":300,"width":688,"height":560},"columns":2,"rows":2,"columnGap":28,"rowGap":28}
- Place cards: {"op":"place_in_grid","target":{"semanticName":"Menu card"},"gridRef":"card-grid"}
- Linked text style: {"op":"create_design_style","ref":"item-title-style","kind":"text","style":{"name":"Menu item title","value":{"fontFamily":"DM Serif Display","fontSize":31,"fontWeight":700,"lineHeight":1.05}}}
- Attach style: {"op":"attach_design_style","target":{"role":"item-name"},"styleRef":"item-title-style","kind":"text","allowAll":true}`;
}

export function createLLMHandoffPackage({ context, request = '', scope = 'page', skillsUrl = DEFAULT_SKILLS_PATH, apiBase = '', visuals = [] } = {}) {
  if (!context) throw new Error('No AI context is available.');
  const instructions = createLLMInstructions(context, { scope });
  const examples = commandExamples(context.design.revision);
  const endpointBase = apiBase || '';
  const endpoints = {
    skills: `${endpointBase}/api/ai/skills`,
    capabilities: `${endpointBase}/api/ai/capabilities`,
    context: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/context`,
    validate: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/commands/validate`,
    preview: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/commands/preview`,
    apply: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/commands/apply`,
    render: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/render`,
    agentConcepts: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/agent/concepts`,
    agentCompile: `${endpointBase}/api/designs/${context.design.id || ':designId'}/ai/agent/compile`,
    imageGenerate: `${endpointBase}/api/ai/images/generate`
  };
  const visualManifest = visuals.length ? visuals.map((item, index) => ({
    order: index + 1,
    label: item.label || `Visual ${index + 1}`,
    pageIndex: item.pageIndex ?? null,
    kind: item.kind || 'page-render',
    attachedSeparately: true
  })) : [];
  const visualSection = visualManifest.length
    ? `

VISUAL ATTACHMENTS
${safeJson(visualManifest)}
These images are attached to this request in the listed order. Inspect them before writing commands.`
    : `

VISUAL ATTACHMENTS
No image is attached. Rely on structured context only.`;
  const prompt = `${instructions}

DESIGN COMMONS SKILL
${skillsUrl}

USER REQUEST
${request.trim() || 'Create or improve the design according to the context and return a command bundle.'}${visualSection}

DESIGN COMMONS CONTEXT
${safeJson(context)}

EXAMPLES
${safeJson(examples.map(item => item.batch))}

Return only the JSON command bundle.`;
  return {
    schemaVersion: 1,
    generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    skillsUrl,
    instructions,
    request,
    context,
    visuals: visualManifest,
    capabilities: context.capabilities || getAICapabilities(),
    examples,
    endpoints,
    prompt
  };
}

const MODE_KEY = 'canvasforge-ai-mode';

export const AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS = {
  fast: {
    id: 'fast',
    name: 'Fast',
    description: 'Lowest credit cost for quick edits and straightforward layouts.',
    supportsRaster: true,
    supportsSvg: true
  },
  balanced: {
    id: 'balanced',
    name: 'Balanced',
    description: 'Recommended quality and cost for most design work.',
    supportsRaster: true,
    supportsSvg: true
  },
  best: {
    id: 'best',
    name: 'Best quality',
    description: 'Highest-quality model route for complex layouts and image work.',
    supportsRaster: true,
    supportsSvg: true
  }
};

export function loadAIProviderSettings() {
  const activeMode = globalThis.localStorage?.getItem(MODE_KEY) || 'balanced';
  return { activeMode: AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS[activeMode] ? activeMode : 'balanced' };
}

export function saveAIProviderSettings(input = {}) {
  const activeMode = AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS[input.activeMode] ? input.activeMode : 'balanced';
  globalThis.localStorage?.setItem(MODE_KEY, activeMode);
  return { activeMode };
}

export async function sourceToDataUrl(source) {
  if (!source) return null;
  if (typeof source === 'string' && source.startsWith('data:')) return source;
  if (source instanceof Blob) return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => resolve(reader.result);
    reader.onerror = () => reject(reader.error || new Error('Could not read image input.'));
    reader.readAsDataURL(source);
  });
  const response = await fetch(String(source), { credentials: 'include' });
  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Could not load visual context (${response.status}).`);
  return sourceToDataUrl(await response.blob());
}

export async function dataUrlToFile(dataUrl, filename) {
  const response = await fetch(dataUrl);
  const blob = await response.blob();
  return new File([blob], filename, { type: blob.type || 'application/octet-stream' });
}

// FILE: src/ai/visuals.js

export async function sourceToBlob(source) {
  if (!source) throw new Error('No image is available.');
  const response = await fetch(source, { credentials: 'include' });
  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Could not load image (${response.status}).`);
  return response.blob();
}

async function blobToPng(blob) {
  if (blob.type === 'image/png') return blob;
  const bitmap = await createImageBitmap(blob);
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  canvas.width = bitmap.width;
  canvas.height = bitmap.height;
  canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(bitmap, 0, 0);
  bitmap.close?.();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => canvas.toBlob(result => result ? resolve(result) : reject(new Error('Could not convert image to PNG.')), 'image/png'));
}

export async function copyImageToClipboard(source) {
  if (!navigator.clipboard?.write || typeof ClipboardItem === 'undefined') throw new Error('This browser cannot copy images directly. Open the image and copy it from there.');
  const blob = await blobToPng(await sourceToBlob(source));
  await navigator.clipboard.write([new ClipboardItem({ 'image/png': blob })]);
}

export function downloadSource(source, filename = 'canvasforge-ai-context.png') {
  const anchor = document.createElement('a');
  anchor.href = source;
  anchor.download = filename;
  anchor.rel = 'noopener';
  anchor.click();
}

function Login() {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [ownerToken, setOwnerToken] = useState('');
  const [mode, setMode] = useState('signin');
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);
  const login = useEditorStore(state => state.login);
  const register = useEditorStore(state => state.register);
  const tokenLogin = useEditorStore(state => state.tokenLogin);
  const submit = async event => {
    event.preventDefault(); setBusy(true); setError('');
    try {
      if (mode === 'register') await register({ name, email, password });
      else if (mode === 'token') await tokenLogin(ownerToken);
      else await login(email, password);
    } catch (nextError) { setError(nextError.message); }
    finally { setBusy(false); }
  };
  return <main className="login-screen">
    <div className="login-theme"><ThemeToggle compact/></div>
    <form onSubmit={submit}>
      <div className="auth-brand"><span>DC</span><div><h1>{APP_NAME}</h1><p>Design, collaborate, and create with AI.</p></div></div>
      <div className="segmented"><button type="button" className={mode === 'signin' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setMode('signin')}>Sign in</button><button type="button" className={mode === 'register' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setMode('register')}>Create account</button></div>
      {mode === 'token' ? <label>Owner token<input autoFocus type="password" value={ownerToken} onChange={event => setOwnerToken(event.target.value)}/></label> : <>
        {mode === 'register' && <label>Your name<input autoFocus value={name} onChange={event => setName(event.target.value)} required/></label>}
        <label>Email<input autoFocus={mode === 'signin'} type="email" value={email} onChange={event => setEmail(event.target.value)} required/></label>
        <label>Password<input type="password" minLength={mode === 'register' ? 10 : undefined} value={password} onChange={event => setPassword(event.target.value)} required/></label>
      </>}
      <button className="primary auth-submit" disabled={busy}>{busy ? (mode === 'register' ? 'Creating account…' : 'Signing in…') : (mode === 'register' ? 'Create personal workspace' : mode === 'token' ? 'Use owner token' : 'Sign in')}</button>
      {error && <div className="error">{error}</div>}
      <button type="button" className="auth-owner-link" onClick={() => setMode(mode === 'token' ? 'signin' : 'token')}>{mode === 'token' ? 'Back to account sign in' : 'Self-hosted owner access'}</button>
      {mode === 'register' && <small>A personal workspace is created automatically. You can create or join organizations later.</small>}
    </form>
  </main>;
}

function InviteAccept({ token }) {
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const apply = useEditorStore(state => state.applyAuth);
  return <main className="login-screen"><form onSubmit={async event => { event.preventDefault(); try { apply(await api.acceptInvite({ token, name, password })); } catch (nextError) { setError(nextError.message); } }}>
    <div className="auth-brand"><span>DC</span><div><h1>Join {APP_NAME}</h1><p>Accept your workspace invitation.</p></div></div>
    <label>Your name<input value={name} onChange={event => setName(event.target.value)} required/></label>
    <label>Create password<input type="password" minLength="10" value={password} onChange={event => setPassword(event.target.value)} required/></label>
    <button className="primary auth-submit">Accept invitation</button>{error && <div className="error">{error}</div>}
  </form></main>;
}

function SharedViewer({ token }) {
  const [data, setData] = useState(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const load = async () => {
    try {
      const result = await api.publicShare(token, password);
      setData(result);
      useEditorStore.setState({ design: result.design, document: result.design.document, pageIndex: 0, selection: [] });
    } catch (nextError) { setError(nextError.message); }
  };
  const copyDesign = () => {
    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data.design.document, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const anchor = document.createElement('a');
    anchor.href = url;
    anchor.download = `${designFileName(data.design.title)}.design-commons.json`;
    anchor.click();
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 1000);
  };
  useEffect(() => { load(); }, []);
  if (!data) return <main className="shared-gate"><section><h1>Shared {APP_NAME} design</h1>{error && <p className="error">{error}</p>}<input type="password" placeholder="Share password" value={password} onChange={event => setPassword(event.target.value)}/><button className="primary" onClick={load}>Open design</button></section></main>;
  return <div className="shared-view"><header><strong>{data.design.title}</strong><span className="ui-badge tone-neutral">View only</span><div className="shared-actions">{data.share.allowCopy && <button onClick={copyDesign}>Copy design JSON</button>}{data.share.allowDownload && <button onClick={() => window.print()}>Print / save PDF</button>}<ThemeToggle compact/></div></header><CanvasEditor renderMode/><PageStrip readOnly/></div>;
}

function Dashboard() {
  const [designs, setDesigns] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [team, setTeam] = useState(false);
  const [account, setAccount] = useState(() => new URLSearchParams(location.search).has('billing'));
  const [marketplace, setMarketplace] = useState(false);
  const [status, setStatus] = useState('');
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [view, setView] = useState(() => localStorage.getItem('design-commons-dashboard-view') || localStorage.getItem('canvasforge-dashboard-view') || 'grid');
  const [openMenu, setOpenMenu] = useState('');
  const loadDesign = useEditorStore(state => state.loadDesign);
  const createDesign = useEditorStore(state => state.createDesign);
  const workspaces = useEditorStore(state => state.workspaces);
  const currentWorkspaceId = useEditorStore(state => state.currentWorkspaceId);
  const setWorkspace = useEditorStore(state => state.setWorkspace);
  const user = useEditorStore(state => state.user);
  const role = useEditorStore(state => state.role);
  const logout = useEditorStore(state => state.logout);
  const createWorkspace = useEditorStore(state => state.createWorkspace);
  const billingSummary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const refreshCommercialData = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshCommercialData);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const load = () => api.listDesigns(status).then(setDesigns).finally(() => setLoading(false));
  useEffect(() => { setLoading(true); load(); refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {}); }, [currentWorkspaceId, status]);
  useEffect(() => { localStorage.setItem('design-commons-dashboard-view', view); }, [view]);
  useEffect(() => {
    const close = event => { if (!event.target.closest?.('.design-card-menu')) setOpenMenu(''); };
    document.addEventListener('pointerdown', close); return () => document.removeEventListener('pointerdown', close);
  }, []);
  const filtered = useMemo(() => designs.filter(design => !query || `${design.title} ${design.status || ''}`.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())), [designs, query]);
  const create = async size => createDesign({ title: 'Untitled design', width: size[0], height: size[1] });
  const handleDelete = async (id, title) => {
    if (!confirm(`Delete "${title}"? This cannot be undone.`)) return;
    try { await api.deleteDesign(id); notify(`Deleted "${title}"`, 'success'); load(); }
    catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };
  const presets = [[1080, 1080, 'Square post'], [1080, 1920, 'Story'], [1920, 1080, 'Presentation'], [816, 1056, 'Letter']];
  const currentWorkspace = workspaces.find(item => item.id === currentWorkspaceId);
  return <main className="dashboard">
    <header className="dashboard-header"><div className="dashboard-brand"><span>DC</span><div><h1>{APP_NAME}</h1><p>{user?.name} · {currentWorkspace?.type === 'personal' ? 'Personal workspace' : currentWorkspace?.name || role}</p></div></div><div className="dashboard-actions"><select value={currentWorkspaceId} onChange={event => setWorkspace(event.target.value)}>{workspaces.map(workspace => <option key={workspace.id} value={workspace.id}>{workspace.type === 'personal' ? `Personal · ${workspace.name}` : workspace.name}</option>)}</select><button title="Create organization" onClick={async () => { const name = prompt('Organization name'); if (name) await createWorkspace({ name, type: 'organization' }); }}><Building2 size={15}/>New organization</button>{currentWorkspace?.type !== 'personal' && ['owner', 'admin'].includes(role) && <button onClick={() => setTeam(true)}>Team</button>}<button onClick={() => setMarketplace(true)}><ShoppingBag size={15}/>Marketplace</button><button onClick={() => setAccount(true)}><WalletCards size={15}/>{Number(billingSummary?.credits?.available || 0).toLocaleString()} credits</button><ThemeToggle compact/><button onClick={logout}>Sign out</button></div></header>
    <section className="dashboard-hero"><div><span className="eyebrow">Creative workspace</span><h2>What will you design today?</h2><p>Start with a format, open a recent design, or use AI to turn an idea into an editable canvas.</p></div></section>
    <section className="new-design"><div className="section-heading"><div><h2>Create a design</h2><p>Choose a common format to get started.</p></div></div><div>{presets.map(([width, height, name]) => <button key={name} onClick={() => create([width, height])}><span className="preset-shape" style={{ aspectRatio: `${width}/${height}` }}/><strong>{name}</strong><small>{width} × {height}</small></button>)}</div></section>
    <section className="design-library"><div className="section-heading"><div><h2>Your designs</h2><p>{filtered.length} design{filtered.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in this workspace</p></div><div className="dashboard-library-tools"><label className="dashboard-search"><Search size={15}/><input value={query} onChange={event => setQuery(event.target.value)} placeholder="Search designs"/></label><select value={status} onChange={event => setStatus(event.target.value)}><option value="">All statuses</option><option value="draft">Draft</option><option value="ready_for_review">Ready for review</option><option value="changes_requested">Changes requested</option><option value="approved">Approved</option><option value="archived">Archived</option></select><div className="view-toggle"><button className={view === 'grid' ? 'active' : ''} title="Grid view" onClick={() => setView('grid')}><Grid2X2 size={15}/></button><button className={view === 'list' ? 'active' : ''} title="List view" onClick={() => setView('list')}><List size={16}/></button></div></div></div>
      {loading ? <div className="design-grid">{Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, index) => <SkeletonCard key={index}/>)}</div> : filtered.length ? <div className={`design-grid ${view === 'list' ? 'list-view' : ''}`}>{filtered.map(design => <article key={design.id} className="design-card"><button className="design-open" onClick={() => loadDesign(design.id)}><div className="design-thumb" style={{ aspectRatio: `${design.width}/${design.height}` }}>{design.thumbnail_url ? <img src={design.thumbnail_url}/> : <span>{design.width} × {design.height}</span>}</div><div className="design-card-copy"><strong>{design.title}</strong><small>{new Date(design.updated_at).toLocaleString()}</small></div><span className={`design-status ${design.status || 'draft'}`}>{design.status?.replaceAll('_', ' ') || 'draft'}</span></button><div className="design-card-menu"><button className="design-more" title="Design actions" onClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); setOpenMenu(value => value === design.id ? '' : design.id); }}><MoreHorizontal size={16}/></button>{openMenu === design.id && <div className="design-menu-popover"><button className="danger" onClick={() => handleDelete(design.id, design.title)}><Trash2 size={14}/>Delete design</button></div>}</div></article>)}</div> : <div className="dashboard-empty"><Search size={22}/><strong>No designs found</strong><p>Try a different search or status filter.</p></div>}
    </section>
    {team && <TeamDialog onClose={() => setTeam(false)}/>} {account && <AccountCenter onClose={() => setAccount(false)}/>} {marketplace && <MarketplaceDialog onClose={() => setMarketplace(false)}/>}
  </main>;
}

function Editor() {
  const editorRef = useRef();
  const titleRef = useRef();
  const titleCancelledRef = useRef(false);
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const status = useEditorStore(state => state.status);
  const role = useEditorStore(state => state.role);
  const commit = useEditorStore(state => state.commitDocument);
  const save = useEditorStore(state => state.save);
  const beginHistory = useEditorStore(state => state.beginHistoryTransaction);
  const commitHistory = useEditorStore(state => state.commitHistoryTransaction);
  const cancelHistory = useEditorStore(state => state.cancelHistoryTransaction);
  const leftPanelOpen = useEditorStore(state => state.leftPanelOpen);
  const rightPanelOpen = useEditorStore(state => state.rightPanelOpen);
  const leftPanelWidth = useEditorStore(state => state.leftPanelWidth);
  const rightPanelWidth = useEditorStore(state => state.rightPanelWidth);
  const setWorkspacePreference = useEditorStore(state => state.setWorkspacePreference);
  const recoveryPending = useEditorStore(state => state.recoveryPending);
  const tabConflict = useEditorStore(state => state.tabConflict);
  const continueRecovery = useEditorStore(state => state.continueRecovery);
  const discardRecovery = useEditorStore(state => state.discardRecovery);
  const reloadConflict = useEditorStore(state => state.reloadConflict);
  const takeOverConflict = useEditorStore(state => state.takeOverConflict);
  const closeDesign = useEditorStore(state => state.closeDesign);
  const toasts = useEditorStore(state => state.toasts);
  const dismissToast = useEditorStore(state => state.dismissToast);
  const canEdit = ['owner', 'admin', 'designer'].includes(role);
  const [title, setTitle] = useState(document.title || '');
  useEffect(() => { if (titleRef.current !== globalThis.document.activeElement) setTitle(document.title || ''); }, [document.title]);
  useEffect(() => { if (window.innerWidth <= 900 && leftPanelOpen && rightPanelOpen) setWorkspacePreference('rightPanelOpen', false); }, []);
  useEffect(() => { if (!canEdit || status !== 'dirty' || recoveryPending || tabConflict) return; const id = setTimeout(() => save({ createVersion: false }).catch(() => {}), 1200); return () => clearTimeout(id); }, [document, status, canEdit, recoveryPending, tabConflict]);
  useEffect(() => { const handler = event => { titleRef.current?.blur(); if (['dirty', 'saving', 'offline', 'save-failed', 'recovered', 'conflict'].includes(useEditorStore.getState().status)) { event.preventDefault(); event.returnValue = ''; } }; window.addEventListener('beforeunload', handler); return () => window.removeEventListener('beforeunload', handler); }, []);
  const commitTitle = () => { if (titleCancelledRef.current) { titleCancelledRef.current = false; setTitle(document.title || ''); cancelHistory(); return; } const value = title.trim() || 'Untitled design'; setTitle(value); if (value !== document.title) { const next = structuredClone(document); next.title = value; commit(next); } commitHistory(); };
  const beginResize = (side, event) => { event.preventDefault(); const start = event.clientX; const initial = side === 'left' ? leftPanelWidth : rightPanelWidth; const move = pointerEvent => { const delta = pointerEvent.clientX - start; setWorkspacePreference(side === 'left' ? 'leftPanelWidth' : 'rightPanelWidth', Math.max(240, Math.min(560, initial + (side === 'left' ? delta : -delta)))); }; const up = () => { window.removeEventListener('pointermove', move); window.removeEventListener('pointerup', up); }; window.addEventListener('pointermove', move); window.addEventListener('pointerup', up, { once: true }); };
  const downloadLocal = () => { const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(document, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' }); const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob); const anchor = globalThis.document.createElement('a'); anchor.href = url; anchor.download = `${designFileName(document.title)}.recovery.json`; anchor.click(); setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 1000); };
  const shellStyle = { '--left-panel-width': leftPanelOpen ? `${leftPanelWidth}px` : '0px', '--right-panel-width': rightPanelOpen ? `${rightPanelWidth}px` : '0px' };
  return <div className={`app-shell ${leftPanelOpen ? '' : 'left-collapsed'} ${rightPanelOpen ? '' : 'right-collapsed'}`} style={shellStyle}>
    <TopToolbar editorRef={editorRef}/><AIPanel/>
    {recoveryPending && <div className="workspace-banner recovery-banner"><div><strong>A newer local recovery was found.</strong><span>Review it before {APP_NAME} saves over the server version.</span></div><div><button onClick={downloadLocal}>Download JSON</button><button onClick={() => discardRecovery()}>Discard recovery</button><button className="primary" onClick={continueRecovery}>Continue recovered version</button></div></div>}
    {tabConflict && <div className="workspace-banner conflict-banner"><div><strong>This design is open in another tab.</strong><span>Autosave is paused to prevent one tab from overwriting the other.</span></div><div><button onClick={downloadLocal}>Download local copy</button><button onClick={() => reloadConflict()}>Reload server version</button><button className="danger" onClick={() => takeOverConflict()}>Take over and save</button><button onClick={closeDesign}>Dashboard</button></div></div>}
    {leftPanelOpen && <LeftPanel editorRef={editorRef}/>} {leftPanelOpen && <div className="panel-resizer left-resizer" onPointerDown={event => beginResize('left', event)}/>}
    <main className="editor-main"><div className="document-title"><input ref={titleRef} disabled={!canEdit} value={title} onFocus={() => { titleCancelledRef.current = false; beginHistory(); }} onChange={event => setTitle(event.target.value)} onBlur={commitTitle} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur(); if (event.key === 'Escape') { titleCancelledRef.current = true; setTitle(document.title || ''); event.currentTarget.blur(); } }}/>{!canEdit && <span className="read-only-label">{role} access · read only</span>}</div><CanvasEditor ref={editorRef} readOnly={!canEdit}/></main>
    {rightPanelOpen && <div className="panel-resizer right-resizer" onPointerDown={event => beginResize('right', event)}/>} {rightPanelOpen && <RightPanel editorRef={editorRef}/>}<PageStrip/>
    <div className="toast-stack">{toasts.map(toast => <button key={toast.id} className={`toast ${toast.type}`} onClick={() => { try { if (toast.type === 'error') navigator.clipboard?.writeText(toast.message); } catch { console.log(toast.message); } dismissToast(toast.id); }}>{toast.message}</button>)}</div>
  </div>;
}

export default function App() {
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const share = params.get('share');
  const invite = params.get('invite');
  const session = useEditorStore(state => state.session);
  const user = useEditorStore(state => state.user);
  const design = useEditorStore(state => state.design);
  const hydrate = useEditorStore(state => state.hydrateAuth);
  const [checking, setChecking] = useState(!!session && !user);
  useEffect(() => { if (session && !user) hydrate().finally(() => setChecking(false)); }, []);
  if (share) return <SharedViewer token={share}/>;
  if (invite && !session) return <InviteAccept token={invite}/>;
  if (checking) return <div className="loading-screen"><span className="loading-orb"/>Loading {APP_NAME}…</div>;
  if (!session) return <Login/>;
  if (!design) return <Dashboard/>;
  return <Editor/>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AccountCenter.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Coins, CreditCard, ReceiptText, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import BillingActions from './BillingActions.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function AccountCenter({ onClose }) {
  const summary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const ledger = useEditorStore(state => state.creditLedger);
  const refresh = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshCommercialData);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.commercialBusy);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);

  useEffect(() => {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
    const result = params.get('billing');
    if (result === 'success') notify('Payment completed. Refreshing your credits and billing status…', 'success');
    if (result === 'card-added') notify('Payment card linked successfully.', 'success');
    if (result === 'cancelled') notify('Checkout was cancelled. No charge was made.', 'error');
    if (result) {
      params.delete('billing'); params.delete('session_id');
      history.replaceState({}, '', `${location.pathname}${params.size ? `?${params}` : ''}${location.hash}`);
    }
    refresh().catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error'));
  }, []);

  return <Modal title="Billing, cards and credits" onClose={onClose} wide className="account-center-modal">
    <div className="account-summary-grid">
      <article><CreditCard size={19}/><span>Current plan</span><b>{summary?.plan?.name || 'Free'}</b><small>{summary?.subscription?.status || 'Active'}</small></article>
      <article><Coins size={19}/><span>Available credits</span><b>{Number(summary?.credits?.available || 0).toLocaleString()}</b><small>{Number(summary?.credits?.monthlyRemaining || 0).toLocaleString()} monthly remaining</small></article>
      <article><Sparkles size={19}/><span>Marketplace earnings</span><b>{Number(summary?.credits?.earned || 0).toLocaleString()}</b><small>Available for AI and marketplace purchases</small></article>
    </div>

    <BillingActions showPlans/>

    <section className="credit-ledger"><div className="section-heading"><div><h3>Credit activity</h3><p>Payments, monthly grants, AI charges, marketplace earnings and refunds appear here.</p></div><button disabled={busy} onClick={() => refresh()}>{busy ? 'Refreshing…' : 'Refresh'}</button></div>{ledger.length ? <div className="credit-ledger-list">{ledger.map(item => <div key={item.id}><ReceiptText size={15}/><span><b>{item.description || item.entryType?.replaceAll('_', ' ') || 'Credit entry'}</b><small>{new Date(item.createdAt || item.created_at).toLocaleString()}</small></span><strong className={Number(item.amount) >= 0 ? 'positive' : 'negative'}>{Number(item.amount) >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{Number(item.amount).toLocaleString()}</strong></div>)}</div> : <p className="empty-panel-state">No credit activity yet. Buy a credit package above to get started.</p>}</section>
  </Modal>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIAgentPanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { Check, CircleStop, ImagePlus, ListChecks, MessageSquareText, Pause, Play, RefreshCw, RotateCcw, Sparkles, Upload } from 'lucide-react';
import { AGENT_STATES } from '../ai/agent.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

const statusLabel = value => String(value || 'idle').replaceAll('_', ' ');

export default function AIAgentPanel({ onOpenConcepts, onOpenFinalPreview }) {
  const agent = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAgent);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.aiBusy);
  const error = useEditorStore(state => state.aiError);
  const assets = useEditorStore(state => state.assets);
  const brands = useEditorStore(state => state.brands);
  const start = useEditorStore(state => state.startAIAgent);
  const answer = useEditorStore(state => state.answerAIAgent);
  const steer = useEditorStore(state => state.steerAIAgent);
  const pause = useEditorStore(state => state.pauseAIAgent);
  const resume = useEditorStore(state => state.resumeAIAgent);
  const cancel = useEditorStore(state => state.cancelAIAgent);
  const reset = useEditorStore(state => state.resetAIAgent);
  const uploadMany = useEditorStore(state => state.uploadMany);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const aiPreview = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPreview);

  const [instruction, setInstruction] = useState('');
  const [provider, setProvider] = useState('auto');
  const [brandId, setBrandId] = useState('');
  const [useBrand, setUseBrand] = useState(true);
  const [useAssets, setUseAssets] = useState(true);
  const [assetIds, setAssetIds] = useState([]);
  const [answerText, setAnswerText] = useState('');
  const [steeringText, setSteeringText] = useState('');
  const uploadRef = useRef(null);

  const selectedAssets = useMemo(() => assets.filter(asset => assetIds.includes(asset.id)), [assets, assetIds]);
  const active = agent && ![AGENT_STATES.COMPLETED, AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED, AGENT_STATES.FAILED].includes(agent.status);
  const canStart = instruction.trim() && !busy;

  const begin = async () => {
    try {
      const result = await start(instruction, { provider, brandId: brandId || brands[0]?.id || null, useBrand, useAssets, assetIds });
      if (result?.concepts?.length) onOpenConcepts?.();
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  const submitAnswer = async value => {
    try {
      const result = await answer(value);
      setAnswerText('');
      if (result?.concepts?.length) onOpenConcepts?.();
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  const submitSteering = async () => {
    try {
      await steer(steeringText);
      setSteeringText('');
      notify('Steering instruction queued. Resume when you are ready to generate the next variants.', 'success');
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  const upload = async event => {
    const files = [...(event.target.files || [])];
    event.target.value = '';
    if (!files.length) return;
    try {
      const uploaded = await uploadMany(files);
      setAssetIds(current => [...new Set([...current, ...uploaded.map(asset => asset.id)])]);
      notify(`${uploaded.length} image${uploaded.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} added to this request.`, 'success');
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  if (!agent || !active) return <>
    {agent && <section className={`ai-card ai-agent-finished ${agent.status}`}>
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Check size={16}/><strong>{agent.status === AGENT_STATES.COMPLETED ? 'Agent session completed' : `Agent session ${statusLabel(agent.status)}`}</strong></div><span className={`ai-status ${agent.status}`}>{statusLabel(agent.status)}</span></div>
      <p>{agent.instruction}</p>
      <button className="full" onClick={reset}><RotateCcw size={15}/>Start a new agent session</button>
    </section>}
    <section className="ai-card ai-agent-start">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Sparkles size={17}/><strong>Design agent</strong></div><span className="ai-status ready">3 concepts first</span></div>
      <p>The agent classifies the request, plans the work, uses your selected images, creates three low-quality directions, and waits for approval before compiling editable commands.</p>
      <label><span>What should the agent accomplish?</span><textarea rows="7" value={instruction} onChange={event => setInstruction(event.target.value)} placeholder={'Revise the current menu into a polished tropical design. Keep all wording and prices. Use the logo and drink photos I select below.'}/></label>
      <div className="ai-field-grid">
        <label><span>Agent provider</span><select value={provider} onChange={event => setProvider(event.target.value)}><option value="auto">Server, then local fallback</option><option value="server">Configured server agent</option><option value="local">Local structured fallback</option></select></label>
        <label><span>Brand kit</span><select value={brandId || brands[0]?.id || ''} onChange={event => setBrandId(event.target.value)}><option value="">Automatic</option>{brands.map(brand => <option key={brand.id} value={brand.id}>{brand.title}</option>)}</select></label>
      </div>
      <div className="ai-checks"><label><input type="checkbox" checked={useBrand} onChange={event => setUseBrand(event.target.checked)}/>Use brand styles</label><label><input type="checkbox" checked={useAssets} onChange={event => setUseAssets(event.target.checked)}/>Search asset library first</label></div>
      <div className="ai-request-assets">
        <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><ImagePlus size={15}/><strong>Images for this request</strong></div><button type="button" onClick={() => uploadRef.current?.click()}><Upload size={14}/>Upload</button></div>
        <input ref={uploadRef} type="file" accept="image/*" multiple hidden onChange={upload}/>
        <p>Select images the agent must consider. Uploaded images enter your managed asset library and are included by exact asset ID.</p>
        <div className="ai-request-asset-grid">
          {assets.slice(0, 18).map(asset => <button type="button" key={asset.id} className={assetIds.includes(asset.id) ? 'selected' : ''} onClick={() => setAssetIds(current => current.includes(asset.id) ? current.filter(id => id !== asset.id) : [...current, asset.id])} title={asset.original_name || asset.name}>
            <img src={asset.thumbnail_url || asset.preview_url || asset.url}/><span>{assetIds.includes(asset.id) ? 'Must use' : 'Available'}</span>
          </button>)}
        </div>
        {!!selectedAssets.length && <small>{selectedAssets.length} asset{selectedAssets.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} attached to the brief.</small>}
      </div>
      <button className="primary full ai-generate" disabled={!canStart} onClick={begin}>{busy ? <RefreshCw className="spin" size={16}/> : <Sparkles size={16}/>} {busy ? 'Understanding and planning…' : 'Start agent'}</button>
      {error && <div className="ai-error">{error}</div>}
    </section>
  </>;

  return <>
    <section className="ai-card ai-agent-status-card">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Sparkles size={17}/><strong>Active agent session</strong></div><span className={`ai-status ${agent.status}`}>{statusLabel(agent.status)}</span></div>
      <div className="ai-agent-intent"><b>{statusLabel(agent.classification.intent)}</b><span>{Math.round(agent.classification.confidence * 100)}% confidence · {agent.classification.scope}</span></div>
      <p>{agent.brief.goal}</p>
      <div className="ai-agent-controls">
        {agent.paused ? <button onClick={() => resume().catch(cause => notify(cause.message, 'error'))}><Play size={14}/>Resume</button> : <button onClick={pause} disabled={busy && agent.status === AGENT_STATES.COMPILING_DESIGN}><Pause size={14}/>Pause</button>}
        <button className="danger" onClick={cancel}><CircleStop size={14}/>Stop</button>
        <button onClick={reset}><RotateCcw size={14}/>New session</button>
      </div>
    </section>

    {agent.status === AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_CLARIFICATION && <section className="ai-card ai-agent-questions">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><MessageSquareText size={16}/><strong>A few details will improve the concepts</strong></div></div>
      {agent.questions.map((question, index) => <p key={index}><b>{index + 1}.</b> {question}</p>)}
      <textarea rows="4" value={answerText} onChange={event => setAnswerText(event.target.value)} placeholder="Answer naturally, or use the recommended assumptions."/>
      <div className="button-row wrap"><button className="primary" disabled={busy || !answerText.trim()} onClick={() => submitAnswer(answerText)}>Continue</button><button disabled={busy} onClick={() => submitAnswer('Use your recommended assumptions and preserve the existing content.')}>Use recommended assumptions</button></div>
    </section>}

    <section className="ai-card ai-agent-plan">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><ListChecks size={16}/><strong>Agent plan</strong></div><span>{agent.tasks.filter(task => task.status === 'completed').length}/{agent.tasks.length}</span></div>
      <div className="ai-agent-task-list">{agent.tasks.map(task => <div key={task.id} className={task.status}><span className="ai-agent-task-dot">{task.status === 'completed' ? '✓' : task.status === 'in_progress' ? '●' : '○'}</span><div><b>{task.title}</b>{task.details && <small>{task.details}</small>}</div></div>)}</div>
    </section>

    {!!agent.concepts.length && <section className="ai-card ai-agent-concepts-summary">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><ImagePlus size={16}/><strong>Concept directions</strong></div><span className="ai-status ready">{agent.concepts.length} variants</span></div>
      <p>Select, compare, or refine the low-quality previews before any editable changes are applied.</p>
      <div className="ai-agent-concept-mini">{agent.concepts.map(concept => <button key={concept.id} className={agent.selectedConceptId === concept.id ? 'selected' : ''} onClick={onOpenConcepts}><b>{concept.title}</b><span>{concept.description}</span></button>)}</div>
      <button className="primary full" onClick={onOpenConcepts}><ImagePlus size={15}/>Compare three previews</button>
    </section>}

    {aiPreview && agent.status === AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_FINAL_APPROVAL && <section className="ai-card ai-agent-final">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Check size={16}/><strong>Editable reconstruction ready</strong></div><span className="ai-status ready">Final approval</span></div>
      <p>The selected visual direction has been compiled into structured objects and checked for overlaps, overflow, and other design problems.</p>
      <button className="primary full" onClick={onOpenFinalPreview}><Check size={15}/>Review and apply editable design</button>
    </section>}

    <section className="ai-card ai-agent-steering">
      <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><MessageSquareText size={16}/><strong>Interrupt or steer</strong></div>{agent.steering.length > 0 && <span>{agent.steering.length} instruction{agent.steering.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}</span>}</div>
      <textarea rows="3" value={steeringText} onChange={event => setSteeringText(event.target.value)} placeholder="Use the uploaded leaf image instead. Make the title smaller. Stop generating new assets."/>
      <button className="full" disabled={!steeringText.trim()} onClick={submitSteering}><Pause size={14}/>Pause and queue instruction</button>
    </section>

    {error && <div className="ai-error">{error}</div>}
  </>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIAssetGenerator.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { FileImage, ImagePlus, Sparkles, Upload, VectorSquare } from 'lucide-react';
import { AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS } from '../ai/providers.js';
import { imageElement, svgElement } from '../lib/document.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function AIAssetGenerator({ notify }) {
  const generate = useEditorStore(state => state.generateAIAsset);
  const addElement = useEditorStore(state => state.addElement);
  const defaultMode = useEditorStore(state => state.aiMode);
  const [kind, setKind] = useState('raster');
  const [mode, setMode] = useState(defaultMode || 'balanced');
  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState('');
  const [references, setReferences] = useState([]);
  const [aspectRatio, setAspectRatio] = useState('1:1');
  const [transparent, setTransparent] = useState(false);
  const [addToCanvas, setAddToCanvas] = useState(true);
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);
  const [result, setResult] = useState(null);
  const previews = useMemo(() => references.map(file => ({ file, url: URL.createObjectURL(file) })), [references]);
  useEffect(() => () => previews.forEach(item => URL.revokeObjectURL(item.url)), [previews]);

  const submit = async () => {
    setBusy(true);
    try {
      const generated = await generate({ kind, mode, prompt, references, aspectRatio, transparent });
      setResult(generated);
      if (addToCanvas) addElement(generated.kind === 'svg' ? svgElement(generated.svg, { name: generated.asset.original_name || 'AI SVG' }) : imageElement(generated.asset));
      notify(`Generated ${generated.kind === 'svg' ? 'SVG' : 'image'} added to AI generated assets${addToCanvas ? ' and the canvas' : ''}.`, 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
    finally { setBusy(false); }
  };

  return <div className="ai-asset-generator">
    <div className="ai-asset-kind">
      <button className={kind === 'raster' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setKind('raster')}><FileImage size={16}/><b>Raster image</b><span>Generate a PNG from text or references</span></button>
      <button className={kind === 'svg' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setKind('svg')}><VectorSquare size={16}/><b>Editable SVG</b><span>Create safe vector artwork</span></button>
    </div>
    <label><span>Quality</span><select value={mode} onChange={event => setMode(event.target.value)}>{Object.values(AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS).map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>)}</select><small>{AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS[mode]?.description}</small></label>
    <label><span>Describe the asset</span><textarea rows="5" value={prompt} onChange={event => setPrompt(event.target.value)} placeholder="A clean tropical cocktail illustration with lime, mint, and subtle grain, isolated on a transparent background."/></label>
    <div className="ai-asset-options"><label><span>Aspect ratio</span><select value={aspectRatio} onChange={event => setAspectRatio(event.target.value)}><option>1:1</option><option>4:3</option><option>3:4</option><option>16:9</option><option>9:16</option></select></label>{kind === 'raster' && <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={transparent} onChange={event => setTransparent(event.target.checked)}/>Transparent background</label>}<label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={addToCanvas} onChange={event => setAddToCanvas(event.target.checked)}/>Add to canvas</label></div>
    <label className="ai-reference-upload"><Upload size={16}/><span>Add reference images</span><input type="file" accept="image/*" multiple onChange={event => setReferences([...event.target.files].slice(0, 6))}/></label>
    {!!previews.length && <div className="ai-reference-previews">{previews.map(item => <div key={`${item.file.name}-${item.file.size}`}><img src={item.url}/><span>{item.file.name}</span></div>)}</div>}
    <button className="primary full" disabled={busy || !prompt.trim()} onClick={submit}>{busy ? <Sparkles className="spin" size={16}/> : <ImagePlus size={16}/>} {busy ? 'Generating asset…' : `Generate ${kind === 'svg' ? 'SVG' : 'image'}`}</button>
    {result && <div className="ai-generated-result"><img src={result.dataUrl}/><div><strong>{result.asset.original_name}</strong><span>{result.creditsCharged ? `${result.creditsCharged} credits charged · ` : ''}Saved to your asset library.</span></div></div>}
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIConceptDialog.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Check, Image, RefreshCw, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import PreviewCanvas from './PreviewCanvas.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function AIConceptDialog({ onClose, onFinalPreview }) {
  const agent = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAgent);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.aiBusy);
  const select = useEditorStore(state => state.selectAIAgentConcept);
  const refine = useEditorStore(state => state.refineAIAgentConcept);
  const approve = useEditorStore(state => state.approveAIAgentConcept);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const [selectedId, setSelectedId] = useState(agent?.selectedConceptId || agent?.concepts?.[0]?.id || '');
  const [feedback, setFeedback] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const first = agent?.selectedConceptId || agent?.concepts?.[0]?.id || '';
    if (!agent?.concepts?.some(concept => concept.id === selectedId)) setSelectedId(first);
  }, [agent?.concepts, agent?.selectedConceptId, selectedId]);

  if (!agent?.concepts?.length) return null;
  const selected = agent.concepts.find(concept => concept.id === selectedId) || agent.concepts[0];

  const choose = conceptId => {
    setSelectedId(conceptId);
    select(conceptId);
  };

  const makeRefinements = async () => {
    try {
      await refine(selected.id, feedback);
      setFeedback('');
      notify('Three new refinements are ready to compare.', 'success');
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  const approveDirection = async () => {
    try {
      await approve(selected.id);
      notify('Visual direction approved. The editable reconstruction is ready for final review.', 'success');
      onClose?.();
      onFinalPreview?.();
    } catch (cause) {
      notify(cause.message, 'error');
    }
  };

  return <Modal title="Choose a visual direction" onClose={onClose} wide className="ai-concept-modal">
    <div className="ai-concept-intro"><Sparkles size={18}/><div><strong>These are low-quality concept previews</strong><p>Choose the direction, combine it with steering feedback, or generate three incremental refinements. No canvas changes are applied at this stage.</p></div></div>
    <div className="ai-concept-grid">
      {agent.concepts.map((concept, index) => <article key={concept.id} className={`ai-concept-card ${selected.id === concept.id ? 'selected' : ''}`}>
        <button className="ai-concept-preview" onClick={() => choose(concept.id)}>
          {concept.previewUrl ? <img src={concept.previewUrl} alt={concept.title}/> : concept.document ? <PreviewCanvas document={concept.document} pageIndex={concept.pageIndex || 0}/> : <div className="ai-concept-missing"><Image size={28}/><span>{concept.previewError || 'Preview unavailable'}</span></div>}
        </button>
        <div className="ai-concept-copy"><div><span className="ai-concept-number">{index + 1}</span><div><strong>{concept.title}</strong><small>{concept.previewMode === 'image' ? 'Image-generation preview' : 'Structured editable fallback'}</small></div></div><p>{concept.description}</p></div>
        <button className={selected.id === concept.id ? 'primary full' : 'full'} onClick={() => choose(concept.id)}>{selected.id === concept.id ? <><Check size={15}/>Selected</> : 'Choose this direction'}</button>
        <details><summary>Concept prompt and construction plan</summary><p>{concept.prompt}</p><code>Seed {concept.seed}</code>{concept.conceptSpec?.assetManifest?.length > 0 && <ul>{concept.conceptSpec.assetManifest.map((asset, assetIndex) => <li key={asset.key || assetIndex}>{asset.description} · {asset.sourcePreference}</li>)}</ul>}</details>
      </article>)}
    </div>
    <section className="ai-concept-refine">
      <div><strong>Increment the selected preview</strong><p>Describe the next change. The agent will keep the selected concept as the parent and return three new variants.</p></div>
      <textarea rows="3" value={feedback} onChange={event => setFeedback(event.target.value)} placeholder="Keep this layout, but make it less busy, move the title higher, and use the uploaded product photo."/>
      <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={onClose}>Close</button><button disabled={busy || !feedback.trim()} onClick={makeRefinements}><RefreshCw className={busy ? 'spin' : ''} size={15}/>{busy ? 'Generating…' : 'Generate 3 refinements'}</button><button className="primary" disabled={busy || !selected} onClick={approveDirection}><Check size={16}/>Approve visual direction</button></div>
    </section>
  </Modal>;
}
