// FILE: src/components/AIPanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  Bot, Brush, Clipboard, Code2, Coins, Eye, FileImage, Image, Play, RefreshCw,
  ShieldCheck, Sparkles, Trash2, WandSparkles, X
} from 'lucide-react';
import LLMCommandDialog from './LLMCommandDialog.jsx';
import AIPreviewDialog from './AIPreviewDialog.jsx';
import AIAssetGenerator from './AIAssetGenerator.jsx';
import AIUsagePanel from './AIUsagePanel.jsx';
import AIScreenshotAnnotator from './AIScreenshotAnnotator.jsx';
import AIAgentPanel from './AIAgentPanel.jsx';
import AIConceptDialog from './AIConceptDialog.jsx';
import AccountCenter from './AccountCenter.jsx';
import { AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS } from '../ai/providers.js';
import { copyImageToClipboard } from '../ai/visuals.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { APP_NAME } from '../lib/appMeta.js';

const copyText = async value => {
  const text = typeof value === 'string' ? value : JSON.stringify(value, null, 2);
  try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); } catch {
    const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
    textarea.value = text; textarea.style.position = 'fixed'; textarea.style.opacity = '0';
    document.body.appendChild(textarea); textarea.select(); document.execCommand('copy'); textarea.remove();
  }
};

export default function AIPanel() {
  const open = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPanelOpen);
  const toggle = useEditorStore(state => state.toggleAIPanel);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.aiBusy);
  const error = useEditorStore(state => state.aiError);
  const plan = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPlan);
  const preview = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPreview);
  const renders = useEditorStore(state => state.aiRenders);
  const render = useEditorStore(state => state.aiRender);
  const annotation = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAnnotation);
  const documentRevision = useEditorStore(state => state.documentRevision);
  const pageCount = useEditorStore(state => state.document?.pages?.length || 0);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const brands = useEditorStore(state => state.brands);
  const agent = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAgent);
  const aiMode = useEditorStore(state => state.aiMode);
  const setAIMode = useEditorStore(state => state.setAIMode);
  const billingSummary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const prepareWithAssets = useEditorStore(state => state.prepareAIPlanWithAssets);
  const resolveAssetRequests = useEditorStore(state => state.resolveAIAssetRequests);
  const assetPromptList = useEditorStore(state => state.getAIAssetPromptList);
  const aiTheme = useEditorStore(state => state.aiTheme);
  const aiAssetRequests = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAssetRequests);
  const aiAssetResults = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAssetResults);
  const aiAssetLoop = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAssetLoop);
  const previewCommands = useEditorStore(state => state.previewAICommands);
  const clear = useEditorStore(state => state.clearAIPlan);
  const renderImages = useEditorStore(state => state.renderAIImages);
  const setAnnotation = useEditorStore(state => state.setAIAnnotation);
  const getContext = useEditorStore(state => state.getAIContext);
  const refreshCommercialData = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshCommercialData);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);

  const [mode, setMode] = useState('agent');
  const [tab, setTab] = useState('design');
  const [instruction, setInstruction] = useState('');
  const [scope, setScope] = useState('page');
  const [brandId, setBrandId] = useState('');
  const [useBrand, setUseBrand] = useState(true);
  const [useAssets, setUseAssets] = useState(true);
  const [useVisuals, setUseVisuals] = useState(true);
  const [themeHint, setThemeHint] = useState('');
  const [assetMode, setAssetMode] = useState('reuse-only');
  const [assetRounds, setAssetRounds] = useState(1);
  const [commandsOpen, setCommandsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [commandDraft, setCommandDraft] = useState('');
  const [llmDialogOpen, setLlmDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [visualPreviewOpen, setVisualPreviewOpen] = useState(false);
  const [conceptDialogOpen, setConceptDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [annotatorOpen, setAnnotatorOpen] = useState(false);
  const [selectedRenderIndex, setSelectedRenderIndex] = useState(0);
  const [billingOpen, setBillingOpen] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => { if (plan) setCommandDraft(JSON.stringify(plan, null, 2)); }, [plan]);
  useEffect(() => { if (selectedRenderIndex >= renders.length) setSelectedRenderIndex(0); }, [renders.length]);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (agent?.concepts?.length && ['awaiting_concept_selection', 'awaiting_concept_approval'].includes(agent.status)) setConceptDialogOpen(true);
  }, [agent?.concepts?.[0]?.id]);
  useEffect(() => { if (open) refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {}); }, [open]);

  const lintCounts = preview?.lint?.counts || {};
  const blockingCount = preview?.blockingIssues?.length || 0;
  const commandCount = plan?.commands?.length || 0;
  const selectedBrand = brandId || brands[0]?.id || '';
  const canGenerate = instruction.trim() && !busy;
  const currentRender = renders[selectedRenderIndex] || render || null;
  const annotationStale = annotation && annotation.revision !== documentRevision;
  const displayedImage = !annotationStale && annotation?.dataUrl ? annotation.dataUrl : currentRender?.url;
  const credits = billingSummary?.credits?.available;
  const contextSummary = useMemo(() => {
    const context = getContext?.();
    if (!context) return null;
    return `${context.design.pageCount} page${context.design.pageCount === 1 ? '' : 's'} · ${context.currentPage.elements.length} objects · ${context.assets.length} assets`;
  }, [open, selection, renders.length, annotation?.dataUrl, getContext]);

  const refreshVisuals = async () => {
    try {
      const result = await renderImages({ multiplier: 1, scope });
      setSelectedRenderIndex(0);
      notify(`${result.length} fresh page screenshot${result.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} ready.`, 'success');
      return result;
    } catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); throw nextError; }
  };

  const generate = async () => {
    try {
      const missingDocumentPages = scope === 'document' && renders.length < pageCount;
      if (useVisuals && (!annotation || annotationStale || !renders.length || missingDocumentPages)) await refreshVisuals();
      const result = await prepareWithAssets(instruction, { scope, mode: aiMode, brandId: selectedBrand, useBrand, useAssets, useVisuals, themeHint, assetMode, assetRounds });
      await refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {});
      if (result?.preview) setVisualPreviewOpen(true);
      else notify('Theme and asset prompts are ready below. Generate the assets manually or resolve them in CanvasForge.', 'success');
    } catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); }
  };

  const previewEditedCommands = () => {
    try {
      previewCommands(JSON.parse(commandDraft));
      setVisualPreviewOpen(true);
      notify('Command bundle validated. A visual preview is ready for approval.', 'success');
    } catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); }
  };

  const copyScreenshot = async () => {
    if (!displayedImage) return notify('Render a screenshot first.', 'error');
    try { await copyImageToClipboard(displayedImage); notify('Screenshot copied as an image. Paste it directly into your chat.', 'success'); }
    catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); }
  };

  if (!open) return null;
  const tabs = [
    ['design', WandSparkles, 'Design'],
    ['assets', FileImage, 'Assets'],
    ['manual', Code2, 'Manual'],
    ['usage', Coins, 'Usage']
  ];

  return <aside className="ai-panel" aria-label="AI designer">
    <header className="ai-panel-header">
      <div><span className="ai-panel-icon"><Sparkles size={18}/></span><div><strong>{APP_NAME} Agent</strong><small>{contextSummary}</small></div></div>
      <button className="icon-button" title="Close AI Designer" onClick={() => toggle(false)}><X size={18}/></button>
    </header>

    <nav className="ai-mode-tabs"><button className={mode === 'agent' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setMode('agent')}><Sparkles size={15}/>Agent</button><button className={mode === 'commands' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setMode('commands')}><Code2 size={15}/>Direct commands</button></nav>

    <div className="ai-panel-body">
      {mode === 'agent' ? <AIAgentPanel onOpenConcepts={() => setConceptDialogOpen(true)} onOpenFinalPreview={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(true)}/> : <>
      {tab === 'design' && <>
        <section className="ai-card ai-compose">
          <div className="ai-section-title"><div><WandSparkles size={17}/><strong>Automated design workflow</strong></div></div>
          <div className="ai-credit-actions"><div><Coins size={17}/><span><b>{Number(credits || 0).toLocaleString()}</b><small>credits available</small></span></div><button className="primary" onClick={() => setBillingOpen(true)}>Add credits</button><button onClick={() => setBillingOpen(true)}>Add card</button></div>
          <label><span>Describe the design or change</span><textarea rows="7" value={instruction} onChange={event => setInstruction(event.target.value)} placeholder="Improve this menu using the current layout and content. Strengthen hierarchy, align prices, and use the marked screenshot instructions."/></label>
          <div className="ai-field-grid">
            <label><span>Scope</span><select value={scope} onChange={event => setScope(event.target.value)}><option value="page">Current page</option><option value="selection" disabled={!selection.length}>Selection ({selection.length})</option><option value="document">All pages</option></select></label>
            <label><span>Quality</span><select value={aiMode} onChange={event => setAIMode(event.target.value)}>{Object.values(AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS).map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>)}</select></label>
            {!!brands.length && <label><span>Brand kit</span><select value={brandId} onChange={event => setBrandId(event.target.value)}><option value="">Automatic</option>{brands.map(brand => <option key={brand.id} value={brand.id}>{brand.title}</option>)}</select></label>}
          </div>
          <small className="ai-mode-help">{AI_MODE_DEFINITIONS[aiMode]?.description}</small>
          <div className="ai-checks"><label><input type="checkbox" checked={useVisuals} onChange={event => setUseVisuals(event.target.checked)}/>Send fresh screenshot{scope === 'document' ? 's' : ''}</label><label><input type="checkbox" checked={useBrand} onChange={event => setUseBrand(event.target.checked)}/>Use brand styles</label><label><input type="checkbox" checked={useAssets} onChange={event => setUseAssets(event.target.checked)}/>Use asset library</label></div>

          <div className="ai-asset-workflow">
            <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><FileImage size={16}/><strong>Theme and asset workflow</strong></div><span className="ui-badge tone-neutral">{assetMode.replace('-', ' ')}</span></div>
            <label><span>Theme direction</span><input value={themeHint} onChange={event => setThemeHint(event.target.value)} placeholder="Warm retro cocktail bar, thick outlined illustrations, cream/coral/yellow palette"/><small>Leave blank to let the designer infer one theme from the page and brand.</small></label>
            <div className="ai-field-grid"><label><span>Asset strategy</span><select value={assetMode} onChange={event => setAssetMode(event.target.value)}><option value="reuse-only">Reuse existing assets only</option><option value="prompts">Plan assets and give me prompts</option><option value="auto-generate">Automatically create missing assets</option></select></label>{assetMode === 'auto-generate' && <label><span>Asset passes</span><select value={assetRounds} onChange={event => setAssetRounds(Number(event.target.value))}><option value="1">1 pass</option><option value="2">2 passes</option><option value="3">3 passes</option></select></label>}</div>
            <small>{assetMode === 'reuse-only' ? 'The AI searches the workspace library and uses native shapes or SVG when nothing fits.' : assetMode === 'prompts' ? 'The AI creates a consistent theme and a production-ready prompt list without spending image-generation credits.' : 'The AI plans missing assets, reuses close matches, generates only the gaps, then replans the page using the new asset IDs.'}</small>
          </div>

          <div className="ai-visual-context">
            <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Image size={16}/><strong>Visual context</strong></div>{render?.status && <span className={`ai-status ${render.status}`}>{render.status}{Number.isFinite(render.progress) ? ` ${render.progress}%` : ''}</span>}</div>
            {displayedImage ? <img className="ai-visual-current" src={displayedImage} alt="AI visual context"/> : <div className="ai-visual-empty">Render the current design, then optionally draw instructions on it.</div>}
            {renders.length > 1 && <div className="ai-render-thumbnails">{renders.map((item, index) => <button key={item.jobId || item.url} className={selectedRenderIndex === index ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setSelectedRenderIndex(index)}><img src={item.url}/><span>Page {item.pageIndex + 1}</span></button>)}</div>}
            {annotationStale && <div className="ai-stale-note">The annotated screenshot is older than the current canvas and will be replaced before generation.</div>}
            <div className="button-row wrap"><button disabled={busy} onClick={refreshVisuals}><RefreshCw className={busy ? 'spin' : ''} size={14}/>{scope === 'document' ? 'Render all pages' : 'Refresh screenshot'}</button><button disabled={!currentRender?.url} onClick={() => setAnnotatorOpen(true)}><Brush size={14}/>Draw instructions</button><button disabled={!displayedImage} onClick={copyScreenshot}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy image</button>{annotation?.dataUrl && <button onClick={() => setAnnotation(null)}><Trash2 size={14}/>Remove drawing</button>}</div>
          </div>

          <button className="primary full ai-generate" disabled={!canGenerate} onClick={generate}>{busy ? <RefreshCw className="spin" size={16}/> : <Sparkles size={16}/>} {busy ? 'Preparing visual AI preview…' : 'Generate preview'}</button>
          {error && <div className="ai-error">{error}</div>}
        </section>

        {!!aiAssetRequests.length && <section className="ai-card ai-asset-plan-card">
          <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><FileImage size={17}/><strong>Theme asset plan</strong></div>{aiAssetLoop && <span className={`ai-status ${aiAssetLoop.status === 'complete' ? 'ready' : 'processing'}`}>{aiAssetLoop.completed}/{aiAssetLoop.total}</span>}</div>
          {aiTheme && <div className="ai-theme-summary"><b>{aiTheme.name}</b><span>{aiTheme.summary || aiTheme.visualStyle || 'Coherent page theme'}</span>{!!aiTheme.palette?.length && <div>{aiTheme.palette.map(color => <i key={color} style={{ background: color }} title={color}/>)}</div>}</div>}
          <div className="ai-asset-request-list">{aiAssetRequests.map(request => { const result = aiAssetResults.find(item => item.request.key === request.key); return <article key={request.key}><div><b>{request.name}</b><span>{request.kind} · {request.aspectRatio} · {request.role}</span></div><small>{request.purpose || request.prompt}</small><em className={result ? 'resolved' : ''}>{result ? `${result.resolution.replaceAll('-', ' ')} · ${result.asset.original_name || result.asset.name}` : request.reuseAssetId ? 'Existing asset selected' : 'Prompt ready'}</em></article>; })}</div>
          <div className="button-row wrap"><button onClick={() => copyText(assetPromptList().map(item => `${item.index}. ${item.name} (${item.kind}, ${item.aspectRatio}${item.transparent ? ', transparent' : ''})\n${item.prompt}`).join('\n\n'))}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy asset prompts</button><button disabled={busy || aiAssetRequests.every(request => aiAssetResults.some(item => item.request.key === request.key))} onClick={async () => { try { await resolveAssetRequests(null, { preferExisting: true }); notify('Asset plan resolved. Generate the design again to place the new assets.', 'success'); } catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); } }}><Sparkles size={14}/>Resolve assets now</button></div>
        </section>}

        {plan && preview && <section className="ai-card ai-preview-card">
          <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Bot size={17}/><strong>Proposed changes</strong></div><span className="ai-status ready">{commandCount} commands</span></div>
          <div className="ai-diff-summary"><div><b>{preview.diff.added.length}</b><span>Added</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.changed.length}</b><span>Changed</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.removed.length}</b><span>Removed</span></div><div><b>{(preview.warnings || []).length}</b><span>Warnings</span></div></div>
          <div className="ai-lint"><div><ShieldCheck size={16}/><strong>Design checks</strong></div><span>{blockingCount} blocking · {lintCounts.warning || 0} warnings · {lintCounts.info || 0} notes</span></div>
          {!!preview.lint.issues.length && <div className="ai-issues">{preview.lint.issues.slice(0, 8).map(issue => <div key={issue.id} className={issue.severity}><b>{issue.rule.replaceAll('-', ' ')}</b><span>{issue.message}</span></div>)}</div>}
          <button className="ai-command-toggle" onClick={() => setCommandsOpen(value => !value)}><Code2 size={15}/>{commandsOpen ? 'Hide command JSON' : 'Review or edit command JSON'}</button>
          {commandsOpen && <div className="ai-command-editor"><textarea rows="14" value={commandDraft} onChange={event => setCommandDraft(event.target.value)}/><div className="button-row"><button onClick={previewEditedCommands}><Play size={14}/>Validate preview</button><button onClick={() => copyText(commandDraft)}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy</button></div></div>}
          <div className="ai-apply-row"><button onClick={clear}><Trash2 size={15}/>Discard</button><button className="primary" onClick={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(true)}><Eye size={16}/>Preview and approve</button></div>
        </section>}

        {!!aiAssetRequests.length && <section className="ai-card ai-asset-plan-card">
          <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><FileImage size={17}/><strong>Theme asset plan</strong></div>{aiAssetLoop && <span className={`ai-status ${aiAssetLoop.status === 'complete' ? 'ready' : 'processing'}`}>{aiAssetLoop.completed}/{aiAssetLoop.total}</span>}</div>
          {aiTheme && <div className="ai-theme-summary"><b>{aiTheme.name}</b><span>{aiTheme.summary || aiTheme.visualStyle || 'Coherent page theme'}</span>{!!aiTheme.palette?.length && <div>{aiTheme.palette.map(color => <i key={color} style={{ background: color }} title={color}/>)}</div>}</div>}
          <div className="ai-asset-request-list">{aiAssetRequests.map(request => { const result = aiAssetResults.find(item => item.request.key === request.key); return <article key={request.key}><div><b>{request.name}</b><span>{request.kind} · {request.aspectRatio} · {request.role}</span></div><small>{request.purpose || request.prompt}</small><em className={result ? 'resolved' : ''}>{result ? `${result.resolution.replaceAll('-', ' ')} · ${result.asset.original_name || result.asset.name}` : request.reuseAssetId ? 'Existing asset selected' : 'Prompt ready'}</em></article>; })}</div>
          <div className="button-row wrap"><button onClick={() => copyText(assetPromptList().map(item => `${item.index}. ${item.name} (${item.kind}, ${item.aspectRatio}${item.transparent ? ', transparent' : ''})\n${item.prompt}`).join('\n\n'))}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy asset prompts</button><button disabled={busy || aiAssetRequests.every(request => aiAssetResults.some(item => item.request.key === request.key))} onClick={async () => { try { await resolveAssetRequests(null, { preferExisting: true }); notify('Asset plan resolved. Generate the design again to place the new assets.', 'success'); } catch (nextError) { notify(nextError.message, 'error'); } }}><Sparkles size={14}/>Resolve assets now</button></div>
        </section>}

        {plan && preview && <section className="ai-card ai-preview-card">
          <div className="ai-card-heading"><div><Bot size={17}/><strong>Proposed changes</strong></div><span className="ai-status ready">{commandCount} commands</span></div>
          <div className="ai-diff-summary"><div><b>{preview.diff.added.length}</b><span>Added</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.changed.length}</b><span>Changed</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.removed.length}</b><span>Removed</span></div><div><b>{(preview.warnings || []).length}</b><span>Warnings</span></div></div>
          <div className="ai-lint"><div><ShieldCheck size={16}/><strong>Design checks</strong></div><span>{blockingCount} blocking · {lintCounts.warning || 0} warnings · {lintCounts.info || 0} notes</span></div>
          {!!preview.lint.issues.length && <div className="ai-issues">{preview.lint.issues.slice(0, 8).map(issue => <div key={issue.id} className={issue.severity}><b>{issue.rule.replaceAll('-', ' ')}</b><span>{issue.message}</span></div>)}</div>}
          <button className="ai-command-toggle" onClick={() => setCommandsOpen(value => !value)}><Code2 size={15}/>{commandsOpen ? 'Hide command JSON' : 'Review or edit command JSON'}</button>
          {commandsOpen && <div className="ai-command-editor"><textarea rows="14" value={commandDraft} onChange={event => setCommandDraft(event.target.value)}/><div className="button-row"><button onClick={previewEditedCommands}><Play size={14}/>Validate preview</button><button onClick={() => copyText(commandDraft)}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy</button></div></div>}
          <div className="ai-apply-row"><button onClick={clear}><Trash2 size={15}/>Discard</button><button className="primary" onClick={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(true)}><Eye size={16}/>Preview and approve</button></div>
        </section>}
      </>}

      {tab === 'assets' && <section className="ai-card"><div className="ai-section-title"><div><FileImage size={17}/><strong>Generate assets</strong></div></div><AIAssetGenerator notify={notify}/></section>}

      {tab === 'manual' && <section className="ai-card ai-manual-card">
        <div className="ai-section-title"><div><Code2 size={17}/><strong>Manual chat workflow</strong></div></div>
        <p>This optional workflow does not use your CanvasForge credits. Copy the generated prompt and screenshot into an external chat, then paste its JSON response back for validation and approval.</p>
        <div className="ai-manual-steps"><div><b>1</b><span>Render and optionally mark the screenshot.</span></div><div><b>2</b><span>Copy the full prompt and image into your chat.</span></div><div><b>3</b><span>Paste the returned command bundle and preview it safely.</span></div></div>
        <button className="primary full" onClick={() => setLlmDialogOpen(true)}><Code2 size={16}/>Open manual handoff</button>
      </section>}

      {tab === 'usage' && <section className="ai-card"><div className="ai-section-title"><div><Coins size={17}/><strong>Credits and AI usage</strong></div></div><AIUsagePanel/></section>}
    </>}</div>

    {llmDialogOpen && <LLMCommandDialog onClose={() => setLlmDialogOpen(false)}/>}
    {conceptDialogOpen && agent?.concepts?.length > 0 && <AIConceptDialog onClose={() => setConceptDialogOpen(false)} onFinalPreview={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(true)}/>}
    {visualPreviewOpen && plan && preview && <AIPreviewDialog onClose={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(false)}/>}
    {billingOpen && <AccountCenter onClose={() => setBillingOpen(false)}/>}
    {annotatorOpen && currentRender?.url && <AIScreenshotAnnotator source={currentRender.url} initialActions={annotation?.sourceUrl === currentRender.url ? annotation.actions : []} onClose={() => setAnnotatorOpen(false)} onSave={result => { setAnnotation({ ...result, sourceUrl: currentRender.url, pageIndex: currentRender.pageIndex, revision: documentRevision }); setAnnotatorOpen(false); notify('Annotated screenshot will be sent as the primary visual instruction.', 'success'); }}/>}
  </aside>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIPreviewDialog.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { AlertTriangle, Check, Eye, RefreshCw, ShieldCheck, Sparkles, Trash2, WandSparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import PreviewCanvas from './PreviewCanvas.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function AIPreviewDialog({ onClose, onApplied }) {
  const plan = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPlan);
  const preview = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPreview);
  const apply = useEditorStore(state => state.applyAIPlan);
  const clear = useEditorStore(state => state.clearAIPlan);
  const refine = useEditorStore(state => state.applyAIPlanAndRefine);
  const aiBusy = useEditorStore(state => state.aiBusy);
  const applySafeFixes = useEditorStore(state => state.applyAISafeFixes);
  const autoRefine = useEditorStore(state => state.autoRefineAIPlan);
  const candidates = useEditorStore(state => state.aiCandidates);
  const selectCandidate = useEditorStore(state => state.selectAICandidate);
  const currentPageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const agent = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAgent);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const isAgentPreview = !!agent && ['compiling_design', 'awaiting_final_approval', 'assembling_design', 'rendering', 'critiquing', 'correcting'].includes(agent.status);
  const preferredPageIndex = isAgentPreview ? Math.max(0, (preview?.document?.pages?.length || 1) - 1) : (currentPageIndex || 0);
  const [pageIndex, setPageIndex] = useState(preferredPageIndex);
  const [showReference, setShowReference] = useState(true);
  const [referenceMode, setReferenceMode] = useState('overlay');
  const [referenceOpacity, setReferenceOpacity] = useState(.45);
  const [referenceSplit, setReferenceSplit] = useState(.5);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!preview?.document?.pages?.length) return;
    const preferred = isAgentPreview ? preview.document.pages.length - 1 : (currentPageIndex || 0);
    setPageIndex(Math.min(Math.max(0, preferred), preview.document.pages.length - 1));
  }, [preview?.generatedAt, currentPageIndex, agent?.id, isAgentPreview]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const reference = preview?.document?.pages?.[pageIndex]?.referenceImage;
    if (!reference) return;
    setReferenceMode(reference.mode || 'overlay');
    setReferenceOpacity(reference.opacity ?? .45);
    setReferenceSplit(reference.split ?? .5);
  }, [preview?.generatedAt, pageIndex]);

  if (!plan || !preview) return null;
  const blocking = preview.blockingIssues || [];
  const warnings = preview.warnings || [];
  const lintIssues = preview.lint?.issues || [];
  const designScore = preview.lint?.score || { overall: 100, categories: {} };
  const safeFixCount = preview.lint?.safeFixCount || 0;

  const pages = preview.document?.pages || [];
  const loopLimitReached = !!agent && (agent.correctionLoop || 0) >= (agent.maxCorrectionLoops || 3);

  const approve = () => {
    try {
      apply({ approved: true, keepAgentOpen: false });
      notify('AI changes approved and applied. The canvas now shows the new design.', 'success');
      onApplied?.();
      onClose?.();
    } catch (error) {
      notify(error.message, 'error');
    }
  };
  const discard = () => {
    clear();
    onClose?.();
  };

  const approveRenderAndRefine = async () => {
    try {
      notify('Applying this draft, rendering it, and running the next visual correction loop…', 'success');
      await refine({ multiplier: 1 });
      notify('A visual-correction preview is ready.', 'success');
    } catch (error) {
      notify(error.message, 'error');
    }
  };
  const fixSafely = () => {
    try { applySafeFixes(); notify('Safe design-check fixes were applied to the preview.', 'success'); }
    catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };
  const refineAutomatically = async () => {
    try {
      notify('Running up to three scored visual-refinement rounds…', 'success');
      const result = await autoRefine({ rounds: 3, multiplier: 1 });
      notify(`${result.completed} refinement round${result.completed === 1 ? '' : 's'} completed.`, 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };

  return <Modal title="Preview and approve AI changes" onClose={onClose} wide className="ai-preview-modal">
    <div className="ai-preview-layout">
      <section className="ai-preview-visual">
        <header>
          <div><Eye size={17}/><strong>Visual preview</strong></div>
          <span>{pages[pageIndex]?.name || `Page ${pageIndex + 1}`}</span>
        </header>
        {pages[pageIndex]?.referenceImage && <div className="ai-reference-compare-controls"><label><input type="checkbox" checked={showReference} onChange={event => setShowReference(event.target.checked)}/>Show reference</label><select value={referenceMode} onChange={event => setReferenceMode(event.target.value)}><option value="overlay">Overlay</option><option value="difference">Difference</option><option value="split">Split</option></select><label>Opacity <input type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={referenceOpacity} onChange={event => setReferenceOpacity(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>{referenceMode === 'split' && <label>Split <input type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={referenceSplit} onChange={event => setReferenceSplit(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>}</div>}
        <PreviewCanvas document={preview.document} pageIndex={pageIndex} showReference={showReference} referenceMode={referenceMode} referenceOpacity={referenceOpacity} referenceSplit={referenceSplit}/>
        {pages.length > 1 && <div className="ai-preview-page-tabs">
          {pages.map((page, index) => <button key={page.id || index} className={index === pageIndex ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setPageIndex(index)}>
            <b>{index + 1}</b><span>{page.name || `Page ${index + 1}`}</span><small>{page.elements?.length || 0} objects</small>
          </button>)}
        </div>}
      </section>
      <aside className="ai-preview-review">
        <div className="ai-preview-summary-grid">
          <div><b>{plan.commands?.length || 0}</b><span>Commands</span></div>
          <div><b>{preview.diff?.added?.length || 0}</b><span>Added</span></div>
          <div><b>{preview.diff?.changed?.length || 0}</b><span>Changed</span></div>
          <div><b>{preview.diff?.removed?.length || 0}</b><span>Removed</span></div>
        </div>
        <section className="ai-design-score">
          <header><div><Sparkles size={17}/><strong>Design score</strong></div><b>{designScore.overall}</b></header>
          <div className="ai-score-bars">{Object.entries(designScore.categories || {}).map(([key, value]) => <label key={key}><span>{key.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1')}</span><meter min="0" max="100" value={value}/><b>{value}</b></label>)}</div>
        </section>
        <div className={`ai-preview-safety ${blocking.length ? 'blocked' : 'ready'}`}>
          {blocking.length ? <AlertTriangle size={18}/> : <ShieldCheck size={18}/>}<div><strong>{blocking.length ? `${blocking.length} blocking issue${blocking.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}` : 'Ready for approval'}</strong><span>{blocking.length ? 'The design cannot be applied until these checks are resolved.' : 'The original document remains unchanged until you approve.'}</span></div>
        </div>
        {!!lintIssues.length && <details open={blocking.length > 0} className="ai-preview-findings"><summary>Design checks ({lintIssues.length})</summary><div>{lintIssues.slice(0, 20).map(issue => <article key={issue.id} className={issue.severity}><b>{issue.rule.replaceAll('-', ' ')}</b><span>{issue.message}</span></article>)}</div></details>}
        {!!warnings.length && <details className="ai-preview-findings"><summary>Command warnings ({warnings.length})</summary><div>{warnings.slice(0, 20).map((warning, index) => <article key={index} className="warning"><span>{warning}</span></article>)}</div></details>}
        <details className="ai-preview-findings"><summary>Change summary</summary><div className="ai-preview-change-list">
          {(preview.diff?.added || []).slice(0, 12).map(item => <article key={`a-${item.id}`}><b>Added</b><span>{item.semanticName || item.name || item.type}</span></article>)}
          {(preview.diff?.changed || []).slice(0, 12).map(item => <article key={`c-${item.id}`}><b>Changed</b><span>{item.semanticName || item.name || item.type}</span></article>)}
          {(preview.diff?.removed || []).slice(0, 12).map(item => <article key={`r-${item.id}`}><b>Removed</b><span>{item.semanticName || item.name || item.type}</span></article>)}
        </div></details>
        {!!candidates.length && <details className="ai-preview-findings"><summary>Scored candidates ({candidates.length})</summary><div className="ai-candidate-list">{candidates.slice(0, 8).map((candidate, index) => <button key={candidate.id} onClick={() => selectCandidate(candidate.id)}><span>Version {candidates.length - index}</span><b>{candidate.score}</b><small>{new Date(candidate.generatedAt).toLocaleTimeString()}</small></button>)}</div></details>}
        <div className="ai-preview-actions">
          <button onClick={discard}><Trash2 size={15}/>Discard</button>
          <button onClick={onClose}>Keep editing commands</button>
          <button disabled={!safeFixCount || aiBusy} onClick={fixSafely}><WandSparkles size={16}/>Apply {safeFixCount || ''} safe fixes</button>
          <button disabled={blocking.length > 0 || aiBusy} onClick={refineAutomatically}><Sparkles className={aiBusy ? 'spin' : ''} size={16}/>{aiBusy ? 'Refining…' : 'Auto-refine ×3'}</button>
          <button disabled={blocking.length > 0 || aiBusy || loopLimitReached} onClick={approveRenderAndRefine}><RefreshCw className={aiBusy ? 'spin' : ''} size={16}/>{aiBusy ? 'Rendering…' : loopLimitReached ? 'Correction limit reached' : agent ? `Apply & run correction ${(agent.correctionLoop || 0) + 1}/${agent.maxCorrectionLoops || 3}` : 'Apply, render & refine'}</button>
          <button className="primary" disabled={blocking.length > 0 || aiBusy} onClick={approve}><Check size={16}/>{blocking.length ? 'Approval blocked' : 'Approve and apply'}</button>
        </div>
      </aside>
    </div>
  </Modal>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIScreenshotAnnotator.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { ArrowUpRight, Minus, Pencil, Redo2, Save, Square, Trash2, Undo2 } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';

const drawArrow = (context, from, to, width, color) => {
  const angle = Math.atan2(to.y - from.y, to.x - from.x);
  const head = Math.max(12, width * 4);
  context.beginPath();
  context.moveTo(from.x, from.y);
  context.lineTo(to.x, to.y);
  context.strokeStyle = color;
  context.lineWidth = width;
  context.lineCap = 'round';
  context.stroke();
  context.beginPath();
  context.moveTo(to.x, to.y);
  context.lineTo(to.x - head * Math.cos(angle - Math.PI / 6), to.y - head * Math.sin(angle - Math.PI / 6));
  context.lineTo(to.x - head * Math.cos(angle + Math.PI / 6), to.y - head * Math.sin(angle + Math.PI / 6));
  context.closePath();
  context.fillStyle = color;
  context.fill();
};

export default function AIScreenshotAnnotator({ source, initialActions = [], onSave, onClose }) {
  const canvasRef = useRef();
  const imageRef = useRef();
  const currentRef = useRef(null);
  const [actions, setActions] = useState(initialActions);
  const [redo, setRedo] = useState([]);
  const [tool, setTool] = useState('pen');
  const [color, setColor] = useState('#ef4444');
  const [width, setWidth] = useState(6);
  const [ready, setReady] = useState(false);

  const redraw = (items = actions, active = currentRef.current) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    const image = imageRef.current;
    if (!canvas || !image) return;
    const context = canvas.getContext('2d');
    context.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    context.drawImage(image, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    const render = action => {
      context.save();
      context.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
      context.strokeStyle = action.color;
      context.fillStyle = action.color;
      context.lineWidth = action.width;
      context.lineCap = 'round';
      context.lineJoin = 'round';
      if (action.tool === 'pen') {
        context.beginPath();
        action.points.forEach((point, index) => index ? context.lineTo(point.x, point.y) : context.moveTo(point.x, point.y));
        context.stroke();
      } else if (action.tool === 'rect') {
        context.strokeRect(action.start.x, action.start.y, action.end.x - action.start.x, action.end.y - action.start.y);
      } else if (action.tool === 'line') {
        context.beginPath(); context.moveTo(action.start.x, action.start.y); context.lineTo(action.end.x, action.end.y); context.stroke();
      } else if (action.tool === 'arrow') drawArrow(context, action.start, action.end, action.width, action.color);
      context.restore();
    };
    items.forEach(render);
    if (active) render(active);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const image = new Image();
    image.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
    image.onload = () => {
      imageRef.current = image;
      const scale = Math.min(1, 1040 / image.naturalWidth, 680 / image.naturalHeight);
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      canvas.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(image.naturalWidth * scale));
      canvas.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(image.naturalHeight * scale));
      setReady(true);
      requestAnimationFrame(() => redraw(initialActions, null));
    };
    image.onerror = () => setReady(false);
    image.src = source;
  }, [source]);

  useEffect(() => { if (ready) redraw(); }, [actions, ready]);

  const point = event => {
    const rect = canvasRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    return { x: (event.clientX - rect.left) * canvasRef.current.width / rect.width, y: (event.clientY - rect.top) * canvasRef.current.height / rect.height };
  };
  const down = event => {
    if (!ready) return;
    event.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(event.pointerId);
    const start = point(event);
    currentRef.current = tool === 'pen'
      ? { tool, color, width, points: [start] }
      : { tool, color, width, start, end: start };
    redraw(actions, currentRef.current);
  };
  const move = event => {
    const current = currentRef.current;
    if (!current) return;
    const next = point(event);
    if (current.points) current.points.push(next); else current.end = next;
    redraw(actions, current);
  };
  const up = () => {
    if (!currentRef.current) return;
    setActions(value => [...value, currentRef.current]);
    currentRef.current = null;
    setRedo([]);
  };
  const undo = () => setActions(value => {
    if (!value.length) return value;
    setRedo(items => [value.at(-1), ...items]);
    return value.slice(0, -1);
  });
  const redoAction = () => setRedo(value => {
    if (!value.length) return value;
    setActions(items => [...items, value[0]]);
    return value.slice(1);
  });
  const save = () => onSave({ dataUrl: canvasRef.current.toDataURL('image/png'), actions, width: canvasRef.current.width, height: canvasRef.current.height });

  const tools = [['pen', Pencil, 'Draw'], ['line', Minus, 'Line'], ['arrow', ArrowUpRight, 'Arrow'], ['rect', Square, 'Box']];
  return <Modal title="Draw instructions on screenshot" onClose={onClose} wide className="ai-annotator-modal">
    <div className="ai-annotator-toolbar">
      <div className="ai-annotator-tools">{tools.map(([id, Icon, label]) => <button key={id} className={tool === id ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setTool(id)}><Icon size={15}/>{label}</button>)}</div>
      <label>Colour <input type="color" value={color} onChange={event => setColor(event.target.value)}/></label>
      <label>Size <input type="range" min="2" max="24" value={width} onChange={event => setWidth(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>
      <button disabled={!actions.length} onClick={undo}><Undo2 size={14}/>Undo</button>
      <button disabled={!redo.length} onClick={redoAction}><Redo2 size={14}/>Redo</button>
      <button disabled={!actions.length} onClick={() => { setActions([]); setRedo([]); }}><Trash2 size={14}/>Clear</button>
    </div>
    <div className="ai-annotator-stage">{!ready && <span>Loading screenshot…</span>}<canvas ref={canvasRef} onPointerDown={down} onPointerMove={move} onPointerUp={up} onPointerCancel={up}/></div>
    <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={onClose}>Cancel</button><button className="primary" disabled={!ready} onClick={save}><Save size={15}/>Use annotated screenshot</button></div>
  </Modal>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AIUsagePanel.jsx

import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Coins, Gauge, RefreshCw, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import BillingActions from './BillingActions.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function AIUsagePanel() {
  const summary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const usage = useEditorStore(state => state.aiUsage);
  const load = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshCommercialData);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.commercialBusy);
  useEffect(() => { load().catch(() => {}); }, []);
  const available = summary?.credits?.available ?? usage?.availableCredits ?? 0;
  const monthly = summary?.credits?.monthlyRemaining ?? usage?.monthlyRemaining ?? 0;
  const earned = summary?.credits?.earned ?? 0;
  return <div className="ai-usage-panel">
    <BillingActions compact/>
    <div className="ai-usage-grid">
      <article><Coins size={18}/><b>{available.toLocaleString()}</b><span>Available credits</span></article>
      <article><Gauge size={18}/><b>{monthly.toLocaleString()}</b><span>Monthly credits left</span></article>
      <article><Sparkles size={18}/><b>{earned.toLocaleString()}</b><span>Marketplace earnings</span></article>
    </div>
    <button disabled={busy} onClick={() => load()}><RefreshCw className={busy ? 'spin' : ''} size={15}/>{busy ? 'Refreshing…' : 'Refresh usage'}</button>
    {!!usage?.recent?.length && <div className="ai-usage-list"><strong>Recent AI usage</strong>{usage.recent.slice(0, 12).map(item => <div key={item.id}><span>{item.jobType?.replaceAll('_', ' ') || 'AI job'}</span><b>−{item.credits} credits</b><small>{new Date(item.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</small></div>)}</div>}
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/AppearancePanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { ArrowDown, ArrowUp, Eye, EyeOff, Library, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import PaintEditor from './PaintEditor.jsx';
import PresetBrowser from './PresetBrowser.jsx';
import {
  APPEARANCE_PRESETS, BLEND_MODES, collectDocumentColors, normalizeAppearance,
  normalizeHex, paintPrimaryColor, solidPaint
} from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { readMigratedStorage, writeStorage } from '../lib/appMeta.js';

const STYLE_KEY = 'appearanceStyles';
const loadStyles = () => { try { return JSON.parse(readMigratedStorage(STYLE_KEY, '[]') || '[]'); } catch { return []; } };
const writeStyles = styles => writeStorage(STYLE_KEY, JSON.stringify(styles));
const id = prefix => `${prefix}-${crypto.randomUUID?.() || `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(16).slice(2)}`}`;
const Field = ({ label, children }) => <label className="field"><span>{label}</span>{children}</label>;
const Slider = ({ label, value, min, max, step = 1, onChange }) => <label className="paint-range"><span>{label} {Math.round(Number(value) * (step < 1 ? 100 : 1))}{step < 1 ? '%' : ''}</span><input type="range" value={value} min={min} max={max} step={step} onChange={event => onChange(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>;

function LayerHeader({ title, enabled, onToggle, onUp, onDown, onDelete, children }) {
  return <div className="appearance-layer-header">
    <button type="button" className="appearance-layer-visibility" title={enabled ? 'Hide layer' : 'Show layer'} onClick={onToggle}>{enabled ? <Eye size={14}/> : <EyeOff size={14}/>}</button>
    <strong>{title}</strong>
    <span className="appearance-layer-header-actions">{children}<button type="button" title="Move up" onClick={onUp}><ArrowUp size={13}/></button><button type="button" title="Move down" onClick={onDown}><ArrowDown size={13}/></button><button type="button" title="Delete layer" onClick={onDelete}><Trash2 size={13}/></button></span>
  </div>;
}

export default function AppearancePanel({ element, selected, patch, document }) {
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  const [styles, setStyles] = useState(loadStyles);
  const [presetBrowserOpen, setPresetBrowserOpen] = useState(false);
  const palette = useMemo(() => collectDocumentColors(document), [document]);
  const canFill = !['line', 'image', 'svg', 'qrcode'].includes(element.type);
  const canStroke = !['svg', 'qrcode'].includes(element.type);
  const stackable = ['rect', 'frame', 'ellipse', 'shape', 'line', 'path'].includes(element.type);

  const commitAppearance = producer => patch(item => {
    const current = normalizeAppearance(item);
    const next = normalizeAppearance({ ...item, appearance: producer(current, item) });
    const primaryFill = next.fills.find(layer => layer.enabled) || next.fills[0];
    const primaryStroke = next.strokes.find(layer => layer.enabled) || next.strokes[0];
    const primaryShadow = next.shadows.find(layer => layer.enabled) || next.shadows[0];
    const legacyFill = primaryFill?.paint?.type === 'none' ? 'transparent' : paintPrimaryColor(primaryFill?.paint, item.fill || '#4f46e5');
    const legacyStroke = primaryStroke?.enabled ? primaryStroke.color : 'transparent';
    const legacyStrokeWidth = primaryStroke?.enabled ? primaryStroke.width : 0;
    const legacyShadow = primaryShadow?.enabled ? { ...primaryShadow } : null;
    next.legacySnapshot = { fill: legacyFill, stroke: legacyStroke, strokeWidth: legacyStrokeWidth, effectShadow: item.type === 'text' ? legacyShadow : (item.effect?.shadow || null) };
    return {
      appearance: next,
      fill: legacyFill,
      stroke: legacyStroke,
      strokeWidth: legacyStrokeWidth,
      ...(item.type === 'text' ? { effect: { ...(item.effect || {}), shadow: legacyShadow } } : {})
    };
  });

  const setLayers = (key, layers) => commitAppearance(current => ({ ...current, [key]: layers }));
  const updateLayer = (key, index, next) => setLayers(key, appearance[key].map((layer, layerIndex) => layerIndex === index ? { ...layer, ...next } : layer));
  const removeLayer = (key, index) => {
    const layers = appearance[key].filter((_, layerIndex) => layerIndex !== index);
    setLayers(key, layers.length ? layers : key === 'fills'
      ? [{ id: id('fill'), name: 'Fill', enabled: false, opacity: 1, blendMode: 'source-over', paint: { type: 'none' } }]
      : key === 'strokes'
        ? [{ id: id('stroke'), name: 'Stroke', enabled: false, color: '#111827', opacity: 1, width: 0, alignment: 'center', style: 'solid', dash: 10, gap: 8, lineCap: 'round', lineJoin: 'round', blendMode: 'source-over' }]
        : key === 'shadows'
          ? [{ id: id('shadow'), name: 'Drop shadow', enabled: false, type: 'drop', color: '#000000', opacity: .25, blur: 20, spread: 0, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 8, blendMode: 'source-over' }]
          : []);
  };
  const moveLayer = (key, index, delta) => {
    const layers = [...appearance[key]];
    const target = Math.max(0, Math.min(layers.length - 1, index + delta));
    if (target === index) return;
    [layers[index], layers[target]] = [layers[target], layers[index]];
    setLayers(key, layers);
  };

  const applyAppearance = value => commitAppearance(() => value);
  const saveStyle = (providedName, providedAppearance = appearance) => {
    const name = providedName || prompt('Appearance style name', `${element.name || element.type} style`);
    if (!name?.trim()) return;
    const next = [{ id: id('style'), name: name.trim(), category: 'Custom', appearance: normalizeAppearance({ appearance: providedAppearance }), custom: true }, ...styles].slice(0, 48);
    setStyles(next); writeStyles(next);
  };
  const importStyles = imported => {
    const normalized = imported.map(style => ({ id: id('style'), name: style.name.trim(), category: style.category || 'Imported', appearance: normalizeAppearance({ appearance: style.appearance }), custom: true }));
    const next = [...normalized, ...styles].slice(0, 96);
    setStyles(next); writeStyles(next);
  };
  const removeStyle = styleId => { const next = styles.filter(style => style.id !== styleId); setStyles(next); writeStyles(next); };
  const browserPresets = [...APPEARANCE_PRESETS.map(preset => ({ ...preset, category: preset.category || 'Featured', custom: false })), ...styles.map(style => ({ ...style, category: style.category || 'Custom', custom: true }))];

  return <>
    <div className="appearance-preset-summary"><div><strong>Appearance presets</strong><span>Reusable fill, stroke, shadow, and blur stacks</span></div><button type="button" onClick={() => setPresetBrowserOpen(true)}><Library size={15}/>Browse</button></div>
    <div className="appearance-presets">{APPEARANCE_PRESETS.slice(0, 4).map(preset => <button type="button" key={preset.id} onClick={() => applyAppearance(preset.appearance)}><span style={{ background: paintPrimaryColor(normalizeAppearance({ appearance: preset.appearance }).fill) }}/><b>{preset.name}</b></button>)}</div>

    {canFill && <div className="appearance-stack">
      <div className="saved-style-heading"><strong>Fills</strong><button type="button" disabled={!stackable && appearance.fills.length >= 1} onClick={() => setLayers('fills', [...appearance.fills, { id: id('fill'), name: `Fill ${appearance.fills.length + 1}`, enabled: true, opacity: 1, blendMode: 'source-over', paint: solidPaint('#4f46e5') }])}><Plus size={14}/>Add</button></div>
      {appearance.fills.map((layer, index) => <details className="appearance-layer" key={layer.id || index} open={index === 0}>
        <summary><LayerHeader title={layer.name || `Fill ${index + 1}`} enabled={layer.enabled} onToggle={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); updateLayer('fills', index, { enabled: !layer.enabled }); }} onUp={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('fills', index, -1); }} onDown={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('fills', index, 1); }} onDelete={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); removeLayer('fills', index); }}/></summary>
        <div className="appearance-layer-body"><PaintEditor label={element.type === 'text' ? 'Text fill' : 'Paint'} paint={layer.paint} palette={palette} onChange={paint => updateLayer('fills', index, { paint })}/><Slider label="Layer alpha" value={layer.opacity} min={0} max={1} step={.01} onChange={opacity => updateLayer('fills', index, { opacity })}/><Field label="Blend"><select value={layer.blendMode || 'source-over'} onChange={event => updateLayer('fills', index, { blendMode: event.target.value })}>{BLEND_MODES.map(([value, name]) => <option key={value} value={value}>{name}</option>)}</select></Field></div>
      </details>)}
      {!stackable && <p className="help">Text currently uses the first visible fill. Shape and drawing layers render the complete stack.</p>}
    </div>}

    {canStroke && <div className="appearance-stack">
      <div className="saved-style-heading"><strong>{element.type === 'text' ? 'Outlines' : 'Strokes'}</strong><button type="button" disabled={!stackable && appearance.strokes.length >= 1} onClick={() => setLayers('strokes', [...appearance.strokes, { id: id('stroke'), name: `Stroke ${appearance.strokes.length + 1}`, enabled: true, color: '#111827', opacity: 1, width: 2, alignment: 'center', style: 'solid', dash: 10, gap: 8, lineCap: 'round', lineJoin: 'round', blendMode: 'source-over' }])}><Plus size={14}/>Add</button></div>
      {appearance.strokes.map((stroke, index) => <details className="appearance-layer" key={stroke.id || index} open={index === 0}>
        <summary><LayerHeader title={stroke.name || `Stroke ${index + 1}`} enabled={stroke.enabled} onToggle={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); updateLayer('strokes', index, { enabled: !stroke.enabled, width: Math.max(1, stroke.width || 1) }); }} onUp={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('strokes', index, -1); }} onDown={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('strokes', index, 1); }} onDelete={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); removeLayer('strokes', index); }}/></summary>
        <div className="appearance-layer-body">
          <div className="colour-alpha-row"><label className="compact-field"><span>Colour</span><input type="color" value={normalizeHex(stroke.color)} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { color: event.target.value })}/></label><label className="compact-field grow"><span>Hex</span><input value={stroke.color} onChange={event => /^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(event.target.value) && updateLayer('strokes', index, { color: event.target.value })}/></label></div>
          <Slider label="Alpha" value={stroke.opacity} min={0} max={1} step={.01} onChange={opacity => updateLayer('strokes', index, { opacity })}/><Slider label="Width" value={stroke.width} min={0} max={80} step={.5} onChange={width => updateLayer('strokes', index, { width })}/>
          <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Style"><select value={stroke.style} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { style: event.target.value })}><option value="solid">Solid</option><option value="dashed">Dashed</option><option value="dotted">Dotted</option><option value="custom">Custom</option></select></Field><Field label="Alignment"><select value={stroke.alignment || 'center'} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { alignment: event.target.value })}><option value="inside">Inside</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="outside">Outside</option></select></Field></div>
          <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Cap"><select value={stroke.lineCap} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { lineCap: event.target.value })}><option value="butt">Butt</option><option value="round">Round</option><option value="square">Square</option></select></Field><Field label="Join"><select value={stroke.lineJoin} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { lineJoin: event.target.value })}><option value="miter">Miter</option><option value="round">Round</option><option value="bevel">Bevel</option></select></Field></div>
          {stroke.style !== 'solid' && <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Dash"><input type="number" min="1" value={stroke.dash} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { dash: Math.max(1, Number(event.target.value)) })}/></Field><Field label="Gap"><input type="number" min="1" value={stroke.gap} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { gap: Math.max(1, Number(event.target.value)) })}/></Field></div>}
          <Field label="Blend"><select value={stroke.blendMode || 'source-over'} onChange={event => updateLayer('strokes', index, { blendMode: event.target.value })}>{BLEND_MODES.map(([value, name]) => <option key={value} value={value}>{name}</option>)}</select></Field>
        </div>
      </details>)}
    </div>}

    <div className="appearance-stack">
      <div className="saved-style-heading"><strong>Shadows</strong><button type="button" onClick={() => setLayers('shadows', [...appearance.shadows, { id: id('shadow'), name: `Shadow ${appearance.shadows.length + 1}`, enabled: true, type: 'drop', color: '#000000', opacity: .25, blur: 24, spread: 0, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 10, blendMode: 'source-over' }])}><Plus size={14}/>Add</button></div>
      {appearance.shadows.map((shadow, index) => <details className="appearance-layer" key={shadow.id || index} open={index === 0}>
        <summary><LayerHeader title={shadow.name || `Shadow ${index + 1}`} enabled={shadow.enabled} onToggle={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); updateLayer('shadows', index, { enabled: !shadow.enabled }); }} onUp={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('shadows', index, -1); }} onDown={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); moveLayer('shadows', index, 1); }} onDelete={event => { event?.preventDefault?.(); removeLayer('shadows', index); }}/></summary>
        <div className="appearance-layer-body"><div className="field-grid"><Field label="Type"><select value={shadow.type || 'drop'} onChange={event => updateLayer('shadows', index, { type: event.target.value, name: event.target.value === 'inner' ? 'Inner shadow' : 'Drop shadow' })}><option value="drop">Drop shadow</option><option value="inner">Inner shadow</option></select></Field><Field label="Colour"><input type="color" value={normalizeHex(shadow.color)} onChange={event => updateLayer('shadows', index, { color: event.target.value })}/></Field></div><Slider label="Alpha" value={shadow.opacity} min={0} max={1} step={.01} onChange={opacity => updateLayer('shadows', index, { opacity })}/><Slider label="Blur" value={shadow.blur} min={0} max={160} onChange={blur => updateLayer('shadows', index, { blur })}/><Slider label="Spread" value={shadow.spread || 0} min={-100} max={200} onChange={spread => updateLayer('shadows', index, { spread })}/><div className="field-grid"><Field label="Offset X"><input type="number" min="-200" max="200" value={shadow.offsetX} onChange={event => updateLayer('shadows', index, { offsetX: Number(event.target.value) })}/></Field><Field label="Offset Y"><input type="number" min="-200" max="200" value={shadow.offsetY} onChange={event => updateLayer('shadows', index, { offsetY: Number(event.target.value) })}/></Field></div></div>
      </details>)}
    </div>

    <div className="appearance-stack">
      <div className="saved-style-heading"><strong>Blur effects</strong><button type="button" onClick={() => setLayers('effects', [...appearance.effects, { id: id('effect'), name: 'Layer blur', enabled: true, type: 'layer-blur', amount: 8 }])}><Plus size={14}/>Add</button></div>
      {appearance.effects.map((effect, index) => <div className="appearance-layer appearance-effect-row" key={effect.id || index}><button type="button" onClick={() => updateLayer('effects', index, { enabled: !effect.enabled })}>{effect.enabled ? <Eye size={14}/> : <EyeOff size={14}/>}</button><select value={effect.type} onChange={event => updateLayer('effects', index, { type: event.target.value, name: event.target.value === 'background-blur' ? 'Background blur' : 'Layer blur' })}><option value="layer-blur">Layer blur</option><option value="background-blur">Background blur</option></select><input type="number" min="0" max="160" value={effect.amount} onChange={event => updateLayer('effects', index, { amount: Number(event.target.value) })}/><button type="button" onClick={() => removeLayer('effects', index)}><Trash2 size={13}/></button></div>)}
    </div>

    <Field label="Layer blend mode"><select value={appearance.blendMode} onChange={event => commitAppearance(current => ({ ...current, blendMode: event.target.value }))}>{BLEND_MODES.map(([value, name]) => <option key={value} value={value}>{name}</option>)}</select></Field>
    <div className="saved-style-heading"><strong>Saved appearance styles</strong><button type="button" title="Save selected appearance" onClick={() => saveStyle()}><Plus size={14}/>Save</button></div>
    {!!styles.length && <div className="saved-style-list">{styles.map(style => <div key={style.id}><button type="button" className="saved-style-apply" onClick={() => applyAppearance(style.appearance)}><span style={{ background: paintPrimaryColor(normalizeAppearance({ appearance: style.appearance }).fill) }}/>{style.name}</button><button type="button" title="Delete style" onClick={() => removeStyle(style.id)}><Trash2 size={13}/></button></div>)}</div>}
    {selected.length > 1 && <p className="help">Appearance changes apply to all {selected.length} selected elements while preserving geometry.</p>}
    {presetBrowserOpen && <PresetBrowser presets={browserPresets} currentAppearance={appearance} onApply={applyAppearance} onSave={saveStyle} onImport={importStyles} onDelete={removeStyle} onClose={() => setPresetBrowserOpen(false)}/>}
  </>;
}

================================================================================
// FILE: src/components/BillingActions.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { CheckCircle2, Coins, CreditCard, ExternalLink, LoaderCircle, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';
import { api } from '../lib/api.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

const FALLBACK_PACKAGES = [500, 1000, 2500, 5000].map(credits => ({ credits, label: `${credits.toLocaleString()} credits` }));

function safeRedirect(result) {
  const url = result?.url;
  if (!url) throw new Error('The payment service did not return a checkout link. Ask the workspace owner to finish the Stripe setup.');
  const parsed = new URL(url, location.origin);
  if (!['http:', 'https:'].includes(parsed.protocol)) throw new Error('The payment service returned an invalid checkout link.');
  location.assign(parsed.href);
}

function normalizePackages(status, summary) {
  const source = status?.creditPackages || summary?.creditPackages || [];
  const normalized = source.map(item => {
    const credits = Number(item.credits ?? item.amount ?? item.value);
    if (!Number.isFinite(credits) || credits <= 0) return null;
    return {
      credits,
      label: item.label || `${credits.toLocaleString()} credits`,
      priceLabel: item.priceLabel || item.formattedPrice || ''
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);
  return normalized.length ? normalized : FALLBACK_PACKAGES;
}

export default function BillingActions({ compact = false, showInstructions = true, showPlans = false }) {
  const summary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const refresh = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshCommercialData);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const [status, setStatus] = useState(null);
  const [selectedCredits, setSelectedCredits] = useState(1000);
  const [busyAction, setBusyAction] = useState('');

  const packages = useMemo(() => normalizePackages(status, summary), [status, summary]);
  const available = Number(summary?.credits?.available || 0);
  const configured = status?.configured !== false;
  const hasPaymentMethod = status?.hasPaymentMethod ?? summary?.paymentMethod?.attached ?? summary?.payments?.hasPaymentMethod ?? false;

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    api.billingStatus().then(result => {
      if (cancelled) return;
      setStatus(result);
      const first = normalizePackages(result, summary)[0];
      if (first && !normalizePackages(result, summary).some(item => item.credits === selectedCredits)) setSelectedCredits(first.credits);
    }).catch(() => {
      if (!cancelled) setStatus({ configured: null });
    });
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, []);

  const run = async (action, callback) => {
    setBusyAction(action);
    try { safeRedirect(await callback()); }
    catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
    finally { setBusyAction(''); }
  };

  const buyCredits = () => run('credits', () => api.purchaseCredits({ amount: selectedCredits }));
  const setupCard = () => run('card', () => api.billingSetupCard());
  const openPortal = () => run('portal', () => api.billingPortal());
  const upgrade = plan => run(plan, () => api.billingCheckout({ type: 'subscription', plan }));

  if (compact) return <div className="billing-actions-compact">
    <div className="billing-credit-balance"><Coins size={17}/><span><b>{available.toLocaleString()}</b><small>credits available</small></span></div>
    <select aria-label="Credit package" value={selectedCredits} onChange={event => setSelectedCredits(Number(event.target.value))}>{packages.map(item => <option key={item.credits} value={item.credits}>{item.label}{item.priceLabel ? ` · ${item.priceLabel}` : ''}</option>)}</select>
    <button className="primary" disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={buyCredits}>{busyAction === 'credits' ? <LoaderCircle className="spin" size={14}/> : <Coins size={14}/>}Add credits</button>
    <button disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={setupCard}>{busyAction === 'card' ? <LoaderCircle className="spin" size={14}/> : <CreditCard size={14}/>}Add card</button>
  </div>;

  return <div className="billing-actions">
    {status?.configured === false && <div className="billing-not-configured"><strong>Payments are not available yet.</strong><span>The workspace owner must connect Stripe before cards or credit purchases can be accepted.</span></div>}

    <div className="billing-action-grid">
      <section>
        <div className="billing-action-heading"><Coins size={18}/><div><h3>Add credits</h3><p>Choose a package, continue to checkout, and pay by card.</p></div></div>
        <div className="credit-topup-row">
          <select value={selectedCredits} onChange={event => setSelectedCredits(Number(event.target.value))}>
            {packages.map(item => <option key={item.credits} value={item.credits}>{item.label}{item.priceLabel ? ` · ${item.priceLabel}` : ''}</option>)}
          </select>
          <button className="primary" disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={buyCredits}>{busyAction === 'credits' ? <LoaderCircle className="spin" size={15}/> : <ExternalLink size={15}/>}Continue to checkout</button>
        </div>
        {showInstructions && <ol className="billing-steps"><li>Select the number of credits.</li><li>Complete payment on Stripe’s secure checkout page.</li><li>Return to CanvasForge; credits appear after payment confirmation.</li></ol>}
      </section>

      <section>
        <div className="billing-action-heading"><CreditCard size={18}/><div><h3>{hasPaymentMethod ? 'Payment card' : 'Link a payment card'}</h3><p>{hasPaymentMethod ? 'A card is linked to this workspace.' : 'Add a card without buying credits first.'}</p></div></div>
        <div className="billing-card-status">{hasPaymentMethod ? <><CheckCircle2 size={16}/><span>{status?.paymentMethodLabel || summary?.paymentMethod?.label || 'Card linked'}</span></> : <><CreditCard size={16}/><span>No card linked</span></>}</div>
        <div className="button-row wrap">
          <button className="primary" disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={setupCard}>{busyAction === 'card' ? <LoaderCircle className="spin" size={15}/> : <CreditCard size={15}/>}Add or replace card</button>
          <button disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={openPortal}>{busyAction === 'portal' ? <LoaderCircle className="spin" size={15}/> : <ExternalLink size={15}/>}Billing portal</button>
          <button onClick={() => refresh().catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error'))}><RefreshCw size={15}/>Refresh status</button>
        </div>
        {showInstructions && <ol className="billing-steps"><li>Open card setup.</li><li>Enter the card on Stripe’s secure page.</li><li>Return here to use it for subscriptions and future purchases.</li></ol>}
      </section>
    </div>

    {showPlans && <section className="billing-plan-actions"><div><h3>Upgrade workspace</h3><p>Choose a recurring plan for monthly credits and additional workspace features.</p></div><div className="button-row wrap"><button className="primary" disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={() => upgrade('pro')}>{busyAction === 'pro' ? 'Opening…' : 'Choose Pro'}</button><button disabled={!configured || !!busyAction} onClick={() => upgrade('team')}>{busyAction === 'team' ? 'Opening…' : 'Choose Team'}</button></div></section>}
  </div>;
}

================================================================================
