import React, { forwardRef, useEffect, useImperativeHandle, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { ArrowUpToLine, Brush, Copy, Group, Highlighter, MousePointer2, PenLine, Trash2, Ungroup } from 'lucide-react';
import { ActiveSelection, Canvas, Line, PencilBrush, Point, Rect, util } from 'fabric';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { applyAllFrameLayouts, clone, cloneElementTree, collectDescendantIds, imageElement, pathElement, svgElement, textElement, transformFrameDescendants } from '../lib/document.js';
import { createGuide, elementToObject, objectTransformToPatch, paintToFabric, textObjectToPatch } from '../lib/fabricAdapter.js';
import { reconcileFabricElements } from '../lib/fabricReconciler.js';
import { sanitizeSvgMarkup } from '../lib/svg.js';
import { paintToCss } from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { ensureFontsLoaded } from '../lib/fonts.js';
import {
  ASSET_DRAG_TYPE, CLIPBOARD_PREFIX, ESCAPE_EVENT, LEGACY_ASSET_DRAG_TYPE,
  LEGACY_CLIPBOARD_PREFIX, LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT, LAYER_DRAG_TYPE, LEGACY_LAYER_DRAG_TYPE,
  readMigratedStorage, writeStorage
} from '../lib/appMeta.js';

const round = value => Math.round(value * 100) / 100;
const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
const PAGE_PADDING = 200;
const ALLOWED_CLIPBOARD_TYPES = new Set(['text', 'rect', 'frame', 'ellipse', 'shape', 'line', 'path', 'image', 'svg', 'chart', 'table', 'qrcode']);

const isSvgMarkup = value => /^\s*<svg\b[\s\S]*<\/svg>\s*$/i.test(String(value || ''));
const htmlSvgMarkup = value => String(value || '').match(/<svg\b[\s\S]*?<\/svg>/i)?.[0] || '';
const rgbaFromHex = (hex, opacity = 1) => {
  const value = String(hex || '#111827').replace('#', '');
  const normalized = value.length === 3 ? value.split('').map(char => char + char).join('') : value.padEnd(6, '0').slice(0, 6);
  const parts = [0, 2, 4].map(index => parseInt(normalized.slice(index, index + 2), 16) || 0);
  return `rgba(${parts[0]}, ${parts[1]}, ${parts[2]}, ${clamp(opacity, 0, 1)})`;
};

function Ruler({ axis, length, zoom, onStartGuide, offset = 0 }) {
  const step = zoom >= 1.5 ? 25 : zoom >= .75 ? 50 : 100;
  const ticks = [];
  for (let value = 0; value <= length; value += step) ticks.push(value);
  return <div className={`ruler ruler-${axis}`} onPointerDown={event => {
    event.preventDefault();
    onStartGuide(axis === 'horizontal' ? 'vertical' : 'horizontal', event);
  }}>
    {ticks.map(value => <div key={value} className="ruler-tick" style={axis === 'horizontal' ? { left: value * zoom + offset } : { top: value * zoom + offset }}>
      <span>{value}</span>
    </div>)}
  </div>;
}

function selectedElementIds(canvas) {
  const active = canvas?.getActiveObjects?.() || [];
  return active.filter(object => !object.isGuide && object.elementId).map(object => object.elementId);
}

function sceneTransformPatch(object, element) {
  const localPoint = object.getPointByOrigin?.('left', 'top') || { x: object.left || 0, y: object.top || 0 };
  const point = object.group ? util.transformPoint(localPoint, object.group.calcTransformMatrix()) : localPoint;
  const totalScale = object.getObjectScaling?.() || { x: object.scaleX || 1, y: object.scaleY || 1 };
  const scaleX = Math.abs(totalScale.x || 1);
  const scaleY = Math.abs(totalScale.y || 1);
  const patch = {
    x: point.x,
    y: point.y - Number(object.canvasforgeFrameOffsetY || 0),
    rotation: object.getTotalAngle?.() ?? object.angle ?? 0,
    opacity: object.opacity ?? 1,
    flipX: !!object.flipX,
    flipY: !!object.flipY,
    width: Math.max(element.type === 'text' ? 20 : 1, (object.width || element.width || 1) * scaleX),
    height: Math.max(1, (object.height || element.height || 1) * scaleY)
  };
  if (element.type === 'text') {
    Object.assign(patch, {
      text: object.text,
      styles: object.styles || {},
      fontFamily: object.fontFamily,
      fontSize: Math.max(4, (object.fontSize || element.fontSize || 48) * scaleY),
      fontWeight: object.fontWeight,
      fontStyle: object.fontStyle,
      underline: object.underline,
      linethrough: object.linethrough,
      fill: element.effect?.hollow ? element.fill : (typeof object.fill === 'string' ? object.fill : element.fill),
      textAlign: object.textAlign,
      lineHeight: object.lineHeight,
      charSpacing: object.charSpacing,
      textBackgroundColor: object.textBackgroundColor || ''
    });
  }
  return patch;
}

function describeTarget(target) {
  if (!target) return null;
  const bounds = target.getBoundingRect();
  return {
    x: round(bounds.left),
    y: round(bounds.top),
    width: round(bounds.width),
    height: round(bounds.height),
    rotation: round(target.getTotalAngle?.() ?? target.angle ?? 0)
  };
}

const CanvasEditor = forwardRef(function CanvasEditor({ renderMode = false, readOnly = false }, ref) {
  const canvasEl = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  const scrollRef = useRef(null);
  const stageRef = useRef(null);
  const loadingRef = useRef(false);
  const cropRef = useRef(null);
  const textSnapshotRef = useRef(null);
  const transformSnapshotRef = useRef(null);
  const hierarchyPreviewRef = useRef(null);
  const smartGuideRef = useRef([]);
  const latestRef = useRef({ page: null, pageSize: { width: 1080, height: 1080 }, zoom: 1, renderMode, readOnly });
  const cropModeRef = useRef(false);
  const skipReloadRef = useRef(false);
  const spacePressedRef = useRef(false);
  const nudgeTimerRef = useRef(null);
  const panRef = useRef(null);
  const guideDragRef = useRef(null);
  const selectionSyncRef = useRef(false);
  const renderStateRef = useRef({ pageId: null, signatures: new Map(), objects: new Map() });
  const renderMetaRef = useRef(null);
  const lastPointerRef = useRef(null);
  const drawingSnapshotRef = useRef(null);
  const drawingSettingsRef = useRef({ preset: 'pen', color: '#111827', width: 6, opacity: 1 });

  const [zoom, setZoomState] = useState(renderMode ? 1 : .65);
  const [zoomMenu, setZoomMenu] = useState(false);
  const [contextMenu, setContextMenu] = useState(null);
  const [cropMode, setCropMode] = useState(false);
  const [transformInfo, setTransformInfo] = useState(null);
  const [guidePreview, setGuidePreview] = useState(null);
  const [rulerOrigin, setRulerOrigin] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const [panning, setPanning] = useState(false);
  const [drawingMode, setDrawingMode] = useState(false);
  const [brushPreset, setBrushPreset] = useState('pen');
  const [brushColor, setBrushColor] = useState('#111827');
  const [brushWidth, setBrushWidth] = useState(6);
  const [brushOpacity, setBrushOpacity] = useState(1);
  drawingSettingsRef.current = { preset: brushPreset, color: brushColor, width: brushWidth, opacity: brushOpacity };

  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const setSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.setSelection);
  const updatePage = useEditorStore(state => state.updatePage);
  const updateElements = useEditorStore(state => state.updateElements);
  const addElement = useEditorStore(state => state.addElement);
  const addElements = useEditorStore(state => state.addElements);
  const removeSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.removeSelection);
  const commitDocument = useEditorStore(state => state.commitDocument);
  const pushHistorySnapshot = useEditorStore(state => state.pushHistorySnapshot);
  const beginHistoryTransaction = useEditorStore(state => state.beginHistoryTransaction);
  const commitHistoryTransaction = useEditorStore(state => state.commitHistoryTransaction);
  const upload = useEditorStore(state => state.upload);
  const assets = useEditorStore(state => state.assets);
  const groupSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.groupSelection);
  const ungroupSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.ungroupSelection);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const showRulers = useEditorStore(state => state.showRulers);
  const showGuides = useEditorStore(state => state.showGuides);
  const snapToPage = useEditorStore(state => state.snapToPage);
  const snapToGuides = useEditorStore(state => state.snapToGuides);
  const snapToObjects = useEditorStore(state => state.snapToObjects);
  const snapToGrid = useEditorStore(state => state.snapToGrid);
  const snapToMargins = useEditorStore(state => state.snapToMargins);

  const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex];
  cropModeRef.current = cropMode;
  const pageSize = useMemo(() => ({ width: document?.width || 1080, height: document?.height || 1080 }), [document?.width, document?.height]);
  const isInteractive = !renderMode && !readOnly;
  const pad = isInteractive ? PAGE_PADDING : 0;
  latestRef.current = { page, pageSize, zoom, renderMode, readOnly, snapToPage, snapToGuides, snapToObjects, snapToGrid, snapToMargins };

  const removeSmartGuides = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    smartGuideRef.current.forEach(line => canvas.remove(line));
    smartGuideRef.current = [];
  };

  const addSmartGuide = (axis, value) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    const latest = latestRef.current;
    if (!canvas || latest.renderMode || latest.readOnly) return;
    const line = new Line(axis === 'vertical'
      ? [value, 0, value, latest.pageSize.height]
      : [0, value, latest.pageSize.width, value], {
      stroke: '#ec4899',
      strokeWidth: 1 / latest.zoom,
      strokeDashArray: [4 / latest.zoom, 4 / latest.zoom],
      selectable: false,
      evented: false,
      excludeFromExport: true,
      isSmartGuide: true
    });
    smartGuideRef.current.push(line);
    canvas.add(line);
    canvas.bringObjectToFront(line);
  };

  const snapMovingObject = (object, nativeEvent) => {
    const latest = latestRef.current;
    if (latest.renderMode || latest.readOnly || object?.isGuide || object?.lockMovementX || nativeEvent?.altKey) return;
    removeSmartGuides();
    const threshold = 7 / latest.zoom;
    const bounds = object.getBoundingRect();
    const xEdges = [bounds.left, bounds.left + bounds.width / 2, bounds.left + bounds.width];
    const yEdges = [bounds.top, bounds.top + bounds.height / 2, bounds.top + bounds.height];
    const xTargets = [];
    const yTargets = [];
    if (latest.snapToPage) {
      xTargets.push(0, latest.pageSize.width / 2, latest.pageSize.width);
      yTargets.push(0, latest.pageSize.height / 2, latest.pageSize.height);
    }
    if (latest.snapToMargins) {
      const margins = latest.page?.margins || {};
      xTargets.push(Number(margins.left || 0), latest.pageSize.width - Number(margins.right || 0));
      yTargets.push(Number(margins.top || 0), latest.pageSize.height - Number(margins.bottom || 0));
    }
    if (latest.snapToGrid && latest.page?.grid?.enabled) {
      const step = Math.max(2, Number(latest.page.grid.size || 20) / Math.max(1, Number(latest.page.grid.subdivisions || 1)));
      xEdges.forEach(edge => xTargets.push(Math.round(edge / step) * step));
      yEdges.forEach(edge => yTargets.push(Math.round(edge / step) * step));
    }
    if (latest.snapToGuides) {
      xTargets.push(...(latest.page?.guides?.vertical || []));
      yTargets.push(...(latest.page?.guides?.horizontal || []));
    }
    if (latest.snapToObjects) canvasRef.current.getObjects().forEach(other => {
      if (other === object || other.isGuide || other.isSmartGuide || !other.visible || object.getObjects?.().includes(other)) return;
      const box = other.getBoundingRect();
      xTargets.push(box.left, box.left + box.width / 2, box.left + box.width);
      yTargets.push(box.top, box.top + box.height / 2, box.top + box.height);
    });
    let bestX = null;
    let bestY = null;
    for (const edge of xEdges) for (const target of xTargets) {
      const diff = target - edge;
      if (Math.abs(diff) <= threshold && (!bestX || Math.abs(diff) < Math.abs(bestX.diff))) bestX = { diff, target };
    }
    for (const edge of yEdges) for (const target of yTargets) {
      const diff = target - edge;
      if (Math.abs(diff) <= threshold && (!bestY || Math.abs(diff) < Math.abs(bestY.diff))) bestY = { diff, target };
    }
    if (bestX) { object.left += bestX.diff; addSmartGuide('vertical', bestX.target); }
    if (bestY) { object.top += bestY.diff; addSmartGuide('horizontal', bestY.target); }
    object.setCoords();
  };

  const syncTextObject = (object, { history = false } = {}) => {
    if (!object?.elementId) return;
    const state = useEditorStore.getState();
    const currentPage = state.document?.pages?.[state.pageIndex];
    const element = currentPage?.elements?.find(item => item.id === object.elementId);
    if (!element) return;
    const patch = textObjectToPatch(object, element);
    skipReloadRef.current = true;
    updateElements([element.id], patch, { recordHistory: history });
    object.set({ scaleX: 1, scaleY: 1, width: patch.width, fontSize: patch.fontSize });
    object.initDimensions?.();
    object.setCoords();
  };

  const previewFrameHierarchy = target => {
    if (!target?.elementId || target.type === 'activeselection') return;
    const preview = hierarchyPreviewRef.current;
    if (!preview || preview.frameId !== target.elementId) return;
    const beforePage = preview.beforePage;
    const beforeFrame = beforePage.elements.find(item => item.id === preview.frameId);
    if (!beforeFrame) return;
    const nextPage = clone(beforePage);
    const nextFrame = nextPage.elements.find(item => item.id === preview.frameId);
    Object.assign(nextFrame, objectTransformToPatch(target, beforeFrame));
    transformFrameDescendants(nextPage, nextFrame.id, beforeFrame, nextFrame);
    applyAllFrameLayouts(nextPage);
    for (const [id, initial] of preview.children) {
      const beforeElement = beforePage.elements.find(item => item.id === id);
      const nextElement = nextPage.elements.find(item => item.id === id);
      if (!beforeElement || !nextElement || !initial.object) continue;
      initial.object.set({
        left: nextElement.x,
        top: nextElement.y,
        angle: nextElement.rotation || 0,
        scaleX: initial.scaleX * nextElement.width / Math.max(1, beforeElement.width),
        scaleY: initial.scaleY * nextElement.height / Math.max(1, beforeElement.height)
      });
      initial.object.setCoords();
    }
    canvasRef.current?.requestRenderAll();
  };

  const syncModifiedTarget = target => {
    if (!target || target.isGuide) return;
    const state = useEditorStore.getState();
    const currentPage = state.document?.pages?.[state.pageIndex];
    if (!currentPage) return;
    const targets = target instanceof ActiveSelection || target.type === 'activeselection' ? target.getObjects() : [target];
    const patches = {};
    for (const object of targets) {
      const element = currentPage.elements.find(item => item.id === object.elementId);
      if (!element) continue;
      patches[element.id] = targets.length > 1
        ? sceneTransformPatch(object, element)
        : (element.type === 'text' ? textObjectToPatch(object, element) : objectTransformToPatch(object, element));
    }
    if (!Object.keys(patches).length) return;
    const before = transformSnapshotRef.current || clone(state.document);
    const next = clone(state.document);
    const nextPage = next.pages[state.pageIndex];
    const previousPage = before.pages[state.pageIndex];
    nextPage.elements = nextPage.elements.map(element => patches[element.id] ? { ...element, ...patches[element.id] } : element);
    const patchedIds = new Set(Object.keys(patches));
    const rootPatchedIds = new Set([...patchedIds].filter(id => {
      let parentId = nextPage.elements.find(item => item.id === id)?.parentId;
      while (parentId) {
        if (patchedIds.has(parentId)) return false;
        parentId = nextPage.elements.find(item => item.id === parentId)?.parentId;
      }
      return true;
    }));
    for (const id of rootPatchedIds) {
      const item = nextPage.elements.find(element => element.id === id);
      if (!item || item.locked) continue;
      const descendants = collectDescendantIds(nextPage, item.id);
      const center = { x: item.x + item.width / 2, y: item.y + item.height / 2 };
      const containers = nextPage.elements.filter(frame => frame.type === 'frame' && frame.id !== item.id && !patchedIds.has(frame.id) && !descendants.has(frame.id) && center.x >= frame.x && center.x <= frame.x + frame.width && center.y >= frame.y && center.y <= frame.y + frame.height);
      containers.sort((a, b) => a.width * a.height - b.width * b.height);
      item.parentId = containers[0]?.id || null;
    }
    const rootFrames = nextPage.elements.filter(element => patchedIds.has(element.id) && element.type === 'frame').filter(frame => {
      let parentId = previousPage.elements.find(item => item.id === frame.id)?.parentId;
      while (parentId) {
        if (patchedIds.has(parentId)) return false;
        parentId = previousPage.elements.find(item => item.id === parentId)?.parentId;
      }
      return true;
    });
    for (const frame of rootFrames) {
      const previous = previousPage.elements.find(item => item.id === frame.id);
      if (previous) transformFrameDescendants(nextPage, frame.id, previous, frame);
    }
    applyAllFrameLayouts(nextPage);
    skipReloadRef.current = false;
    commitDocument(next, { recordHistory: false });
    pushHistorySnapshot(before);
    transformSnapshotRef.current = null;
  };

  const syncGuide = object => {
    if (!object?.isGuide) return;
    const axis = object.guideAxis;
    const limit = axis === 'vertical' ? pageSize.width : pageSize.height;
    const value = round(axis === 'vertical' ? object.left : object.top);
    skipReloadRef.current = true;
    updatePage(currentPage => {
      if (value < 0 || value > limit) currentPage.guides[axis].splice(object.guideIndex, 1);
      else {
        const values = [...currentPage.guides[axis]];
        values[object.guideIndex] = value;
        currentPage.guides[axis] = values.sort((a, b) => a - b);
      }
    });
  };

  const startGuideDrag = (axis, event) => {
    if (readOnly || renderMode) return;
    const calculate = pointerEvent => {
      const rect = stageRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (!rect) return null;
      const pageLeft = rect.left + pad;
      const pageTop = rect.top + pad;
      const raw = axis === 'vertical' ? pointerEvent.clientX - pageLeft : pointerEvent.clientY - pageTop;
      return { rect, pageLeft, pageTop, value: round(raw / zoom) };
    };
    const first = calculate(event);
    if (!first) return;
    const token = { cancelled: false };
    guideDragRef.current = token;
    setGuidePreview({ axis, value: first.value });
    const move = pointerEvent => {
      const next = calculate(pointerEvent);
      if (!token.cancelled && next) setGuidePreview({ axis, value: next.value });
    };
    const up = pointerEvent => {
      const next = calculate(pointerEvent);
      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', move);
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', up);
      setGuidePreview(null);
      guideDragRef.current = null;
      if (token.cancelled || !next) return;
      const within = axis === 'vertical'
        ? pointerEvent.clientX >= next.pageLeft && pointerEvent.clientX <= next.pageLeft + pageSize.width * zoom
        : pointerEvent.clientY >= next.pageTop && pointerEvent.clientY <= next.pageTop + pageSize.height * zoom;
      const limit = axis === 'vertical' ? pageSize.width : pageSize.height;
      if (within && next.value >= 0 && next.value <= limit) controller.addGuide(axis, next.value);
    };
    window.addEventListener('pointermove', move);
    window.addEventListener('pointerup', up, { once: true });
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!canvasEl.current || canvasRef.current) return;
    const canvas = new Canvas(canvasEl.current, {
      preserveObjectStacking: true,
      selection: !renderMode && !readOnly,
      stopContextMenu: true,
      fireRightClick: true,
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      uniformScaling: false,
      uniScaleKey: 'shiftKey',
      centeredScaling: false,
      selectionFullyContained: false,
      selectionColor: 'rgba(79, 70, 229, .10)',
      selectionBorderColor: '#4f46e5',
      selectionLineWidth: 1,
      selectionDashArray: [6, 4]
    });
    canvasRef.current = canvas;

    const onSelection = () => {
      if (selectionSyncRef.current) return;
      const ids = selectedElementIds(canvas);
      const state = useEditorStore.getState();
      const currentPage = state.document?.pages?.[state.pageIndex];
      const groupIds = new Set((currentPage?.elements || []).filter(element => ids.includes(element.id)).map(element => element.groupId).filter(Boolean));
      const expandedIds = groupIds.size
        ? [...new Set([...ids, ...(currentPage?.elements || []).filter(element => groupIds.has(element.groupId) && !element.hidden && !element.locked).map(element => element.id)])]
        : ids;
      if (expandedIds.length !== ids.length || expandedIds.some(id => !ids.includes(id))) {
        const objects = canvas.getObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide && !object.isSmartGuide && expandedIds.includes(object.elementId));
        selectionSyncRef.current = true;
        canvas.discardActiveObject();
        if (objects.length === 1) canvas.setActiveObject(objects[0]);
        else if (objects.length > 1) canvas.setActiveObject(new ActiveSelection(objects, { canvas }));
        canvas.requestRenderAll();
        selectionSyncRef.current = false;
      }
      setSelection(expandedIds);
    };
    canvas.on('selection:created', onSelection);
    canvas.on('selection:updated', onSelection);
    canvas.on('selection:cleared', () => { if (!selectionSyncRef.current) setSelection([]); });
    canvas.on('before:transform', event => {
      transformSnapshotRef.current = clone(useEditorStore.getState().document);
      hierarchyPreviewRef.current = null;
      if (event.target?.elementId) {
        const state = useEditorStore.getState();
        const currentPage = state.document?.pages?.[state.pageIndex];
        const element = currentPage?.elements?.find(item => item.id === event.target.elementId);
        if (element?.type === 'frame') {
          const descendantIds = collectDescendantIds(currentPage, element.id);
          hierarchyPreviewRef.current = {
            frameId: element.id,
            beforePage: clone(currentPage),
            children: new Map([...descendantIds].map(id => {
              const object = canvas.getObjects().find(item => item.elementId === id);
              return [id, object ? { object, scaleX: object.scaleX || 1, scaleY: object.scaleY || 1 } : null];
            }).filter(([, value]) => value))
          };
        }
      }
      if (event.target) {
        event.target.centeredScaling = !!event.e?.altKey;
        event.target.snapAngle = event.e?.shiftKey ? 15 : 0;
        event.target.snapThreshold = event.e?.shiftKey ? 7 : 0;
      }
    });
    canvas.on('object:moving', event => {
      const { target } = event;
      if (target?.isGuide) {
        if (target.guideAxis === 'vertical') target.top = 0;
        else target.left = 0;
        target.setCoords();
      } else { snapMovingObject(target, event.e); previewFrameHierarchy(target); }
      setTransformInfo(describeTarget(target));
    });
    canvas.on('object:scaling', ({ target }) => {
      const preserve = target?.maintainAspectRatio || target?.getObjects?.().every(object => object.maintainAspectRatio);
      if (preserve && target) {
        const scale = Math.max(Math.abs(target.scaleX || 1), Math.abs(target.scaleY || 1));
        target.set({ scaleX: Math.sign(target.scaleX || 1) * scale, scaleY: Math.sign(target.scaleY || 1) * scale });
        target.setCoords();
      }
      previewFrameHierarchy(target);
      setTransformInfo(describeTarget(target));
    });
    canvas.on('object:rotating', ({ target }) => { previewFrameHierarchy(target); setTransformInfo(describeTarget(target)); });
    canvas.on('object:modified', ({ target }) => {
      removeSmartGuides();
      setTransformInfo(null);
      if (target?.isGuide) { syncGuide(target); transformSnapshotRef.current = null; }
      else syncModifiedTarget(target);
      hierarchyPreviewRef.current = null;
    });
    canvas.on('path:created', ({ path }) => {
      if (!path || readOnly || renderMode) return;
      const settings = drawingSettingsRef.current;
      const width = Math.max(1, (path.width || 1) * Math.abs(path.scaleX || 1));
      const height = Math.max(1, (path.height || 1) * Math.abs(path.scaleY || 1));
      const stroke = {
        enabled: true, color: settings.color, opacity: settings.preset === 'highlighter' ? Math.min(.38, settings.opacity) : settings.opacity, width: Math.max(1, Number(path.strokeWidth || settings.width)),
        style: 'solid', dash: 10, gap: 8, lineCap: 'round', lineJoin: 'round', alignment: 'center', blendMode: settings.preset === 'highlighter' ? 'multiply' : 'source-over'
      };
      const element = pathElement(path.path || [], {
        x: path.left || 0, y: path.top || 0, width, height,
        opacity: 1, brush: { preset: settings.preset, smoothing: .5, pressure: true },
        appearance: {
          fills: [{ enabled: false, paint: { type: 'none' }, opacity: 1, blendMode: 'source-over' }],
          strokes: [stroke], shadows: [], effects: [], fill: { type: 'none' }, stroke,
          shadow: { enabled: false, color: '#000000', opacity: .25, blur: 0, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 },
          blendMode: settings.preset === 'highlighter' ? 'multiply' : 'source-over'
        },
        stroke: settings.color, strokeWidth: Math.max(1, Number(path.strokeWidth || settings.width))
      });
      canvas.remove(path);
      addElement(element);
      drawingSnapshotRef.current = null;
    });
    canvas.on('text:editing:entered', () => { textSnapshotRef.current = clone(useEditorStore.getState().document); });
    canvas.on('text:changed', ({ target }) => syncTextObject(target, { history: false }));
    canvas.on('text:editing:exited', () => {
      if (textSnapshotRef.current) pushHistorySnapshot(textSnapshotRef.current);
      textSnapshotRef.current = null;
    });
    canvas.on('mouse:dblclick', ({ target }) => {
      if (!target || renderMode || readOnly) return;
      selectionSyncRef.current = true;
      canvas.discardActiveObject();
      canvas.setActiveObject(target);
      selectionSyncRef.current = false;
      setSelection(target.elementId ? [target.elementId] : []);
      if (target.elementType === 'text') {
        target.enterEditing?.();
        target.setSelectionStart?.(target.text?.length || 0);
        target.setSelectionEnd?.(target.text?.length || 0);
        canvas.requestRenderAll();
      }
      if (target.elementType === 'image') setCropMode(true);
    });
    canvas.on('mouse:down', event => {
      if (event.e) lastPointerRef.current = canvas.getScenePoint(event.e);
      if (canvas.isDrawingMode && !drawingSnapshotRef.current) drawingSnapshotRef.current = clone(useEditorStore.getState().document);
      if (event.e?.button === 2 && !readOnly) {
        const target = event.target;
        if (target) canvas.setActiveObject(target);
        const x = clamp(event.e.clientX, 8, window.innerWidth - 190);
        const y = clamp(event.e.clientY, 8, window.innerHeight - 310);
        setContextMenu({ x, y, isGuide: !!target?.isGuide });
        canvas.requestRenderAll();
        return;
      }
      setContextMenu(null);
      const target = event.target;
      if (event.e?.altKey && target && !target.isGuide) {
        const pointer = canvas.getScenePoint(event.e);
        const stack = canvas.getObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide && !object.isSmartGuide && object.visible && object.containsPoint(pointer));
        if (stack.length > 1) {
          const current = stack.indexOf(target);
          const next = stack[(current - 1 + stack.length) % stack.length];
          canvas.setActiveObject(next);
          canvas.requestRenderAll();
          setSelection([next.elementId]);
        }
      }
      if (cropModeRef.current && target?.elementType === 'image') {
        cropRef.current = {
          object: target,
          point: new Point(event.e.clientX, event.e.clientY),
          startX: target.cropX || 0,
          startY: target.cropY || 0,
          snapshot: clone(useEditorStore.getState().document)
        };
        target.lockMovementX = true;
        target.lockMovementY = true;
      }
    });
    canvas.on('mouse:move', event => {
      if (event.e) lastPointerRef.current = canvas.getScenePoint(event.e);
      const crop = cropRef.current;
      if (!crop || !cropModeRef.current) return;
      const dx = event.e.clientX - crop.point.x;
      const dy = event.e.clientY - crop.point.y;
      const object = crop.object;
      const state = useEditorStore.getState();
      const element = state.document.pages[state.pageIndex].elements.find(item => item.id === object.elementId);
      const maxX = Math.max(0, (element.nativeWidth || object.getElement().naturalWidth) - object.width);
      const maxY = Math.max(0, (element.nativeHeight || object.getElement().naturalHeight) - object.height);
      object.set({
        cropX: clamp(crop.startX - dx / (object.scaleX || 1), 0, maxX),
        cropY: clamp(crop.startY - dy / (object.scaleY || 1), 0, maxY)
      });
      canvas.requestRenderAll();
    });
    canvas.on('mouse:up', () => {
      const crop = cropRef.current;
      if (!crop) return;
      const object = crop.object;
      object.lockMovementX = false;
      object.lockMovementY = false;
      const state = useEditorStore.getState();
      const nextDoc = clone(state.document);
      const next = nextDoc.pages[state.pageIndex].elements.find(item => item.id === object.elementId);
      if (next) {
        next.cropX = object.cropX;
        next.cropY = object.cropY;
        skipReloadRef.current = true;
        commitDocument(nextDoc, { recordHistory: false });
        pushHistorySnapshot(crop.snapshot);
      }
      cropRef.current = null;
    });

    return () => {
      canvas.dispose();
      canvasRef.current = null;
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas || !document || !page) return;
    if (skipReloadRef.current && !renderMode) {
      skipReloadRef.current = false;
      return;
    }
    let cancelled = false;
    const selected = new Set(selection);
    const load = async () => {
      loadingRef.current = true;
      await ensureFontsLoaded((page.elements || []).flatMap(element => element.type === 'text' ? [element.fontFamily] : ['chart', 'table'].includes(element.type) ? [element.options?.fontFamily] : []).filter(Boolean));
      const current = canvasRef.current;
      if (!current || cancelled) return;
      const pad = !renderMode && !readOnly ? PAGE_PADDING : 0;
      const meta = { pageId: page.id, width: pageSize.width, height: pageSize.height, zoom, renderMode, readOnly };
      const previousMeta = renderMetaRef.current;
      const full = !previousMeta || Object.keys(meta).some(key => previousMeta[key] !== meta[key]);
      current.discardActiveObject();
      removeSmartGuides();
      if (full) {
        current.clear();
        renderStateRef.current = { pageId: null, signatures: new Map(), objects: new Map() };
        current.setDimensions({ width: pageSize.width * zoom + pad * 2, height: pageSize.height * zoom + pad * 2 });
        current.setZoom(zoom);
        current.viewportTransform[4] = pad;
        current.viewportTransform[5] = pad;
      }
      const oldBackgrounds = current.getObjects().filter(object => object.isPageBackground);
      oldBackgrounds.forEach(object => current.remove(object));
      if (pad > 0) {
        current.set({ backgroundColor: '' });
        current.backgroundColor = '';
      } else {
        current.set({ backgroundColor: page.transparentBackground ? '' : paintToFabric(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, pageSize.width, pageSize.height, '#ffffff') });
      }
      current.getObjects().filter(object => object.isGuide || object.isSmartGuide).forEach(object => current.remove(object));
      try {
        const result = await reconcileFabricElements({
          canvas: current, page, renderState: renderStateRef, createObject: elementToObject,
          selectedIds: selected, readOnly, renderMode, full
        });
        if (cancelled || !result) return;
        if (!renderMode && !readOnly && showGuides) {
          (page.guides?.vertical || []).forEach((value, index) => current.add(createGuide('vertical', value, pageSize, index, page.guides.locked)));
          (page.guides?.horizontal || []).forEach((value, index) => current.add(createGuide('horizontal', value, pageSize, index, page.guides.locked)));
        }
        const active = result.active || [];
        if (!renderMode && !readOnly && !drawingMode && active.length === 1) current.setActiveObject(active[0]);
        if (!renderMode && !readOnly && !drawingMode && active.length > 1) current.setActiveObject(new ActiveSelection(active, { canvas: current }));
        renderMetaRef.current = meta;
        current.requestRenderAll();
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to reconcile canvas elements', error);
      }
      loadingRef.current = false;
      if (renderMode) {
        const exportBridge = {
          ready: true,
          dataUrl(format = 'png', multiplier = 1, quality = .92) {
            return canvas.toDataURL({ format: format === 'jpeg' ? 'jpeg' : 'png', multiplier, quality, enableRetinaScaling: false });
          },
          svg() { return canvas.toSVG({ suppressPreamble: false }); }
        };
        window.__DESIGN_COMMONS_EXPORT__ = exportBridge;
        window.__CANVASFORGE_EXPORT__ = exportBridge;
      }
    };
    load();
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, [document, pageIndex, zoom, renderMode, readOnly, showGuides, drawingMode]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas || renderMode || readOnly) return;
    canvas.isDrawingMode = drawingMode;
    canvas.selection = !drawingMode;
    canvas.skipTargetFind = drawingMode;
    if (drawingMode) {
      canvas.discardActiveObject();
      setSelection([]);
      const brush = new PencilBrush(canvas);
      const presetWidth = brushPreset === 'marker' ? Math.max(12, brushWidth * 1.8) : brushPreset === 'highlighter' ? Math.max(18, brushWidth * 2.6) : brushWidth;
      const opacity = brushPreset === 'highlighter' ? Math.min(.38, brushOpacity) : brushOpacity;
      brush.color = rgbaFromHex(brushColor, opacity);
      brush.width = Math.max(1, presetWidth);
      brush.decimate = brushPreset === 'pen' ? 1.5 : 2.5;
      brush.strokeLineCap = 'round';
      brush.strokeLineJoin = 'round';
      canvas.freeDrawingBrush = brush;
    }
    canvas.getObjects().filter(object => object.elementId).forEach(object => {
      object.selectable = !drawingMode && !object.lockMovementX;
      object.evented = !drawingMode && !object.lockMovementX;
    });
    canvas.requestRenderAll();
    return () => {
      if (canvasRef.current) {
        canvasRef.current.isDrawingMode = false;
        canvasRef.current.skipTargetFind = false;
      }
    };
  }, [drawingMode, brushPreset, brushColor, brushWidth, brushOpacity, renderMode, readOnly]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const area = scrollRef.current;
    if (!area || renderMode) return;
    const onWheel = event => {
      if (!event.ctrlKey && !event.metaKey) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      setZoomState(current => clamp(current * (event.deltaY > 0 ? .9 : 1.1), .15, 2));
    };
    area.addEventListener('wheel', onWheel, { passive: false });
    return () => area.removeEventListener('wheel', onWheel);
  }, [renderMode]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!showRulers || !isInteractive) {
      setRulerOrigin({ x: 0, y: 0 });
      return;
    }

    const area = scrollRef.current;
    const stage = stageRef.current;
    if (!area || !stage) return;

    let animationFrame = 0;
    const sync = () => {
      cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrame);
      animationFrame = requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        const areaRect = area.getBoundingClientRect();
        const stageRect = stage.getBoundingClientRect();
        const next = {
          x: round(stageRect.left + pad - areaRect.left),
          y: round(stageRect.top + pad - areaRect.top)
        };
        setRulerOrigin(current => current.x === next.x && current.y === next.y ? current : next);
      });
    };

    sync();
    area.addEventListener('scroll', sync, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener('resize', sync);
    const observer = typeof ResizeObserver !== 'undefined' ? new ResizeObserver(sync) : null;
    observer?.observe(area);
    observer?.observe(stage);

    return () => {
      cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrame);
      area.removeEventListener('scroll', sync);
      window.removeEventListener('resize', sync);
      observer?.disconnect();
    };
  }, [showRulers, isInteractive, pad, zoom, pageSize.width, pageSize.height]);

  const pasteAnchor = () => {
    const point = lastPointerRef.current || { x: pageSize.width / 2, y: pageSize.height / 2 };
    return { x: clamp(point.x, 0, pageSize.width), y: clamp(point.y, 0, pageSize.height) };
  };

  const addPastedElements = elements => {
    if (!elements.length) return false;
    const anchor = pasteAnchor();
    const positioned = elements.map((element, index) => ({
      ...element,
      x: clamp(anchor.x - element.width / 2 + index * 18, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.width - element.width)),
      y: clamp(anchor.y - element.height / 2 + index * 18, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.height - element.height))
    }));
    addElements(positioned);
    return true;
  };

  const pasteCanvasForgePayload = payload => {
    if (!String(payload || '').startsWith(CLIPBOARD_PREFIX) && !String(payload || '').startsWith(LEGACY_CLIPBOARD_PREFIX)) return false;
    if (payload.length > 2_000_000) throw new Error('Clipboard content is too large.');
    const prefix = payload.startsWith(CLIPBOARD_PREFIX) ? CLIPBOARD_PREFIX : LEGACY_CLIPBOARD_PREFIX;
    const parsed = JSON.parse(payload.slice(prefix.length));
    if (!Array.isArray(parsed) || parsed.length > 500) throw new Error('Clipboard content is not a valid Design Commons selection.');
    const items = parsed.filter(element => element && ALLOWED_CLIPBOARD_TYPES.has(element.type));
    if (!items.length) throw new Error('No supported elements were found in the clipboard.');
    const copies = cloneElementTree(items, { offsetX: 24, offsetY: 24 });
    addElements(copies);
    return true;
  };

  const pasteSvgMarkup = markup => {
    if (!markup) return false;
    const safe = sanitizeSvgMarkup(markup);
    const viewBox = safe.match(/viewBox=["']\s*[-\d.]+\s+[-\d.]+\s+([\d.]+)\s+([\d.]+)["']/i);
    const ratio = viewBox ? Math.max(.1, Number(viewBox[1]) / Math.max(1, Number(viewBox[2]))) : 1;
    const width = Math.min(520, pageSize.width * .65);
    const height = Math.min(520, width / ratio);
    return addPastedElements([svgElement(safe, { name: 'Pasted SVG', width, height })]);
  };

  const pastePlainText = value => {
    const text = String(value || '').replace(/\r\n/g, '\n').slice(0, 50_000);
    if (!text.trim()) return false;
    if (pasteCanvasForgePayload(text)) return true;
    if (isSvgMarkup(text)) return pasteSvgMarkup(text);
    const lineCount = Math.max(1, text.split('\n').length);
    return addPastedElements([textElement({
      name: 'Pasted text', text, width: Math.min(680, pageSize.width * .72),
      height: Math.min(pageSize.height * .55, Math.max(90, lineCount * 64)), fontSize: lineCount > 4 ? 36 : 48,
      autoFit: true, minFontSize: 10
    })]);
  };

  const pasteFiles = async files => {
    const rasterFiles = [];
    const svgElements = [];
    for (const file of files || []) {
      if (!file) continue;
      if (file.type === 'image/svg+xml' || /\.svg$/i.test(file.name || '')) {
        const safe = sanitizeSvgMarkup(await file.text());
        svgElements.push(svgElement(safe, { name: file.name || 'Pasted SVG' }));
      } else if (file.type?.startsWith('image/')) rasterFiles.push(file);
    }
    const imageElements = [];
    for (const file of rasterFiles.slice(0, 20)) {
      const asset = await upload(file);
      imageElements.push(imageElement(asset));
    }
    return addPastedElements([...svgElements, ...imageElements]);
  };

  const pasteFromDataTransfer = async data => {
    const items = [...(data?.items || [])];
    const files = items.filter(item => item.kind === 'file').map(item => item.getAsFile()).filter(Boolean);
    if (files.length && await pasteFiles(files)) return true;
    const html = data?.getData?.('text/html') || '';
    const plain = data?.getData?.('text/plain') || '';
    const svg = isSvgMarkup(plain) ? plain : htmlSvgMarkup(html);
    if (svg) return pasteSvgMarkup(svg);
    return pastePlainText(plain);
  };

  const pasteFromNavigator = async () => {
    if (navigator.clipboard?.read) {
      try {
        const clipboardItems = await navigator.clipboard.read();
        const files = [];
        let svg = '';
        let text = '';
        for (const item of clipboardItems) {
          for (const type of item.types) {
            const blob = await item.getType(type);
            if (type === 'image/svg+xml') svg ||= await blob.text();
            else if (type.startsWith('image/')) files.push(new File([blob], `pasted-${Date.now()}.${type.split('/')[1] || 'png'}`, { type }));
            else if (type === 'text/html') svg ||= htmlSvgMarkup(await blob.text());
            else if (type === 'text/plain') text ||= await blob.text();
          }
        }
        if (files.length && await pasteFiles(files)) return true;
        if (svg) return pasteSvgMarkup(svg);
        if (text && pastePlainText(text)) return true;
      } catch {}
    }
    let text = '';
    try { text = await navigator.clipboard.readText(); } catch {}
    if (text && pastePlainText(text)) return true;
    const local = readMigratedStorage('clipboard') || '';
    return local ? pasteCanvasForgePayload(local) : false;
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (renderMode || readOnly) return;
    const onKeyDown = async event => {
      const activeElement = globalThis.document.activeElement;
      const formEditing = activeElement?.tagName === 'INPUT' || activeElement?.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' || activeElement?.tagName === 'SELECT';
      const activeObject = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObject();
      const editingText = !!activeObject?.isEditing;
      if (event.code === 'Space' && !formEditing && !editingText) {
        spacePressedRef.current = true;
        event.preventDefault();
      }
      if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 's') {
        event.preventDefault();
        useEditorStore.getState().save({ allowRecovered: true }).catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error'));
        return;
      }
      if (formEditing && event.key !== 'Escape') return;
      if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'z') {
        event.preventDefault();
        event.shiftKey ? useEditorStore.getState().redo() : useEditorStore.getState().undo();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'y') {
        event.preventDefault();
        useEditorStore.getState().redo();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'c') {
        if (editingText) return;
        event.preventDefault();
        await controller.copy();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
        if (editingText) return;
        event.preventDefault();
        await controller.paste();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'd') {
        if (editingText) return;
        event.preventDefault();
        controller.duplicate();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'a') {
        if (editingText) return;
        event.preventDefault();
        controller.selectAll();
      } else if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'g') {
        if (editingText) return;
        event.preventDefault();
        try { event.shiftKey ? controller.ungroup() : controller.group(); }
        catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
      } else if (!editingText && (event.key === 'Delete' || event.key === 'Backspace')) {
        event.preventDefault();
        controller.delete();
      } else if (!editingText && ['ArrowLeft', 'ArrowRight', 'ArrowUp', 'ArrowDown'].includes(event.key)) {
        event.preventDefault();
        if (!nudgeTimerRef.current) beginHistoryTransaction();
        const distance = event.shiftKey ? 10 : 1;
        const dx = event.key === 'ArrowLeft' ? -distance : event.key === 'ArrowRight' ? distance : 0;
        const dy = event.key === 'ArrowUp' ? -distance : event.key === 'ArrowDown' ? distance : 0;
        controller.nudge(dx, dy, { recordHistory: true });
        clearTimeout(nudgeTimerRef.current);
        nudgeTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
          commitHistoryTransaction();
          nudgeTimerRef.current = null;
        }, 220);
      } else if (event.key === 'Enter' && activeObject?.elementType === 'text' && !editingText) {
        event.preventDefault();
        activeObject.enterEditing?.();
        activeObject.selectAll?.();
        canvasRef.current.requestRenderAll();
      } else if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        if (drawingMode) setDrawingMode(false);
        else if (guidePreview) { if (guideDragRef.current) guideDragRef.current.cancelled = true; setGuidePreview(null); }
        else if (cropModeRef.current) setCropMode(false);
        else if (editingText) activeObject.exitEditing?.();
        else if (activeObject) {
          canvasRef.current.discardActiveObject();
          canvasRef.current.requestRenderAll();
          setSelection([]);
        } else {
          setContextMenu(null);
          setZoomMenu(false);
          window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent(ESCAPE_EVENT));
          window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent(LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT));
        }
      }
    };
    const onKeyUp = event => {
      if (event.code === 'Space') spacePressedRef.current = false;
    };
    const onPaste = async event => {
      if (event.target?.tagName === 'INPUT' || event.target?.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' || event.target?.isContentEditable) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      try {
        const handled = await pasteFromDataTransfer(event.clipboardData);
        if (!handled) notify('The clipboard did not contain supported image, SVG, text, or CanvasForge content.', 'error');
      } catch (error) {
        event.preventDefault();
        notify(`Paste failed: ${error.message}`, 'error');
      }
    };
    window.addEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown);
    window.addEventListener('keyup', onKeyUp);
    window.addEventListener('paste', onPaste);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown);
      window.removeEventListener('keyup', onKeyUp);
      window.removeEventListener('paste', onPaste);
      clearTimeout(nudgeTimerRef.current);
    };
  }, [cropMode, selection, document, readOnly, guidePreview, pageIndex, pageSize.width, pageSize.height]);

  const beginPan = event => {
    if (renderMode || !(event.button === 1 || spacePressedRef.current)) return;
    const area = scrollRef.current;
    if (!area) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    event.stopPropagation();
    panRef.current = { x: event.clientX, y: event.clientY, left: area.scrollLeft, top: area.scrollTop };
    setPanning(true);
    const move = pointerEvent => {
      if (!panRef.current) return;
      area.scrollLeft = panRef.current.left - (pointerEvent.clientX - panRef.current.x);
      area.scrollTop = panRef.current.top - (pointerEvent.clientY - panRef.current.y);
    };
    const up = () => {
      panRef.current = null;
      setPanning(false);
      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', move);
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', up);
    };
    window.addEventListener('pointermove', move);
    window.addEventListener('pointerup', up, { once: true });
  };

  const commitObjectPositions = changes => {
    updatePage(currentPage => {
      currentPage.elements = currentPage.elements.map(element => changes[element.id] ? { ...element, ...changes[element.id] } : element);
    });
  };

  const dropAsset = event => {
    if (readOnly || renderMode) return;
    const assetId = event.dataTransfer?.getData(ASSET_DRAG_TYPE) || event.dataTransfer?.getData(LEGACY_ASSET_DRAG_TYPE);
    if (!assetId) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === assetId);
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!asset || !canvas) return;
    const pointer = canvas.getScenePoint(event.nativeEvent || event);
    const stack = canvas.getObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide && !object.isSmartGuide && object.visible && object.containsPoint(pointer));
    const targetObject = stack.at(-1);
    const targetElement = page.elements.find(item => item.id === targetObject?.elementId);
    if (targetElement?.type === 'image' && targetElement.isImageFrame) {
      updateElements([targetElement.id], {
        src: asset.preview_url || asset.url,
        assetId: asset.id,
        nativeWidth: asset.width || 1000,
        nativeHeight: asset.height || 1000,
        cropX: null,
        cropY: null,
        cropZoom: 1,
        isImageFrame: true
      });
      setSelection([targetElement.id]);
      notify(`Placed ${asset.original_name || 'image'} in the selected frame.`, 'success');
      return;
    }
    const element = imageElement(asset, {
      x: clamp(pointer.x - 260, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.width - 520)),
      y: clamp(pointer.y - 180, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.height - 360))
    });
    addElement(element);
  };

  const reference = page?.referenceImage;
  const referenceStyle = reference?.visible !== false ? {
    opacity: reference?.opacity ?? .45,
    objectFit: reference?.fit === 'stretch' ? 'fill' : (reference?.fit || 'contain'),
    mixBlendMode: reference?.mode === 'difference' ? 'difference' : 'normal',
    clipPath: reference?.mode === 'split' ? `inset(0 ${Math.max(0, 100 - (reference.split ?? .5) * 100)}% 0 0)` : 'none'
  } : null;

  const controller = {
    canvas: () => canvasRef.current,
    setDrawingMode(value = true) { setDrawingMode(!!value); },
    toggleDrawingMode() { setDrawingMode(value => !value); },
    setBrush(preset, options = {}) {
      if (preset) setBrushPreset(preset);
      if (options.color) setBrushColor(options.color);
      if (Number.isFinite(options.width)) setBrushWidth(options.width);
      if (Number.isFinite(options.opacity)) setBrushOpacity(options.opacity);
      setDrawingMode(true);
    },
    setZoom(value) { setZoomState(clamp(value, .15, 2)); setZoomMenu(false); },
    zoomIn() { setZoomState(value => clamp(value + .1, .15, 2)); },
    zoomOut() { setZoomState(value => clamp(value - .1, .15, 2)); },
    fit() {
      const area = scrollRef.current;
      if (!area) return;
      setZoomState(clamp(Math.min((area.clientWidth - 100) / pageSize.width, (area.clientHeight - 100) / pageSize.height), .15, 1));
      setZoomMenu(false);
    },
    fitWidth() {
      const area = scrollRef.current;
      if (!area) return;
      setZoomState(clamp((area.clientWidth - 100) / pageSize.width, .15, 2));
      setZoomMenu(false);
    },
    fitSelection() {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const area = scrollRef.current;
      const objects = canvas?.getActiveObjects?.().filter(object => !object.isGuide) || [];
      if (!area || !objects.length) return controller.fit();
      const boxes = objects.map(object => object.getBoundingRect());
      const left = Math.min(...boxes.map(box => box.left));
      const right = Math.max(...boxes.map(box => box.left + box.width));
      const top = Math.min(...boxes.map(box => box.top));
      const bottom = Math.max(...boxes.map(box => box.top + box.height));
      setZoomState(clamp(Math.min((area.clientWidth - 120) / Math.max(1, right - left), (area.clientHeight - 120) / Math.max(1, bottom - top)), .15, 2));
      setZoomMenu(false);
    },
    insertElement(element) {
      const stage = stageRef.current;
      const area = scrollRef.current;
      if (!stage || !area) return addElement(element);
      const stageRect = stage.getBoundingClientRect();
      const areaRect = area.getBoundingClientRect();
      const offset = !renderMode && !readOnly ? PAGE_PADDING : 0;
      const visibleX = clamp((areaRect.left + areaRect.width / 2 - stageRect.left - offset) / zoom - element.width / 2, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.width - element.width));
      const visibleY = clamp((areaRect.top + areaRect.height / 2 - stageRect.top - offset) / zoom - element.height / 2, 0, Math.max(0, pageSize.height - element.height));
      addElement({ ...element, x: round(visibleX), y: round(visibleY) });
    },
    addGuide(axis, value) {
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        currentPage.guides[axis].push(round(value));
        currentPage.guides[axis].sort((a, b) => a - b);
      });
    },
    setGuide(axis, index, value) {
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        currentPage.guides[axis][index] = round(clamp(value, 0, axis === 'vertical' ? pageSize.width : pageSize.height));
        currentPage.guides[axis].sort((a, b) => a - b);
      });
    },
    toggleGuideLock() { updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.guides.locked = !currentPage.guides.locked; }); },
    clearGuides() { updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.guides.vertical = []; currentPage.guides.horizontal = []; }); },
    delete() {
      const active = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObject();
      if (active?.isGuide) {
        updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.guides[active.guideAxis].splice(active.guideIndex, 1); });
        return;
      }
      removeSelection();
    },
    nudge(dx, dy, options = {}) {
      if (!selection.length) return;
      updateElements(selection, element => ({ x: element.x + dx, y: element.y + dy }), options);
    },
    duplicate() {
      if (!selection.length) return;
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        const included = new Set([...selection, ...collectDescendantIds(currentPage, selection)]);
        const source = currentPage.elements.filter(element => included.has(element.id)).sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
        const copies = cloneElementTree(source, { offsetX: 24, offsetY: 24 }).map((element, index) => ({
          ...element,
          name: selection.includes(source[index]?.id) ? `${element.name || element.type} copy` : element.name,
          zIndex: currentPage.elements.length + index
        }));
        currentPage.elements.push(...copies);
        setSelection(copies.map(element => element.id));
      });
    },
    async copy() {
      const included = new Set([...selection, ...collectDescendantIds(page, selection)]);
      const items = page.elements.filter(element => included.has(element.id)).sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
      if (!items.length) return;
      const payload = `${CLIPBOARD_PREFIX}${JSON.stringify(items)}`;
      writeStorage('clipboard', payload);
      try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(payload); } catch {}
    },
    async paste() {
      try {
        const handled = await pasteFromNavigator();
        if (!handled) notify('The clipboard did not contain a supported image, SVG, text, or CanvasForge object.', 'info');
      } catch (error) {
        notify(`Paste failed: ${error.message}`, 'error');
      }
    },
    copyStyle() {
      const element = page.elements.find(item => item.id === selection[0]);
      if (!element) return;
      const keys = element.type === 'text'
        ? ['fontFamily', 'fontSize', 'fontWeight', 'fontStyle', 'underline', 'linethrough', 'fill', 'textAlign', 'lineHeight', 'charSpacing', 'textBackgroundColor', 'effect', 'appearance']
        : element.type === 'image' ? ['mask', 'radius', 'filters', 'opacity', 'appearance'] : ['fill', 'stroke', 'strokeWidth', 'radius', 'opacity', 'appearance'];
      writeStorage('style', JSON.stringify({ type: element.type, style: Object.fromEntries(keys.map(key => [key, clone(element[key])])) }));
    },
    pasteStyle() {
      try {
        const saved = JSON.parse(readMigratedStorage('style', 'null') || 'null');
        if (!saved || !selection.length) return;
        updateElements(selection, clone(saved.style));
      } catch (error) {
        notify(`Could not paste style: ${error.message}`, 'error');
      }
    },
    align(kind) {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const objects = canvas?.getActiveObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide) || [];
      if (!objects.length) return;
      const boxes = objects.map(object => ({ object, box: object.getBoundingRect() }));
      const multi = boxes.length > 1;
      const left = multi ? Math.min(...boxes.map(item => item.box.left)) : 0;
      const right = multi ? Math.max(...boxes.map(item => item.box.left + item.box.width)) : pageSize.width;
      const top = multi ? Math.min(...boxes.map(item => item.box.top)) : 0;
      const bottom = multi ? Math.max(...boxes.map(item => item.box.top + item.box.height)) : pageSize.height;
      const changes = {};
      boxes.forEach(({ object, box }) => {
        let dx = 0;
        let dy = 0;
        if (kind === 'left') dx = left - box.left;
        if (kind === 'center') dx = (left + right) / 2 - (box.left + box.width / 2);
        if (kind === 'right') dx = right - (box.left + box.width);
        if (kind === 'top') dy = top - box.top;
        if (kind === 'middle') dy = (top + bottom) / 2 - (box.top + box.height / 2);
        if (kind === 'bottom') dy = bottom - (box.top + box.height);
        changes[object.elementId] = { x: (object.left || 0) + dx, y: (object.top || 0) + dy };
      });
      commitObjectPositions(changes);
    },
    distribute(axis) {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const objects = (canvas?.getActiveObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide) || []).map(object => ({ object, box: object.getBoundingRect() }));
      if (objects.length < 3) return;
      objects.sort((a, b) => axis === 'horizontal' ? a.box.left - b.box.left : a.box.top - b.box.top);
      const start = axis === 'horizontal' ? objects[0].box.left : objects[0].box.top;
      const end = axis === 'horizontal' ? objects.at(-1).box.left + objects.at(-1).box.width : objects.at(-1).box.top + objects.at(-1).box.height;
      const total = objects.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (axis === 'horizontal' ? item.box.width : item.box.height), 0);
      const gap = (end - start - total) / (objects.length - 1);
      let cursor = start;
      const changes = {};
      objects.forEach(({ object, box }) => {
        const delta = cursor - (axis === 'horizontal' ? box.left : box.top);
        changes[object.elementId] = axis === 'horizontal' ? { x: object.left + delta } : { y: object.top + delta };
        cursor += (axis === 'horizontal' ? box.width : box.height) + gap;
      });
      commitObjectPositions(changes);
    },
    equalSpacing(axis) { controller.distribute(axis); },
    matchSize(mode) {
      if (selection.length < 2) return;
      const source = page.elements.find(element => element.id === selection[0]);
      if (!source) return;
      updateElements(selection.slice(1), element => ({
        ...(mode !== 'height' ? { width: source.width } : {}),
        ...(mode !== 'width' ? { height: source.height } : {}),
        ...(element.type === 'text' && mode !== 'width' ? { fontSize: source.fontSize } : {})
      }));
    },
    order(action) {
      if (!selection.length) return;
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        const selectedSet = new Set(selection);
        const selectedItems = currentPage.elements.filter(element => selectedSet.has(element.id));
        const rest = currentPage.elements.filter(element => !selectedSet.has(element.id));
        let next;
        if (action === 'front') next = [...rest, ...selectedItems];
        else if (action === 'back') next = [...selectedItems, ...rest];
        else {
          next = [...currentPage.elements];
          const direction = action === 'forward' ? 1 : -1;
          const indexes = next.map((element, index) => selectedSet.has(element.id) ? index : -1).filter(index => index >= 0);
          const ordered = direction > 0 ? indexes.reverse() : indexes;
          ordered.forEach(index => {
            const target = clamp(index + direction, 0, next.length - 1);
            if (target === index || selectedSet.has(next[target]?.id)) return;
            [next[index], next[target]] = [next[target], next[index]];
          });
        }
        currentPage.elements = next.map((element, index) => ({ ...element, zIndex: index }));
      });
    },
    reorderLayer(from, to) {
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        const items = [...currentPage.elements].sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
        const [item] = items.splice(from, 1);
        items.splice(to, 0, item);
        currentPage.elements = items.map((element, index) => ({ ...element, zIndex: index }));
      });
    },
    selectAll() {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const objects = canvas?.getObjects().filter(object => !object.isGuide && !object.isSmartGuide && object.visible && object.selectable) || [];
      if (!objects.length) return;
      selectionSyncRef.current = true;
      canvas.discardActiveObject();
      canvas.setActiveObject(objects.length === 1 ? objects[0] : new ActiveSelection(objects, { canvas }));
      selectionSyncRef.current = false;
      canvas.requestRenderAll();
      setSelection(objects.map(object => object.elementId).filter(Boolean));
    },
    clearSelection() {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      selectionSyncRef.current = true;
      canvas?.discardActiveObject();
      selectionSyncRef.current = false;
      canvas?.requestRenderAll();
      setSelection([]);
    },
    group() {
      const id = groupSelection();
      notify('Objects grouped. Click any member to select and move the whole group.', 'success');
      return id;
    },
    ungroup() {
      const ids = ungroupSelection();
      notify('Group removed. Objects can now be selected independently.', 'success');
      return ids;
    },
    select(id, additive = false) {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const object = canvas?.getObjects().find(item => item.elementId === id);
      if (!object) return;
      if (additive) {
        const current = canvas.getActiveObjects();
        canvas.setActiveObject(new ActiveSelection([...new Set([...current.filter(item => item !== object), object])], { canvas }));
      } else canvas.setActiveObject(object);
      canvas.requestRenderAll();
    },
    setTextStyle(patch) {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const objects = canvas?.getActiveObjects().filter(object => object.elementType === 'text') || [];
      if (!objects.length) return;
      const before = clone(useEditorStore.getState().document);
      objects.forEach(object => {
        if (object.isEditing && object.selectionStart !== object.selectionEnd) object.setSelectionStyles(patch, object.selectionStart, object.selectionEnd);
        else object.set(patch);
        object.setCoords();
        syncTextObject(object, { history: false });
      });
      pushHistorySnapshot(before);
      canvas.requestRenderAll();
    },
    setLink(url) {
      const object = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObjects().find(item => item.elementType === 'text');
      if (!object || !object.isEditing || object.selectionStart === object.selectionEnd) return;
      const id = object.elementId;
      const start = object.selectionStart;
      const end = object.selectionEnd;
      updateElements([id], element => ({
        links: [...(element.links || []).filter(link => link.end <= start || link.start >= end), ...(url ? [{ start, end, href: url }] : [])]
      }));
      object.setSelectionStyles(url ? { underline: true, fill: '#2563eb' } : { underline: false, fill: page.elements.find(element => element.id === id)?.fill || '#111827' }, start, end);
      syncTextObject(object, { history: false });
    },
    clearTextFormatting() {
      const object = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObjects().find(item => item.elementType === 'text');
      if (!object) return;
      const defaults = { fontWeight: 400, fontStyle: 'normal', underline: false, linethrough: false, deltaY: 0, textBackgroundColor: '', stroke: null, strokeWidth: 0 };
      if (object.isEditing && object.selectionStart !== object.selectionEnd) object.setSelectionStyles(defaults, object.selectionStart, object.selectionEnd);
      else object.set(defaults);
      syncTextObject(object, { history: true });
      canvasRef.current.requestRenderAll();
    },
    applyList(type) {
      const object = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObjects().find(item => item.elementType === 'text');
      if (!object) return;
      const lines = (object.text || '').split('\n')
        .map(line => line.replace(/^\s*(?:[•*-]|\d+[.)])\s+/, ''))
        .map((line, index) => type === 'bullet' ? `• ${line}` : type === 'number' ? `${index + 1}. ${line}` : line);
      object.set({ text: lines.join('\n') });
      syncTextObject(object, { history: true });
    },
    setCropMode(value = true) { setCropMode(value); },
    cropZoom(delta) {
      const id = selection[0];
      const element = page.elements.find(item => item.id === id && item.type === 'image');
      if (!element) return;
      const oldZoom = element.cropZoom || 1;
      const nextZoom = clamp(oldZoom + delta, 1, 8);
      const oldScale = Math.max(element.width / element.nativeWidth, element.height / element.nativeHeight) * oldZoom;
      const oldCropW = element.width / oldScale;
      const oldCropH = element.height / oldScale;
      const cx = (element.cropX ?? Math.max(0, (element.nativeWidth - oldCropW) / 2)) + oldCropW / 2;
      const cy = (element.cropY ?? Math.max(0, (element.nativeHeight - oldCropH) / 2)) + oldCropH / 2;
      const newScale = Math.max(element.width / element.nativeWidth, element.height / element.nativeHeight) * nextZoom;
      const newCropW = element.width / newScale;
      const newCropH = element.height / newScale;
      updateElements([id], {
        cropZoom: nextZoom,
        cropX: clamp(cx - newCropW / 2, 0, Math.max(0, element.nativeWidth - newCropW)),
        cropY: clamp(cy - newCropH / 2, 0, Math.max(0, element.nativeHeight - newCropH))
      });
    },
    resetCrop() {
      const id = selection[0];
      const element = page.elements.find(item => item.id === id && item.type === 'image');
      if (!element) return;
      updateElements([id], { cropZoom: 1, cropX: null, cropY: null, cropAnchorX: .5, cropAnchorY: .5 });
    },
    async exportSelectionAsset({ multiplier = 2 } = {}) {
      const canvas = canvasRef.current;
      const rootIds = selection.length ? selection : selectedElementIds(canvas);
      if (!canvas || !rootIds.length) throw new Error('Select an object or group first.');
      const idSet = new Set(rootIds);
      collectDescendantIds(page, idSet).forEach(id => idSet.add(id));
      const selectedGroupIds = new Set(page.elements.filter(item => idSet.has(item.id) && item.groupId).map(item => item.groupId));
      page.elements.forEach(item => { if (item.groupId && selectedGroupIds.has(item.groupId)) idSet.add(item.id); });
      const ids = [...idSet];
      const selectedElements = page.elements.filter(item => idSet.has(item.id) && !item.hidden);
      if (selectedElements.length === 1 && selectedElements[0].type === 'svg' && selectedElements[0].svg) {
        return {
          dataUrl: `data:image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8,${encodeURIComponent(sanitizeSvgMarkup(selectedElements[0].svg))}`,
          mimeType: 'image/svg+xml',
          width: selectedElements[0].width,
          height: selectedElements[0].height,
          elementIds: ids
        };
      }
      const objects = canvas.getObjects().filter(object => object.elementId && ids.includes(object.elementId) && !object.isGuide && !object.isSmartGuide && !object.isPageBackground);
      if (!objects.length) throw new Error('The selected object is not ready to export yet.');
      const currentActive = canvas.getActiveObject?.();
      const currentIds = new Set(currentActive?.type === 'activeselection' ? currentActive.getObjects().map(object => object.elementId) : currentActive?.elementId ? [currentActive.elementId] : []);
      const canReuseActive = currentIds.size === ids.length && ids.every(id => currentIds.has(id));
      const active = canReuseActive ? currentActive : objects.length === 1 ? objects[0] : new ActiveSelection(objects, { canvas });
      const temporarySelection = active !== currentActive && objects.length > 1;
      active.setCoords?.();
      const dataUrl = active.toDataURL({ format: 'png', multiplier: Math.max(1, Math.min(4, Number(multiplier) || 2)), enableRetinaScaling: false, withoutTransform: false });
      const bounds = active.getBoundingRect?.() || { width: selectedElements[0]?.width || 1, height: selectedElements[0]?.height || 1 };
      if (temporarySelection) active.destroy?.();
      return { dataUrl, mimeType: 'image/png', width: Math.max(1, bounds.width), height: Math.max(1, bounds.height), elementIds: ids };
    },
    removeGuideFromMenu() {
      const active = canvasRef.current?.getActiveObject();
      if (!active?.isGuide) return;
    }
  };

  useImperativeHandle(ref, () => controller, [document, page, selection, zoom, cropMode, drawingMode, brushPreset, brushColor, brushWidth, brushOpacity]);

  if (!document || !page) return <div className="canvas-empty">No design loaded.</div>;
  const selectionHasGroup = page.elements.some(element => selection.includes(element.id) && element.groupId);
  const stageStyle = {
    width: pageSize.width * zoom + pad * 2,
    height: pageSize.height * zoom + pad * 2
  };
  const pageSurfaceStyle = {
    left: pad,
    top: pad,
    width: pageSize.width * zoom,
    height: pageSize.height * zoom,
    ...(page.transparentBackground ? {} : { background: paintToCss(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, '#ffffff') })
  };
  return <div className={`canvas-editor ${renderMode ? 'render-mode' : ''} ${readOnly ? 'read-only' : ''} ${panning ? 'is-panning' : ''} ${drawingMode ? 'is-drawing' : ''} ${showRulers ? 'show-rulers' : 'hide-rulers'}`}>
    {isInteractive && <div className="canvas-draw-toolbar" role="toolbar" aria-label="Drawing tools">
      <button className={!drawingMode ? 'active' : ''} title="Select and move objects" onClick={() => setDrawingMode(false)}><MousePointer2 size={16}/><span>Select</span></button>
      <button className={drawingMode && brushPreset === 'pen' ? 'active' : ''} title="Pen" onClick={() => { setBrushPreset('pen'); setDrawingMode(true); }}><PenLine size={16}/><span>Pen</span></button>
      <button className={drawingMode && brushPreset === 'marker' ? 'active' : ''} title="Marker" onClick={() => { setBrushPreset('marker'); setDrawingMode(true); }}><Brush size={16}/><span>Marker</span></button>
      <button className={drawingMode && brushPreset === 'highlighter' ? 'active' : ''} title="Highlighter" onClick={() => { setBrushPreset('highlighter'); setDrawingMode(true); }}><Highlighter size={16}/><span>Highlight</span></button>
      <span className="draw-toolbar-divider"/>
      <label title="Stroke colour"><input type="color" value={brushColor} onChange={event => setBrushColor(event.target.value)}/></label>
      <label className="draw-range" title="Stroke width"><span>{brushWidth}px</span><input type="range" min="1" max="60" step="1" value={brushWidth} onChange={event => setBrushWidth(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>
      <label className="draw-range" title="Stroke opacity"><span>{Math.round(brushOpacity * 100)}%</span><input type="range" min="0.05" max="1" step="0.05" value={brushOpacity} onChange={event => setBrushOpacity(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>
    </div>}
    {isInteractive && showRulers && <>
      <div className="ruler-corner" />
      <Ruler axis="horizontal" length={pageSize.width} zoom={zoom} onStartGuide={startGuideDrag} offset={rulerOrigin.x} />
      <Ruler axis="vertical" length={pageSize.height} zoom={zoom} onStartGuide={startGuideDrag} offset={rulerOrigin.y} />
    </>}
    <div className="canvas-scroll" ref={scrollRef} onPointerDown={beginPan} onContextMenu={event => event.preventDefault()}>
      <div className="canvas-stage" ref={stageRef} style={stageStyle} onDrop={dropAsset} onDragOver={event => { if (event.dataTransfer?.types?.includes(ASSET_DRAG_TYPE) || event.dataTransfer?.types?.includes(LEGACY_ASSET_DRAG_TYPE)) { event.preventDefault(); event.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy'; } }}>
        {isInteractive && <div className={`canvas-page-surface ${page.transparentBackground ? 'transparent' : ''}`} style={pageSurfaceStyle}/>}
        <canvas ref={canvasEl} />
        <div style={{ position: 'absolute', left: pad, top: pad, width: pageSize.width * zoom, height: pageSize.height * zoom, zIndex: 10, pointerEvents: 'none' }}>
          {reference?.src && referenceStyle && <><img className={`canvas-reference-image mode-${reference.mode || 'overlay'}`} src={reference.src} alt={reference.name || 'Page reference'} style={referenceStyle}/>{reference.mode === 'split' && <div className="canvas-reference-divider" style={{ left: `${(reference.split ?? .5) * 100}%` }}/>}<span className="canvas-reference-badge">Reference · not exported</span></>}
          {page.grid?.enabled && !renderMode && <div className="canvas-grid" style={{ '--grid-size': `${Math.max(4, (page.grid.size || 20) / Math.max(1, page.grid.subdivisions || 1)) * zoom}px` }} />}
          {!renderMode && (page.designGrids || []).filter(grid => grid.enabled !== false).map(grid => { const margin = Math.max(0, Number(grid.margin || 0)) * zoom; const columns = Math.max(1, Number(grid.columns || 12)); return <div key={grid.id} className="canvas-column-grid" style={{ left: margin, right: margin, '--column-count': columns, '--column-gap': `${Math.max(0, Number(grid.gutter || 0)) * zoom}px`, '--column-color': grid.color || '#7c3aed', '--column-opacity': grid.opacity ?? .18 }}>{Array.from({ length: columns }, (_, index) => <span key={index}/>)}</div>; })}
          {!renderMode && (page.baselineGrids || []).filter(grid => grid.enabled !== false).map(grid => <div key={grid.id} className="canvas-baseline-grid" style={{ '--baseline-step': `${Math.max(2, Number(grid.step || 8)) * zoom}px`, '--baseline-offset': `${Math.max(0, Number(grid.offset || 0)) * zoom}px`, '--baseline-color': grid.color || '#0ea5e9', '--baseline-opacity': grid.opacity ?? .22 }}/>) }
          {!renderMode && Object.values(page.margins || {}).some(Number) && <div className="canvas-margin-guides" style={{ left: `${Number(page.margins?.left || 0) * zoom}px`, top: `${Number(page.margins?.top || 0) * zoom}px`, right: `${Number(page.margins?.right || 0) * zoom}px`, bottom: `${Number(page.margins?.bottom || 0) * zoom}px` }}/>} 
          {!renderMode && Object.values(document.print?.safeArea || {}).some(Number) && <div className="canvas-print-safe-area" style={{ left: `${Number(document.print.safeArea.left || 0) * zoom}px`, top: `${Number(document.print.safeArea.top || 0) * zoom}px`, right: `${Number(document.print.safeArea.right || 0) * zoom}px`, bottom: `${Number(document.print.safeArea.bottom || 0) * zoom}px` }}><span>Print safe area</span></div>}
          {guidePreview && <div className={`guide-preview ${guidePreview.axis}`} style={guidePreview.axis === 'vertical' ? { left: guidePreview.value * zoom } : { top: guidePreview.value * zoom }}><span>{guidePreview.value}</span></div>}
          {!renderMode && !readOnly && cropMode && <div className="crop-mode-badge">Crop mode · drag image · Esc to finish</div>}
          {transformInfo && <div className="transform-info">X {transformInfo.x} · Y {transformInfo.y} · W {transformInfo.width} · H {transformInfo.height} · {transformInfo.rotation}°</div>}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>;
});

export default CanvasEditor;
