// FILE: src/components/CommonsPublishDialog.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { BadgeCheck, Coins, Copyright, ExternalLink, ShieldCheck, UploadCloud } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { dataUrlToFile } from '../ai/providers.js';
import { buildCommonsListingPayload, COMMONS_LICENSES, COMMONS_RIGHTS_BASES, validateCommonsRights } from '../lib/commons.js';

const splitList = value => String(value || '').split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean);
const safeName = value => String(value || 'commons-asset').replace(/[^a-z0-9_-]+/gi, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '').toLowerCase().slice(0, 70) || 'commons-asset';

async function sha256(file) {
  if (!globalThis.crypto?.subtle) return '';
  const bytes = await file.arrayBuffer();
  const digest = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', bytes);
  return [...new Uint8Array(digest)].map(value => value.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
}

export default function CommonsPublishDialog({ onClose, editorRef, sourceAsset = null, selectedElements = [], onPublished }) {
  const upload = useEditorStore(state => state.upload);
  const publishAsset = useEditorStore(state => state.publishAsset);
  const design = useEditorStore(state => state.design);
  const user = useEditorStore(state => state.user);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const [title, setTitle] = useState(sourceAsset?.original_name || selectedElements[0]?.name || 'Shared design asset');
  const [description, setDescription] = useState(sourceAsset?.description || '');
  const [tagsText, setTagsText] = useState((sourceAsset?.tags || selectedElements.flatMap(item => item.tags || [])).join(', '));
  const [priceCredits, setPriceCredits] = useState(0);
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);
  const [rights, setRights] = useState({
    basis: 'original',
    copyrightOwner: user?.name || '',
    sourceUrl: '',
    licenceId: 'canvasforge-standard',
    customLicence: '',
    attribution: '',
    evidenceNote: '',
    ownsRights: false,
    allowsRedistribution: false,
    noRestrictedContent: false,
    acceptsTakedown: false
  });
  const validation = useMemo(() => validateCommonsRights(rights), [rights]);
  const patchRights = next => setRights(current => ({ ...current, ...next }));

  const submit = async () => {
    const name = title.trim();
    if (!name) return notify('Enter a Commons listing title.', 'error');
    if (!validation.valid) return notify(validation.errors[0], 'error');
    setBusy(true);
    try {
      let asset = sourceAsset;
      let contentHash = '';
      if (!asset) {
        const exported = await editorRef?.current?.exportSelectionAsset?.({ multiplier: 2 });
        if (!exported?.dataUrl) throw new Error('Select an object or group before publishing it to the Commons.');
        const extension = exported.mimeType === 'image/svg+xml' ? 'svg' : 'png';
        const file = await dataUrlToFile(exported.dataUrl, `${safeName(name)}.${extension}`);
        contentHash = await sha256(file);
        asset = await upload(file, {
          tags: [...new Set(['commons-source', 'canvas-object', ...splitList(tagsText)])],
          sourceType: 'canvas_object',
          sourceJobId: design?.id || ''
        });
      }
      const payload = buildCommonsListingPayload({ title: name, description, tags: splitList(tagsText), priceCredits }, { ...rights, contentHash });
      const listing = await publishAsset(asset.id, payload);
      notify('Submitted to the Design Commons with a rights declaration.', 'success');
      onPublished?.({ listing, asset });
      onClose?.();
    } catch (error) {
      notify(error.message || 'Could not publish this asset.', 'error', 8000);
    } finally { setBusy(false); }
  };

  return <Modal title="Share to the Design Commons" onClose={onClose} wide className="commons-publish-modal">
    <div className="commons-intro"><div><UploadCloud size={22}/><span><strong>Publish a reusable asset</strong><small>Other creators can install it. Paid listings earn credits when they are purchased.</small></span></div><span className="ui-badge tone-neutral">{sourceAsset ? 'Asset library item' : `${selectedElements.length || 1} selected object${selectedElements.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}`}</span></div>

    <div className="commons-publish-grid">
      <section>
        <h3>Listing</h3>
        <label className="field"><span>Title</span><input value={title} onChange={event => setTitle(event.target.value)} maxLength="200"/></label>
        <label className="field"><span>Description</span><textarea rows="5" value={description} onChange={event => setDescription(event.target.value)} placeholder="Explain what the asset is and suitable uses."/></label>
        <label className="field"><span>Tags</span><input value={tagsText} onChange={event => setTagsText(event.target.value)} placeholder="cocktail, vector, menu, illustration"/></label>
        <label className="field"><span>Credit price</span><input type="number" min="0" step="1" value={priceCredits} onChange={event => setPriceCredits(Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0))}/><small>Set 0 to share it for free.</small></label>
        <div className="commons-earning-note"><Coins size={16}/><span>Paid listings are credited through the existing marketplace earnings ledger.</span></div>
      </section>

      <section>
        <div className="commons-rights-heading"><Copyright size={18}/><div><h3>Rights verification</h3><p>This is an attestation, not an automatic legal determination. False declarations can lead to removal and account action.</p></div></div>
        <label className="field"><span>Rights basis</span><select value={rights.basis} onChange={event => patchRights({ basis: event.target.value })}>{COMMONS_RIGHTS_BASES.map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.label}</option>)}</select></label>
        {rights.basis !== 'public-domain' && <label className="field"><span>Copyright owner / rights holder</span><input value={rights.copyrightOwner} onChange={event => patchRights({ copyrightOwner: event.target.value })}/></label>}
        {['licensed', 'client-authorized', 'public-domain'].includes(rights.basis) && <label className="field"><span>Source or licence URL</span><div className="field-with-icon"><ExternalLink size={14}/><input type="url" value={rights.sourceUrl} onChange={event => patchRights({ sourceUrl: event.target.value })} placeholder="https://…"/></div></label>}
        <label className="field"><span>Reuse licence</span><select value={rights.licenceId} onChange={event => patchRights({ licenceId: event.target.value })}>{COMMONS_LICENSES.map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.label}</option>)}</select></label>
        {rights.licenceId === 'custom' && <label className="field"><span>Custom licence terms</span><textarea rows="3" value={rights.customLicence} onChange={event => patchRights({ customLicence: event.target.value })}/></label>}
        <label className="field"><span>Attribution text, when required</span><input value={rights.attribution} onChange={event => patchRights({ attribution: event.target.value })} placeholder="Creator name and source"/></label>
        <label className="field"><span>Evidence note</span><textarea rows="3" value={rights.evidenceNote} onChange={event => patchRights({ evidenceNote: event.target.value })} placeholder="Optional: describe where the original file or permission record is kept."/></label>
        <div className="commons-attestations">
          <label><input type="checkbox" checked={rights.ownsRights} onChange={event => patchRights({ ownsRights: event.target.checked })}/><span>I own the rights or have documented permission to publish this work.</span></label>
          <label><input type="checkbox" checked={rights.allowsRedistribution} onChange={event => patchRights({ allowsRedistribution: event.target.checked })}/><span>The rights allow other CanvasForge users to download, edit, and reuse it under the selected licence.</span></label>
          <label><input type="checkbox" checked={rights.noRestrictedContent} onChange={event => patchRights({ noRestrictedContent: event.target.checked })}/><span>It does not unlawfully include third-party logos, characters, private information, or a person likeness.</span></label>
          <label><input type="checkbox" checked={rights.acceptsTakedown} onChange={event => patchRights({ acceptsTakedown: event.target.checked })}/><span>I accept the Commons reporting, takedown, and dispute process.</span></label>
        </div>
        <div className={`commons-validation ${validation.valid ? 'valid' : 'invalid'}`}>{validation.valid ? <><BadgeCheck size={16}/>Rights declaration complete</> : <><ShieldCheck size={16}/>{validation.errors[0]}</>}</div>
      </section>
    </div>

    <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={onClose}>Cancel</button><button className="primary" disabled={busy || !validation.valid || !title.trim()} onClick={submit}>{busy ? 'Preparing asset…' : 'Submit to Commons'}</button></div>
  </Modal>;
}

// FILE: src/components/DataMergePanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Database, Repeat2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { applyCommandBatch } from '../ai/engine.js';

function parseDelimited(text) {
  const lines = String(text || '').trim().split(/\r?\n/).filter(Boolean);
  if (!lines.length) return { columns: [], rows: [] };
  const delimiter = lines[0].includes('\t') ? '\t' : ',';
  const split = line => line.split(delimiter).map(value => value.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g, ''));
  const columns = split(lines[0]);
  const rows = lines.slice(1).map(line => Object.fromEntries(split(line).map((value, index) => [columns[index] || `Column ${index + 1}`, value])));
  return { columns, rows };
}

export default function DataMergePanel() {
  const [name, setName] = useState('Menu data');
  const [text, setText] = useState('name,description,price\nItem one,Description,$15\nItem two,Description,$15');
  const [sourceId, setSourceId] = useState('');
  const [direction, setDirection] = useState('grid');
  const [columns, setColumns] = useState(2);
  const [gap, setGap] = useState(24);
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const addSource = useEditorStore(state => state.addDataSource);
  const commit = useEditorStore(state => state.commitDocument);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const assets = useEditorStore(state => state.assets);
  const brands = useEditorStore(state => state.brands);
  const components = useEditorStore(state => state.components);
  const revision = useEditorStore(state => state.documentRevision);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const parsed = useMemo(() => parseDelimited(text), [text]);

  const create = () => {
    const source = addSource({ name, ...parsed });
    setSourceId(source.id);
    notify(`Created ${source.name} with ${source.rows.length} rows.`, 'success');
  };
  const repeat = async () => {
    if (!selection.length || !sourceId) return;
    try {
      const result = applyCommandBatch(document, { schemaVersion: 1, baseRevision: revision, commands: [{ op: 'create_repeater', pageIndex, target: { selected: true }, sourceId, direction, columns, gap }] }, { pageIndex, selection, assets, brands, components, revision });
      commit(result.document);
      notify('Created data-driven repeated layout.', 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };

  return <div className="data-merge-panel">
    <label className="field"><span>Data source name</span><input value={name} onChange={event => setName(event.target.value)}/></label>
    <label className="field"><span>Paste CSV or tab-separated data</span><textarea rows="9" value={text} onChange={event => setText(event.target.value)}/></label>
    <small>{parsed.columns.length} columns · {parsed.rows.length} rows</small>
    <button className="primary full" disabled={!parsed.rows.length} onClick={create}><Database size={15}/>Create or refresh source</button>
    <label className="field"><span>Source</span><select value={sourceId} onChange={event => setSourceId(event.target.value)}><option value="">Choose data source</option>{(document.dataSources || []).map(source => <option key={source.id} value={source.id}>{source.name} · {source.rows.length} rows</option>)}</select></label>
    <div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Repeat direction</span><select value={direction} onChange={event => setDirection(event.target.value)}><option value="grid">Grid</option><option value="vertical">Vertical</option><option value="horizontal">Horizontal</option></select></label><label className="field"><span>Columns</span><input type="number" min="1" max="20" value={columns} onChange={event => setColumns(Number(event.target.value) || 1)}/></label></div>
    <label className="field"><span>Gap</span><input type="number" min="0" value={gap} onChange={event => setGap(Number(event.target.value) || 0)}/></label>
    <button className="full" disabled={!selection.length || !sourceId} onClick={repeat}><Repeat2 size={15}/>Repeat selected template from data</button>
    <p className="help">Name text and image layers with content keys such as <code>name</code>, <code>description</code>, <code>price</code>, or <code>image</code>. Repeated instances fill those keys from each row.</p>
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/DesignSystemPanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Link2, Merge, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { normalizeAppearance, solidPaint } from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS, findDuplicateDesignStyles } from '../lib/designSystem.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

const LABELS = { text: 'Text', color: 'Colour', effect: 'Effect', stroke: 'Stroke', spacing: 'Spacing', radius: 'Radius', grid: 'Grid' };

function styleFromElement(kind, element) {
  if (!element) {
    if (kind === 'text') return { fontFamily: 'DM Sans', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 500, lineHeight: 1.3, charSpacing: 0 };
    if (kind === 'color') return { paint: solidPaint('#231f20') };
    if (kind === 'effect') return { appearance: normalizeAppearance({}).shadows };
    if (kind === 'stroke') return { color: '#231f20', width: 1, opacity: 1, style: 'solid' };
    if (kind === 'spacing') return { padding: { top: 24, right: 24, bottom: 24, left: 24 } };
    if (kind === 'radius') return { radius: 16 };
    return { columns: 12, gutter: 24, margin: 48 };
  }
  if (kind === 'text') return { fontFamily: element.fontFamily, fontSize: element.fontSize, fontWeight: element.fontWeight, fontStyle: element.fontStyle, lineHeight: element.lineHeight, charSpacing: element.charSpacing, textAlign: element.textAlign };
  if (kind === 'color') return { paint: solidPaint(element.fill || '#111827') };
  if (kind === 'effect') return { appearance: normalizeAppearance(element) };
  if (kind === 'stroke') return { color: element.stroke || '#111827', width: element.strokeWidth || 0, opacity: normalizeAppearance(element).stroke?.opacity ?? 1, style: normalizeAppearance(element).stroke?.style || 'solid' };
  if (kind === 'spacing') return { padding: element.type === 'frame' ? element.layout?.padding || 0 : element.internalPadding || 0 };
  if (kind === 'radius') return { radius: element.radius || 0 };
  return { columns: 12, gutter: 24, margin: 48 };
}

export default function DesignSystemPanel() {
  const [kind, setKind] = useState('text');
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const createStyle = useEditorStore(state => state.createDesignStyle);
  const updateStyle = useEditorStore(state => state.updateDesignStyle);
  const removeStyle = useEditorStore(state => state.deleteDesignStyle);
  const attachStyle = useEditorStore(state => state.attachDesignStyle);
  const deduplicate = useEditorStore(state => state.deduplicateDesignStyles);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const page = document.pages[pageIndex];
  const selected = page?.elements?.find(element => selection.includes(element.id));
  const styles = document.designSystem?.styles?.[kind] || [];
  const duplicates = useMemo(() => findDuplicateDesignStyles(document), [document]);

  const create = () => {
    const name = prompt(`${LABELS[kind]} style name`, selected?.role ? `${selected.role} style` : `New ${LABELS[kind].toLowerCase()} style`);
    if (!name) return;
    try {
      const style = createStyle(kind, { name, semanticRole: selected?.role || '', value: styleFromElement(kind, selected) });
      if (selected && kind !== 'grid') attachStyle(kind, style.id);
      notify(`Created linked ${LABELS[kind].toLowerCase()} style.`, 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };

  const edit = style => {
    const draft = prompt(`Edit ${style.name} as JSON`, JSON.stringify(style.value, null, 2));
    if (!draft) return;
    try { updateStyle(kind, style.id, { value: JSON.parse(draft) }); }
    catch (error) { notify(`Could not update style: ${error.message}`, 'error'); }
  };

  return <div className="design-system-panel">
    <div className="design-style-tabs">{DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS.map(value => <button key={value} className={kind === value ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setKind(value)}>{LABELS[value]}</button>)}</div>
    <div className="panel-heading"><div><h4>{LABELS[kind]} styles</h4><small>Linked styles update every attached object.</small></div><button onClick={create}><Plus size={14}/>New</button></div>
    <div className="design-style-list">{styles.map(style => <article key={style.id}>
      <button className="design-style-main" onClick={() => edit(style)}><strong>{style.name}</strong><small>{style.semanticRole || 'No semantic role'}</small></button>
      {selected && kind !== 'grid' && <button title="Attach to selection" onClick={() => attachStyle(kind, style.id)}><Link2 size={14}/></button>}
      <button title="Delete style" onClick={() => removeStyle(kind, style.id)}><Trash2 size={14}/></button>
    </article>)}</div>
    {!styles.length && <p className="help">Create a style from the selected object or from professional defaults.</p>}
    <button className="full" disabled={!duplicates.length} onClick={() => { const groups = deduplicate(); notify(`Merged ${groups.length} duplicate style group${groups.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}.`, 'success'); }}><Merge size={14}/>Merge duplicate styles ({duplicates.length})</button>
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/EditorDialogs.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { api } from '../lib/api.js';

const Field = ({ label, children }) => <label className="field"><span>{label}</span>{children}</label>;

export function ResizeDialog({ onClose }) {
  const document = useEditorStore(s => s.document);
  const magicResize = useEditorStore(s => s.magicResize);
  const save = useEditorStore(s => s.save);
  const [width, setWidth] = useState(document.width);
  const [height, setHeight] = useState(document.height);
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);
  const presets = [[1080, 1080, 'Square'], [1080, 1920, 'Story'], [1920, 1080, 'Presentation'], [816, 1056, 'Letter'], [794, 1123, 'A4']];

  return <Modal title="Magic resize" onClose={onClose}>
    <p className="help">Elements follow their constraints and auto-layout groups reflow. A restorable version is saved first.</p>
    <div className="preset-grid">{presets.map(([presetWidth, presetHeight, name]) => <button key={name} onClick={() => { setWidth(presetWidth); setHeight(presetHeight); }}>{name}<small>{presetWidth} × {presetHeight}</small></button>)}</div>
    <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Width"><input type="number" min="1" value={width} onChange={event => setWidth(Number(event.target.value))}/></Field><Field label="Height"><input type="number" min="1" value={height} onChange={event => setHeight(Number(event.target.value))}/></Field></div>
    <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={onClose}>Cancel</button><button className="primary" disabled={busy || width < 1 || height < 1} onClick={async () => { setBusy(true); try { await save({ createVersion: true, versionLabel: `Before resize to ${width}×${height}` }); magicResize(width, height); onClose(); } finally { setBusy(false); } }}>{busy ? 'Saving version…' : 'Resize design'}</button></div>
  </Modal>;
}

export function TemplateDialog({ onClose }) {
  const save = useEditorStore(state => state.saveCurrentAsTemplate);
  const templateFolders = useEditorStore(state => state.templateFolders);
  const refresh = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshResources);
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('New template');
  const [category, setCategory] = useState('Custom');
  const [tags, setTags] = useState('');
  const [description, setDescription] = useState('');
  const [visibility, setVisibility] = useState('workspace');
  const [folderId, setFolderId] = useState('');
  const [publish, setPublish] = useState(false);
  const [priceCredits, setPriceCredits] = useState(0);
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);

  return <Modal title="Save as template" onClose={onClose}>
    <Field label="Title"><input value={title} onChange={event => setTitle(event.target.value)}/></Field>
    <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Category"><input value={category} onChange={event => setCategory(event.target.value)}/></Field><Field label="Folder"><select value={folderId} onChange={event => setFolderId(event.target.value)}><option value="">My templates</option>{templateFolders.map(folder => <option key={folder.id} value={folder.id}>{folder.name}</option>)}</select></Field></div>
    <Field label="Tags"><input value={tags} onChange={event => setTags(event.target.value)} placeholder="social, restaurant"/></Field>
    <Field label="Description"><textarea value={description} onChange={event => setDescription(event.target.value)}/></Field>
    <Field label="Workspace visibility"><select value={visibility} onChange={event => setVisibility(event.target.value)}><option value="workspace">Everyone in this workspace</option><option value="private">Only me</option></select></Field>
    <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={publish} onChange={event => setPublish(event.target.checked)}/>Publish an immutable marketplace copy after saving</label>
    {publish && <Field label="Marketplace price"><select value={priceCredits} onChange={event => setPriceCredits(Number(event.target.value))}><option value="0">Free</option><option value="25">25 credits</option><option value="50">50 credits</option><option value="100">100 credits</option><option value="250">250 credits</option></select></Field>}
    <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={onClose}>Cancel</button><button className="primary" disabled={busy || !title.trim()} onClick={async () => { setBusy(true); try { const template = await save({ title, category, description, visibility, folderId: folderId || null, tags: tags.split(',').map(value => value.trim()).filter(Boolean) }); if (publish) await api.publishMarketplaceListing({ listingType: 'template', sourceTemplateId: template.id, title, description, tags: tags.split(',').map(value => value.trim()).filter(Boolean), priceType: priceCredits ? 'credits' : 'free', priceCredits }); await refresh(); onClose(); } finally { setBusy(false); } }}>{busy ? 'Saving…' : publish ? 'Save and publish' : 'Save template'}</button></div>
  </Modal>;
}

export function ShareDialog({ onClose }) {
  const shares = useEditorStore(s => s.shares);
  const create = useEditorStore(s => s.createShare);
  const refresh = useEditorStore(s => s.refreshResources);
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [days, setDays] = useState(30);
  const [allowDownload, setAllowDownload] = useState(true);
  const [allowCopy, setAllowCopy] = useState(false);
  const [created, setCreated] = useState(null);
  const link = created ? `${location.origin}/?share=${created.token}` : '';

  return <Modal title="Share design" onClose={onClose}>
    <Field label="Optional password"><input type="password" value={password} onChange={event => setPassword(event.target.value)}/></Field>
    <Field label="Expires in days"><input type="number" min="1" value={days} onChange={event => setDays(Number(event.target.value))}/></Field>
    <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={allowDownload} onChange={event => setAllowDownload(event.target.checked)}/>Allow downloads</label>
    <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={allowCopy} onChange={event => setAllowCopy(event.target.checked)}/>Allow copying the design JSON</label>
    <button className="primary full" onClick={async () => setCreated(await create({ password: password || undefined, allowDownload, allowCopy, expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + days * 86400000).toISOString() }))}>Create share link</button>
    {link && <div className="share-result"><input readOnly value={link}/><button onClick={() => navigator.clipboard.writeText(link)}>Copy</button></div>}
    <h3>Existing links</h3>
    <div className="compact-list">{shares.map(share => <div key={share.id}><span>{share.token_hint}… {share.revoked_at ? 'Revoked' : ''}</span>{!share.revoked_at && <button onClick={async () => { await api.revokeShare(share.id); await refresh(); }}>Revoke</button>}</div>)}</div>
  </Modal>;
}

export function ReviewDialog({ onClose }) {
  const design = useEditorStore(s => s.design);
  const comments = useEditorStore(s => s.comments);
  const selection = useEditorStore(s => s.selection);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(s => s.pageIndex);
  const document = useEditorStore(s => s.document);
  const members = useEditorStore(s => s.members);
  const add = useEditorStore(s => s.addComment);
  const resolve = useEditorStore(s => s.resolveComment);
  const setStatus = useEditorStore(s => s.setStatus);
  const loadMembers = useEditorStore(s => s.loadMembers);
  const [body, setBody] = useState('');
  const [replyTo, setReplyTo] = useState(null);

  React.useEffect(() => { loadMembers().catch(() => {}); }, []);

  const { roots, children } = useMemo(() => {
    const byParent = new Map();
    for (const comment of comments) {
      if (!comment.parent_id) continue;
      const list = byParent.get(comment.parent_id) || [];
      list.push(comment);
      byParent.set(comment.parent_id, list);
    }
    return { roots: comments.filter(comment => !comment.parent_id), children: byParent };
  }, [comments]);

  const renderComment = (comment, depth = 0) => <React.Fragment key={comment.id}>
    <article className={`${comment.resolved_at ? 'resolved' : ''} ${depth ? 'comment-reply' : ''}`}>
      <header><strong>{comment.author_name}</strong><small>{new Date(comment.created_at).toLocaleString()}</small></header>
      <p>{comment.body}</p>
      <footer>
        <span>{comment.element_id ? 'Element comment' : comment.page_id ? 'Page comment' : 'Design comment'}</span>
        <button onClick={() => { setReplyTo(comment); setBody(`@${String(comment.author_name).replace(/\s+/g, '')} `); }}>Reply</button>
        <button onClick={() => resolve(comment.id, !comment.resolved_at)}>{comment.resolved_at ? 'Reopen' : 'Resolve'}</button>
      </footer>
    </article>
    {(children.get(comment.id) || []).map(reply => renderComment(reply, depth + 1))}
  </React.Fragment>;

  return <Modal title="Review and approval" onClose={onClose} wide>
    <Field label="Status"><select value={design.status || 'draft'} onChange={event => setStatus(event.target.value)}><option value="draft">Draft</option><option value="ready_for_review">Ready for review</option><option value="changes_requested">Changes requested</option><option value="approved">Approved</option><option value="archived">Archived</option></select></Field>
    {design.approved_version_id && <p className="approval-record">Approved version: <code>{design.approved_version_id}</code></p>}
    <div className="mention-help">Mention teammates with {members.slice(0, 4).map(member => <button key={member.id} onClick={() => setBody(value => `${value}${value && !value.endsWith(' ') ? ' ' : ''}@${String(member.name).replace(/\s+/g, '')} `)}>@{String(member.name).replace(/\s+/g, '')}</button>)}</div>
    {replyTo && <div className="replying-to">Replying to {replyTo.author_name}<button onClick={() => setReplyTo(null)}>Cancel</button></div>}
    <div className="comment-compose"><textarea value={body} onChange={event => setBody(event.target.value)} placeholder="Add a page or selected-element comment…"/><button className="primary" disabled={!body.trim()} onClick={async () => { await add({ body, pageId: document.pages[pageIndex].id, elementId: selection[0] || null, parentId: replyTo?.id || null }); setBody(''); setReplyTo(null); }}>Comment</button></div>
    <div className="comment-list">{roots.length ? roots.map(comment => renderComment(comment)) : <p>No comments yet.</p>}</div>
  </Modal>;
}

import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ArrowRight, BarChart3, Box, ChevronDown, ChevronRight, Circle, Code2, CornerUpLeft, Database, Diamond, Eye, EyeOff, FolderPlus, Grid3X3, Group, Heart, Hexagon, ImagePlus, Layers,
  LayoutTemplate, Lock, LockOpen, MessageCircle, Minus, Palette, Pentagon, Plus, QrCode, Shapes, Sparkles, Square, Star, Table2, Triangle,
  Type, Ungroup, Upload
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import {
  baseElement, chartElement, ellipseElement, frameElement, imageElement, imageFrameElement, qrElement,
  rectElement, reparentElements, shapeElement, svgElement, tableElement, textElement
} from '../lib/document.js';

import { normalizeAppearance, solidPaint } from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { ASSET_DRAG_TYPE, LAYER_DRAG_TYPE, LEGACY_LAYER_DRAG_TYPE, readMigratedStorage, writeStorage } from '../lib/appMeta.js';
import DataMergePanel from './DataMergePanel.jsx';
import CommonsPublishDialog from './CommonsPublishDialog.jsx';

const splitList = value => String(value || '').split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean);

function layerRows(elements, collapsed, query = '') {
  const sorted = [...elements].sort((a, b) => b.zIndex - a.zIndex);
  const byId = new Map(sorted.map(element => [element.id, element]));
  if (query) return sorted.filter(element => `${element.name || ''} ${element.type} ${element.role || ''} ${element.semanticName || ''}`.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())).map(element => {
    let depth = 0, parent = element.parentId ? byId.get(element.parentId) : null;
    while (parent && depth < 12) { depth++; parent = parent.parentId ? byId.get(parent.parentId) : null; }
    return { element, depth, childCount: sorted.filter(item => item.parentId === element.id).length };
  });
  const children = new Map();
  sorted.forEach(element => {
    const key = element.parentId && byId.has(element.parentId) ? element.parentId : null;
    if (!children.has(key)) children.set(key, []);
    children.get(key).push(element);
  });
  const rows = [];
  const walk = (parentId, depth) => {
    for (const element of children.get(parentId) || []) {
      const childCount = (children.get(element.id) || []).length;
      rows.push({ element, depth, childCount });
      if (childCount && !collapsed.has(element.id)) walk(element.id, depth + 1);
    }
  };
  walk(null, 0);
  return rows;
}

export default function LeftPanel({ editorRef }) {

  const [renamingLayer, setRenamingLayer] = useState(null);
  const [layerName, setLayerName] = useState('');
  const [collapsedLayers, setCollapsedLayers] = useState(() => new Set());
  const [folder, setFolder] = useState('');
  const [templateFolder, setTemplateFolder] = useState('');
  const [selectedAssetId, setSelectedAssetId] = useState(null);
  const [assetUsage, setAssetUsage] = useState([]);
  const [replacementId, setReplacementId] = useState('');
  const [commonsAsset, setCommonsAsset] = useState(null);
  const uploadRef = useRef();

  const assets = useEditorStore(s => s.assets);

  const templateFolders = useEditorStore(s => s.templateFolders);

  const components = useEditorStore(s => s.components);
  const brands = useEditorStore(s => s.brands);

  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(s => s.pageIndex);
  const selection = useEditorStore(s => s.selection);
  const groupSelection = useEditorStore(s => s.groupSelection);
  const ungroupSelection = useEditorStore(s => s.ungroupSelection);
  const role = useEditorStore(s => s.role);
  const addElement = useEditorStore(s => s.addElement);
  const uploadMany = useEditorStore(s => s.uploadMany);
  const applyTemplate = useEditorStore(s => s.applyTemplate);
  const updateElements = useEditorStore(s => s.updateElements);
  const refresh = useEditorStore(s => s.refreshResources);
  const loadDesign = useEditorStore(s => s.loadDesign);
  const saveComponent = useEditorStore(s => s.saveSelectionAsComponent);
  const updateComponent = useEditorStore(s => s.updateComponentFromSelection);
  const insertComponent = useEditorStore(s => s.insertComponent);
  const applyBrand = useEditorStore(s => s.applyBrand);
  const createBrand = useEditorStore(s => s.createBrand);
  const updateBrand = useEditorStore(s => s.updateBrand);
  const updatePage = useEditorStore(s => s.updatePage);
  const showRulers = useEditorStore(s => s.showRulers);
  const showGuides = useEditorStore(s => s.showGuides);
  const snapToPage = useEditorStore(s => s.snapToPage);
  const snapToGuides = useEditorStore(s => s.snapToGuides);
  const snapToObjects = useEditorStore(s => s.snapToObjects);
  const snapToGrid = useEditorStore(s => s.snapToGrid);
  const snapToMargins = useEditorStore(s => s.snapToMargins);
  const setWorkspacePreference = useEditorStore(s => s.setWorkspacePreference);
  const notify = useEditorStore(s => s.notify);
  const publishAsset = useEditorStore(s => s.publishAsset);
  const publishTemplate = useEditorStore(s => s.publishTemplate);

  const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex];
  const canEdit = ['owner', 'admin', 'designer'].includes(role);
  const canAdmin = ['owner', 'admin'].includes(role);
  const selectedAsset = assets.find(asset => asset.id === selectedAssetId) || null;
  const selectedElement = page?.elements?.find(element => element.id === selection[0]) || null;
  const sorted = [...(page?.elements || [])].sort((a, b) => b.zIndex - a.zIndex);
  const visibleLayerRows = layerRows(page?.elements || [], collapsedLayers, layerQuery);
  const filteredLayers = visibleLayerRows.map(row => row.element);
  const groupNumbers = new Map();
  sorted.forEach(element => { if (element.groupId && !groupNumbers.has(element.groupId)) groupNumbers.set(element.groupId, groupNumbers.size + 1); });
  const selectionHasGroup = sorted.some(element => selection.includes(element.id) && element.groupId);
  const tools = [
    { id: 'text', label: 'Text', category: 'Text', Icon: Type, create: () => textElement() },
    { id: 'rectangle', label: 'Rectangle', category: 'Shapes', Icon: Square, create: () => rectElement() },
    { id: 'frame', label: 'Frame / container', category: 'Layout', Icon: Box, create: () => frameElement() },
    { id: 'image-frame', label: 'Image frame', category: 'Layout', Icon: ImagePlus, create: () => imageFrameElement() },
    { id: 'ellipse', label: 'Ellipse', category: 'Shapes', Icon: Circle, create: () => ellipseElement() },
    { id: 'triangle', label: 'Triangle', category: 'Shapes', Icon: Triangle, create: () => shapeElement('triangle') },

    { id: 'svg', label: 'Custom SVG', category: 'Vectors', Icon: Code2, create: () => svgElement() },
    { id: 'line', label: 'Line', category: 'Lines', Icon: Minus, create: () => baseElement('line', { name: 'Line', width: 300, height: 0, stroke: '#111827', strokeWidth: 5, appearance: { fill: { type: 'none' }, stroke: { enabled: true, color: '#111827', opacity: 1, width: 5, style: 'solid', dash: 10, gap: 8, lineCap: 'round', lineJoin: 'round' }, shadow: { enabled: false, color: '#000000', opacity: .25, blur: 0, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 }, blendMode: 'source-over' } }) },
    { id: 'chart', label: 'Chart', category: 'Data', Icon: BarChart3, create: () => chartElement() },

  };

  const onDropLayer = (event, target) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    const sourceId = event.dataTransfer.getData(LAYER_DRAG_TYPE) || event.dataTransfer.getData(LEGACY_LAYER_DRAG_TYPE);
    if (!sourceId || sourceId === target.id || !page) return;
    const draggedIds = selection.includes(sourceId) ? selection : [sourceId];
    try {
      updatePage(currentPage => {
        const nextParentId = target.type === 'frame' ? target.id : (target.parentId || null);
        reparentElements(currentPage, draggedIds, nextParentId);
        if (target.type !== 'frame') {
          const ascending = [...currentPage.elements].sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
          const moving = ascending.filter(item => draggedIds.includes(item.id));
          const rest = ascending.filter(item => !draggedIds.includes(item.id));
          const targetIndex = Math.max(0, rest.findIndex(item => item.id === target.id));
          rest.splice(targetIndex + 1, 0, ...moving);
          currentPage.elements = rest.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, zIndex: index }));
        }
      });
      if (target.type === 'frame') setCollapsedLayers(current => { const next = new Set(current); next.delete(target.id); return next; });
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };

    const replacement = assets.find(asset => asset.id === replacementId);

    const result = await api.replaceAssetEverywhere(selectedAsset.id, replacementId);

      {tab === 'add' && <>
        <h3>Add elements</h3>
        <input className="search-input" placeholder="Search elements" value={addQuery} onChange={event => setAddQuery(event.target.value)}/>
        {!!recentTools.length && !addQuery && <><h4 className="panel-subheading">Recently used</h4><div className="add-grid compact">{recentTools.map(id => tools.find(tool => tool.id === id)).filter(Boolean).map(tool => <button key={tool.id} disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => addTool(tool)}>{React.createElement(tool.Icon)}{tool.label}</button>)}</div></>}

        {!visibleTools.length && <p className="empty-panel-state">No elements match "{addQuery}".</p>}
      </>}

      {tab === 'assets' && <>
        <div className="panel-heading"><h3>Asset library</h3><button title="New folder" disabled={!canEdit} onClick={async () => { const name = prompt('Folder name'); if (name) { await api.createAssetFolder(name); await refresh(); } }}><FolderPlus size={16}/></button></div>
        <input className="search-input" placeholder="Search assets" value={query} onChange={event => setQuery(event.target.value)}/>

        <div className="asset-grid">{filteredAssets.map(asset => <div className={`asset-card ${selectedAssetId === asset.id ? 'selected' : ''}`} key={asset.id} draggable={canEdit} onDragStart={event => { event.dataTransfer.setData(ASSET_DRAG_TYPE, asset.id); event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'copy'; }} onClick={() => setSelectedAssetId(asset.id)}>
          <button className="asset-image" onDoubleClick={() => { if (!canEdit) return; const element = imageElement(asset); if (editorRef.current?.insertElement) editorRef.current.insertElement(element); else addElement(element); }}><img src={asset.thumbnail_url || asset.preview_url || asset.url}/></button>
          <span>{asset.original_name}</span>
          <button className="favorite" title="Favourite" onClick={async event => { event.stopPropagation(); await updateAsset(asset.id, { favorite: !asset.favorite }); }}>{asset.favorite ? '★' : '☆'}</button>
        </div>)}</div>
        {selectedAsset && <div className="asset-details">
          <strong>{selectedAsset.original_name}</strong>
          <small>{selectedAsset.width || '?'} × {selectedAsset.height || '?'} · used in {assetUsage.length} design{assetUsage.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}</small>
          <label>Name<input defaultValue={selectedAsset.original_name} onBlur={event => event.target.value.trim() && updateAsset(selectedAsset.id, { originalName: event.target.value.trim() })}/></label>
          <label>Folder<select value={selectedAsset.folder_id || ''} onChange={event => updateAsset(selectedAsset.id, { folderId: event.target.value || null })}><option value="">Unfiled</option>{folders.map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>)}</select></label>
          <label>Tags<input defaultValue={(selectedAsset.tags || []).join(', ')} onBlur={event => updateAsset(selectedAsset.id, { tags: splitList(event.target.value) })} placeholder="menu, logo, photo"/></label>
          <div className="button-row wrap"><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => { const element = imageElement(selectedAsset); if (editorRef.current?.insertElement) editorRef.current.insertElement(element); else addElement(element); }}>Add</button><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { assetId: selectedAsset.id, src: selectedAsset.preview_url || selectedAsset.url, name: selectedAsset.original_name, opacity: .45, visible: true, mode: 'overlay', fit: 'contain', split: .5 }; })}>Use as reference</button>{selectedElement?.type === 'image' && selectedElement.isImageFrame && <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => updateElements([selectedElement.id], { src: selectedAsset.preview_url || selectedAsset.url, assetId: selectedAsset.id, nativeWidth: selectedAsset.width || 1000, nativeHeight: selectedAsset.height || 1000, cropX: null, cropY: null, cropZoom: 1, isImageFrame: true })}>Fill selected frame</button>}<button onClick={() => notify(assetUsage.length ? `Used in: ${assetUsage.map(item => item.title).join(', ')}` : 'This asset is not used in any design.')}>Usage</button><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => setCommonsAsset(selectedAsset)}>Share to Commons</button></div>
          {assets.length > 1 && <div className="replace-asset"><select value={replacementId} onChange={event => setReplacementId(event.target.value)}><option value="">Replacement asset…</option>{assets.filter(asset => asset.id !== selectedAsset.id).map(asset => <option key={asset.id} value={asset.id}>{asset.original_name}</option>)}</select><button disabled={!canEdit || !replacementId} onClick={replaceEverywhere}>Replace everywhere</button></div>}
          <button className="danger full" disabled={!canEdit} onClick={async () => { try { await api.deleteAsset(selectedAsset.id); setSelectedAssetId(null); await refresh(); } catch (error) { notify(error.message + (error.payload?.usage ? ` Used in: ${error.payload.usage.map(item => item.title).join(', ')}` : ''), 'error', 8000); } }}>Delete asset</button>
        </div>}
      </>}

      {tab === 'layers' && <>
        <div className="panel-heading"><div><h3>Objects & layers</h3><small className="panel-heading-help">Top objects appear first</small></div><span className="count-badge">{sorted.length}</span></div>
        <div className="object-list-actions">
          <button disabled={!sorted.length} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.selectAll()}>Select all</button>
          <button disabled={!selection.length} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.clearSelection()}>Clear</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit || selection.length < 2} onClick={() => { try { groupSelection(); notify('Objects grouped.', 'success'); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }}><Group size={14}/>Group</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit || !selectionHasGroup} onClick={() => { try { ungroupSelection(); notify('Objects ungrouped.', 'success'); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }}><Ungroup size={14}/>Ungroup</button>
        </div>
        <p className="object-list-help">Drag onto a frame to make an object its child. Drag elsewhere to change stacking. Shift/Ctrl/Cmd-click selects multiple objects.</p>
        <input className="search-input" placeholder="Search objects, roles, or types" value={layerQuery} onChange={event => setLayerQuery(event.target.value)}/>
        <div className="layer-list hierarchy-layer-list">{visibleLayerRows.map(({ element, depth, childCount }) => {
          const groupNumber = element.groupId ? groupNumbers.get(element.groupId) : null;
          const collapsed = collapsedLayers.has(element.id);
          return <div key={element.id} draggable={canEdit && renamingLayer !== element.id}
            onDragStart={event => { event.dataTransfer.setData(LAYER_DRAG_TYPE, element.id); event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move'; }}
            onDragOver={event => { if (canEdit) { event.preventDefault(); event.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move'; } }}
            onDrop={event => canEdit && onDropLayer(event, element)}
            className={`layer-row ${selection.includes(element.id) ? 'selected' : ''} ${element.groupId ? 'grouped' : ''} ${element.type === 'frame' ? 'frame-layer' : ''}`}
            style={{ '--layer-depth': depth }}
            onClick={event => editorRef.current?.select(element.id, event.shiftKey || event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)}>
            <span className="layer-indent"/>
            {childCount ? <button className="layer-expand" title={collapsed ? 'Expand children' : 'Collapse children'} onClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); setCollapsedLayers(current => { const next = new Set(current); collapsed ? next.delete(element.id) : next.add(element.id); return next; }); }}>{collapsed ? <ChevronRight size={14}/> : <ChevronDown size={14}/>}</button> : <span className="layer-expand-placeholder"/>}
            <span className="drag-handle">⋮⋮</span>
            <span className="layer-copy">{renamingLayer === element.id ? <input className="layer-name-input" autoFocus value={layerName} onClick={event => event.stopPropagation()} onChange={event => setLayerName(event.target.value)} onBlur={() => { const name = layerName.trim(); if (name) updateElements([element.id], { name }); setRenamingLayer(null); }} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur(); if (event.key === 'Escape') setRenamingLayer(null); }}/> : <span className="layer-name" onDoubleClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); setRenamingLayer(element.id); setLayerName(element.name || element.type); }}>{element.name || element.type}</span>}<small>{element.type}{element.role ? ` · ${element.role}` : ''}{childCount ? ` · ${childCount} child${childCount === 1 ? '' : 'ren'}` : ''}</small></span>
            <span className="layer-group-indicator" title={element.groupId ? `Object group ${groupNumber}` : element.layoutGroupId ? 'Auto-layout group' : element.parentId ? 'Inside frame' : ''}>{element.groupId ? `G${groupNumber}` : element.layoutGroupId ? '↔' : element.parentId ? '↳' : ''}</span>
            {element.parentId && <button title="Move out of frame" disabled={!canEdit} onClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); updatePage(currentPage => reparentElements(currentPage, [element.id], null)); }}><CornerUpLeft size={14}/></button>}
            <button title={element.hidden ? 'Show' : 'Hide'} disabled={!canEdit} onClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); updateElements([element.id], { hidden: !element.hidden }); }}>{element.hidden ? <EyeOff size={15}/> : <Eye size={15}/>}</button>
            <button title={element.locked ? 'Unlock' : 'Lock'} disabled={!canEdit} onClick={event => { event.stopPropagation(); updateElements([element.id], { locked: !element.locked }); }}>{element.locked ? <Lock size={15}/> : <LockOpen size={15}/>}</button>
          </div>;
        })}</div>
        {!filteredLayers.length && <p className="empty-panel-state">No objects found.</p>}
      </>}

      {tab === 'layout' && <>
        <h3>Layout and guides</h3>
        <section className="reference-image-panel">
          <div className="panel-heading"><div><h4>Reference image</h4><small className="panel-heading-help">Editor-only visual target; never exported</small></div>{page?.referenceImage && <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = null; })}>Clear</button>}</div>
          <label className="field"><span>Asset</span><select disabled={!canEdit} value={page?.referenceImage?.assetId || ''} onChange={event => { const asset = assets.find(item => item.id === event.target.value); updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = asset ? { assetId: asset.id, src: asset.preview_url || asset.url, name: asset.original_name, opacity: currentPage.referenceImage?.opacity ?? .45, visible: true, mode: currentPage.referenceImage?.mode || 'overlay', fit: currentPage.referenceImage?.fit || 'contain', split: currentPage.referenceImage?.split ?? .5 } : null; }); }}><option value="">No reference</option>{assets.map(asset => <option key={asset.id} value={asset.id}>{asset.original_name}</option>)}</select></label>
          {page?.referenceImage && <>
            <label className="check"><input disabled={!canEdit} type="checkbox" checked={page.referenceImage.visible !== false} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { ...currentPage.referenceImage, visible: event.target.checked }; })}/>Show reference overlay</label>
            <label className="paint-range"><span>Opacity {Math.round((page.referenceImage.opacity ?? .45) * 100)}%</span><input disabled={!canEdit} type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={page.referenceImage.opacity ?? .45} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { ...currentPage.referenceImage, opacity: Number(event.target.value) }; })}/></label>
            <div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Compare</span><select disabled={!canEdit} value={page.referenceImage.mode || 'overlay'} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { ...currentPage.referenceImage, mode: event.target.value }; })}><option value="overlay">Overlay</option><option value="difference">Difference</option><option value="split">Split view</option></select></label><label className="field"><span>Fit</span><select disabled={!canEdit} value={page.referenceImage.fit || 'contain'} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { ...currentPage.referenceImage, fit: event.target.value }; })}><option value="contain">Contain</option><option value="cover">Cover</option><option value="stretch">Stretch</option></select></label></div>
            {page.referenceImage.mode === 'split' && <label className="paint-range"><span>Split {Math.round((page.referenceImage.split ?? .5) * 100)}%</span><input disabled={!canEdit} type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={page.referenceImage.split ?? .5} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.referenceImage = { ...currentPage.referenceImage, split: Number(event.target.value) }; })}/></label>}
          </>}
        </section>
        <div className="stack-buttons">
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.addGuide('vertical', document.width / 2)}>Add vertical centre guide</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.addGuide('horizontal', document.height / 2)}>Add horizontal centre guide</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => { const axis = confirm('Create a vertical guide? Press Cancel for horizontal.') ? 'vertical' : 'horizontal'; const value = Number(prompt('Guide position', axis === 'vertical' ? document.width / 2 : document.height / 2)); if (Number.isFinite(value)) editorRef.current?.addGuide(axis, value); }}>Add guide at position…</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.toggleGuideLock()}>{page?.guides?.locked ? 'Unlock guides' : 'Lock guides'}</button>
          <button disabled={!canEdit || !(page?.guides?.vertical?.length || page?.guides?.horizontal?.length)} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.clearGuides()}>Clear guides</button>
        </div>
        <h4 className="panel-subheading">View</h4>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={showRulers} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('showRulers', event.target.checked)}/>Show rulers</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={showGuides} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('showGuides', event.target.checked)}/>Show guides</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!page?.grid?.enabled} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.grid = { ...(currentPage.grid || {}), enabled: event.target.checked }; })}/>Show grid</label>
        {page?.grid?.enabled && <div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Grid size</span><input type="number" min="4" max="200" value={page.grid.size || 20} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.grid = { ...(currentPage.grid || {}), size: Math.max(4, Number(event.target.value) || 20) }; })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Subdivisions</span><input type="number" min="1" max="10" value={page.grid.subdivisions || 1} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.grid = { ...(currentPage.grid || {}), subdivisions: Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Number(event.target.value) || 1)) }; })}/></label></div>}
        <section className="professional-grid-panel">
          <div className="panel-heading"><div><h4>Column grid</h4><small className="panel-heading-help">Professional layout columns, gutters, and outside margins</small></div><label className="switch-compact"><input type="checkbox" checked={page?.designGrids?.[0]?.enabled !== false && !!page?.designGrids?.length} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { const existing = currentPage.designGrids?.[0] || { id: `grid-${Date.now()}`, name: 'Primary columns', columns: 12, gutter: 24, margin: 48, color: '#7c3aed', opacity: .18 }; currentPage.designGrids = event.target.checked ? [{ ...existing, enabled: true }, ...(currentPage.designGrids || []).slice(1)] : (currentPage.designGrids || []).map((grid, index) => index ? grid : { ...grid, enabled: false }); })}/></label></div>
          {!!page?.designGrids?.length && <div className="field-grid four"><label className="field"><span>Columns</span><input type="number" min="1" max="48" value={page.designGrids[0].columns || 12} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.designGrids[0].columns = Math.max(1, Math.min(48, Number(event.target.value) || 12)); })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Gutter</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page.designGrids[0].gutter || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.designGrids[0].gutter = Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0); })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Margin</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page.designGrids[0].margin || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.designGrids[0].margin = Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0); })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Opacity</span><input type="number" min="0" max="1" step=".05" value={page.designGrids[0].opacity ?? .18} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.designGrids[0].opacity = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(event.target.value) || 0)); })}/></label></div>}
        </section>
        <section className="professional-grid-panel">
          <div className="panel-heading"><div><h4>Baseline grid</h4><small className="panel-heading-help">Align text across cards, columns, and pages</small></div><label className="switch-compact"><input type="checkbox" checked={page?.baselineGrids?.[0]?.enabled !== false && !!page?.baselineGrids?.length} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { const existing = currentPage.baselineGrids?.[0] || { id: `baseline-${Date.now()}`, name: 'Baseline grid', step: 8, offset: 0, color: '#0ea5e9', opacity: .22 }; currentPage.baselineGrids = event.target.checked ? [{ ...existing, enabled: true }, ...(currentPage.baselineGrids || []).slice(1)] : (currentPage.baselineGrids || []).map((grid, index) => index ? grid : { ...grid, enabled: false }); })}/></label></div>
          {!!page?.baselineGrids?.length && <div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Baseline step</span><input type="number" min="2" max="96" value={page.baselineGrids[0].step || 8} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.baselineGrids[0].step = Math.max(2, Number(event.target.value) || 8); })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Start offset</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page.baselineGrids[0].offset || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.baselineGrids[0].offset = Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0); })}/></label></div>}
        </section>
        <h4 className="panel-subheading">Margins</h4>
        <div className="field-grid margin-grid"><label className="field"><span>Top</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page?.margins?.top || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), top: Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0) }; })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Right</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page?.margins?.right || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), right: Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0) }; })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Bottom</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page?.margins?.bottom || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), bottom: Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0) }; })}/></label><label className="field"><span>Left</span><input type="number" min="0" value={page?.margins?.left || 0} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), left: Math.max(0, Number(event.target.value) || 0) }; })}/></label></div>
        <h4 className="panel-subheading">Snapping</h4>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={snapToPage} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('snapToPage', event.target.checked)}/>Snap to page</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={snapToGuides} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('snapToGuides', event.target.checked)}/>Snap to guides</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={snapToObjects} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('snapToObjects', event.target.checked)}/>Snap to objects</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={snapToGrid} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('snapToGrid', event.target.checked)}/>Snap to grid</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={snapToMargins} onChange={event => setWorkspacePreference('snapToMargins', event.target.checked)}/>Snap to margins</label>
        <p className="help">Hold Alt/Option while dragging to temporarily bypass snapping.</p>
      </>}
 
      {tab === 'data' && <>
        <h3>Data-driven design</h3>
        <DataMergePanel/>
      </>}
 
      {tab === 'templates' && <>
        <div className="panel-heading"><h3>Template library</h3><button title="New template folder" disabled={!canEdit} onClick={async () => { const name = prompt('Template folder name'); if (name) { await api.createTemplateFolder(name); await refresh(); } }}><FolderPlus size={16}/></button></div>
        <input className="search-input" placeholder="Search templates" value={query} onChange={event => setQuery(event.target.value)}/>
        <select value={templateFolder} onChange={event => setTemplateFolder(event.target.value)}><option value="">All template folders</option>{templateFolders.map(item => <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>)}</select>
        <div className="template-list">{filteredTemplates.map(template => <div className="template-card" key={template.id}>
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => confirm('Replace the current design with this template?') && applyTemplate(template.id)}><div className="template-preview">{template.category}</div><strong>{template.title}</strong><small>{(template.tags || []).join(' · ')}</small></button>
          <div className="template-card-actions">{canEdit && <button className="mini" onClick={async () => { const rawPrice = prompt('Credit price (0 for free)', '0'); if (rawPrice == null) return; const priceCredits = Math.max(0, Number(rawPrice) || 0); try { await publishTemplate(template.id, { title: template.title, description: template.description || '', priceType: priceCredits ? 'credits' : 'free', priceCredits, tags: template.tags || [] }); notify('Template marketplace listing created.', 'success'); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }}>Publish</button>}{canEdit && template.visibility !== 'public' && <button className="danger mini" onClick={async () => { await api.deleteTemplate(template.id); await refresh(); }}>Delete</button>}</div>
        </div>)}</div>
      </>}

      {tab === 'components' && <>
        <div className="panel-heading"><h3>Reusable components</h3><button disabled={!canEdit || !selection.length} onClick={async () => { const title = prompt('Component name', 'New component'); if (title) await saveComponent({ title, category: 'Custom', linked: confirm('Create as linked component?') }); }}><Plus size={16}/></button></div>
        <p className="help">Linked components can synchronize changes to every saved design that uses them.</p>
        <div className="component-list">{components.map(component => <div key={component.id}>
          <button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => insertComponent(component)}><Box size={18}/><span><strong>{component.title}</strong><small>{component.linked ? 'Linked' : 'Detached'} · {component.elements.length} elements</small></span></button>
          {canEdit && component.linked && <button className="mini" disabled={!selection.length} title="Replace master from selection and sync linked instances" onClick={async () => { if (confirm('Replace this master component from the current selection and synchronize linked instances?')) { const item = await updateComponent(component); notify(`Updated component and synchronized ${item.changedDesigns || 0} design${item.changedDesigns === 1 ? '' : 's'}.`, 'success'); } }}>Update</button>}
          {canEdit && <button className="danger mini" onClick={async () => { await api.deleteComponent(component.id); await refresh(); }}>×</button>}
        </div>)}</div>
      </>}

      {tab === 'brand' && <>
        <div className="panel-heading"><h3>Brand kits</h3>{canAdmin && <button onClick={async () => { const title = prompt('Brand kit name'); if (title) await createBrand({ title, colors: ['#111827', '#4f46e5', '#f59e0b', '#ffffff'], fonts: ['Arial', 'Georgia'], logos: [], textStyles: [] }); }}><Plus size={16}/></button>}</div>
        {brands.map(brand => <article className="brand-card" key={brand.id}>
          <strong>{brand.title}</strong>
          <div className="swatches">{brand.colors.map(color => <span key={color} style={{ background: color }} title={color}/>)}</div>
          <small>{brand.fonts.join(' · ')}</small>
          {!!brand.logos?.length && <small>{brand.logos.length} logo{brand.logos.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} · {brand.textStyles?.length || 0} text style{brand.textStyles?.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}</small>}
          <div className="button-row"><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => applyBrand(brand, { colors: true, fonts: true })}>Apply all</button><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => applyBrand(brand, { colors: true, fonts: false })}>Colours</button><button disabled={!canEdit} onClick={() => applyBrand(brand, { colors: false, fonts: true })}>Fonts</button></div>
          {selection.length > 0 && <div className="swatches editable">{brand.colors.map(color => <button disabled={!canEdit} key={color} style={{ background: color }} onClick={() => updateElements(selection, item => { const appearance = normalizeAppearance(item); const fills = appearance.fills.map((layer, index) => index === 0 ? { ...layer, enabled: true, paint: solidPaint(color) } : layer); return { fill: color, appearance: { ...appearance, fills, fill: fills[0].paint } }; })}/>)}</div>}
          {canAdmin && <div className="stack-buttons compact"><button onClick={() => editBrand(brand)}>Edit kit</button><button onClick={() => addLogoToBrand(brand)} disabled={!selectedAsset}>Add selected asset as logo</button><button onClick={() => addTextStyleToBrand(brand)} disabled={selectedElement?.type !== 'text'}>Save selected text style</button><button className="danger" onClick={async () => { if (confirm(`Delete brand kit "${brand.title}"?`)) { await api.deleteBrandKit(brand.id); await refresh(); } }}>Delete kit</button></div>}
        </article>)}
      </>}
    </div>
    {commonsAsset && <CommonsPublishDialog onClose={() => setCommonsAsset(null)} editorRef={editorRef} sourceAsset={commonsAsset} selectedElements={[]}/>}
  </aside>;
}

// FILE: src/components/LLMCommandDialog.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Brush, Clipboard, Code2, ExternalLink, Eye, FileText, Image, Play, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import AIPreviewDialog from './AIPreviewDialog.jsx';
import AIScreenshotAnnotator from './AIScreenshotAnnotator.jsx';
import { copyImageToClipboard } from '../ai/visuals.js';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

const copyText = async value => {
  const text = typeof value === 'string' ? value : JSON.stringify(value, null, 2);
  try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); } catch {
    const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
    textarea.value = text;
    textarea.style.position = 'fixed';
    textarea.style.opacity = '0';
    document.body.appendChild(textarea);
    textarea.select();
    document.execCommand('copy');
    textarea.remove();
  }
};

export default function LLMCommandDialog({ onClose }) {
  const design = useEditorStore(state => state.design);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const preview = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPreview);
  const plan = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPlan);
  const renders = useEditorStore(state => state.aiRenders);
  const render = useEditorStore(state => state.aiRender);
  const annotation = useEditorStore(state => state.aiAnnotation);
  const documentRevision = useEditorStore(state => state.documentRevision);
  const getPackage = useEditorStore(state => state.getAIHandoffPackage);
  const previewText = useEditorStore(state => state.previewLLMText);
  const renderImages = useEditorStore(state => state.renderAIImages);
  const setAnnotation = useEditorStore(state => state.setAIAnnotation);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const [tab, setTab] = useState('prompt');
  const [request, setRequest] = useState('');
  const [scope, setScope] = useState('page');
  const [responseText, setResponseText] = useState('');
  const [showPrompt, setShowPrompt] = useState(false);
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);
  const [visualPreviewOpen, setVisualPreviewOpen] = useState(false);
  const [annotatorOpen, setAnnotatorOpen] = useState(false);
  const [selectedRenderIndex, setSelectedRenderIndex] = useState(0);

  const handoff = useMemo(() => {
    try { return getPackage(request, { scope }); } catch { return null; }
  }, [getPackage, request, scope, renders.length, annotation?.dataUrl, selection, design?.id]);
  const skillsUrl = handoff?.skillsUrl || new URL('skills.md', document.baseURI).href;
  const currentRender = renders[selectedRenderIndex] || render || null;
  const displayedImage = annotation?.revision === documentRevision && annotation?.dataUrl ? annotation.dataUrl : currentRender?.url;

  const copy = async (value, message) => { await copyText(value); notify(message, 'success'); };
  const parsePreview = () => {
    try {
      previewText(responseText, { instruction: request });
      setTab('paste');
      setVisualPreviewOpen(true);
      notify('LLM command response parsed and validated. Review the visual preview before applying.', 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };
  const refreshRender = async () => {
    setBusy(true);
    try {
      const result = await renderImages({ multiplier: 1, scope });
      setSelectedRenderIndex(0);
      notify(`${result.length} fresh screenshot${result.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} ready for the manual handoff.`, 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
    finally { setBusy(false); }
  };
  const copyImage = async () => {
    try { await copyImageToClipboard(displayedImage); notify('Screenshot copied. Paste it into the external chat after the prompt.', 'success'); }
    catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };

  return <Modal title="Manual AI handoff" onClose={onClose} wide>
      <div className="llm-dialog-intro"><Sparkles size={18}/><div><strong>Copy the complete prompt and visual context out, paste safe commands back</strong><p>The direct agent/API tab is hidden. This workflow keeps the external chat manual and requires Design Commons preview approval before changes are applied.</p></div></div>
    <div className="llm-dialog-tabs" role="tablist">
      {[['prompt', '1. Prompt and screenshot'], ['paste', '2. Paste commands']].map(([id, label]) => <button key={id} className={tab === id ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setTab(id)}>{label}</button>)}
    </div>

    {tab === 'prompt' && handoff && <div className="llm-dialog-section">
      <div className="llm-field-grid">
        <label className="field"><span>Request for the LLM</span><textarea rows="5" value={request} onChange={event => setRequest(event.target.value)} placeholder="Improve this design, preserve the current content, follow my screenshot markings, and return Design Commons commands only."/></label>
        <label className="field"><span>Scope</span><select value={scope} onChange={event => setScope(event.target.value)}><option value="page">Current page</option><option value="selection" disabled={!selection.length}>Current selection ({selection.length})</option><option value="document">Whole design</option></select><small>The full prompt includes the matching page/object context.</small></label>
      </div>

      <div className="llm-manual-visual">
        <div className="llm-render-row"><div><Image size={16}/><span>{displayedImage ? 'Copy this image separately and paste it into the chat with the full prompt.' : 'Render the design so the external chat can see it.'}</span></div><div className="button-row wrap"><button disabled={busy} onClick={refreshRender}><Image size={14}/>{busy ? 'Rendering…' : scope === 'document' ? 'Render all pages' : 'Render page'}</button><button disabled={!currentRender?.url} onClick={() => setAnnotatorOpen(true)}><Brush size={14}/>Draw on screenshot</button><button disabled={!displayedImage} onClick={copyImage}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy screenshot</button></div></div>
        {displayedImage && <img className="llm-manual-screenshot" src={displayedImage} alt="Screenshot for external AI"/>}
        {renders.length > 1 && <div className="ai-render-thumbnails">{renders.map((item, index) => <button key={item.jobId || item.url} className={selectedRenderIndex === index ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setSelectedRenderIndex(index)}><img src={item.url}/><span>Page {item.pageIndex + 1}</span></button>)}</div>}
      </div>

      <div className="llm-copy-grid">
        <button className="primary" onClick={() => copy(handoff.prompt, 'Full LLM prompt copied.')}><Clipboard size={15}/>Copy full prompt</button>
        <button onClick={() => copy(handoff.instructions, 'Design Commons instructions copied.')}><FileText size={15}/>Instructions</button>
        <button onClick={() => copy(handoff.context, 'Current design context copied.')}><Code2 size={15}/>Design context</button>
        <button onClick={() => copy({ capabilities: handoff.capabilities, examples: handoff.examples }, 'Command reference copied.')}><Code2 size={15}/>Commands and examples</button>
      </div>
      <div className="llm-resource-row"><span><b>Agent skill:</b> <code>{skillsUrl}</code></span><button onClick={() => copy(skillsUrl, 'SKILLS.md URL copied.')}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy URL</button><button onClick={() => window.open(skillsUrl, '_blank', 'noopener')}><ExternalLink size={14}/>Open</button></div>
      <button className="llm-prompt-toggle" onClick={() => setShowPrompt(value => !value)}>{showPrompt ? 'Hide generated prompt' : 'Review generated prompt'}</button>
      {showPrompt && <textarea className="llm-generated-prompt" readOnly rows="18" value={handoff.prompt}/>}
      <div className="modal-actions"><button className="primary" onClick={() => setTab('paste')}>Continue to paste response</button></div>
    </div>}

    {tab === 'paste' && <div className="llm-dialog-section">
      <div className="llm-paste-help"><Code2 size={17}/><p>Paste the LLM response below. Design Commons extracts the command JSON, validates every operation, renders a visual preview, and waits for your explicit approval.</p></div>
      <label className="field"><span>LLM command response</span><textarea className="llm-response-text" rows="16" value={responseText} onChange={event => setResponseText(event.target.value)} placeholder={'Paste a response containing:\n{\n  "schemaVersion": 1,\n  "baseRevision": 0,\n  "commands": [...]\n}'}/></label>
      <div className="button-row wrap"><button className="primary" disabled={!responseText.trim()} onClick={parsePreview}><Play size={15}/>Parse, validate, and preview</button><button onClick={() => copy(handoff?.prompt || '', 'Full LLM prompt copied again.')}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy prompt again</button></div>
      {plan && preview && <div className="llm-preview-summary">
        <div><b>{plan.commands.length}</b><span>commands</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.added.length}</b><span>added</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.changed.length}</b><span>changed</span></div><div><b>{preview.diff.removed.length}</b><span>removed</span></div>
        <p>{preview.lint.issues.length} design-check finding{preview.lint.issues.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} · {(preview.warnings || []).length} execution warning{(preview.warnings || []).length === 1 ? '' : 's'}</p>
        <div className="modal-actions"><button onClick={() => copy(plan, 'Validated command bundle copied.')}><Clipboard size={14}/>Copy validated JSON</button><button className="primary" onClick={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(true)}><Eye size={15}/>Preview and approve</button></div>
      </div>}
    </div>}
    {visualPreviewOpen && plan && preview && <AIPreviewDialog onClose={() => setVisualPreviewOpen(false)} onApplied={onClose}/>}
    {annotatorOpen && currentRender?.url && <AIScreenshotAnnotator source={currentRender.url} initialActions={annotation?.sourceUrl === currentRender.url ? annotation.actions : []} onClose={() => setAnnotatorOpen(false)} onSave={result => { setAnnotation({ ...result, sourceUrl: currentRender.url, pageIndex: currentRender.pageIndex, revision: documentRevision }); setAnnotatorOpen(false); notify('Annotated screenshot is ready to copy and is described in the full prompt.', 'success'); }}/>}
  </Modal>;
}

// FILE: src/components/MarketplaceDialog.jsx

import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Box, Coins, Download, Image, Search, ShoppingBag, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import Modal from './Modal.jsx';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

export default function MarketplaceDialog({ onClose }) {
  const listings = useEditorStore(state => state.marketplaceListings);
  const load = useEditorStore(state => state.loadMarketplace);
  const acquire = useEditorStore(state => state.acquireMarketplaceListing);
  const summary = useEditorStore(state => state.billingSummary);
  const busy = useEditorStore(state => state.commercialBusy);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [type, setType] = useState('');
  useEffect(() => { load().catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error')); }, []);
  const filtered = useMemo(() => listings.filter(item => (!type || item.listingType === type || item.listing_type === type) && (!query || `${item.title} ${item.description || ''} ${(item.tags || []).join(' ')}`.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase()))), [listings, query, type]);
  const install = async listing => {
    try {
      await acquire(listing.id);
      notify(`${listing.title} was added to this workspace.`, 'success');
    } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); }
  };
  return <Modal title="CanvasForge Design Commons" onClose={onClose} wide className="marketplace-modal">
    <div className="marketplace-hero"><div><span><Sparkles size={17}/>Design Commons</span><h2>Reusable assets and templates from CanvasForge creators</h2><p>Install free items or spend credits. Asset publishers must submit a rights declaration.</p></div><div><Coins size={18}/><b>{Number(summary?.credits?.available || 0).toLocaleString()}</b><span>credits available</span></div></div>
    <div className="marketplace-tools"><label><Search size={15}/><input value={query} onChange={event => setQuery(event.target.value)} placeholder="Search assets and templates"/></label><select value={type} onChange={event => setType(event.target.value)}><option value="">Everything</option><option value="asset">Assets</option><option value="template">Templates</option></select><button disabled={busy} onClick={() => load({ q: query, type })}>{busy ? 'Loading…' : 'Refresh'}</button></div>
    {filtered.length ? <div className="marketplace-grid">{filtered.map(item => {
      const listingType = item.listingType || item.listing_type;
      const priceType = item.priceType || item.price_type || 'free';
      const credits = Number(item.priceCredits ?? item.price_credits ?? 0);
      return <article key={item.id}><div className="marketplace-preview">{item.previewUrl || item.preview_url ? <img src={item.previewUrl || item.preview_url}/> : listingType === 'template' ? <Box size={32}/> : <Image size={32}/>}</div><div className="marketplace-copy"><span className="ui-badge tone-neutral">{listingType}</span><h3>{item.title}</h3><p>{item.description || 'Shared by a CanvasForge creator.'}</p><small>{item.creatorName || item.creator_name || 'Community creator'}{item.licenceId || item.licence_id ? ` · ${item.licenceId || item.licence_id}` : ''}</small>{listingType === 'asset' && <span className="commons-rights-badge">Rights attested</span>}</div><button className="primary" onClick={() => install(item)}><Download size={15}/>{priceType === 'free' || !credits ? 'Install free' : `${credits.toLocaleString()} credits`}</button></article>;
    })}</div> : <div className="dashboard-empty"><ShoppingBag size={24}/><strong>No marketplace items found</strong><p>Try a different search or publish the first item in this category.</p></div>}
  </Modal>;
}
