// FILE: src/components/Modal.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useId, useRef } from 'react';
import { X } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Modal({ title, children, onClose, wide = false, className = '' }) {
  const titleId = useId();
  const modalRef = useRef(null);
  useEffect(() => {
    const previous = document.activeElement;
    const onKeyDown = event => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') onClose?.();
      if (event.key !== 'Tab') return;
      const focusable = [...(modalRef.current?.querySelectorAll('button:not([disabled]), input:not([disabled]), select:not([disabled]), textarea:not([disabled]), [tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])') || [])];
      if (!focusable.length) return;
      const first = focusable[0];
      const last = focusable.at(-1);
      if (event.shiftKey && document.activeElement === first) { event.preventDefault(); last.focus(); }
      else if (!event.shiftKey && document.activeElement === last) { event.preventDefault(); first.focus(); }
    };
    document.addEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => modalRef.current?.querySelector('button, input, select, textarea')?.focus());
    return () => { document.removeEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown); previous?.focus?.(); };
  }, [onClose]);

  return <div className="modal-backdrop" onMouseDown={event => event.target === event.currentTarget && onClose?.()}>
    <section ref={modalRef} role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby={titleId} className={`modal ${wide ? 'wide' : ''} ${className}`.trim()}>
      <header><div><span className="modal-kicker">CanvasForge</span><h2 id={titleId}>{title}</h2></div><button className="icon-button" title="Close dialog" aria-label="Close dialog" onClick={onClose}><X size={18}/></button></header>
      <div className="modal-body">{children}</div>
    </section>
  </div>;
}

================================================================================
// FILE: src/components/PageStrip.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Copy, GripVertical, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { clone, cloneElementTree, defaultRegions, uuid } from '../lib/document.js';
import { paintToCss, solidPaint } from '../lib/appearance.js';

export default function PageStrip({ readOnly = false }) {
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const setPageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.setPageIndex);
  const commit = useEditorStore(state => state.commitDocument);
  const role = useEditorStore(state => state.role);
  const [renaming, setRenaming] = useState(null);
  const [name, setName] = useState('');
  if (!document) return null;
  const editable = !readOnly && ['owner', 'admin', 'designer'].includes(role);
  const mutate = fn => {
    if (!editable) return;
    const doc = clone(document);
    fn(doc);
    commit(doc);
  };
  const add = () => mutate(doc => {
    doc.pages.push({ id: uuid(), name: `Page ${doc.pages.length + 1}`, background: '#ffffff', backgroundPaint: solidPaint('#ffffff'), transparentBackground: false, grid: { enabled: false, size: 20, subdivisions: 1 }, margins: { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 }, guides: { vertical: [], horizontal: [], locked: false }, regions: defaultRegions(doc.width, doc.height), elements: [] });
    setTimeout(() => setPageIndex(doc.pages.length - 1), 0);
  });
  const duplicate = () => mutate(doc => {
    const source = doc.pages[pageIndex];
    const copy = clone(source);
    copy.id = uuid();
    copy.name = `${copy.name} copy`;
    const maps = {};
    copy.elements = cloneElementTree(copy.elements, { maps });
    const copiedGroups = (doc.layoutGroups || []).filter(group => group.pageId === source.id).map(group => ({
      ...clone(group),
      id: maps.layoutMap?.get(group.id) || uuid(),
      pageId: copy.id,
      elementIds: group.elementIds.map(elementId => maps.idMap?.get(elementId)).filter(Boolean)
    }));
    doc.layoutGroups = [...(doc.layoutGroups || []), ...copiedGroups];
    doc.pages.splice(pageIndex + 1, 0, copy);
    setTimeout(() => setPageIndex(pageIndex + 1), 0);
  });
  const remove = () => {
    if (document.pages.length === 1) return;
    mutate(doc => {
      const removedId = doc.pages[pageIndex].id;
      doc.pages.splice(pageIndex, 1);
      doc.layoutGroups = (doc.layoutGroups || []).filter(group => group.pageId !== removedId);
      setTimeout(() => setPageIndex(Math.max(0, pageIndex - 1)), 0);
    });
  };
  const reorder = (from, to) => {
    if (!editable || from === to) return;
    mutate(doc => {
      const [item] = doc.pages.splice(from, 1);
      doc.pages.splice(to, 0, item);
      setTimeout(() => setPageIndex(to), 0);
    });
  };
  const finishRename = index => {
    const value = name.trim();
    if (value) mutate(doc => { doc.pages[index].name = value; });
    setRenaming(null);
  };
  return <footer className="page-strip">
    <div className="page-strip-heading"><strong>Pages</strong><span>{document.pages.length}</span></div>
    {editable && <div className="page-actions"><button onClick={add}><Plus size={15}/>Page</button><button onClick={duplicate}><Copy size={15}/>Duplicate</button><button title={document.pages.length === 1 ? 'A design must contain at least one page.' : 'Delete page'} onClick={remove} disabled={document.pages.length === 1}><Trash2 size={15}/>Delete</button></div>}
    <div className="page-tabs page-thumbnails">{document.pages.map((page, index) => <div role="button" tabIndex={0} key={page.id} draggable={editable && renaming !== index} onDragStart={event => event.dataTransfer.setData('text/page-index', String(index))} onDragOver={event => editable && event.preventDefault()} onDrop={event => reorder(Number(event.dataTransfer.getData('text/page-index')), index)} className={`page-tab-card ${index === pageIndex ? 'active' : ''}`} onClick={() => setPageIndex(index)} onKeyDown={event => { if (!['Enter', ' '].includes(event.key) || renaming === index) return; event.preventDefault(); setPageIndex(index); }}>
      <GripVertical className="page-drag-handle" size={13}/>
      <span className={`page-preview ${page.transparentBackground ? 'transparent' : ''}`} style={{ background: page.transparentBackground ? undefined : paintToCss(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, '#ffffff') }}><b>{index + 1}</b><i>{page.elements?.length || 0}</i></span>
      {renaming === index ? <input autoFocus value={name} onClick={event => event.stopPropagation()} onChange={event => setName(event.target.value)} onBlur={() => finishRename(index)} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur(); if (event.key === 'Escape') setRenaming(null); }}/> : <span className="page-tab-name" onDoubleClick={event => { if (!editable) return; event.stopPropagation(); setRenaming(index); setName(page.name); }}>{page.name}</span>}
    </div>)}</div>
  </footer>;
}

================================================================================
// FILE: src/components/PaintEditor.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Pipette, Plus, RotateCw, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import {
  PATTERN_TYPES, defaultGradientStops, normalizeHex, normalizePaint, paintToCss
} from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { GRADIENT_PRESETS } from '../lib/presets.js';
import { readMigratedStorage, writeStorage } from '../lib/appMeta.js';

const RECENT_KEY = 'recentColors';
const loadRecent = () => {
  try { return JSON.parse(readMigratedStorage(RECENT_KEY) || '[]').filter(value => /^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(value)).slice(0, 12); }
  catch { return []; }
};
const saveRecent = color => {
  const value = normalizeHex(color);
  const recent = [value, ...loadRecent().filter(item => item !== value)].slice(0, 12);
  writeStorage(RECENT_KEY, JSON.stringify(recent));
};

function ColorAlphaControl({ color, opacity = 1, onChange, label = 'Colour', palette = [] }) {
  const [draft, setDraft] = useState(normalizeHex(color));
  const applyColor = next => {
    const value = normalizeHex(next, color || '#000000');
    setDraft(value);
    saveRecent(value);
    onChange({ color: value, opacity });
  };
  const pick = async () => {
    if (!globalThis.EyeDropper) return;
    try { applyColor((await new globalThis.EyeDropper().open()).sRGBHex); } catch {}
  };
  const swatches = [...new Set([...loadRecent(), ...palette])].slice(0, 18);
  return <div className="colour-alpha-control">
    <div className="colour-alpha-row">
      <label className="compact-field"><span>{label}</span><input type="color" value={normalizeHex(color)} onChange={event => applyColor(event.target.value)}/></label>
      <label className="compact-field grow"><span>Hex</span><input value={draft} onChange={event => setDraft(event.target.value)} onBlur={() => applyColor(draft)} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur(); if (event.key === 'Escape') { setDraft(normalizeHex(color)); event.currentTarget.blur(); } }}/></label>
      {globalThis.EyeDropper && <button type="button" className="icon-button paint-eyedropper" title="Pick a colour from the screen" onClick={pick}><Pipette size={15}/></button>}
    </div>
    <label className="paint-range"><span>Alpha {Math.round((opacity ?? 1) * 100)}%</span><input type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={opacity ?? 1} onChange={event => onChange({ color: normalizeHex(color), opacity: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>
    {!!swatches.length && <div className="paint-swatches">{swatches.map(value => <button type="button" key={value} title={value} style={{ background: value }} onClick={() => applyColor(value)}/>)}</div>}
  </div>;
}

function GradientStops({ paint, onChange, palette }) {
  const stops = paint.stops || defaultGradientStops();
  const updateStop = (index, patch) => onChange({ ...paint, stops: stops.map((stop, stopIndex) => stopIndex === index ? { ...stop, ...patch } : stop) });
  const removeStop = index => {
    if (stops.length <= 2) return;
    onChange({ ...paint, stops: stops.filter((_, stopIndex) => stopIndex !== index) });
  };
  const addStop = () => {
    const ordered = [...stops].sort((a, b) => a.offset - b.offset);
    let best = { gap: -1, index: 0 };
    for (let index = 0; index < ordered.length - 1; index++) {
      const gap = ordered[index + 1].offset - ordered[index].offset;
      if (gap > best.gap) best = { gap, index };
    }
    const first = ordered[best.index], second = ordered[best.index + 1];
    onChange({ ...paint, stops: [...stops, { offset: (first.offset + second.offset) / 2, color: first.color, opacity: (first.opacity + second.opacity) / 2 }].sort((a, b) => a.offset - b.offset) });
  };
  const reverse = () => onChange({ ...paint, stops: stops.map(stop => ({ ...stop, offset: 1 - stop.offset })).sort((a, b) => a.offset - b.offset) });
  return <div className="gradient-editor">
    <div className="gradient-track" style={{ background: paintToCss(paint) }}>{stops.map((stop, index) => <button type="button" key={`${index}-${stop.offset}`} style={{ left: `${stop.offset * 100}%`, background: stop.color }} title={`${Math.round(stop.offset * 100)}%`} onClick={() => {}}/>)}</div>
    <div className="paint-inline-actions"><button type="button" onClick={addStop}><Plus size={14}/>Add stop</button><button type="button" onClick={reverse}><RotateCw size={14}/>Reverse</button></div>
    {stops.map((stop, index) => <div className="gradient-stop-card" key={index}>
      <ColorAlphaControl label={`Stop ${index + 1}`} color={stop.color} opacity={stop.opacity} palette={palette} onChange={value => updateStop(index, value)}/>
      <div className="gradient-stop-position"><label><span>Position</span><input type="range" min="0" max="1" step=".01" value={stop.offset} onChange={event => updateStop(index, { offset: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label><b>{Math.round(stop.offset * 100)}%</b><button type="button" title="Remove stop" disabled={stops.length <= 2} onClick={() => removeStop(index)}><Trash2 size={14}/></button></div>
    </div>)}
  </div>;
}

export default function PaintEditor({ label = 'Fill', paint, onChange, allowNone = true, palette = [] }) {
  const value = useMemo(() => normalizePaint(paint), [paint]);
  const changeType = type => {
    if (type === 'none') onChange({ type: 'none' });
    else if (type === 'solid') onChange({ type: 'solid', color: value.type === 'solid' ? value.color : '#4f46e5', opacity: value.type === 'solid' ? value.opacity : 1 });
    else if (type === 'linear') onChange({ type: 'linear', angle: value.angle || 0, stops: value.stops || defaultGradientStops() });
    else if (type === 'radial') onChange({ type: 'radial', centerX: .5, centerY: .5, radius: .7, stops: value.stops || defaultGradientStops() });
    else onChange({ type: 'pattern', pattern: 'stripes', foreground: '#4f46e5', background: '#ffffff', foregroundOpacity: 1, backgroundOpacity: 1, scale: 24, spacing: 12, lineWidth: 4, angle: 45 });
  };
  return <div className="paint-editor">
    <div className="paint-editor-heading"><strong>{label}</strong><span className="paint-preview" style={{ background: paintToCss(value) }}/></div>
    <select value={value.type} onChange={event => changeType(event.target.value)}>
      {allowNone && <option value="none">None / transparent</option>}
      <option value="solid">Solid</option><option value="linear">Linear gradient</option><option value="radial">Radial gradient</option><option value="pattern">Pattern</option>
    </select>
    <details className="gradient-preset-library">
      <summary>Gradient presets ({GRADIENT_PRESETS.length})</summary>
      <div className="filter-presets">{GRADIENT_PRESETS.slice(0, 24).map(preset => <button key={preset.id} onClick={() => onChange(preset.paint)}><span style={{ display:'inline-block', width:16, height:16, borderRadius:4, background: paintToCss(preset.paint), marginRight:4 }}/>{preset.name}</button>)}</div>
    </details>
    {value.type === 'solid' && <ColorAlphaControl color={value.color} opacity={value.opacity} palette={palette} onChange={next => onChange({ ...value, ...next })}/>}
    {['linear', 'radial'].includes(value.type) && <>
      {value.type === 'linear' && <label className="paint-range"><span>Angle {Math.round(value.angle)}°</span><input type="range" min="-180" max="180" step="1" value={value.angle} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, angle: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>}
      {value.type === 'radial' && <div className="field-grid"><label className="compact-field"><span>Centre X</span><input type="number" min="0" max="100" value={Math.round(value.centerX * 100)} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, centerX: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(event.target.value) / 100)) })}/></label><label className="compact-field"><span>Centre Y</span><input type="number" min="0" max="100" value={Math.round(value.centerY * 100)} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, centerY: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(event.target.value) / 100)) })}/></label><label className="compact-field"><span>Radius</span><input type="number" min="5" max="200" value={Math.round(value.radius * 100)} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, radius: Math.max(.05, Math.min(2, Number(event.target.value) / 100)) })}/></label></div>}
      <GradientStops paint={value} palette={palette} onChange={onChange}/>
    </>}
    {value.type === 'pattern' && <>
      <label className="compact-field"><span>Pattern</span><select value={value.pattern} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, pattern: event.target.value })}>{PATTERN_TYPES.map(([id, name]) => <option key={id} value={id}>{name}</option>)}</select></label>
      <ColorAlphaControl label="Foreground" color={value.foreground} opacity={value.foregroundOpacity} palette={palette} onChange={next => onChange({ ...value, foreground: next.color, foregroundOpacity: next.opacity })}/>
      <ColorAlphaControl label="Background" color={value.background} opacity={value.backgroundOpacity} palette={palette} onChange={next => onChange({ ...value, background: next.color, backgroundOpacity: next.opacity })}/>
      <label className="paint-range"><span>Scale {Math.round(value.scale)}px</span><input type="range" min="6" max="160" value={value.scale} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, scale: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>
      <label className="paint-range"><span>Spacing {Math.round(value.spacing)}px</span><input type="range" min="2" max="100" value={value.spacing} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, spacing: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>
      <label className="paint-range"><span>Line / dot size {Math.round(value.lineWidth)}px</span><input type="range" min="1" max="40" value={value.lineWidth} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, lineWidth: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>
      {['stripes', 'crosshatch', 'zigzag'].includes(value.pattern) && <label className="paint-range"><span>Angle {Math.round(value.angle)}°</span><input type="range" min="-180" max="180" value={value.angle} onChange={event => onChange({ ...value, angle: Number(event.target.value) })}/></label>}
    </>}
  </div>;
}

================================================================================
// FILE: src/components/PresetBrowser.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { Check, Download, Heart, Plus, Search, Trash2, Upload, X } from 'lucide-react';
import {
  colorWithOpacity, normalizeAppearance, paintToCss
} from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { APP_SLUG, readMigratedStorage, writeStorage } from '../lib/appMeta.js';

const FAVOURITES_KEY = 'presetFavourites';
const RECENTS_KEY = 'presetRecents';

const readIds = key => {
  try {
    const value = JSON.parse(readMigratedStorage(key, '[]') || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(value) ? value.filter(Boolean).slice(0, 30) : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
};

const writeIds = (key, ids) => writeStorage(key, JSON.stringify(ids));

function previewStyle(appearance) {
  const value = normalizeAppearance({ appearance });
  const stroke = value.stroke;
  const shadow = value.shadow;
  return {
    background: paintToCss(value.fill, '#f8fafc'),
    borderColor: stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : 'transparent',
    borderWidth: stroke.enabled ? `${Math.max(1, Math.min(8, stroke.width))}px` : '1px',
    borderStyle: stroke.enabled && stroke.style !== 'solid' ? (stroke.style === 'dotted' ? 'dotted' : 'dashed') : 'solid',
    boxShadow: shadow.enabled
      ? `${Math.max(-16, Math.min(16, shadow.offsetX))}px ${Math.max(-16, Math.min(16, shadow.offsetY))}px ${Math.max(0, Math.min(36, shadow.blur))}px ${colorWithOpacity(shadow.color, shadow.opacity)}`
      : '0 10px 28px rgba(15, 23, 42, .08)',
    mixBlendMode: value.blendMode === 'source-over' ? 'normal' : value.blendMode
  };
}

function PresetCard({ preset, favourite, onFavourite, onApply, onDelete }) {
  return <article className="preset-browser-card">
    <button
      type="button"
      className="preset-browser-card-main"
      onClick={() => onApply(preset)}
      title={`Apply ${preset.name}`}
    >
      <span className="preset-browser-preview-wrap">
        <span className="preset-browser-preview-grid"/>
        <span className="preset-browser-preview" style={previewStyle(preset.appearance)}>
          <span className="preset-browser-preview-title">Aa</span>
          <span className="preset-browser-preview-pill"/>
        </span>
        <span className="preset-browser-apply"><Check size={14}/>Apply</span>
      </span>
      <span className="preset-browser-card-copy">
        <strong>{preset.name}</strong>
        <small>{preset.category || 'Featured'}</small>
      </span>
    </button>
    <button
      type="button"
      className={`preset-browser-favourite ${favourite ? 'active' : ''}`}
      aria-label={favourite ? `Remove ${preset.name} from favourites` : `Add ${preset.name} to favourites`}
      title={favourite ? 'Remove from favourites' : 'Add to favourites'}
      onClick={() => onFavourite(preset.id)}
    ><Heart size={16} fill={favourite ? 'currentColor' : 'none'}/></button>
    {preset.custom && <button
      type="button"
      className="preset-browser-delete"
      aria-label={`Delete ${preset.name}`}
      title="Delete custom preset"
      onClick={() => onDelete(preset.id)}
    ><Trash2 size={15}/></button>}
  </article>;
}

export default function PresetBrowser({ presets, currentAppearance, onApply, onSave, onImport, onDelete, onClose }) {
  const searchRef = useRef(null);
  const importRef = useRef(null);
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [category, setCategory] = useState('all');
  const [scope, setScope] = useState('all');
  const [favourites, setFavourites] = useState(() => readIds(FAVOURITES_KEY));
  const [recents, setRecents] = useState(() => readIds(RECENTS_KEY));
  const [saveOpen, setSaveOpen] = useState(false);
  const [saveName, setSaveName] = useState('');
  const [importError, setImportError] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => searchRef.current?.focus(), 40);
    const onKeyDown = event => event.key === 'Escape' && onClose();
    window.addEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown);
    return () => {
      clearTimeout(timer);
      window.removeEventListener('keydown', onKeyDown);
    };
  }, [onClose]);

  const categories = useMemo(() => [...new Set(presets.map(preset => preset.category || 'Featured'))].sort(), [presets]);
  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    const normalizedQuery = query.trim().toLowerCase();
    return presets.filter(preset => {
      if (category !== 'all' && (preset.category || 'Featured') !== category) return false;
      if (scope === 'favourites' && !favourites.includes(preset.id)) return false;
      if (scope === 'recent' && !recents.includes(preset.id)) return false;
      if (!normalizedQuery) return true;
      return `${preset.name} ${preset.category || ''}`.toLowerCase().includes(normalizedQuery);
    }).sort((a, b) => {
      if (scope === 'recent') return recents.indexOf(a.id) - recents.indexOf(b.id);
      return Number(!!b.custom) - Number(!!a.custom) || a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
    });
  }, [presets, category, scope, favourites, recents, query]);

  const toggleFavourite = id => {
    const next = favourites.includes(id) ? favourites.filter(item => item !== id) : [id, ...favourites];
    setFavourites(next);
    writeIds(FAVOURITES_KEY, next);
  };

  const apply = preset => {
    const next = [preset.id, ...recents.filter(id => id !== preset.id)].slice(0, 20);
    setRecents(next);
    writeIds(RECENTS_KEY, next);
    onApply(preset.appearance);
  };

  const saveCurrent = () => {
    const name = saveName.trim();
    if (!name) return;
    onSave(name, currentAppearance);
    setSaveName('');
    setSaveOpen(false);
  };

  const importFile = async event => {
    const file = event.target.files?.[0];
    event.target.value = '';
    if (!file) return;
    setImportError('');
    try {
      const parsed = JSON.parse(await file.text());
      const source = Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : parsed?.presets;
      if (!Array.isArray(source)) throw new Error('The file does not contain a presets array.');
      const imported = source.filter(item => item && typeof item.name === 'string' && item.appearance && typeof item.appearance === 'object');
      if (!imported.length) throw new Error('No valid appearance presets were found.');
      onImport(imported);
    } catch (error) {
      setImportError(error.message || 'The preset file could not be imported.');
    }
  };

  const customPresets = presets.filter(preset => preset.custom);
  const exportPresets = () => {
    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify({ schemaVersion: 1, presets: customPresets.map(({ id, name, category, appearance }) => ({ id, name, category, appearance })) }, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const anchor = document.createElement('a');
    anchor.href = url;
    anchor.download = `${APP_SLUG}-appearance-presets.json`;
    anchor.click();
    setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 1000);
  };

  return <div className="preset-browser-backdrop" onMouseDown={event => event.target === event.currentTarget && onClose()}>
    <section className="preset-browser" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="preset-browser-title">
      <header className="preset-browser-header">
        <div>
          <h2 id="preset-browser-title">Appearance presets</h2>
          <p>Apply a reusable fill, border, shadow, and blend-mode combination.</p>
        </div>
        <button type="button" className="preset-browser-close" aria-label="Close preset browser" onClick={onClose}><X size={20}/></button>
      </header>

      <div className="preset-browser-controls">
        <label className="preset-browser-search"><Search size={19}/><input ref={searchRef} value={query} onChange={event => setQuery(event.target.value)} placeholder="Search presets"/></label>
        <select value={category} onChange={event => setCategory(event.target.value)} aria-label="Filter by category">
          <option value="all">All categories</option>
          {categories.map(value => <option key={value} value={value}>{value}</option>)}
        </select>
        <div className="preset-browser-tabs" role="tablist" aria-label="Preset filters">
          {[['all', 'All'], ['favourites', 'Favourites'], ['recent', 'Recent']].map(([id, label]) => <button key={id} type="button" role="tab" aria-selected={scope === id} className={scope === id ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => setScope(id)}>{label}</button>)}
        </div>
        <span className="preset-browser-count">{filtered.length} {filtered.length === 1 ? 'preset' : 'presets'}</span>
      </div>

      <div className="preset-browser-content">
        {filtered.length ? <div className="preset-browser-grid">{filtered.map(preset => <PresetCard
          key={preset.id}
          preset={preset}
          favourite={favourites.includes(preset.id)}
          onFavourite={toggleFavourite}
          onApply={apply}
          onDelete={onDelete}
        />)}</div> : <div className="preset-browser-empty">
          <span><Search size={26}/></span>
          <h3>No matching presets</h3>
          <p>Try another search, category, or preset filter.</p>
          <button type="button" onClick={() => { setQuery(''); setCategory('all'); setScope('all'); }}>Clear filters</button>
        </div>}
      </div>

      <footer className="preset-browser-footer">
        <div className="preset-browser-footer-primary">
          {!saveOpen ? <button type="button" onClick={() => setSaveOpen(true)}><Plus size={17}/>Save current</button> : <div className="preset-browser-save-form">
            <input autoFocus value={saveName} onChange={event => setSaveName(event.target.value)} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') saveCurrent(); if (event.key === 'Escape') setSaveOpen(false); }} placeholder="Preset name"/>
            <button type="button" className="primary" disabled={!saveName.trim()} onClick={saveCurrent}>Save</button>
            <button type="button" onClick={() => { setSaveOpen(false); setSaveName(''); }}>Cancel</button>
          </div>}
          {importError && <span className="preset-browser-error">{importError}</span>}
        </div>
        <div className="preset-browser-footer-actions">
          <button type="button" onClick={() => importRef.current?.click()}><Upload size={17}/>Import</button>
          <button type="button" disabled={!customPresets.length} onClick={exportPresets}><Download size={17}/>Export</button>
          <input ref={importRef} hidden type="file" accept="application/json,.json" onChange={importFile}/>
        </div>
      </footer>
    </section>
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/PreviewCanvas.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useLayoutEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { StaticCanvas } from 'fabric';
import { elementToObject, paintToFabric } from '../lib/fabricAdapter.js';
import { ensureFontsLoaded } from '../lib/fonts.js';

const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));

export default function PreviewCanvas({ document, pageIndex = 0, showReference = false, referenceMode = null, referenceOpacity = null, referenceSplit = null }) {
  const hostRef = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  const [scale, setScale] = useState(.5);
  const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex] || document?.pages?.[0];

  useLayoutEffect(() => {
    const host = hostRef.current;
    if (!host || !document) return;
    const update = () => {
      const rect = host.getBoundingClientRect();
      const availableWidth = Math.max(180, rect.width - 28);
      const availableHeight = Math.max(240, rect.height - 28);
      setScale(clamp(Math.min(availableWidth / document.width, availableHeight / document.height), .08, 1));
    };
    update();
    const observer = new ResizeObserver(update);
    observer.observe(host);
    return () => observer.disconnect();
  }, [document?.width, document?.height]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!canvasRef.current || !document || !page) return;
    let cancelled = false;
    const canvas = new StaticCanvas(canvasRef.current, {
      selection: false,
      renderOnAddRemove: false,
      enableRetinaScaling: false
    });
    const render = async () => {
      const fonts = (page.elements || []).flatMap(element => element.type === 'text'
        ? [element.fontFamily]
        : ['chart', 'table'].includes(element.type) ? [element.options?.fontFamily] : []).filter(Boolean);
      await ensureFontsLoaded(fonts);
      if (cancelled) return;
      canvas.setDimensions({
        width: Math.max(1, Math.round(document.width * scale)),
        height: Math.max(1, Math.round(document.height * scale))
      });
      canvas.setZoom(scale);
      canvas.backgroundColor = page.transparentBackground
        ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0)'
        : paintToFabric(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, document.width, document.height, '#ffffff');
      for (const element of [...(page.elements || [])].sort((a, b) => (a.zIndex || 0) - (b.zIndex || 0))) {
        if (cancelled || element.hidden) continue;
        try {
          const object = await elementToObject(element);
          object.set({ selectable: false, evented: false, hasControls: false, hasBorders: false });
          canvas.add(object);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Failed to render preview element', element, error);
        }
      }
      canvas.requestRenderAll();
    };
    render();
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
      canvas.dispose();
    };
  }, [document, pageIndex, page, scale]);

  if (!document || !page) return <div className="ai-preview-empty">No preview is available.</div>;
  const reference = page.referenceImage;
  const mode = referenceMode || reference?.mode || 'overlay';
  const opacity = referenceOpacity ?? reference?.opacity ?? .45;
  const split = referenceSplit ?? reference?.split ?? .5;
  const referenceStyle = reference ? {
    opacity,
    objectFit: reference.fit === 'stretch' ? 'fill' : (reference.fit || 'contain'),
    mixBlendMode: mode === 'difference' ? 'difference' : 'normal',
    clipPath: mode === 'split' ? `inset(0 ${Math.max(0, 100 - split * 100)}% 0 0)` : 'none'
  } : null;
  return <div ref={hostRef} className={`ai-preview-canvas-host ${page.transparentBackground ? 'transparent' : ''}`}>
    <div className="ai-preview-canvas-frame" style={{ width: document.width * scale, height: document.height * scale }}>
      <canvas ref={canvasRef}/>
      {showReference && reference?.src && <><img className={`ai-preview-reference mode-${mode}`} src={reference.src} alt={reference.name || 'Reference image'} style={referenceStyle}/>{mode === 'split' && <div className="ai-preview-reference-divider" style={{ left: `${split * 100}%` }}/>}</>}
    </div>
  </div>;
}

import React from 'react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';

const NumberField = ({ label, value, onChange, min = 0, max = 500 }) => <label className="field"><span>{label}</span><input type="number" min={min} max={max} value={value ?? 0} onChange={event => onChange(Number(event.target.value) || 0)}/></label>;

export default function PrintPanel() {
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const updatePrint = useEditorStore(state => state.updatePrintSettings);
  const print = document.print || {};
  const patchInset = (key, side, value) => updatePrint({ [key]: { ...(print[key] || {}), [side]: value } });
  return <div className="print-panel">
    <div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Colour space</span><select value={print.colorSpace || 'rgb'} onChange={event => updatePrint({ colorSpace: event.target.value })}><option value="rgb">RGB</option><option value="cmyk">CMYK</option><option value="spot">Spot colour</option></select></label><label className="field"><span>PDF preset</span><select value={print.pdfPreset || 'screen'} onChange={event => updatePrint({ pdfPreset: event.target.value })}><option value="screen">Screen</option><option value="print">High-quality print</option><option value="pdf-x-1a">PDF/X-1a</option><option value="pdf-x-3">PDF/X-3</option><option value="pdf-x-4">PDF/X-4</option></select></label></div>
    <label className="field"><span>ICC profile</span><input value={print.iccProfile || ''} onChange={event => updatePrint({ iccProfile: event.target.value })}/></label>
    <h4 className="panel-subheading">Bleed</h4><div className="field-grid four">{['top','right','bottom','left'].map(side => <NumberField key={side} label={side} value={print.bleed?.[side]} onChange={value => patchInset('bleed', side, value)}/>)}</div>
    <h4 className="panel-subheading">Safe area</h4><div className="field-grid four">{['top','right','bottom','left'].map(side => <NumberField key={side} label={side} value={print.safeArea?.[side]} onChange={value => patchInset('safeArea', side, value)}/>)}</div>
    <h4 className="panel-subheading">Slug</h4><div className="field-grid four">{['top','right','bottom','left'].map(side => <NumberField key={side} label={side} value={print.slug?.[side]} onChange={value => patchInset('slug', side, value)}/>)}</div>
    <div className="print-checks"><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.marks?.crop} onChange={event => updatePrint({ marks: { ...(print.marks || {}), crop: event.target.checked } })}/>Crop marks</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.marks?.registration} onChange={event => updatePrint({ marks: { ...(print.marks || {}), registration: event.target.checked } })}/>Registration marks</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.marks?.colorBars} onChange={event => updatePrint({ marks: { ...(print.marks || {}), colorBars: event.target.checked } })}/>Colour bars</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.marks?.pageInformation} onChange={event => updatePrint({ marks: { ...(print.marks || {}), pageInformation: event.target.checked } })}/>Page information</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={print.embedFonts !== false} onChange={event => updatePrint({ embedFonts: event.target.checked })}/>Embed fonts</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.outlineFonts} onChange={event => updatePrint({ outlineFonts: event.target.checked })}/>Outline fonts</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.flattenTransparency} onChange={event => updatePrint({ flattenTransparency: event.target.checked })}/>Flatten transparency</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!print.overprintPreview} onChange={event => updatePrint({ overprintPreview: event.target.checked })}/>Overprint preview</label></div>
    <NumberField label="Minimum effective image DPI" min={36} max={2400} value={print.minimumEffectiveDpi || 150} onChange={minimumEffectiveDpi => updatePrint({ minimumEffectiveDpi })}/>
  </div>;
}

// FILE: src/components/RightPanel.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import {
  AlignCenter, AlignLeft, AlignRight, Bold, ChevronRight, Crop, EyeOff, FlipHorizontal2,
  FlipVertical2, Italic, Link, List, ListOrdered, Lock, Minus, Plus,
  RotateCcw, Share2, Strikethrough, Subscript, Superscript, Underline
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import PaintEditor from './PaintEditor.jsx';
import AppearancePanel from './AppearancePanel.jsx';
import DesignSystemPanel from './DesignSystemPanel.jsx';
import PrintPanel from './PrintPanel.jsx';
import CommonsPublishDialog from './CommonsPublishDialog.jsx';
import { collectDocumentColors, paintPrimaryColor, paintToCss } from '../lib/appearance.js';
import { IMAGE_PRESETS, TEXT_PRESETS, scaleAppearancePreset, scaleImageFilters } from '../lib/presets.js';
import { FONT_CATEGORIES, ensureFontLoaded, getFontLoadReport } from '../lib/fonts.js';
import { inspectSvgMarkup, sanitizeSvgMarkup } from '../lib/svg.js';

const Field = ({ label, children }) => <label className="field"><span>{label}</span>{children}</label>;


function SvgSourceEditor({ element, onApply, notify }) {
  const [draft, setDraft] = useState(element.svg || '');
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const inspection = inspectSvgMarkup(draft);
  useEffect(() => { setDraft(element.svg || ''); setError(''); }, [element.id, element.svg]);
  const apply = () => {
    try {
      const svg = sanitizeSvgMarkup(draft);
      onApply({ svg });
      setDraft(svg);
      setError('');
      notify('Custom SVG updated.', 'success');
    } catch (nextError) {
      setError(nextError.message);
    }
  };
  return <>
    <p className="help">Paste a complete SVG document or a single SVG path beginning with M/m. Scripts, event handlers, embedded HTML, and external resources are removed.</p>
    <textarea className="data-editor" rows="12" value={draft} onChange={event => setDraft(event.target.value)} spellCheck="false"/>
    {error && <p className="error">{error}</p>}
    {!error && inspection.issues.length > 0 && <div className="svg-diagnostics">{inspection.issues.map((issue, index) => <small key={index}>{issue}</small>)}</div>}
    <div className="button-row"><button className="primary" onClick={apply}>Apply SVG</button><button onClick={() => setDraft(element.svg || '')}>Reset</button></div>
    <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={element.preserveAspectRatio !== false} onChange={event => onApply({ preserveAspectRatio: event.target.checked })}/>Preserve aspect ratio</label>
  </>;
}

function NumberField({ label, value, onChange, min, max, step = 1, disabled = false }) {
  const format = input => Number.isFinite(input) ? String(Math.round(input * 100) / 100) : '';
  const [draft, setDraft] = useState(format(value));
  const [invalid, setInvalid] = useState(false);
  useEffect(() => setDraft(format(value)), [value]);
  const commit = () => {
    if (draft.trim() === '') { setDraft(format(value)); setInvalid(false); return; }
    let next = Number(draft);
    if (!Number.isFinite(next)) { setInvalid(true); return; }
    if (Number.isFinite(min)) next = Math.max(min, next);
    if (Number.isFinite(max)) next = Math.min(max, next);
    setInvalid(false);
    setDraft(format(next));
    onChange(next);
  };
  return <Field label={label}><input className={invalid ? 'invalid' : ''} disabled={disabled} type="number" value={draft} min={min} max={max} step={step} placeholder={Number.isFinite(value) ? '' : 'Mixed'} onChange={event => { setDraft(event.target.value); setInvalid(false); }} onBlur={commit} onKeyDown={event => {
    if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur();
    if (event.key === 'Escape') { setDraft(format(value)); setInvalid(false); event.currentTarget.blur(); }
  }}/></Field>;
}


function HexField({ value, onChange, disabled = false }) {
  const [draft, setDraft] = useState(value || '#ffffff');
  const [invalid, setInvalid] = useState(false);
  useEffect(() => setDraft(value || '#ffffff'), [value]);
  const commit = () => {
    if (/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(draft)) { setInvalid(false); onChange(draft); }
    else { setInvalid(true); setDraft(value || '#ffffff'); }
  };
  return <Field label="Hex"><input disabled={disabled} className={invalid ? 'invalid' : ''} value={draft} onChange={event => { setDraft(event.target.value); setInvalid(false); }} onBlur={commit} onKeyDown={event => { if (event.key === 'Enter') event.currentTarget.blur(); if (event.key === 'Escape') { setDraft(value || '#ffffff'); event.currentTarget.blur(); } }}/></Field>;
}
function RangeField({ label, value, onChange, min, max, step }) {
  const begin = useEditorStore(state => state.beginHistoryTransaction);
  const commit = useEditorStore(state => state.commitHistoryTransaction);
  const display = Number.isFinite(value) ? Math.round(value * 100) / 100 : 'Mixed';
  return <Field label={`${label} ${display}`}><input type="range" value={Number.isFinite(value) ? value : min} min={min} max={max} step={step} onPointerDown={begin} onPointerUp={commit} onPointerCancel={commit} onChange={event => onChange(Number(event.target.value))}/></Field>;
}

const InspectorSection = ({ title, children, open = true }) => <details className="inspector-section" open={open}><summary><span>{title}</span><ChevronRight className="inspector-chevron" size={15}/></summary><div className="inspector-section-body">{children}</div></details>;
const commonValue = (items, key, fallback) => {
  if (!items.length) return fallback;
  const first = items[0]?.[key];
  return items.every(item => Object.is(item?.[key], first)) ? first : undefined;
};

export default function RightPanel({ editorRef }) {
  const replaceRef = useRef();
  const [layoutGap, setLayoutGap] = useState(24);
  const [layoutAlign, setLayoutAlign] = useState('center');
  const [imagePresetIntensity, setImagePresetIntensity] = useState(1);
  const [textPresetIntensity, setTextPresetIntensity] = useState(1);
  const [fontReport, setFontReport] = useState(null);
  const [commonsOpen, setCommonsOpen] = useState(false);
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const assets = useEditorStore(state => state.assets);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const updateElements = useEditorStore(state => state.updateElements);
  const updatePage = useEditorStore(state => state.updatePage);
  const commitDocument = useEditorStore(state => state.commitDocument);
  const upload = useEditorStore(state => state.upload);
  const createAutoLayout = useEditorStore(state => state.createAutoLayout);
  const detachAutoLayout = useEditorStore(state => state.detachAutoLayout);
  const magicResize = useEditorStore(state => state.magicResize);
  const save = useEditorStore(state => state.save);
  const role = useEditorStore(state => state.role);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex];
  const selected = (page?.elements || []).filter(element => selection.includes(element.id));
  const element = selected[0];
  const canEdit = ['owner', 'admin', 'designer'].includes(role);
  const selectedType = selected.length && selected.every(item => item.type === selected[0].type) ? selected[0].type : null;
  const frameLayout = element?.type === 'frame' ? (element.layout || {}) : {};
  const framePadding = typeof frameLayout.padding === 'number'
    ? { top: frameLayout.padding, right: frameLayout.padding, bottom: frameLayout.padding, left: frameLayout.padding }
    : { top: 32, right: 32, bottom: 32, left: 32, ...(frameLayout.padding || {}) };
  const childSizing = element?.layoutSizing || {};
  const patchFrameLayout = next => patchOne({ layout: { ...frameLayout, ...next } });
  const patchFramePadding = next => patchFrameLayout({ padding: { ...framePadding, ...next } });
  const patch = (values, options) => canEdit && selection.length && updateElements(selection, values, options);
  const patchOne = (values, options) => canEdit && element && updateElements([element.id], values, options);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (element?.type !== 'text' || !element.fontFamily) { setFontReport(null); return; }
    let active = true;
    ensureFontLoaded(element.fontFamily).then(report => { if (active) setFontReport(report); });
    return () => { active = false; };
  }, [element?.id, element?.fontFamily]);
  const applyTextPreset = preset => patch(item => {
    const nextAppearance = scaleAppearancePreset(preset.appearance, textPresetIntensity);
    return {
      ...preset.typography,
      appearance: nextAppearance,
      fill: nextAppearance.fill.type === 'none' ? 'transparent' : paintPrimaryColor(nextAppearance.fill, item.fill || '#111827'),
      stroke: nextAppearance.stroke.enabled ? nextAppearance.stroke.color : 'transparent',
      strokeWidth: nextAppearance.stroke.enabled ? nextAppearance.stroke.width : 0,
      effect: { ...(item.effect || {}), shadow: nextAppearance.shadow.enabled ? { ...nextAppearance.shadow } : null }
    };
  });

  const replaceImage = async event => {
    const file = event.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file || element?.type !== 'image') return;
    try {
      const asset = await upload(file);
      patchOne({ src: asset.preview_url || asset.url, assetId: asset.id, nativeWidth: asset.width || 1000, nativeHeight: asset.height || 1000, cropX: null, cropY: null, cropZoom: 1 });
    } catch (error) {
      notify(`Image replacement failed: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
    event.target.value = '';
  };

  if (!element) {
    const updateDocument = values => {
      const next = structuredClone(document);
      Object.assign(next, values);
      commitDocument(next);
    };
    return <aside className="right-panel">
      <InspectorSection title="Page">
        <label className="check"><input disabled={!canEdit} type="checkbox" checked={!!page?.transparentBackground} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.transparentBackground = event.target.checked; })}/>Transparent background</label>
        {!page?.transparentBackground ? <PaintEditor label="Page background" paint={page?.backgroundPaint ?? page?.background} palette={collectDocumentColors(document)} allowNone={false} onChange={backgroundPaint => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.backgroundPaint = backgroundPaint; currentPage.background = paintPrimaryColor(backgroundPaint, currentPage.background || '#ffffff'); })}/> : <p className="help">The page is transparent. Turn off transparency to edit its colour, gradient, or pattern.</p>}
        <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Width" value={document.width} min={1} disabled/><NumberField label="Height" value={document.height} min={1} disabled/></div>
        <button className="full" disabled={!canEdit} onClick={async () => { try { await save({ createVersion: true, versionLabel: `Before orientation swap to ${document.height}×${document.width}` }); magicResize(document.height, document.width); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }}>Swap orientation</button>
        <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Unit"><select disabled={!canEdit} value={document.unit || 'px'} onChange={event => updateDocument({ unit: event.target.value })}><option value="px">Pixels</option><option value="in">Inches</option><option value="cm">Centimetres</option><option value="mm">Millimetres</option><option value="pt">Points</option></select></Field><NumberField label="DPI" value={document.dpi || 96} min={36} max={1200} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={dpi => updateDocument({ dpi })}/></div>
      </InspectorSection>
      <InspectorSection title="Grid and margins" open={false}>
        <label className="check"><input disabled={!canEdit} type="checkbox" checked={!!page?.grid?.enabled} onChange={event => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.grid = { ...(currentPage.grid || {}), enabled: event.target.checked }; })}/>Show grid</label>
        <NumberField label="Grid size" value={page?.grid?.size || 20} min={4} max={200} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={size => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.grid = { ...(currentPage.grid || {}), size }; })}/>
        <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Top" value={page?.margins?.top || 0} min={0} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={top => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), top }; })}/><NumberField label="Right" value={page?.margins?.right || 0} min={0} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={right => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), right }; })}/><NumberField label="Bottom" value={page?.margins?.bottom || 0} min={0} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={bottom => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), bottom }; })}/><NumberField label="Left" value={page?.margins?.left || 0} min={0} disabled={!canEdit} onChange={left => updatePage(currentPage => { currentPage.margins = { ...(currentPage.margins || {}), left }; })}/></div>
      </InspectorSection>
      <InspectorSection title="Design system" open={false}><DesignSystemPanel/></InspectorSection>
      <InspectorSection title="Print production" open={false}><PrintPanel/></InspectorSection>
      <p className="help inspector-empty-help">Select an object to edit its position, size, appearance, and content. Drag from a ruler to add a guide.</p>
    </aside>;
  }

  const effect = element.effect || {};
  const imageFilters = element.filters || {};
  const constraints = element.constraints || {};
  const transformValues = {
    x: commonValue(selected, 'x'), y: commonValue(selected, 'y'), width: commonValue(selected, 'width'), height: commonValue(selected, 'height'),
    rotation: commonValue(selected, 'rotation'), opacity: commonValue(selected, 'opacity')
  };
  const allLocked = selected.every(item => item.locked);
  const allHidden = selected.every(item => item.hidden);
  const allAspect = selected.every(item => item.constraints?.maintainAspectRatio);
  const selectedSourceAsset = selected.length === 1 && selected[0].type === 'image' && selected[0].assetId ? assets.find(asset => asset.id === selected[0].assetId) || null : null;

  return <aside className="right-panel">
    {selected.length > 1 && <div className="multi-selection-banner"><strong>{selected.length} elements selected</strong><span>Blank fields contain mixed values.</span></div>}
    <button className="commons-quick-publish" disabled={!canEdit || !selected.length} onClick={() => setCommonsOpen(true)}><Share2 size={16}/><span><strong>Share to Design Commons</strong><small>Publish this selected object or group for other creators.</small></span></button>
    <InspectorSection title="Transform">
      <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="X" value={transformValues.x} onChange={x => patch({ x })}/><NumberField label="Y" value={transformValues.y} onChange={y => patch({ y })}/><NumberField label="W" value={transformValues.width} min={1} onChange={width => patch({ width })}/><NumberField label="H" value={transformValues.height} min={1} onChange={height => patch({ height })}/></div>
      <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Rotate" value={transformValues.rotation} onChange={rotation => patch({ rotation })}/><NumberField label="Opacity" value={transformValues.opacity} min={0} max={1} step={.05} onChange={opacity => patch({ opacity: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, opacity)) })}/></div>
      <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={allAspect} onChange={event => patch(elementItem => ({ constraints: { ...(elementItem.constraints || {}), maintainAspectRatio: event.target.checked } }))}/>Lock aspect ratio</label>
      <div className="icon-row"><button title="Flip horizontally" onClick={() => patch(item => ({ flipX: !item.flipX }))}><FlipHorizontal2 size={16}/></button><button title="Flip vertically" onClick={() => patch(item => ({ flipY: !item.flipY }))}><FlipVertical2 size={16}/></button><button title="Reset rotation" onClick={() => patch({ rotation: 0 })}><RotateCcw size={16}/></button><button className={allLocked ? 'active' : ''} title={allLocked ? 'Unlock' : 'Lock'} onClick={() => patch({ locked: !allLocked })}><Lock size={16}/></button><button className={allHidden ? 'active' : ''} title={allHidden ? 'Show' : 'Hide'} onClick={() => patch({ hidden: !allHidden })}><EyeOff size={16}/></button></div>
      {selected.length > 1 && <div className="button-row wrap"><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.matchSize('width')}>Match width</button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.matchSize('height')}>Match height</button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.matchSize('both')}>Match size</button></div>}
    </InspectorSection>

    <InspectorSection title="AI semantics" open={false}>
      <Field label="Semantic role"><select value={element.role || ''} onChange={event => patch({ role: event.target.value })}><option value="">Unspecified</option>{['headline','subheadline','body','caption','price','call-to-action','logo','hero-image','background-image','decoration','legal','chart-title','chart-data','container','item-name','item-description','item-price','badge','divider','footer','header','illustration'].map(roleName => <option key={roleName} value={roleName}>{roleName.replaceAll('-', ' ')}</option>)}</select></Field>
      <Field label="Semantic name"><input value={element.semanticName || ''} onChange={event => patch({ semanticName: event.target.value })} placeholder="Primary offer headline"/></Field>
      <Field label="AI tags"><input value={(element.tags || []).join(', ')} onChange={event => patch({ tags: event.target.value.split(',').map(value => value.trim()).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 50) })} placeholder="offer, promotion, primary"/></Field>
      <Field label="Content key"><input value={element.contentKey || ''} onChange={event => patch({ contentKey: event.target.value })} placeholder="campaign.headline"/></Field>
      <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={element.aiEditable !== false} onChange={event => patch({ aiEditable: event.target.checked })}/>AI may edit this element</label>
      <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.userLocked} onChange={event => patch({ userLocked: event.target.checked })}/>Protect from AI commands</label>
    </InspectorSection>

    <InspectorSection title="Layout and constraints" open={false}>
      <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Horizontal"><select value={constraints.horizontal || 'scale'} onChange={event => patch({ constraints: { ...constraints, horizontal: event.target.value } })}><option value="scale">Scale</option><option value="left">Left</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="right">Right</option><option value="stretch">Stretch</option></select></Field><Field label="Vertical"><select value={constraints.vertical || 'scale'} onChange={event => patch({ constraints: { ...constraints, vertical: event.target.value } })}><option value="scale">Scale</option><option value="top">Top</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="bottom">Bottom</option><option value="stretch">Stretch</option></select></Field></div>
      {selected.length > 1 && <><div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Layout gap" value={layoutGap} min={0} onChange={setLayoutGap}/><Field label="Align"><select value={layoutAlign} onChange={event => setLayoutAlign(event.target.value)}><option value="start">Start</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="end">End</option></select></Field></div><div className="button-row"><button onClick={() => createAutoLayout({ direction: 'horizontal', gap: layoutGap, align: layoutAlign })}>Horizontal auto-layout</button><button onClick={() => createAutoLayout({ direction: 'vertical', gap: layoutGap, align: layoutAlign })}>Vertical auto-layout</button></div></>}
      {element.layoutGroupId && <button className="full" onClick={() => detachAutoLayout(element.layoutGroupId)}>Detach auto-layout</button>}
    </InspectorSection>

    {selectedType === 'frame' && <InspectorSection title="Frame layout">
      <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={frameLayout.enabled !== false} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ enabled: event.target.checked })}/>Enable automatic layout</label>
      <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Direction"><select value={frameLayout.direction || 'vertical'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ direction: event.target.value })}><option value="vertical">Vertical</option><option value="horizontal">Horizontal</option></select></Field><Field label="Wrap"><select value={frameLayout.wrap ? 'wrap' : 'nowrap'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ wrap: event.target.value === 'wrap' })}><option value="nowrap">No wrap</option><option value="wrap">Wrap</option></select></Field></div>
      <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Align"><select value={frameLayout.align || 'start'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ align: event.target.value })}><option value="start">Start</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="end">End</option><option value="stretch">Stretch</option></select></Field><Field label="Justify"><select value={frameLayout.justify || 'start'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ justify: event.target.value })}><option value="start">Start</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="end">End</option><option value="space-between">Space between</option></select></Field></div>
      <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Main gap" value={frameLayout.gap ?? 24} min={0} onChange={gap => patchFrameLayout({ gap })}/><NumberField label="Row gap" value={frameLayout.rowGap ?? frameLayout.gap ?? 24} min={0} onChange={rowGap => patchFrameLayout({ rowGap })}/><NumberField label="Column gap" value={frameLayout.columnGap ?? frameLayout.gap ?? 24} min={0} onChange={columnGap => patchFrameLayout({ columnGap })}/></div>
      <div className="field-grid four"><NumberField label="Pad top" value={framePadding.top} min={0} onChange={top => patchFramePadding({ top })}/><NumberField label="Pad right" value={framePadding.right} min={0} onChange={right => patchFramePadding({ right })}/><NumberField label="Pad bottom" value={framePadding.bottom} min={0} onChange={bottom => patchFramePadding({ bottom })}/><NumberField label="Pad left" value={framePadding.left} min={0} onChange={left => patchFramePadding({ left })}/></div>
      <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Frame width"><select value={frameLayout.widthMode || 'fixed'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ widthMode: event.target.value })}><option value="fixed">Fixed</option><option value="hug">Hug content</option></select></Field><Field label="Frame height"><select value={frameLayout.heightMode || 'fixed'} onChange={event => patchFrameLayout({ heightMode: event.target.value })}><option value="fixed">Fixed</option><option value="hug">Hug content</option></select></Field></div>
      <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.clipChildren} onChange={event => patchOne({ clipChildren: event.target.checked })}/>Clip children to frame</label>
      <p className="help">Drag layers into this frame to create a nested hierarchy. Children can use fixed, fill-container, or hug-content sizing.</p>
    </InspectorSection>}

    {element.parentId && <InspectorSection title="Child layout" open={false}>
      <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Width"><select value={childSizing.width || 'fixed'} onChange={event => patchOne({ layoutSizing: { ...childSizing, width: event.target.value } })}><option value="fixed">Fixed</option><option value="fill">Fill container</option><option value="hug">Hug content</option></select></Field><Field label="Height"><select value={childSizing.height || 'fixed'} onChange={event => patchOne({ layoutSizing: { ...childSizing, height: event.target.value } })}><option value="fixed">Fixed</option><option value="fill">Fill container</option><option value="hug">Hug content</option></select></Field></div>
      <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Grow" value={childSizing.grow || 0} min={0} max={100} step={.1} onChange={grow => patchOne({ layoutSizing: { ...childSizing, grow } })}/><Field label="Self align"><select value={childSizing.alignSelf || 'auto'} onChange={event => patchOne({ layoutSizing: { ...childSizing, alignSelf: event.target.value } })}><option value="auto">Automatic</option><option value="start">Start</option><option value="center">Centre</option><option value="end">End</option><option value="stretch">Stretch</option></select></Field></div>
    </InspectorSection>}

    {selectedType === 'text' && <>
      <InspectorSection title="Text presets">
        <label className="paint-range"><span>Preset intensity {Math.round(textPresetIntensity * 100)}%</span><input type="range" min=".25" max="2" step=".05" value={textPresetIntensity} onChange={event => setTextPresetIntensity(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>
        <div className="filter-presets">{TEXT_PRESETS.map(preset => <button key={preset.id} onClick={() => applyTextPreset(preset)} style={{ fontFamily: preset.typography.fontFamily, fontWeight: preset.typography.fontWeight }}>{preset.name}</button>)}</div>
      </InspectorSection>
      <InspectorSection title="Rich text">
        <Field label="Font"><select value={element.fontFamily || 'Arial'} onChange={async event => { const fontFamily = event.target.value; const report = await ensureFontLoaded(fontFamily); setFontReport(report); editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontFamily }); }}>{FONT_CATEGORIES.map(group => <optgroup key={group.label} label={group.label}>{group.fonts.map(font => <option key={font} value={font} style={{ fontFamily: font }}>{font}</option>)}</optgroup>)}</select></Field>
        {fontReport && <p className={`font-status ${fontReport.status}`}><strong>{fontReport.status === 'loaded' ? 'Font loaded' : 'Font fallback warning'}</strong><span>{fontReport.status === 'loaded' ? `${fontReport.fontFamily} is available from ${fontReport.source}.` : `${fontReport.fontFamily} could not be confirmed. Export may use a fallback font.`}</span></p>}
        <NumberField label="Size" value={commonValue(selected, 'fontSize')} min={4} onChange={fontSize => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontSize })}/>
        <div className="icon-row"><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontWeight: element.fontWeight === 700 ? 400 : 700 })}><Bold size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontStyle: element.fontStyle === 'italic' ? 'normal' : 'italic' })}><Italic size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ underline: !element.underline })}><Underline size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ linethrough: !element.linethrough })}><Strikethrough size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontSize: Math.max(6, element.fontSize * .65), deltaY: -element.fontSize * .35 })}><Superscript size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ fontSize: Math.max(6, element.fontSize * .65), deltaY: element.fontSize * .25 })}><Subscript size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => { const url = prompt('Link URL'); if (url) editorRef.current?.setLink(url); }}><Link size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.clearTextFormatting()}><RotateCcw size={16}/></button></div>
        <div className="icon-row"><button className={element.textAlign === 'left' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ textAlign: 'left' })}><AlignLeft size={16}/></button><button className={element.textAlign === 'center' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ textAlign: 'center' })}><AlignCenter size={16}/></button><button className={element.textAlign === 'right' ? 'active' : ''} onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setTextStyle({ textAlign: 'right' })}><AlignRight size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.applyList('bullet')}><List size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.applyList('number')}><ListOrdered size={16}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.applyList('none')}><Minus size={16}/></button></div>
        <RangeField label="Line height" value={element.lineHeight || 1.16} min={.7} max={3} step={.02} onChange={lineHeight => patch({ lineHeight })}/><RangeField label="Letter spacing" value={element.charSpacing || 0} min={-100} max={500} step={5} onChange={charSpacing => patch({ charSpacing })}/><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.autoFit} onChange={event => patch({ autoFit: event.target.checked })}/>Measure and shrink text to fit the frame</label>{element.autoFit && <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Minimum size" value={element.minFontSize || 8} min={4} max={element.fontSize || 1000} onChange={minFontSize => patch({ minFontSize })}/><NumberField label="Maximum lines" value={element.maxLines || 0} min={0} max={100} onChange={maxLines => patch({ maxLines })}/></div>}<Field label="Overflow"><select value={element.overflowBehavior || 'visible'} onChange={event => patch({ overflowBehavior: event.target.value })}><option value="visible">Visible</option><option value="clip">Clip to text frame</option><option value="ellipsis">Fit, then clip</option></select></Field><Field label="Vertical alignment"><select value={element.verticalAlign || 'top'} onChange={event => patch({ verticalAlign: event.target.value })}><option value="top">Top</option><option value="middle">Middle</option><option value="bottom">Bottom</option></select></Field>
        <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Columns" value={element.columns || 1} min={1} max={12} onChange={columns => patch({ columns })}/><NumberField label="Column gap" value={element.columnGap || 24} min={0} max={400} onChange={columnGap => patch({ columnGap })}/></div>
        <div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Widow lines" value={element.widowLines || 2} min={1} max={10} onChange={widowLines => patch({ widowLines })}/><NumberField label="Orphan lines" value={element.orphanLines || 2} min={1} max={10} onChange={orphanLines => patch({ orphanLines })}/></div>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.hyphenation} onChange={event => patch({ hyphenation: event.target.checked })}/>Automatic hyphenation</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.hangingPunctuation} onChange={event => patch({ hangingPunctuation: event.target.checked })}/>Hanging punctuation</label>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.opticalMargin} onChange={event => patch({ opticalMargin: event.target.checked })}/>Optical margin alignment</label>
        <NumberField label="Baseline grid step" value={element.baselineGridStep || 0} min={0} max={200} onChange={baselineGridStep => patch({ baselineGridStep })}/>
        <Field label="OpenType features"><input value={element.opentypeFeatures || ''} onChange={event => patch({ opentypeFeatures: event.target.value })} placeholder="liga, kern, smcp"/></Field>
      </InspectorSection>
      <InspectorSection title="Text shape and highlight" open={false}>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!effect.hollow} onChange={event => patch({ effect: { ...effect, hollow: event.target.checked } })}/>Hollow text</label>
        <RangeField label="Curve" value={effect.curve || 0} min={-100} max={100} step={1} onChange={curve => patch({ effect: { ...effect, curve } })}/>
        <Field label="Text highlight"><input type="color" value={element.textBackgroundColor || '#ffffff'} onChange={event => patch({ textBackgroundColor: event.target.value })}/></Field>
        <button className="full" onClick={() => patch({ textBackgroundColor: '' })}>Remove highlight</button>
        <p className="help">Use the Appearance section for gradient text, outlines, shadows, alpha, and blend modes.</p>
      </InspectorSection>
    </>}

    {selectedType === 'image' && <>
      {selected.length === 1 && <InspectorSection title="Crop, frame and mask"><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!element.isImageFrame} onChange={event => patchOne({ isImageFrame: event.target.checked })}/>Reusable image frame</label>{element.isImageFrame && <Field label="Frame label"><input value={element.frameLabel || 'Drop an image'} onChange={event => patchOne({ frameLabel: event.target.value })}/></Field>}<div className="button-row"><button className="primary" onClick={() => editorRef.current?.setCropMode(true)}><Crop size={15}/>Crop</button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.cropZoom(-.15)}><Minus size={15}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.cropZoom(.15)}><Plus size={15}/></button><button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.resetCrop()}><RotateCcw size={15}/></button></div><RangeField label="Crop zoom" value={element.cropZoom || 1} min={1} max={8} step={.05} onChange={cropZoom => patchOne({ cropZoom })}/><Field label="Mask"><select value={element.mask || 'rect'} onChange={event => patchOne({ mask: event.target.value })}><option value="rect">Rectangle</option><option value="rounded">Rounded</option><option value="circle">Ellipse</option><option value="triangle">Triangle</option><option value="hexagon">Hexagon</option><option value="star">Star</option><option value="heart">Heart</option><option value="arch">Arch</option><option value="blob">Blob</option></select></Field>{element.mask === 'rounded' && <RangeField label="Corner radius" value={element.radius || 24} min={0} max={200} step={1} onChange={radius => patchOne({ radius })}/>}<button className="full" onClick={() => replaceRef.current?.click()}>Replace image</button><input hidden ref={replaceRef} type="file" accept="image/*" onChange={replaceImage}/></InspectorSection>}
      <InspectorSection title={`Image filters${selected.length > 1 ? ` (${selected.length})` : ''}`}>
        {selected.length > 1 && <p className="help">Presets and adjustments apply to every selected picture.</p>}
        <div className="button-row"><button onClick={() => patch({ filters: { brightness: 0, contrast: 0, saturation: 0, hue: 0, blur: 0, vibrance: 0, noise: 0, pixelate: 0, gamma: 1, tint: '#ffffff', tintOpacity: 0, grayscale: false, sepia: false } })}><RotateCcw size={14}/>Reset filters</button></div>
        <label className="paint-range"><span>Preset intensity {Math.round(imagePresetIntensity * 100)}%</span><input type="range" min="0" max="2" step=".05" value={imagePresetIntensity} onChange={event => setImagePresetIntensity(Number(event.target.value))}/></label>
        <div className="filter-presets image-filter-presets">{IMAGE_PRESETS.map(preset => <button key={preset.id} onClick={() => patch({ filters: scaleImageFilters(preset.filters, imagePresetIntensity) })}>{preset.name}</button>)}</div>
        {[['Brightness', 'brightness', -1, 1, .02], ['Contrast', 'contrast', -1, 1, .02], ['Saturation', 'saturation', -1, 1, .02], ['Vibrance', 'vibrance', -1, 1, .02], ['Hue', 'hue', -1, 1, .02], ['Gamma', 'gamma', .2, 3, .02], ['Blur', 'blur', 0, 1, .01], ['Film grain', 'noise', 0, 500, 5], ['Pixelate', 'pixelate', 0, 50, 1]].map(([label, key, min, max, step]) => <RangeField key={key} label={label} value={imageFilters[key] ?? (key === 'gamma' ? 1 : 0)} min={min} max={max} step={step} onChange={value => patch(item => ({ filters: { ...(item.filters || {}), [key]: value } }))}/>)}
        <div className="field-grid"><Field label="Tint"><input type="color" value={imageFilters.tint || '#ffffff'} onChange={event => patch(item => ({ filters: { ...(item.filters || {}), tint: event.target.value } }))}/></Field><NumberField label="Tint %" value={Math.round((imageFilters.tintOpacity || 0) * 100)} min={0} max={100} onChange={value => patch(item => ({ filters: { ...(item.filters || {}), tintOpacity: value / 100 } }))}/></div>
        <label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!imageFilters.grayscale} onChange={event => patch(item => ({ filters: { ...(item.filters || {}), grayscale: event.target.checked } }))}/>Grayscale</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={!!imageFilters.sepia} onChange={event => patch(item => ({ filters: { ...(item.filters || {}), sepia: event.target.checked } }))}/>Sepia</label>
      </InspectorSection>
    </>}

    {selectedType === 'svg' && <InspectorSection title="Custom SVG"><SvgSourceEditor element={element} onApply={patchOne} notify={notify}/></InspectorSection>}

    {selectedType === 'chart' && <InspectorSection title="Chart data"><Field label="Type"><select value={element.chartType} onChange={event => patchOne({ chartType: event.target.value })}>{['bar', 'line', 'area', 'pie', 'donut', 'kpi'].map(type => <option key={type}>{type}</option>)}</select></Field><Field label="Labels (comma separated)"><textarea value={(element.data.labels || []).join(', ')} onChange={event => patchOne({ data: { ...element.data, labels: event.target.value.split(',').map(value => value.trim()) } })}/></Field><Field label="Values (comma separated)"><textarea value={(element.data.series?.[0]?.values || []).join(', ')} onChange={event => patchOne({ data: { ...element.data, series: [{ ...(element.data.series?.[0] || { name: 'Series 1' }), values: event.target.value.split(',').map(Number) }] } })}/></Field><Field label="Series name"><input value={element.data.series?.[0]?.name || ''} onChange={event => patchOne({ data: { ...element.data, series: [{ ...(element.data.series?.[0] || {}), name: event.target.value }] } })}/></Field><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={element.options?.showLegend !== false} onChange={event => patchOne({ options: { ...element.options, showLegend: event.target.checked } })}/>Show legend</label><label className="check"><input type="checkbox" checked={element.options?.showLabels !== false} onChange={event => patchOne({ options: { ...element.options, showLabels: event.target.checked } })}/>Show labels</label></InspectorSection>}

    {selectedType === 'table' && <InspectorSection title="Table data"><p className="help">Paste tab-separated cells, one row per line.</p><textarea className="data-editor" value={(element.cells || []).map(row => row.join('\t')).join('\n')} onChange={event => { const cells = event.target.value.split('\n').map(row => row.split('\t')); patchOne({ cells, rows: cells.length, columns: Math.max(1, ...cells.map(row => row.length)) }); }}/><div className="field-grid"><NumberField label="Header rows" value={element.options?.headerRows ?? 1} min={0} onChange={headerRows => patchOne({ options: { ...element.options, headerRows } })}/><NumberField label="Font size" value={element.options?.fontSize || 22} min={8} onChange={fontSize => patchOne({ options: { ...element.options, fontSize } })}/></div><Field label="Header colour"><input type="color" value={element.options?.headerFill || '#111827'} onChange={event => patchOne({ options: { ...element.options, headerFill: event.target.value } })}/></Field></InspectorSection>}

    {selectedType === 'qrcode' && <InspectorSection title="QR code"><Field label="Content"><textarea value={element.value} onChange={event => patchOne({ value: event.target.value })}/></Field><div className="field-grid"><Field label="Foreground"><input type="color" value={element.foreground} onChange={event => patchOne({ foreground: event.target.value })}/></Field><Field label="Background"><input type="color" value={element.background} onChange={event => patchOne({ background: event.target.value })}/></Field></div><Field label="Error correction"><select value={element.errorCorrection || 'M'} onChange={event => patchOne({ errorCorrection: event.target.value })}><option>L</option><option>M</option><option>Q</option><option>H</option></select></Field></InspectorSection>}

    {selectedType === 'shape' && <InspectorSection title="Shape options" open={false}><Field label="Shape"><select value={element.shapeKind || 'triangle'} onChange={event => patchOne({ shapeKind: event.target.value })}>{[['triangle','Triangle'],['diamond','Diamond'],['pentagon','Pentagon'],['hexagon','Hexagon'],['star','Star'],['burst','Burst'],['heart','Heart'],['arrow','Arrow'],['chevron','Chevron'],['speech','Speech bubble']].map(([id,name]) => <option key={id} value={id}>{name}</option>)}</select></Field>{['star','burst'].includes(element.shapeKind) && <><NumberField label="Points" value={element.shapeOptions?.points || (element.shapeKind === 'burst' ? 12 : 5)} min={3} max={32} onChange={points => patchOne({ shapeOptions: { ...(element.shapeOptions || {}), points } })}/><RangeField label="Inner radius" value={element.shapeOptions?.innerRatio || .46} min={.1} max={.9} step={.01} onChange={innerRatio => patchOne({ shapeOptions: { ...(element.shapeOptions || {}), innerRatio } })}/></>}</InspectorSection>}

    {['rect', 'frame'].includes(selectedType) && <InspectorSection title="Corners" open={false}><RangeField label="Corner radius" value={element.radius || 0} min={0} max={Math.min(element.width, element.height) / 2} step={1} onChange={radius => patch({ radius })}/><button className="full" onClick={() => patch({ radius: Math.min(element.width, element.height) / 2 })}>Make pill</button></InspectorSection>}

    {element.type !== 'qrcode' && <InspectorSection title="Appearance"><AppearancePanel element={element} selected={selected} patch={patch} document={document}/></InspectorSection>}

    {!selectedType && selected.length > 1 && <p className="help inspector-empty-help">The selection contains different element types. Common transform controls remain available above.</p>}
    {commonsOpen && <CommonsPublishDialog onClose={() => setCommonsOpen(false)} editorRef={editorRef} sourceAsset={selectedSourceAsset} selectedElements={selected}/>}
  </aside>;
}

import Modal from'./Modal.jsx';import{useEditorStore}from'../store.js';import{api}from'../lib/api.js';
export default function TeamDialog({onClose}){const members=useEditorStore(s=>s.members),load=useEditorStore(s=>s.loadMembers),role=useEditorStore(s=>s.role),changePassword=useEditorStore(s=>s.changePassword);const[email,setEmail]=useState(''),[inviteRole,setInviteRole]=useState('designer'),[invite,setInvite]=useState(null),[currentPassword,setCurrentPassword]=useState(''),[newPassword,setNewPassword]=useState('');useEffect(()=>{load().catch(()=>{})},[]);return <Modal title="Team, roles and security" onClose={onClose} wide><h3>Invite a member</h3><div className="invite-row"><input type="email" placeholder="person@example.com" value={email} value={`${location.origin}/?invite=${invite.token}`}/><button onClick={()=>navigator.clipboard.writeText(`${location.origin}/?invite=${invite.token}`)}>Copy</button></div>}<table
