disabled={role!=='owner'} value={m.role} onChange={async e=>{await api.updateMember(m.id,e.target.value);await load()}}>{['owner','admin','designer','reviewer','viewer'].map(r=><option key={r}>{r}</option>)}</select></td><td>{role==='owner'&&m.role!=='owner'&&<button className="danger" onClick={async()=>{await api.removeMember(m.id);await load()}}>Remove</button>}</td></tr>)}</tbody></table><h3>Change your password</h3><div className="field-grid"><label className="field"><span>Current password</span><input type="password" value={currentPassword} onChange={e=>setCurrentPassword(e.target.value)}/></label><label className="field"><span>New password</span><input type="password" minLength="10" value={newPassword} onChange={e=>setNewPassword(e.target.value)}/></label></div><button disabled={!currentPassword||newPassword.length<10} onClick={async()=>{await changePassword(currentPassword,newPassword);location.reload()}}>Change password and sign out</button></Modal>}

// FILE: src/components/ThemeToggle.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Laptop, Moon, Sun } from 'lucide-react';
import { applyTheme, getThemePreference, saveThemePreference, subscribeToSystemTheme } from '../lib/theme.js';

const OPTIONS = [
  { id: 'light', label: 'Light theme', Icon: Sun },
  { id: 'dark', label: 'Dark theme', Icon: Moon },
  { id: 'system', label: 'Use system theme', Icon: Laptop }
];

export default function ThemeToggle({ compact = false }) {
  const [preference, setPreference] = useState(getThemePreference);
  useEffect(() => {
    applyTheme(preference);
    const onTheme = event => setPreference(event.detail?.preference || getThemePreference());
    globalThis.addEventListener('canvasforge:theme', onTheme);
    const unsubscribe = subscribeToSystemTheme(() => setPreference(getThemePreference()));
    return () => { globalThis.removeEventListener('canvasforge:theme', onTheme); unsubscribe(); };
  }, []);
  const current = OPTIONS.find(item => item.id === preference) || OPTIONS[2];
  const cycle = () => {
    const index = OPTIONS.findIndex(item => item.id === preference);
    setPreference(saveThemePreference(OPTIONS[(index + 1) % OPTIONS.length].id));
  };
  return <button className={`theme-toggle ${compact ? 'compact' : ''}`} type="button" title={`${current.label}. Click to change.`} aria-label={`${current.label}. Click to change.`} onClick={cycle}>
    <current.Icon size={16}/>{!compact && <span>{current.id === 'system' ? 'Auto' : current.id[0].toUpperCase() + current.id.slice(1)}</span>}
  </button>;
}

// FILE: src/components/TopToolbar.jsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  AlignCenter, AlignHorizontalDistributeCenter, AlignLeft, AlignRight,
  AlignVerticalDistributeCenter, ArrowDown, ArrowDownToLine, ArrowUp,
  ArrowUpToLine, Bell, BookTemplate, ChevronDown, Download, EyeOff, Home,
  Group, Lock, Maximize2, MessageSquare, PanelLeft, PanelRight, Redo2, Save,
  Share2, Sparkles, Trash2, Undo2, Ungroup
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useEditorStore } from '../store.js';
import { api } from '../lib/api.js';
import { ResizeDialog, TemplateDialog, ShareDialog, ReviewDialog } from './EditorDialogs.jsx';
import { ESCAPE_EVENT, LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT } from '../lib/appMeta.js';
import ThemeToggle from './ThemeToggle.jsx';

function saveLabel(status, lastSavedAt) {
  if (status === 'saving') return 'Saving…';
  if (status === 'dirty') return 'Unsaved changes';
  if (status === 'offline') return 'Offline · saved locally';
  if (status === 'save-failed') return 'Save failed';
  if (status === 'conflict') return 'Editing conflict';
  if (status === 'recovered') return 'Recovery found';
  if (status === 'saved' && lastSavedAt) {
    const seconds = Math.floor((Date.now() - lastSavedAt) / 1000);
    if (seconds < 45) return 'Saved just now';
    return `Saved ${new Date(lastSavedAt).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' })}`;
  }
  return status.replaceAll('-', ' ');
}

export default function TopToolbar({ editorRef }) {
  const undo = useEditorStore(state => state.undo);
  const redo = useEditorStore(state => state.redo);
  const history = useEditorStore(state => state.history);
  const future = useEditorStore(state => state.future);
  const save = useEditorStore(state => state.save);
  const status = useEditorStore(state => state.status);
  const lastError = useEditorStore(state => state.lastError);
  const lastSavedAt = useEditorStore(state => state.lastSavedAt);
  const exportDesign = useEditorStore(state => state.exportDesign);
  const refreshExport = useEditorStore(state => state.refreshExport);
  const closeDesign = useEditorStore(state => state.closeDesign);
  const role = useEditorStore(state => state.role);
  const design = useEditorStore(state => state.design);
  const document = useEditorStore(state => state.document);
  const pageIndex = useEditorStore(state => state.pageIndex);
  const selection = useEditorStore(state => state.selection);
  const updateElements = useEditorStore(state => state.updateElements);
  const groupSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.groupSelection);
  const ungroupSelection = useEditorStore(state => state.ungroupSelection);
  const notifications = useEditorStore(state => state.notifications);
  const markNotification = useEditorStore(state => state.markNotification);
  const markAllNotifications = useEditorStore(state => state.markAllNotifications);
  const toggleLeftPanel = useEditorStore(state => state.toggleLeftPanel);
  const toggleRightPanel = useEditorStore(state => state.toggleRightPanel);
  const leftPanelOpen = useEditorStore(state => state.leftPanelOpen);
  const rightPanelOpen = useEditorStore(state => state.rightPanelOpen);
  const notify = useEditorStore(state => state.notify);
  const aiPanelOpen = useEditorStore(state => state.aiPanelOpen);
  const toggleAIPanel = useEditorStore(state => state.toggleAIPanel);

  const [dialog, setDialog] = useState('');
  const [job, setJob] = useState(null);
  const [menu, setMenu] = useState('');
  const [showNotifications, setShowNotifications] = useState(false);
  const [exportScale, setExportScale] = useState(2);
  const unread = notifications.filter(notification => !notification.read_at).length;
  const canDesign = ['owner', 'admin', 'designer'].includes(role);
  const canReview = role !== 'viewer';
  const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex];
  const selected = useMemo(() => (page?.elements || []).filter(element => selection.includes(element.id)), [page, selection]);
  const selectionLocked = selected.length > 0 && selected.every(element => element.locked);
  const selectionHidden = selected.length > 0 && selected.every(element => element.hidden);
  const selectionGrouped = selected.some(element => element.groupId);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!job || !['queued', 'processing'].includes(job.status)) return;
    const id = setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const next = await refreshExport(job.id);
        setJob(next);
        if (next.status === 'completed') window.open(next.output_url, '_blank', 'noopener');
      } catch {}
    }, 800);
    return () => clearInterval(id);
  }, [job?.id, job?.status]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const close = () => { setMenu(''); setShowNotifications(false); };
    const outside = event => {
      if (!event.target.closest?.('.toolbar-menu-wrap, .notification-wrap')) close();
    };
    window.addEventListener(ESCAPE_EVENT, close);
    window.addEventListener(LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT, close);
    globalThis.document.addEventListener('pointerdown', outside);
    return () => { window.removeEventListener(ESCAPE_EVENT, close); window.removeEventListener(LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT, close); globalThis.document.removeEventListener('pointerdown', outside); };
  }, []);

  const goHome = async () => {
    if (['dirty', 'saving'].includes(status) && canDesign) {
      try { await save(); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); return; }
    }
    if (['offline', 'save-failed', 'recovered', 'conflict'].includes(status) && !confirm('Leave the editor? Your unsaved work will remain in local recovery, but it may not be on the server.')) return;
    closeDesign();
  };

  const doExport = async format => {
    setMenu('');
    try {
      setJob(await exportDesign(format, { multiplier: exportScale, ...(format === 'pdf' ? { print: document.print || null, pageSize: { width: document.width, height: document.height, unit: document.unit || 'px', dpi: document.dpi || 96 } } : {}) }));
    } catch (error) {
      notify(`Export failed: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
  };
  const iconButton = (title, icon, onClick, disabled = false, active = false) => <button className={`toolbar-icon-button ${active ? 'active' : ''}`.trim()} data-tooltip={title} title={title} aria-label={title} onClick={onClick} disabled={disabled}>{icon}</button>;
  const toggleMenu = value => setMenu(current => current === value ? '' : value);

  return <>
    <header className="top-toolbar">
      <div className="toolbar-zone toolbar-left">
        <div className="toolbar-brand" aria-label="Design Commons"><span>DC</span><strong>Design Commons</strong></div>
        {iconButton('Back to dashboard', <Home size={17}/>, goHome)}
        {iconButton(leftPanelOpen ? 'Hide left panel' : 'Show left panel', <PanelLeft size={17}/>, toggleLeftPanel, false, leftPanelOpen)}
        <div className="toolbar-divider"/>
        {iconButton('Undo · Ctrl/Cmd+Z', <Undo2 size={17}/>, undo, !history.length || !canDesign)}
        {iconButton('Redo · Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+Z', <Redo2 size={17}/>, redo, !future.length || !canDesign)}
        <button className={`save-button ${status}`} title={lastError || 'Save · Ctrl/Cmd+S'} onClick={() => save().catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error'))} disabled={status === 'saving' || status === 'conflict' || status === 'recovered' || !canDesign}>
          <Save size={16}/><span>{saveLabel(status, lastSavedAt)}</span>
        </button>
        {status === 'save-failed' && <button className="mini retry-save" onClick={() => save().catch(error => notify(error.message, 'error'))}>Retry</button>}
      </div>

      <div className="toolbar-zone toolbar-context">
        {!selection.length ? <>
          <span className="context-label">Page</span>
          <button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.fit()}>Fit page</button>
          <button onClick={() => editorRef.current?.fitWidth()}>Fit width</button>
        </> : <>
          <span className="context-label">{selection.length === 1 ? selected[0]?.name || selected[0]?.type : `${selection.length} elements`}</span>
          <div className="toolbar-menu-wrap">
            <button onClick={() => toggleMenu('align')}>Align <ChevronDown size={14}/></button>
            {menu === 'align' && <div className="toolbar-popover compact-menu">
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('left'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignLeft size={16}/>Left</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('center'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignCenter size={16}/>Horizontal centre</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('right'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignRight size={16}/>Right</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('top'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowUp size={16}/>Top</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('middle'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignCenter size={16}/>Vertical middle</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.align('bottom'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowDown size={16}/>Bottom</button>
              <hr/>
              <button disabled={selection.length < 3} onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.distribute('horizontal'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignHorizontalDistributeCenter size={16}/>Distribute horizontally</button>
              <button disabled={selection.length < 3} onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.distribute('vertical'); setMenu(''); }}><AlignVerticalDistributeCenter size={16}/>Distribute vertically</button>
            </div>}
          </div>
          <div className="toolbar-menu-wrap">
            <button onClick={() => toggleMenu('position')}>Position <ChevronDown size={14}/></button>
            {menu === 'position' && <div className="toolbar-popover compact-menu">
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.order('forward'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowUp size={16}/>Bring forward</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.order('backward'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowDown size={16}/>Send backward</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.order('front'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowUpToLine size={16}/>Bring to front</button>
              <button onClick={() => { editorRef.current?.order('back'); setMenu(''); }}><ArrowDownToLine size={16}/>Send to back</button>
            </div>}
          </div>
          {iconButton('Group selection · Ctrl/Cmd+G', <Group size={16}/>, () => { try { groupSelection(); notify('Objects grouped.', 'success'); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }, !canDesign || selection.length < 2)}
          {iconButton('Ungroup selection · Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+G', <Ungroup size={16}/>, () => { try { ungroupSelection(); notify('Objects ungrouped.', 'success'); } catch (error) { notify(error.message, 'error'); } }, !canDesign || !selectionGrouped)}
          {iconButton(selectionLocked ? 'Unlock selection' : 'Lock selection', <Lock size={16}/>, () => updateElements(selection, { locked: !selectionLocked }), !canDesign, selectionLocked)}
          {iconButton(selectionHidden ? 'Show selection' : 'Hide selection', <EyeOff size={16}/>, () => updateElements(selection, { hidden: !selectionHidden }), !canDesign, selectionHidden)}
          {iconButton('Delete selection', <Trash2 size={16}/>, () => editorRef.current?.delete(), !canDesign)}
        </>}
      </div>

      <div className="toolbar-zone toolbar-right">
        <button className={aiPanelOpen ? 'active ai-toolbar-button' : 'ai-toolbar-button'} onClick={() => toggleAIPanel()} disabled={!canDesign}><Sparkles size={16}/>AI</button>
        <button onClick={() => setDialog('resize')} disabled={!canDesign}><Maximize2 size={16}/>Resize</button>
        <button onClick={() => setDialog('template')} disabled={!canDesign}><BookTemplate size={16}/>Template</button>
        <button onClick={() => setDialog('review')} disabled={!canReview}><MessageSquare size={16}/>Review</button>
        <button onClick={() => setDialog('share')} disabled={!canReview}><Share2 size={16}/>Share</button>
        <ThemeToggle compact/>
        <div className="notification-wrap">
          <button className="notification-button" onClick={() => { setShowNotifications(value => !value); setMenu(''); }} title="Notifications"><Bell size={16}/>{unread > 0 && <span>{unread > 99 ? '99+' : unread}</span>}</button>
          {showNotifications && <div className="notification-popover">
            <header><strong>Notifications</strong><button disabled={!unread} onClick={markAllNotifications}>Mark all read</button></header>
            {notifications.length === 0 ? <p>No notifications.</p> : notifications.slice(0, 20).map(notification => <button key={notification.id} className={notification.read_at ? 'read' : ''} onClick={() => markNotification(notification.id, true)}><strong>{notification.title}</strong><span>{notification.body}</span><small>{new Date(notification.created_at).toLocaleString()}</small></button>)}
          </div>}
        </div>
        <div className="toolbar-menu-wrap">
          <button className="primary download-button" disabled={(!!job && ['queued', 'processing'].includes(job.status)) || !canReview} onClick={() => toggleMenu('download')}><Download size={16}/>Download<ChevronDown size={14}/></button>
          {menu === 'download' && <div className="toolbar-popover download-menu">
            <strong>Download design</strong>
            <label>Resolution<select value={exportScale} onChange={event => setExportScale(Number(event.target.value))}><option value="1">1×</option><option value="2">2×</option><option value="3">3×</option></select></label>
            <button onClick={() => doExport('png')}><span><b>PNG</b><small>High-quality image</small></span></button>
            <button onClick={() => doExport('pdf')}><span><b>PDF</b><small>{document.print?.pdfPreset || 'screen'} · {document.print?.colorSpace || 'rgb'} · print preflight</small></span></button>
            {job && <div className={`export-job ${job.status}`}><span>{job.status} {job.progress || 0}%</span>{['queued', 'processing'].includes(job.status) && <button onClick={async () => setJob(await api.cancelExport(job.id))}>Cancel</button>}{job.status === 'failed' && <button onClick={async () => setJob(await api.retryExport(job.id))}>Retry</button>}</div>}
          </div>}
        </div>
        {iconButton(rightPanelOpen ? 'Hide inspector' : 'Show inspector', <PanelRight size={17}/>, toggleRightPanel, false, rightPanelOpen)}
        <span className={`status-pill ${design.status}`}>{design.status?.replaceAll('_', ' ')}</span>
      </div>
    </header>
    {dialog === 'resize' && <ResizeDialog onClose={() => setDialog('')}/>}
    {dialog === 'template' && <TemplateDialog onClose={() => setDialog('')}/>}
    {dialog === 'share' && <ShareDialog onClose={() => setDialog('')}/>}
    {dialog === 'review' && <ReviewDialog onClose={() => setDialog('')}/>}
  </>;
}

// FILE: src/export-renderer-entry.js
================================================================================
import { StaticCanvas } from 'fabric';
import { elementToObject, paintToFabric } from './lib/fabricAdapter.js';
import { ensureFontsLoaded } from './lib/fonts.js';
import { normalizePrintSettings } from './lib/designSystem.js';

let canvas = null;
let lastPrintSpec = null;

export async function render(document, pageIndex = 0) {
  const page = document.pages[pageIndex];
  if (!page) throw new Error(`Page ${pageIndex} not found.`);
  await ensureFontsLoaded((page.elements || []).flatMap(item => item.type === 'text' ? [item.fontFamily] : ['chart', 'table'].includes(item.type) ? [item.options?.fontFamily] : []).filter(Boolean));
  const element = globalThis.document.getElementById('export-canvas');
  if (!element) throw new Error('Export canvas element is missing.');
  canvas?.dispose?.();
  lastPrintSpec = normalizePrintSettings(document.print, document.width, document.height);
  canvas = new StaticCanvas(element, {
    width: document.width,
    height: document.height,
    backgroundColor: page.transparentBackground ? 'transparent' : paintToFabric(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, document.width, document.height, '#ffffff'),
    enableRetinaScaling: false,
    renderOnAddRemove: false
  });
  const sorted = [...(page.elements || [])].filter(item => !item.hidden).sort((a,b)=>(a.zIndex||0)-(b.zIndex||0));
  for (const item of sorted) {
    const object = await elementToObject(item);
    object.set({ selectable: false, evented: false });
    canvas.add(object);
  }
  canvas.requestRenderAll();
  await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(() => requestAnimationFrame(resolve)));
  return { width: document.width, height: document.height, print: lastPrintSpec };
}

export function dataUrl(format = 'png', multiplier = 1, quality = .92) {
  if (!canvas) throw new Error('Render has not completed.');
  return canvas.toDataURL({ format: format === 'jpeg' ? 'jpeg' : 'png', multiplier, quality, enableRetinaScaling: false });
}

export function svg() {
  if (!canvas) throw new Error('Render has not completed.');
  return canvas.toSVG({ suppressPreamble: false });
}


export function printSpec() {
  return lastPrintSpec ? structuredClone(lastPrintSpec) : null;
}

// FILE: src/lib/api.js

import { readMigratedStorage } from './appMeta.js';
export const apiOrigin = import.meta.env.VITE_API_ORIGIN || '';
const API = apiOrigin;
const PUBLIC_API = import.meta.env.VITE_PUBLIC_API_ORIGIN || '';
const getToken = () => readMigratedStorage('session') || '';
const getWorkspace = () => readMigratedStorage('organization') || '';

async function request(path, options = {}) {
  const headers = new Headers(options.headers || {});
  const token = getToken();
  if (token) headers.set('authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);
  const workspace = getWorkspace();
  if (workspace) {
    headers.set('x-workspace-id', workspace);
    headers.set('x-organization-id', workspace);
  }
  if (options.body && !(options.body instanceof FormData)) headers.set('content-type', 'application/json');
  const response = await fetch(`${API}${path}`, { ...options, headers });
  if (!response.ok) {
    const payload = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
    const error = new Error(payload.error || `${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);
    error.status = response.status;
    error.payload = payload;
    throw error;
  }
  if (response.status === 204) return null;
  return response.json();
}
const jsonBody = value => JSON.stringify(value);

// FILE: src/lib/appearance.js
================================================================================
export const PAINT_TYPES = ['none', 'solid', 'linear', 'radial', 'pattern'];
export const BLEND_MODES = [
  ['source-over', 'Normal'], ['multiply', 'Multiply'], ['screen', 'Screen'], ['overlay', 'Overlay'],
  ['darken', 'Darken'], ['lighten', 'Lighten'], ['color-dodge', 'Colour dodge'],
  ['color-burn', 'Colour burn'], ['hard-light', 'Hard light'], ['soft-light', 'Soft light'],
  ['difference', 'Difference'], ['exclusion', 'Exclusion'], ['hue', 'Hue'],
  ['saturation', 'Saturation'], ['color', 'Colour'], ['luminosity', 'Luminosity']
];
export const PATTERN_TYPES = [
  ['stripes', 'Stripes'], ['dots', 'Dots'], ['grid', 'Grid'], ['checker', 'Checkerboard'],
  ['crosshatch', 'Crosshatch'], ['zigzag', 'Zigzag']
];

const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
const layerId = prefix => `${prefix}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`;
export const clamp01 = value => clamp(Number(value ?? 1), 0, 1);
export const normalizeHex = (value, fallback = '#000000') => {
  const input = String(value || '').trim();
  if (/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(input)) return input.toLowerCase();
  if (/^#[0-9a-f]{3}$/i.test(input)) return `#${input.slice(1).split('').map(char => char + char).join('')}`.toLowerCase();
  return fallback;
};
export const colorWithOpacity = (color, opacity = 1) => {
  const hex = normalizeHex(color);
  const alpha = clamp01(opacity);
  const red = parseInt(hex.slice(1, 3), 16);
  const green = parseInt(hex.slice(3, 5), 16);
  const blue = parseInt(hex.slice(5, 7), 16);
  return `rgba(${red}, ${green}, ${blue}, ${alpha})`;
};

export const solidPaint = (color = '#4f46e5', opacity = 1) => ({ type: 'solid', color: normalizeHex(color, '#4f46e5'), opacity: clamp01(opacity) });
export const nonePaint = () => ({ type: 'none' });
export const defaultGradientStops = () => [
  { offset: 0, color: '#4f46e5', opacity: 1 },
  { offset: 1, color: '#ec4899', opacity: 1 }
];

export function normalizePaint(value, fallback = '#4f46e5') {
  if (typeof value === 'string') {
    if (!value || value === 'transparent') return nonePaint();
    return solidPaint(value, 1);
  }
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : solidPaint(fallback);
  const type = PAINT_TYPES.includes(source.type) ? source.type : 'solid';
  if (type === 'none') return nonePaint();
  if (type === 'solid') return solidPaint(source.color || fallback, source.opacity ?? 1);
  if (type === 'pattern') return {
    type,
    pattern: PATTERN_TYPES.some(([id]) => id === source.pattern) ? source.pattern : 'stripes',
    foreground: normalizeHex(source.foreground || source.color || fallback, fallback),
    background: normalizeHex(source.background || '#ffffff', '#ffffff'),
    foregroundOpacity: clamp01(source.foregroundOpacity ?? source.opacity ?? 1),
    backgroundOpacity: clamp01(source.backgroundOpacity ?? 1),
    scale: clamp(Number(source.scale || 24), 6, 160),
    spacing: clamp(Number(source.spacing || 12), 2, 100),
    lineWidth: clamp(Number(source.lineWidth || 4), 1, 40),
    angle: Number.isFinite(Number(source.angle)) ? Number(source.angle) : 45
  };
  const stops = (Array.isArray(source.stops) && source.stops.length >= 2 ? source.stops : defaultGradientStops())
    .map(stop => ({
      offset: clamp(Number(stop.offset ?? 0), 0, 1),
      color: normalizeHex(stop.color || fallback, fallback),
      opacity: clamp01(stop.opacity ?? 1)
    }))
    .sort((a, b) => a.offset - b.offset);
  if (type === 'linear') return { type, angle: Number(source.angle || 0), stops };
  return {
    type: 'radial',
    centerX: clamp01(source.centerX ?? .5),
    centerY: clamp01(source.centerY ?? .5),
    radius: clamp(Number(source.radius ?? .7), .05, 2),
    stops
  };
}

export function normalizeStroke(value = {}, legacy = {}) {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : {};
  const legacyColor = legacy.stroke && legacy.stroke !== 'transparent' ? legacy.stroke : '#111827';
  const width = Math.max(0, Number(source.width ?? legacy.strokeWidth ?? 0));
  return {
    id: source.id || layerId('stroke'),
    name: String(source.name || 'Stroke').slice(0, 80),
    enabled: source.enabled ?? width > 0,
    color: normalizeHex(source.color || legacyColor, '#111827'),
    opacity: clamp01(source.opacity ?? 1),
    width,
    alignment: ['inside', 'center', 'outside'].includes(source.alignment) ? source.alignment : 'center',
    style: ['solid', 'dashed', 'dotted', 'custom'].includes(source.style) ? source.style : 'solid',
    dash: Math.max(1, Number(source.dash || 10)),
    gap: Math.max(1, Number(source.gap || 8)),
    lineCap: ['butt', 'round', 'square'].includes(source.lineCap) ? source.lineCap : 'round',
    lineJoin: ['miter', 'round', 'bevel'].includes(source.lineJoin) ? source.lineJoin : 'round',
    blendMode: BLEND_MODES.some(([id]) => id === source.blendMode) ? source.blendMode : 'source-over'
  };
}

export function normalizeShadow(value = {}, legacyShadow = null) {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : (legacyShadow || {});
  const legacyEnabled = !!legacyShadow;
  return {
    id: source.id || layerId('shadow'),
    name: String(source.name || (source.type === 'inner' ? 'Inner shadow' : 'Drop shadow')).slice(0, 80),
    enabled: source.enabled ?? legacyEnabled,
    type: source.type === 'inner' ? 'inner' : 'drop',
    color: normalizeHex(source.color || '#000000', '#000000'),
    opacity: clamp01(source.opacity ?? (legacyEnabled ? .3 : .25)),
    blur: clamp(Number(source.blur || 0), 0, 160),
    spread: clamp(Number(source.spread || 0), -100, 200),
    offsetX: clamp(Number(source.offsetX || 0), -200, 200),
    offsetY: clamp(Number(source.offsetY || 0), -200, 200),
    blendMode: BLEND_MODES.some(([id]) => id === source.blendMode) ? source.blendMode : 'source-over'
  };
}

export function normalizeFillLayer(value = {}, fallback = '#4f46e5') {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' && 'paint' in value ? value : { paint: value };
  return {
    id: source.id || layerId('fill'),
    name: String(source.name || 'Fill').slice(0, 80),
    enabled: source.enabled !== false,
    opacity: clamp01(source.opacity ?? 1),
    blendMode: BLEND_MODES.some(([id]) => id === source.blendMode) ? source.blendMode : 'source-over',
    paint: normalizePaint(source.paint, fallback)
  };
}

export function normalizeEffect(value = {}) {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : {};
  return {
    id: source.id || layerId('effect'),
    name: String(source.name || (source.type === 'background-blur' ? 'Background blur' : 'Layer blur')).slice(0, 80),
    enabled: source.enabled !== false,
    type: source.type === 'background-blur' ? 'background-blur' : 'layer-blur',
    amount: clamp(Number(source.amount || 0), 0, 160)
  };
}

function legacyStrokeInput(element = {}, existing = {}) {
  const effectStroke = element.effect?.stroke;
  const useEffectStroke = !!effectStroke && !existing.stroke;
  const stroke = useEffectStroke ? effectStroke : element.stroke;
  const strokeWidth = useEffectStroke
    ? Number(element.effect?.strokeWidth || 0)
    : Number(element.strokeWidth || 0);

  return {
    legacy: {
      stroke: stroke || 'transparent',
      strokeWidth
    },
    layer: {
      name: 'Stroke',
      enabled: !!stroke && stroke !== 'transparent' && strokeWidth > 0,
      color: stroke && stroke !== 'transparent' ? stroke : '#111827',
      width: strokeWidth
    }
  };
}

function repairGeometryLeakedStroke(rawStrokes, element, snapshot, fallbackLayer) {
  if (!snapshot || !rawStrokes.length) return rawStrokes;

  const first = rawStrokes[0];
  if (!first || typeof first !== 'object') return rawStrokes;

  const storedWidth = Number(first.width || 0);
  const intendedWidth = Number(snapshot.strokeWidth || 0);

  // Older builds passed the entire element object into normalizeStroke().
  // Because elements also have a `width` field, that geometry width became
  // the outline width (for example, a 676px text box produced a 676px stroke).
  // The generated layer also inherited the element name, which gives us a
  // reliable migration signal without modifying legitimate custom strokes.
  const looksLikeGeometryLeak =
    first.name === element.name &&
    storedWidth > Math.max(32, intendedWidth * 8) &&
    storedWidth !== intendedWidth;

  if (!looksLikeGeometryLeak) return rawStrokes;
  return [{ ...first, ...fallbackLayer }, ...rawStrokes.slice(1)];
}

export function normalizeAppearance(element = {}) {
  const existing = element.appearance && typeof element.appearance === 'object' ? element.appearance : {};
  const transparentByDefault = ['image', 'line', 'path', 'chart', 'table', 'qrcode'].includes(element.type);
  const fallbackFill = element.type === 'text' ? '#111827' : element.fill || '#4f46e5';
  const sourceFill = existing.fill ?? element.fill ?? (transparentByDefault ? { type: 'none' } : fallbackFill);
  const legacyShadow = element.effect?.shadow || null;
  const strokeInput = legacyStrokeInput(element, existing);
  const legacyStroke = strokeInput.legacy;
  const snapshot = existing.legacySnapshot && typeof existing.legacySnapshot === 'object' ? existing.legacySnapshot : null;
  const changed = (value, previous) => snapshot && JSON.stringify(value ?? null) !== JSON.stringify(previous ?? null);

  let rawFills = Array.isArray(existing.fills) && existing.fills.length ? existing.fills : [sourceFill];
  let rawStrokes = Array.isArray(existing.strokes) && existing.strokes.length
    ? existing.strokes
    : [existing.stroke ?? strokeInput.layer];
  let rawShadows = Array.isArray(existing.shadows) && existing.shadows.length ? existing.shadows : [existing.shadow ?? legacyShadow ?? {}];

  rawStrokes = repairGeometryLeakedStroke(rawStrokes, element, snapshot, strokeInput.layer);

  if (changed(element.fill, snapshot?.fill)) {
    rawFills = [...rawFills];
    rawFills[0] = { ...(rawFills[0] && typeof rawFills[0] === 'object' && 'paint' in rawFills[0] ? rawFills[0] : {}), paint: element.fill };
  }
  if (changed(element.stroke, snapshot?.stroke) || changed(element.strokeWidth, snapshot?.strokeWidth)) {
    rawStrokes = [...rawStrokes];
    rawStrokes[0] = { ...(rawStrokes[0] && typeof rawStrokes[0] === 'object' ? rawStrokes[0] : {}), enabled: element.stroke !== 'transparent' && Number(element.strokeWidth || 0) > 0, color: element.stroke || '#111827', width: Number(element.strokeWidth || 0) };
  }
  if (changed(legacyShadow, snapshot?.effectShadow)) {
    rawShadows = [...rawShadows];
    rawShadows[0] = legacyShadow ? { ...(rawShadows[0] || {}), ...legacyShadow, enabled: true, type: 'drop' } : { ...(rawShadows[0] || {}), enabled: false };
  }

  const fills = rawFills.map(value => normalizeFillLayer(value, fallbackFill)).slice(0, 12);
  const strokes = rawStrokes.map(value => normalizeStroke(value, legacyStroke)).slice(0, 12);
  const shadows = rawShadows.map(value => normalizeShadow(value, legacyShadow)).slice(0, 12);
  const effects = (Array.isArray(existing.effects) ? existing.effects : []).map(normalizeEffect).slice(0, 12);
  const primaryFill = fills.find(layer => layer.enabled) || fills[0] || normalizeFillLayer(sourceFill, fallbackFill);
  const primaryStroke = strokes.find(layer => layer.enabled) || strokes[0] || normalizeStroke({}, legacyStroke);
  const primaryShadow = shadows.find(layer => layer.enabled) || shadows[0] || normalizeShadow({}, legacyShadow);
  return {
    fills,
    strokes,
    shadows,
    effects,
    fill: primaryFill.paint,
    stroke: primaryStroke,
    shadow: primaryShadow,
    blendMode: BLEND_MODES.some(([id]) => id === existing.blendMode) ? existing.blendMode : 'source-over',
    legacySnapshot: {
      fill: element.fill ?? null,
      stroke: element.stroke ?? null,
      strokeWidth: element.strokeWidth ?? null,
      effectShadow: legacyShadow
    }
  };
}

export function paintPrimaryColor(paint, fallback = '#4f46e5') {
  const normalized = normalizePaint(paint, fallback);
  if (normalized.type === 'solid') return normalized.color;
  if (normalized.type === 'pattern') return normalized.foreground;
  return normalized.stops?.[0]?.color || fallback;
}

export function paintToCss(paint, fallback = '#ffffff') {
  const value = normalizePaint(paint, fallback);
  if (value.type === 'none') return 'transparent';
  if (value.type === 'solid') return colorWithOpacity(value.color, value.opacity);
  if (value.type === 'linear') return `linear-gradient(${value.angle}deg, ${value.stops.map(stop => `${colorWithOpacity(stop.color, stop.opacity)} ${Math.round(stop.offset * 100)}%`).join(', ')})`;
  if (value.type === 'radial') return `radial-gradient(circle at ${Math.round(value.centerX * 100)}% ${Math.round(value.centerY * 100)}%, ${value.stops.map(stop => `${colorWithOpacity(stop.color, stop.opacity)} ${Math.round(stop.offset * 100)}%`).join(', ')})`;
  const fg = colorWithOpacity(value.foreground, value.foregroundOpacity);
  const bg = colorWithOpacity(value.background, value.backgroundOpacity);
  const size = Math.max(8, value.scale);
  if (value.pattern === 'dots') return `radial-gradient(${fg} ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px, ${bg} ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px) 0 0/${size}px ${size}px`;
  if (value.pattern === 'grid') return `linear-gradient(${fg} ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px, transparent ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px), linear-gradient(90deg, ${fg} ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px, ${bg} ${Math.max(1, value.lineWidth)}px) 0 0/${size}px ${size}px`;
  if (value.pattern === 'checker') return `conic-gradient(${fg} 25%, ${bg} 0 50%, ${fg} 0 75%, ${bg} 0) 0 0/${size}px ${size}px`;
  return `repeating-linear-gradient(${value.angle}deg, ${fg} 0 ${value.lineWidth}px, ${bg} ${value.lineWidth}px ${Math.max(value.lineWidth + 1, value.spacing)}px)`;
}

export function strokeDashArray(stroke) {
  const value = normalizeStroke(stroke);
  if (!value.enabled || value.style === 'solid') return null;
  if (value.style === 'dotted') return [Math.max(1, value.width), Math.max(value.width * 2, value.gap)];
  return [value.dash, value.gap];
}

export function collectDocumentColors(document) {
  const colors = new Set();
  const addPaint = paint => {
    const value = normalizePaint(paint);
    if (value.type === 'solid') colors.add(value.color);
    else if (value.type === 'pattern') { colors.add(value.foreground); colors.add(value.background); }
    else value.stops?.forEach(stop => colors.add(stop.color));
  };
  for (const page of document?.pages || []) {
    addPaint(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background);
    for (const element of page.elements || []) {
      const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
      appearance.fills.filter(layer => layer.enabled).forEach(layer => addPaint(layer.paint));
      appearance.strokes.filter(layer => layer.enabled).forEach(layer => colors.add(layer.color));
      appearance.shadows.filter(layer => layer.enabled).forEach(layer => colors.add(layer.color));
      if (element.type === 'chart') (element.options?.colors || []).forEach(color => colors.add(normalizeHex(color)));
      if (element.type === 'table') ['headerFill', 'headerText', 'cellFill', 'alternateFill', 'textColor', 'borderColor'].forEach(key => element.options?.[key] && colors.add(normalizeHex(element.options[key])));
    }
  }
  return [...colors].slice(0, 32);
}

export const APP_NAME = 'Design Commons';
export const APP_SLUG = 'design-commons';
export const LEGACY_APP_NAME = 'CanvasForge';
export const LEGACY_APP_SLUG = 'canvasforge';

export const STORAGE_KEYS = {
  session: `${APP_SLUG}-session`,
  organization: `${APP_SLUG}-org`,
  workspace: `${APP_SLUG}-workspace`,
  clipboard: `${APP_SLUG}-clipboard`,
  style: `${APP_SLUG}-style`,
  appearanceStyles: `${APP_SLUG}-appearance-styles`,
  recentTools: `${APP_SLUG}-recent-tools`,
  recentColors: `${APP_SLUG}-recent-colors`,
  presetFavourites: `${APP_SLUG}-preset-favourites`,
  presetRecents: `${APP_SLUG}-preset-recents`
};

export const LEGACY_STORAGE_KEYS = {
  session: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-session`,
  organization: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-org`,
  workspace: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-workspace`,
  clipboard: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-clipboard`,
  style: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-style`,
  appearanceStyles: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-appearance-styles`,
  recentTools: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-recent-tools`,
  recentColors: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-recent-colors`,
  presetFavourites: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-preset-favourites`,
  presetRecents: `${LEGACY_APP_SLUG}-preset-recents`
};

export const CLIPBOARD_PREFIX = 'DESIGN_COMMONS:';
export const LEGACY_CLIPBOARD_PREFIX = 'CANVASFORGE:';
export const ASSET_DRAG_TYPE = 'application/x-design-commons-asset';
export const LEGACY_ASSET_DRAG_TYPE = 'application/x-canvasforge-asset';
export const LAYER_DRAG_TYPE = 'application/x-design-commons-layer';
export const LEGACY_LAYER_DRAG_TYPE = 'application/x-canvasforge-layer';
export const ESCAPE_EVENT = 'design-commons:escape';
export const LEGACY_ESCAPE_EVENT = 'canvasforge:escape';

export function readMigratedStorage(name, fallback = '') {
  const key = STORAGE_KEYS[name];
  const legacyKey = LEGACY_STORAGE_KEYS[name];
  if (!key) return fallback;
  const current = localStorage.getItem(key);
  if (current != null) return current;
  const legacy = legacyKey ? localStorage.getItem(legacyKey) : null;
  if (legacy != null) {
    localStorage.setItem(key, legacy);
    return legacy;
  }
  return fallback;
}

export function writeStorage(name, value) {
  const key = STORAGE_KEYS[name];
  if (!key) return;
  if (value == null) localStorage.removeItem(key);
  else localStorage.setItem(key, String(value));
}

export function removeStorage(name, { includeLegacy = true } = {}) {
  const key = STORAGE_KEYS[name];
  if (key) localStorage.removeItem(key);
  if (includeLegacy && LEGACY_STORAGE_KEYS[name]) localStorage.removeItem(LEGACY_STORAGE_KEYS[name]);
}

export function designFileName(title = 'design') {
  const slug = String(title || 'design').replace(/[^a-z0-9_-]+/gi, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').toLowerCase();
  return slug || `${APP_SLUG}-design`;
}

// FILE: src/lib/commons.js

export const COMMONS_RIGHTS_BASES = [
  { id: 'original', label: 'I created this work and own the rights' },
  { id: 'client-authorized', label: 'The rights holder authorized me to share it' },
  { id: 'licensed', label: 'I have a licence that allows redistribution' },
  { id: 'public-domain', label: 'The work is in the public domain' }
];

export const COMMONS_LICENSES = [
  { id: 'canvasforge-standard', label: 'CanvasForge standard asset licence' },
  { id: 'cc0', label: 'CC0 / public domain dedication' },
  { id: 'cc-by-4.0', label: 'Creative Commons Attribution 4.0' },
  { id: 'cc-by-sa-4.0', label: 'Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 4.0' },
  { id: 'custom', label: 'Custom licence' }
];

const clean = (value, max = 1000) => String(value ?? '').trim().slice(0, max);

export function normalizeCommonsRights(input = {}) {
  return {
    basis: COMMONS_RIGHTS_BASES.some(item => item.id === input.basis) ? input.basis : 'original',
    copyrightOwner: clean(input.copyrightOwner, 240),
    sourceUrl: clean(input.sourceUrl, 2000),
    licenceId: COMMONS_LICENSES.some(item => item.id === input.licenceId) ? input.licenceId : 'canvasforge-standard',
    customLicence: clean(input.customLicence, 2000),
    attribution: clean(input.attribution, 500),
    evidenceNote: clean(input.evidenceNote, 2000),
    ownsRights: input.ownsRights === true,
    allowsRedistribution: input.allowsRedistribution === true,
    noRestrictedContent: input.noRestrictedContent === true,
    acceptsTakedown: input.acceptsTakedown === true,
    attestedAt: input.attestedAt || null,
    contentHash: clean(input.contentHash, 256)
  };
}

export function validateCommonsRights(input = {}) {
  const rights = normalizeCommonsRights(input);
  const errors = [];
  if (!rights.copyrightOwner && rights.basis !== 'public-domain') errors.push('Enter the copyright owner or rights holder.');
  if (['licensed', 'client-authorized', 'public-domain'].includes(rights.basis) && !rights.sourceUrl) errors.push('Provide a source or licence URL for this rights basis.');
  if (rights.licenceId === 'custom' && !rights.customLicence) errors.push('Describe the custom licence terms.');
  if (!rights.ownsRights) errors.push('Confirm that you own the rights or have permission to publish the work.');
  if (!rights.allowsRedistribution) errors.push('Confirm that the rights allow other people to reuse the asset.');
  if (!rights.noRestrictedContent) errors.push('Confirm that the asset does not contain restricted third-party content.');
  if (!rights.acceptsTakedown) errors.push('Accept the Commons takedown and dispute process.');
  return { valid: errors.length === 0, errors, rights };
}

export function buildCommonsListingPayload(input = {}, rightsInput = {}) {
  const validation = validateCommonsRights(rightsInput);
  if (!validation.valid) throw new Error(validation.errors.join(' '));
  const rights = { ...validation.rights, attestedAt: validation.rights.attestedAt || new Date().toISOString() };
  return {
    title: clean(input.title, 200),
    description: clean(input.description, 5000),
    priceType: Number(input.priceCredits || 0) > 0 ? 'credits' : 'free',
    priceCredits: Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(input.priceCredits || 0))),
    tags: Array.isArray(input.tags) ? input.tags.map(tag => clean(tag, 80)).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 40) : [],
    licenceId: rights.licenceId,
    attribution: rights.attribution,
    rightsDeclaration: rights,
    moderationStatus: 'pending_review'
  };
}

// FILE: src/lib/designSystem.js

import { normalizeAppearance, normalizePaint, paintPrimaryColor, solidPaint } from './appearance.js';

const clone = value => structuredClone(value);
const id = prefix => `${prefix}-${globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID?.() || `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(16).slice(2)}`}`;
const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, Number(value)));

export const DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS = ['text', 'color', 'effect', 'stroke', 'spacing', 'radius', 'grid'];
export const ELEMENT_STYLE_REF_FIELDS = {
  text: 'textStyleId',
  color: 'fillStyleId',
  effect: 'effectStyleId',
  stroke: 'strokeStyleId',
  spacing: 'spacingStyleId',
  radius: 'radiusStyleId'
};

export const DEFAULT_PRINT_SETTINGS = {
  trim: { width: null, height: null },
  bleed: { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 },
  safeArea: { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 },
  slug: { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 },
  marks: { crop: false, registration: false, colorBars: false, pageInformation: false },
  colorSpace: 'rgb',
  iccProfile: 'sRGB IEC61966-2.1',
  pdfPreset: 'screen',
  embedFonts: true,
  outlineFonts: false,
  flattenTransparency: false,
  overprintPreview: false,
  minimumEffectiveDpi: 150
};

export const DEFAULT_DESIGN_SYSTEM = {
  tokens: {
    colors: {},
    spacing: { xs: 4, sm: 8, md: 16, lg: 24, xl: 32, '2xl': 48 },
    radii: { none: 0, sm: 4, md: 8, lg: 16, xl: 24, pill: 999 },
    typography: {},
    effects: {}
  },
  styles: { text: [], color: [], effect: [], stroke: [], spacing: [], radius: [], grid: [] }
};

function normalizeInsets(value = {}) {
  if (typeof value === 'number') return { top: Math.max(0, value), right: Math.max(0, value), bottom: Math.max(0, value), left: Math.max(0, value) };
  return {
    top: Math.max(0, Number(value?.top || 0)),
    right: Math.max(0, Number(value?.right || 0)),
    bottom: Math.max(0, Number(value?.bottom || 0)),
    left: Math.max(0, Number(value?.left || 0))
  };
}

export function normalizePrintSettings(value = {}, width = null, height = null) {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : {};
  return {
    ...DEFAULT_PRINT_SETTINGS,
    ...source,
    trim: {
      width: Number(source.trim?.width) > 0 ? Number(source.trim.width) : width,
      height: Number(source.trim?.height) > 0 ? Number(source.trim.height) : height
    },
    bleed: normalizeInsets(source.bleed),
    safeArea: normalizeInsets(source.safeArea),
    slug: normalizeInsets(source.slug),
    marks: { ...DEFAULT_PRINT_SETTINGS.marks, ...(source.marks || {}) },
    colorSpace: ['rgb', 'cmyk', 'spot'].includes(source.colorSpace) ? source.colorSpace : 'rgb',
    pdfPreset: ['screen', 'print', 'pdf-x-1a', 'pdf-x-3', 'pdf-x-4'].includes(source.pdfPreset) ? source.pdfPreset : 'screen',
    minimumEffectiveDpi: clamp(source.minimumEffectiveDpi ?? 150, 36, 2400)
  };
}

function normalizeStyle(kind, style = {}) {
  const value = style.value && typeof style.value === 'object' ? clone(style.value) : {};
  if (kind === 'color') value.paint = normalizePaint(value.paint ?? value.fill ?? style.paint ?? style.fill ?? '#111827');
  if (kind === 'effect' && value.appearance) value.appearance = normalizeAppearance({ appearance: value.appearance });
  if (kind === 'spacing') value.padding = normalizeInsets(value.padding ?? value);
  if (kind === 'radius') value.radius = Math.max(0, Number(value.radius ?? style.radius ?? 0));
  return {
    id: String(style.id || id(`style-${kind}`)),
    name: String(style.name || `${kind[0].toUpperCase()}${kind.slice(1)} style`).slice(0, 160),
    kind,
    description: String(style.description || '').slice(0, 500),
    semanticRole: String(style.semanticRole || '').slice(0, 100),
    value
  };
}

export function normalizeDesignSystem(value = {}) {
  const source = value && typeof value === 'object' ? value : {};
  const styles = {};
  for (const kind of DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS) styles[kind] = (source.styles?.[kind] || []).map(style => normalizeStyle(kind, style));
  return {
    tokens: {
      colors: { ...(source.tokens?.colors || {}) },
      spacing: { ...DEFAULT_DESIGN_SYSTEM.tokens.spacing, ...(source.tokens?.spacing || {}) },
      radii: { ...DEFAULT_DESIGN_SYSTEM.tokens.radii, ...(source.tokens?.radii || {}) },
      typography: { ...(source.tokens?.typography || {}) },
      effects: { ...(source.tokens?.effects || {}) }
    },
    styles
  };
}

export function findDesignStyle(designSystem, kind, styleId) {
  if (!styleId) return null;
  return designSystem?.styles?.[kind]?.find(style => style.id === styleId) || null;
}

export function resolveLinkedElementStyle(element, designSystem) {
  if (!element || !designSystem) return element;
  const text = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'text', element.textStyleId);
  const color = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'color', element.fillStyleId);
  const effect = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'effect', element.effectStyleId);
  const stroke = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'stroke', element.strokeStyleId);
  const spacing = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'spacing', element.spacingStyleId);
  const radius = findDesignStyle(designSystem, 'radius', element.radiusStyleId);
  if (text) Object.assign(element, clone(text.value));
  if (color) {
    const paint = normalizePaint(color.value.paint ?? color.value.fill ?? '#111827');
    element.fill = paint.type === 'none' ? 'transparent' : paintPrimaryColor(paint, element.fill || '#111827');
    const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
    appearance.fills[0] = { ...(appearance.fills[0] || {}), enabled: paint.type !== 'none', paint };
    appearance.fill = paint;
    element.appearance = appearance;
  }
  if (effect?.value?.appearance) element.appearance = normalizeAppearance({ ...element, appearance: effect.value.appearance });
  if (effect?.value?.effect) element.effect = { ...(element.effect || {}), ...clone(effect.value.effect) };
  if (stroke) {
    const value = stroke.value || {};
    element.stroke = value.color || value.stroke || 'transparent';
    element.strokeWidth = Math.max(0, Number(value.width ?? value.strokeWidth ?? 0));
    const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
    appearance.strokes[0] = { ...(appearance.strokes[0] || {}), enabled: element.strokeWidth > 0 && element.stroke !== 'transparent', color: element.stroke, width: element.strokeWidth, opacity: value.opacity ?? 1, style: value.style || 'solid' };
    appearance.stroke = appearance.strokes[0];
    element.appearance = appearance;
  }
  if (spacing) {
    const padding = normalizeInsets(spacing.value?.padding ?? spacing.value);
    if (element.type === 'frame') element.layout = { ...(element.layout || {}), padding };
    else element.internalPadding = padding;
  }
  if (radius) element.radius = Math.max(0, Number(radius.value?.radius || 0));
  return element;
}

export function applyLinkedStyles(document) {
  const designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
  document.designSystem = designSystem;
  for (const page of document.pages || []) for (const element of page.elements || []) resolveLinkedElementStyle(element, designSystem);
  return document;
}

export function upsertDesignStyle(document, kind, input = {}) {
  if (!DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS.includes(kind)) throw new Error(`Unsupported design style kind: ${kind}.`);
  document.designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
  const style = normalizeStyle(kind, input);
  const list = document.designSystem.styles[kind];
  const index = list.findIndex(item => item.id === style.id);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = style;
  else list.push(style);
  applyLinkedStyles(document);
  return style;
}

export function deleteDesignStyle(document, kind, styleId, { detach = true } = {}) {
  document.designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
  document.designSystem.styles[kind] = document.designSystem.styles[kind].filter(style => style.id !== styleId);
  const refField = ELEMENT_STYLE_REF_FIELDS[kind];
  if (detach && refField) for (const page of document.pages || []) for (const element of page.elements || []) if (element[refField] === styleId) element[refField] = null;
  return document;
}

export function attachDesignStyle(document, elements, kind, styleId) {
  const refField = ELEMENT_STYLE_REF_FIELDS[kind];
  if (!refField) throw new Error(`Style kind ${kind} cannot be attached to elements.`);
  const style = findDesignStyle(normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem), kind, styleId);
  if (!style) throw new Error(`Design style not found: ${styleId}.`);
  for (const element of elements || []) { element[refField] = styleId; resolveLinkedElementStyle(element, document.designSystem); }
  return document;
}

function stable(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return `[${value.map(stable).join(',')}]`;
  if (value && typeof value === 'object') return `{${Object.keys(value).sort().map(key => `${key}:${stable(value[key])}`).join(',')}}`;
  return JSON.stringify(value);
}

export function findDuplicateDesignStyles(document) {
  const system = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
  const groups = [];
  for (const kind of DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS) {
    const byValue = new Map();
    for (const style of system.styles[kind]) {
      const key = stable(style.value);
      if (!byValue.has(key)) byValue.set(key, []);
      byValue.get(key).push(style);
    }
    for (const styles of byValue.values()) if (styles.length > 1) groups.push({ kind, canonical: styles[0], duplicates: styles.slice(1) });
  }
  return groups;
}

export function mergeDuplicateDesignStyles(document) {
  document.designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(document.designSystem);
  const groups = findDuplicateDesignStyles(document);
  for (const group of groups) {
    const refField = ELEMENT_STYLE_REF_FIELDS[group.kind];
    const duplicateIds = new Set(group.duplicates.map(style => style.id));
    if (refField) for (const page of document.pages || []) for (const element of page.elements || []) if (duplicateIds.has(element[refField])) element[refField] = group.canonical.id;
    document.designSystem.styles[group.kind] = document.designSystem.styles[group.kind].filter(style => !duplicateIds.has(style.id));
  }
  applyLinkedStyles(document);
  return { document, groups };
}

export function normalizeDataSources(value = []) {
  return (Array.isArray(value) ? value : []).map(source => {
    const rows = Array.isArray(source.rows) ? source.rows.map(row => ({ ...(row || {}) })) : [];
    const columns = Array.isArray(source.columns) && source.columns.length ? source.columns.map(String) : [...new Set(rows.flatMap(row => Object.keys(row)))];
    return { id: String(source.id || id('data')), name: String(source.name || 'Data source').slice(0, 160), columns, rows };
  });
}

function templateValue(template, row) {
  return String(template ?? '').replace(/\{\{\s*([^}]+?)\s*\}\}/g, (_, key) => row?.[key] == null ? '' : String(row[key]));
}

export function applyDataBindings(document) {
  document.dataSources = normalizeDataSources(document.dataSources);
  const sources = new Map(document.dataSources.map(source => [source.id, source]));
  for (const page of document.pages || []) for (const element of page.elements || []) {
    const binding = element.dataBinding;
    if (!binding?.sourceId) continue;
    const source = sources.get(binding.sourceId);
    const row = source?.rows?.[Math.max(0, Number(binding.row || 0))];
    if (!row) continue;
    if (element.type === 'text') element.text = binding.template ? templateValue(binding.template, row) : String(row[binding.key] ?? element.text ?? '');
    if (element.type === 'image' && binding.key && row[binding.key]) element.src = String(row[binding.key]);
  }
  return document;
}

export function createDataSource(document, input = {}) {
  document.dataSources = normalizeDataSources(document.dataSources);
  const source = normalizeDataSources([{ ...input, id: input.id || id('data') }])[0];
  const index = document.dataSources.findIndex(item => item.id === source.id);
  if (index >= 0) document.dataSources[index] = source; else document.dataSources.push(source);
  return source;
}

export function designStyleSchema() {
  return {
    kinds: DESIGN_STYLE_KINDS,
    elementReferenceFields: ELEMENT_STYLE_REF_FIELDS,
    style: { id: 'string', name: 'string', kind: 'text|color|effect|stroke|spacing|radius|grid', semanticRole: 'string', value: 'kind-specific object' },
    examples: {
      text: { name: 'Menu item title', kind: 'text', value: { fontFamily: 'DM Serif Display', fontSize: 31, fontWeight: 700, lineHeight: 1.05 } },
      color: { name: 'Text primary', kind: 'color', value: { paint: solidPaint('#231f20') } },
      spacing: { name: 'Card padding', kind: 'spacing', value: { padding: { top: 24, right: 24, bottom: 24, left: 24 } } },
      radius: { name: 'Card radius', kind: 'radius', value: { radius: 22 } }
    }
  };
}

================================================================================

import { normalizeAppearance, normalizePaint, paintPrimaryColor, solidPaint } from './appearance.js';
import { DEFAULT_SVG_MARKUP, sanitizeSvgMarkup, svgDataUrl } from './svg.js';
import {
  applyDataBindings, applyLinkedStyles, DEFAULT_DESIGN_SYSTEM, DEFAULT_PRINT_SETTINGS,
  normalizeDataSources, normalizeDesignSystem, normalizePrintSettings, resolveLinkedElementStyle
} from './designSystem.js';

export const uuid = () => {
  if (typeof crypto?.randomUUID === 'function') return crypto.randomUUID();
  return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, char => {
    const value = Math.random() * 16 | 0;
    return (char === 'x' ? value : value & 3 | 8).toString(16);
  });
};
export const clone = value => structuredClone(value);
const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, Number(value)));

export const DEFAULT_CONSTRAINTS = { horizontal: 'scale', vertical: 'scale', maintainAspectRatio: false };
export const AI_ELEMENT_ROLES = ['headline', 'subheadline', 'body', 'caption', 'price', 'call-to-action', 'logo', 'hero-image', 'background-image', 'decoration', 'legal', 'chart-title', 'chart-data', 'container', 'item-name', 'item-description', 'item-price', 'badge', 'divider', 'footer', 'header', 'illustration'];
export const LAYOUT_SIZING_MODES = ['fixed', 'hug', 'fill'];

export function defaultRegions(width = 1080, height = 1080) {
  const margin = Math.round(Math.min(width, height) * .055);
  return {
    safe: { x: margin, y: margin, width: Math.max(1, width - margin * 2), height: Math.max(1, height - margin * 2) },
    header: { x: margin, y: margin, width: Math.max(1, width - margin * 2), height: Math.round(height * .16) },
    hero: { x: margin, y: Math.round(height * .18), width: Math.max(1, width - margin * 2), height: Math.round(height * .46) },
    content: { x: margin, y: Math.round(height * .2), width: Math.max(1, width - margin * 2), height: Math.round(height * .62) },
    footer: { x: margin, y: Math.round(height * .84), width: Math.max(1, width - margin * 2), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(height * .11)) },
    full: { x: 0, y: 0, width, height }
  };
}

export function defaultDocument(width = 1080, height = 1080) {
  return {
    schemaVersion: 5,
    title: 'Untitled design',
    width,
    height,
    unit: 'px',
    dpi: 96,
    layoutGroups: [],
    localComponents: [],
    designSystem: clone(DEFAULT_DESIGN_SYSTEM),
    print: { ...clone(DEFAULT_PRINT_SETTINGS), trim: { width, height } },
    dataSources: [],
    ai: { lastRunId: null, lastRenderUrl: null },
    pages: [{
      id: uuid(), name: 'Page 1', background: '#ffffff', backgroundPaint: solidPaint('#ffffff'), transparentBackground: false,
      grid: { enabled: false, size: 20, subdivisions: 1 }, designGrids: [], baselineGrids: [], margins: { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 },
      guides: { vertical: [], horizontal: [], locked: false }, regions: defaultRegions(width, height), elements: []
    }]
  };
}

export function normalizeLayout(layout = {}) {
  const source = layout && typeof layout === 'object' ? layout : {};
  const rawPadding = source.padding ?? 32;
  const padding = typeof rawPadding === 'object'
    ? {
        top: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding.top ?? 0)),
        right: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding.right ?? 0)),
        bottom: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding.bottom ?? 0)),
        left: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding.left ?? 0))
      }
    : { top: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding)), right: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding)), bottom: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding)), left: Math.max(0, Number(rawPadding)) };
  return {
    enabled: source.enabled !== false,
    direction: source.direction === 'horizontal' ? 'horizontal' : 'vertical',
    gap: Math.max(0, Number(source.gap ?? 24)),
    rowGap: Math.max(0, Number(source.rowGap ?? source.gap ?? 24)),
    columnGap: Math.max(0, Number(source.columnGap ?? source.gap ?? 24)),
    padding,
    align: ['start', 'center', 'end', 'stretch'].includes(source.align) ? source.align : 'start',
    justify: ['start', 'center', 'end', 'space-between'].includes(source.justify) ? source.justify : 'start',
    wrap: !!source.wrap,
    widthMode: LAYOUT_SIZING_MODES.includes(source.widthMode) ? source.widthMode : 'fixed',
    heightMode: LAYOUT_SIZING_MODES.includes(source.heightMode) ? source.heightMode : 'fixed'
  };
}

export function baseElement(type, overrides = {}) {
  const element = {
    id: uuid(), type, name: type[0].toUpperCase() + type.slice(1), semanticName: '', role: '', tags: [], contentKey: '',
    aiEditable: true, userLocked: false, parentId: null, groupId: null, layoutRegion: '', createdBy: 'user', sourceId: null,
    x: 120, y: 120, width: 320, height: 180, rotation: 0, opacity: 1, flipX: false, flipY: false,
    locked: false, hidden: false, zIndex: 0, constraints: { ...DEFAULT_CONSTRAINTS },
    layoutSizing: { width: 'fixed', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'auto' },
    textStyleId: null, fillStyleId: null, effectStyleId: null, strokeStyleId: null, spacingStyleId: null, radiusStyleId: null,
    dataBinding: null, componentPropertyId: null, componentVariant: null,
    ...overrides
  };
  element.appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  return element;
}

export function imageFrameElement(overrides = {}) { const placeholder = svgDataUrl('<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 600 400"><rect width="600" height="400" fill="#f3f4f6"/><path d="M175 275l72-82 62 65 48-46 88 93H155z" fill="#cbd5e1"/><circle cx="390" cy="125" r="34" fill="#cbd5e1"/><rect x="12" y="12" width="576" height="376" rx="24" fill="none" stroke="#94a3b8" stroke-width="8" stroke-dasharray="18 14"/></svg>'); return imageElement({ original_name: 'Image frame', url: placeholder, width: 600, height: 400 }, { name: 'Image frame', role: 'hero-image', width: 420, height: 300, isImageFrame: true, frameLabel: 'Drop an image', mask: 'rounded', radius: 24, ...overrides }); }
