export function shapeElement(shapeKind = 'triangle', overrides = {}) {
  const labels = { triangle: 'Triangle', diamond: 'Diamond', pentagon: 'Pentagon', hexagon: 'Hexagon', star: 'Star', burst: 'Burst', heart: 'Heart', arrow: 'Arrow', chevron: 'Chevron', speech: 'Speech bubble' };
  return baseElement('shape', { name: labels[shapeKind] || 'Shape', shapeKind, width: 320, height: 260, fill: '#4f46e5', stroke: 'transparent', strokeWidth: 0, radius: 0, shapeOptions: { sides: shapeKind === 'pentagon' ? 5 : shapeKind === 'hexagon' ? 6 : 5, innerRatio: shapeKind === 'burst' ? .68 : .46, points: shapeKind === 'burst' ? 12 : 5, tailPosition: .28 }, ...overrides });
}

function normalizeElement(element, index) {
  element.id ||= uuid();
  element.zIndex = Number.isFinite(element.zIndex) ? element.zIndex : index;
  element.opacity ??= 1; element.rotation ??= 0; element.flipX ??= false; element.flipY ??= false;
  element.locked ??= false; element.hidden ??= false;
  element.constraints = { ...DEFAULT_CONSTRAINTS, ...(element.constraints || {}) };
  element.layoutSizing = { width: 'fixed', height: 'fixed', grow: 0, alignSelf: 'auto', ...(element.layoutSizing || {}) };
  element.semanticName = String(element.semanticName || '').slice(0, 500);
  element.role = String(element.role || '').slice(0, 100);
  element.tags = Array.isArray(element.tags) ? element.tags.map(tag => String(tag).slice(0, 100)).slice(0, 50) : [];
  element.contentKey = String(element.contentKey || '').slice(0, 200);
  element.aiEditable = element.aiEditable !== false; element.userLocked = !!element.userLocked;
  element.parentId ||= null; element.groupId ||= null; element.layoutRegion = String(element.layoutRegion || '').slice(0, 100);
  element.createdBy ||= 'user'; element.sourceId ||= null;
  for (const key of ['textStyleId', 'fillStyleId', 'effectStyleId', 'strokeStyleId', 'spacingStyleId', 'radiusStyleId', 'componentPropertyId', 'componentVariant']) element[key] ||= null;
  if (element.dataBinding && typeof element.dataBinding !== 'object') element.dataBinding = null;
  element.appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  if (element.type === 'frame') { element.layout = normalizeLayout(element.layout); element.clipChildren ??= false; }
  if (element.type === 'text') { element.styles ||= {}; element.links ||= []; element.effect ||= { shadow: null, stroke: null, strokeWidth: 0, hollow: false, curve: 0 }; element.lineHeight ??= 1.16; element.charSpacing ??= 0; element.textAlign ||= 'left'; element.listType ||= 'none'; element.autoFit ??= false; element.minFontSize = clamp(element.minFontSize || 8, 4, 1000); element.maxLines = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(element.maxLines || 0))); element.overflowBehavior = ['visible', 'clip', 'ellipsis'].includes(element.overflowBehavior) ? element.overflowBehavior : 'visible'; element.verticalAlign = ['top', 'middle', 'bottom'].includes(element.verticalAlign) ? element.verticalAlign : 'top'; element.columns = clamp(element.columns || 1, 1, 12); element.columnGap = Math.max(0, Number(element.columnGap ?? 24)); element.hyphenation = !!element.hyphenation; element.widowLines = clamp(element.widowLines ?? 2, 1, 10); element.orphanLines = clamp(element.orphanLines ?? 2, 1, 10); element.hangingPunctuation = !!element.hangingPunctuation; element.opticalMargin = !!element.opticalMargin; element.baselineGridStep = Math.max(0, Number(element.baselineGridStep || 0)); element.opentypeFeatures = String(element.opentypeFeatures || '').slice(0, 300); element.variableAxes = element.variableAxes && typeof element.variableAxes === 'object' ? element.variableAxes : {}; element.textPath = element.textPath && typeof element.textPath === 'object' ? element.textPath : null; }
  if (element.type === 'image') { element.isImageFrame = !!element.isImageFrame; element.frameLabel = String(element.frameLabel || 'Drop an image').slice(0, 120); element.cropX ??= null; element.cropY ??= null; element.cropZoom ??= 1; element.cropAnchorX ??= .5; element.cropAnchorY ??= .5; element.mask ||= 'rect'; element.filters = { brightness: 0, contrast: 0, saturation: 0, hue: 0, blur: 0, vibrance: 0, noise: 0, pixelate: 0, gamma: 1, tint: '#ffffff', tintOpacity: 0, grayscale: false, sepia: false, ...(element.filters || {}) }; }
  if (element.type === 'shape') { element.shapeKind ||= 'triangle'; element.shapeOptions = { sides: 5, innerRatio: .46, points: 5, tailPosition: .28, ...(element.shapeOptions || {}) }; }
  if (element.type === 'path') { element.pathData = Array.isArray(element.pathData) ? element.pathData : []; element.brush = { preset: 'pen', smoothing: .5, pressure: true, ...(element.brush || {}) }; }
  if (element.type === 'chart') { element.data ||= { labels: [], series: [] }; element.options ||= {}; element.chartType ||= 'bar'; }
  if (element.type === 'table') { element.rows ??= element.cells?.length || 2; element.columns ??= element.cells?.[0]?.length || 2; element.cells ||= Array.from({ length: element.rows }, () => Array(element.columns).fill('')); element.options ||= {}; }
  if (element.type === 'qrcode') { element.value ||= 'https://example.com'; element.foreground ||= '#111827'; element.background ||= '#ffffff'; element.errorCorrection ||= 'M'; element.margin ??= 2; }
  if (element.type === 'svg') { try { element.svg = sanitizeSvgMarkup(element.svg || DEFAULT_SVG_MARKUP); } catch { element.svg = DEFAULT_SVG_MARKUP; } element.preserveAspectRatio = element.preserveAspectRatio !== false; }
  return element;
}

function repairHierarchy(page) {
  const byId = new Map(page.elements.map(element => [element.id, element]));
  for (const element of page.elements) {
    if (!element.parentId || !byId.has(element.parentId) || byId.get(element.parentId)?.type !== 'frame' || element.parentId === element.id) {
      element.parentId = null;
      continue;
    }
    const visited = new Set([element.id]);
    let cursor = byId.get(element.parentId);
    while (cursor) {
      if (visited.has(cursor.id)) { element.parentId = null; break; }
      visited.add(cursor.id);
      cursor = cursor.parentId ? byId.get(cursor.parentId) : null;
    }
  }
}

export function normalizeDocument(document) {
  const doc = clone(document || defaultDocument());
  doc.schemaVersion = 5; doc.pages ||= []; doc.layoutGroups ||= []; doc.localComponents ||= []; doc.designSystem = normalizeDesignSystem(doc.designSystem); doc.print = normalizePrintSettings(doc.print, doc.width, doc.height); doc.dataSources = normalizeDataSources(doc.dataSources); doc.ai = { lastRunId: null, lastRenderUrl: null, ...(doc.ai || {}) };
  doc.pages.forEach((page, pageIndex) => {
    page.id ||= uuid(); page.name ||= `Page ${pageIndex + 1}`; page.background ||= '#ffffff';
    page.backgroundPaint = normalizePaint(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background, '#ffffff'); page.transparentBackground ??= false;
    if (page.referenceImage) page.referenceImage = { assetId: page.referenceImage.assetId || null, src: String(page.referenceImage.src || ''), name: String(page.referenceImage.name || 'Reference image').slice(0, 160), opacity: clamp(page.referenceImage.opacity ?? .45, 0, 1), visible: page.referenceImage.visible !== false, mode: ['overlay', 'difference', 'split'].includes(page.referenceImage.mode) ? page.referenceImage.mode : 'overlay', fit: ['contain', 'cover', 'stretch'].includes(page.referenceImage.fit) ? page.referenceImage.fit : 'contain', split: clamp(page.referenceImage.split ?? .5, 0, 1) };
    else page.referenceImage = null;
    page.grid = { enabled: false, size: 20, subdivisions: 1, ...(page.grid || {}) };
    page.designGrids = Array.isArray(page.designGrids) ? page.designGrids.map((grid, index) => ({ id: grid.id || `grid-${index + 1}`, name: String(grid.name || `Column grid ${index + 1}`).slice(0, 120), enabled: grid.enabled !== false, columns: clamp(grid.columns || 12, 1, 48), gutter: Math.max(0, Number(grid.gutter || 0)), margin: Math.max(0, Number(grid.margin || 0)), color: /^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(grid.color || '') ? grid.color : '#7c3aed', opacity: clamp(grid.opacity ?? .18, 0, 1) })) : [];
    page.baselineGrids = Array.isArray(page.baselineGrids) ? page.baselineGrids.map((grid, index) => ({ id: grid.id || `baseline-${index + 1}`, name: String(grid.name || `Baseline grid ${index + 1}`).slice(0, 120), enabled: grid.enabled !== false, step: clamp(grid.step || 8, 2, 200), offset: Math.max(0, Number(grid.offset || 0)), color: /^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(grid.color || '') ? grid.color : '#0ea5e9', opacity: clamp(grid.opacity ?? .22, 0, 1) })) : [];
    page.margins = { top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0, ...(page.margins || {}) };
    page.guides ||= { vertical: [], horizontal: [], locked: false }; page.guides.vertical ||= []; page.guides.horizontal ||= [];
    page.regions = { ...defaultRegions(doc.width, doc.height), ...(page.regions || {}) }; page.elements ||= [];
    page.elements.forEach(normalizeElement);
    page.elements.forEach(element => resolveLinkedElementStyle(element, doc.designSystem));
    repairHierarchy(page);
  });
  if (!doc.pages.length) doc.pages = defaultDocument(doc.width, doc.height).pages;
  applyLinkedStyles(doc);
  applyDataBindings(doc);
  return doc;
}

export function collectDescendantIds(page, parentIds) {
  const seeds = parentIds instanceof Set
    ? [...parentIds]
    : Array.isArray(parentIds)
      ? parentIds
      : parentIds == null ? [] : [parentIds];
  const pending = new Set(seeds);
  const result = new Set();
  let changed = true;
  while (changed) {
    changed = false;
    for (const element of page?.elements || []) {
      if (element.parentId && pending.has(element.parentId) && !result.has(element.id)) {
        result.add(element.id); pending.add(element.id); changed = true;
      }
    }
  }
  return result;
}

export function cloneElementTree(elements, { offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0, preserveExternalParents = false, componentId = undefined, componentInstanceId = undefined, componentLinked = undefined, maps = null } = {}) {
  const source = clone(elements || []);
  const sourceIds = new Set(source.map(element => element.id));
  const idMap = new Map(source.map(element => [element.id, uuid()]));
  const groupMap = new Map();
  const instanceMap = new Map();
  const layoutMap = new Map();
  if (maps) Object.assign(maps, { idMap, groupMap, instanceMap, layoutMap });
  return source.map((element, index) => {
    if (element.groupId && !groupMap.has(element.groupId)) groupMap.set(element.groupId, uuid());
    if (element.componentInstanceId && !instanceMap.has(element.componentInstanceId)) instanceMap.set(element.componentInstanceId, uuid());
    if (element.layoutGroupId && !layoutMap.has(element.layoutGroupId)) layoutMap.set(element.layoutGroupId, uuid());
    return {
      ...element,
      id: idMap.get(element.id),
      parentId: element.parentId && sourceIds.has(element.parentId) ? idMap.get(element.parentId) : (preserveExternalParents ? element.parentId : null),
      groupId: element.groupId ? groupMap.get(element.groupId) : null,
      layoutGroupId: element.layoutGroupId ? layoutMap.get(element.layoutGroupId) : undefined,
      componentId: componentId === undefined ? element.componentId : componentId,
      componentInstanceId: componentInstanceId === undefined ? (element.componentInstanceId ? instanceMap.get(element.componentInstanceId) : null) : componentInstanceId,
      componentLinked: componentLinked === undefined ? element.componentLinked : componentLinked,
      x: Number(element.x || 0) + offsetX,
      y: Number(element.y || 0) + offsetY,
      zIndex: index
    };
  });
}

export function reparentElements(page, elementIds, parentId = null) {
  const ids = new Set(elementIds || []);
  const target = parentId ? page.elements.find(element => element.id === parentId && element.type === 'frame') : null;
  if (parentId && !target) throw new Error('The target container is not a frame.');
  const descendants = collectDescendantIds(page, ids);
  if (parentId && (ids.has(parentId) || descendants.has(parentId))) throw new Error('A frame cannot be placed inside itself or one of its descendants.');
  page.elements = page.elements.map(element => ids.has(element.id) ? { ...element, parentId: target?.id || null } : element);
  if (target) applyFrameLayout(page, target.id);
  return page;
}

function rotatePoint(x, y, centerX, centerY, radians) {
  const dx = x - centerX, dy = y - centerY;
  return { x: centerX + dx * Math.cos(radians) - dy * Math.sin(radians), y: centerY + dx * Math.sin(radians) + dy * Math.cos(radians) };
}

export function transformFrameDescendants(page, frameId, before, after) {
  if (!before || !after) return page;
  const ids = collectDescendantIds(page, frameId);
  const scaleX = Math.max(.0001, Number(after.width || 1) / Math.max(.0001, Number(before.width || 1)));
  const scaleY = Math.max(.0001, Number(after.height || 1) / Math.max(.0001, Number(before.height || 1)));
  const oldCenter = { x: before.x + before.width / 2, y: before.y + before.height / 2 };
  const newCenter = { x: after.x + after.width / 2, y: after.y + after.height / 2 };
  const angleDelta = Number(after.rotation || 0) - Number(before.rotation || 0);
  const radians = angleDelta * Math.PI / 180;
  page.elements = page.elements.map(element => {
    if (!ids.has(element.id)) return element;
    const center = { x: element.x + element.width / 2, y: element.y + element.height / 2 };
    const scaled = { x: newCenter.x + (center.x - oldCenter.x) * scaleX, y: newCenter.y + (center.y - oldCenter.y) * scaleY };
    const rotated = rotatePoint(scaled.x, scaled.y, newCenter.x, newCenter.y, radians);
    const width = Math.max(1, element.width * scaleX), height = Math.max(1, element.height * scaleY);
    return { ...element, x: rotated.x - width / 2, y: rotated.y - height / 2, width, height, rotation: Number(element.rotation || 0) + angleDelta };
  });
  return page;
}

function layoutLine(items, bounds, layout, horizontal, crossCursor, crossSize, mainGap) {
  const mainStart = horizontal ? bounds.x : bounds.y;
  const mainSize = horizontal ? bounds.width : bounds.height;
  const fixed = items.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (horizontal ? item.width : item.height), 0);
  const growItems = items.filter(item => Number(item.layoutSizing?.grow || 0) > 0 || (horizontal ? item.layoutSizing?.width : item.layoutSizing?.height) === 'fill');
  const baseGap = items.length > 1 ? mainGap : 0;
  const available = Math.max(0, mainSize - fixed - baseGap * Math.max(0, items.length - 1));
  const totalGrow = growItems.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Math.max(1, Number(item.layoutSizing?.grow || 1)), 0);
  if (available > 0 && growItems.length) {
    for (const item of growItems) {
      const share = available * Math.max(1, Number(item.layoutSizing?.grow || 1)) / totalGrow;
      if (horizontal) item.width += share; else item.height += share;
    }
  }
  const occupied = items.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (horizontal ? item.width : item.height), 0);
  let gap = mainGap;
  let cursor = mainStart;
  if (layout.justify === 'center') cursor += (mainSize - occupied - gap * Math.max(0, items.length - 1)) / 2;
  else if (layout.justify === 'end') cursor += mainSize - occupied - gap * Math.max(0, items.length - 1);
  else if (layout.justify === 'space-between' && items.length > 1) gap = Math.max(0, (mainSize - occupied) / (items.length - 1));
  for (const item of items) {
    const align = item.layoutSizing?.alignSelf && item.layoutSizing.alignSelf !== 'auto' ? item.layoutSizing.alignSelf : layout.align;
    const itemCross = horizontal ? item.height : item.width;
    let cross = crossCursor;
    if (align === 'center') cross += (crossSize - itemCross) / 2;
    else if (align === 'end') cross += crossSize - itemCross;
    else if (align === 'stretch') {
      if (horizontal) item.height = Math.max(1, crossSize); else item.width = Math.max(1, crossSize);
    }
    if (horizontal) { item.x = cursor; item.y = cross; cursor += item.width + gap; }
    else { item.y = cursor; item.x = cross; cursor += item.height + gap; }
  }
}

function layoutItems(items, bounds, inputLayout) {
  if (!items.length) return;
  const layout = normalizeLayout(inputLayout);
  if (!layout.enabled) return;
  const horizontal = layout.direction === 'horizontal';
  const mainGap = horizontal ? layout.columnGap : layout.rowGap;
  const crossGap = horizontal ? layout.rowGap : layout.columnGap;
  const mainLimit = horizontal ? bounds.width : bounds.height;
  const lines = [];
  let line = [], used = 0;
  for (const item of items) {
    const size = horizontal ? item.width : item.height;
    const next = line.length ? used + mainGap + size : size;
    if (layout.wrap && line.length && next > mainLimit) { lines.push(line); line = [item]; used = size; }
    else { line.push(item); used = next; }
  }
  if (line.length) lines.push(line);
  const lineCrossSizes = lines.map(itemsInLine => Math.max(1, ...itemsInLine.map(item => horizontal ? item.height : item.width)));
  const totalCross = lineCrossSizes.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) + crossGap * Math.max(0, lines.length - 1);
  let crossCursor = horizontal ? bounds.y : bounds.x;
  const availableCross = horizontal ? bounds.height : bounds.width;
  if (layout.align === 'center' && lines.length > 1) crossCursor += Math.max(0, (availableCross - totalCross) / 2);
  else if (layout.align === 'end' && lines.length > 1) crossCursor += Math.max(0, availableCross - totalCross);
  lines.forEach((itemsInLine, index) => {
    const lineCrossSize = lines.length === 1 ? availableCross : lineCrossSizes[index];
    layoutLine(itemsInLine, bounds, layout, horizontal, crossCursor, lineCrossSize, mainGap);
    crossCursor += lineCrossSize + crossGap;
  });
}

export function applyFrameLayout(page, frameOrId) {
  const frame = typeof frameOrId === 'string'
    ? page?.elements?.find(element => element.id === frameOrId && element.type === 'frame')
    : frameOrId?.type === 'frame' ? frameOrId : null;
  if (!frame) return page;
  const layout = normalizeLayout(frame.layout);
  frame.layout = layout;
  const children = page.elements.filter(element => element.parentId === frame.id).sort((a, b) => a.zIndex - b.zIndex);
  if (!children.length || !layout.enabled) return page;
  const p = layout.padding;
  if (layout.widthMode === 'hug') {
    const contentWidth = layout.direction === 'horizontal'
      ? children.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.width, 0) + layout.columnGap * Math.max(0, children.length - 1)
      : Math.max(...children.map(item => item.width));
    frame.width = Math.max(1, p.left + contentWidth + p.right);
  }
  if (layout.heightMode === 'hug') {
    const contentHeight = layout.direction === 'vertical'
      ? children.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.height, 0) + layout.rowGap * Math.max(0, children.length - 1)
      : Math.max(...children.map(item => item.height));
    frame.height = Math.max(1, p.top + contentHeight + p.bottom);
  }
  layoutItems(children, { x: frame.x + p.left, y: frame.y + p.top, width: Math.max(1, frame.width - p.left - p.right), height: Math.max(1, frame.height - p.top - p.bottom) }, layout);
  for (const child of children.filter(item => item.type === 'frame')) applyFrameLayout(page, child.id);
  return page;
}

export function applyAllFrameLayouts(page) {
  const frames = (page?.elements || []).filter(element => element.type === 'frame');
  const roots = frames.filter(frame => !frame.parentId);
  for (const frame of roots) applyFrameLayout(page, frame.id);
  for (const frame of frames) if (!roots.includes(frame)) applyFrameLayout(page, frame.id);
  return page;
}

function constrainedAxis(mode, position, size, oldSize, newSize) {
  const ratio = newSize / oldSize;
  if (mode === 'left' || mode === 'top') return { position, size };
  if (mode === 'center') return { position: newSize / 2 - (oldSize / 2 - position), size };
  if (mode === 'right' || mode === 'bottom') return { position: newSize - (oldSize - position), size };
  if (mode === 'stretch') return { position: position * ratio, size: size + (newSize - oldSize) };
  return { position: position * ratio, size: size * ratio };
}

export function resizeDocument(source, newWidth, newHeight) {
  const doc = normalizeDocument(source), oldWidth = doc.width, oldHeight = doc.height, sx = newWidth / oldWidth, sy = newHeight / oldHeight;
  doc.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(newWidth)); doc.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(newHeight));
  for (const page of doc.pages) {
    page.guides.vertical = page.guides.vertical.map(value => value * sx); page.guides.horizontal = page.guides.horizontal.map(value => value * sy);
    for (const element of page.elements) {
      const constraints = { ...DEFAULT_CONSTRAINTS, ...element.constraints };
      const horizontal = constrainedAxis(constraints.horizontal, element.x, element.width, oldWidth, newWidth);
      const vertical = constrainedAxis(constraints.vertical, element.y, element.height, oldHeight, newHeight);
      element.x = horizontal.position; element.y = vertical.position; element.width = Math.max(1, horizontal.size); element.height = Math.max(1, vertical.size);
      if (constraints.maintainAspectRatio) { const scale = Math.min(sx, sy); element.width = Math.max(1, element.width * scale / (constraints.horizontal === 'scale' ? sx : 1)); element.height = Math.max(1, element.height * scale / (constraints.vertical === 'scale' ? sy : 1)); }
      if (element.type === 'text' && constraints.horizontal === 'scale' && constraints.vertical === 'scale') element.fontSize = Math.max(4, (element.fontSize || 48) * Math.min(sx, sy));
    }
    applyAllFrameLayouts(page);
  }
  applyAllLayoutGroups(doc); return doc;
}

export function createLayoutGroup(document, pageId, elementIds, options = {}) {
  const doc = normalizeDocument(document), page = doc.pages.find(item => item.id === pageId);
  if (!page || elementIds.length < 2) return doc;
  const id = uuid(), layout = normalizeLayout({ padding: 0, ...options });
  doc.layoutGroups.push({ id, pageId, elementIds: [...elementIds], ...layout });
  for (const element of page.elements) if (elementIds.includes(element.id)) element.layoutGroupId = id;
  applyLayoutGroup(doc, id); return doc;
}

export function applyLayoutGroup(document, groupId) {
  const group = document.layoutGroups?.find(item => item.id === groupId), page = document.pages?.find(item => item.id === group?.pageId);
  if (!group || !page) return document;
  const items = group.elementIds.map(id => page.elements.find(element => element.id === id)).filter(Boolean);
  if (items.length < 2) return document;
  const bounds = { x: Math.min(...items.map(item => item.x)), y: Math.min(...items.map(item => item.y)), width: Math.max(...items.map(item => item.x + item.width)) - Math.min(...items.map(item => item.x)), height: Math.max(...items.map(item => item.y + item.height)) - Math.min(...items.map(item => item.y)) };
  const layout = normalizeLayout({ padding: 0, ...group });
  const p = layout.padding;
  layoutItems(items, { x: bounds.x + p.left, y: bounds.y + p.top, width: Math.max(1, bounds.width - p.left - p.right), height: Math.max(1, bounds.height - p.top - p.bottom) }, layout);
  return document;
}
export function applyAllLayoutGroups(document) { for (const group of document.layoutGroups || []) applyLayoutGroup(document, group.id); for (const page of document.pages || []) applyAllFrameLayouts(page); return document; }
export function detachLayoutGroup(document, groupId) { const doc = normalizeDocument(document); doc.layoutGroups = (doc.layoutGroups || []).filter(group => group.id !== groupId); for (const page of doc.pages) for (const element of page.elements) if (element.layoutGroupId === groupId) delete element.layoutGroupId; return doc; }

function inferComponentProperties(elements = []) {
  return elements.flatMap(element => {
    if (element.type === 'text' && (element.contentKey || element.role)) return [{ id: element.componentPropertyId || uuid(), name: element.contentKey || element.role || element.name, type: 'text', targetContentKey: element.contentKey || '', targetRole: element.role || '', defaultValue: element.text || '' }];
    if (element.type === 'image' && (element.contentKey || element.role)) return [{ id: element.componentPropertyId || uuid(), name: element.contentKey || element.role || element.name, type: 'image', targetContentKey: element.contentKey || '', targetRole: element.role || '', defaultValue: element.assetId || element.src || '' }];
    return [];
  });
}

export function componentFromElements(elements, title = 'Component', options = {}) {
  const source = clone(elements || []);
  if (!source.length) return { title, width: 1, height: 1, elements: [], properties: [], variants: [] };
  const left = Math.min(...source.map(element => element.x)), top = Math.min(...source.map(element => element.y)), right = Math.max(...source.map(element => element.x + element.width)), bottom = Math.max(...source.map(element => element.y + element.height));
  const properties = options.properties || inferComponentProperties(source);
  const propertyByTarget = new Map(properties.map(property => [`${property.targetContentKey || ''}|${property.targetRole || ''}`, property]));
  const normalizedElements = source.map(element => {
    const property = propertyByTarget.get(`${element.contentKey || ''}|${element.role || ''}`);
    return { ...element, x: element.x - left, y: element.y - top, componentPropertyId: property?.id || element.componentPropertyId || null };
  });
  return { title, width: right - left, height: bottom - top, elements: normalizedElements, properties, variants: options.variants || [], defaultVariant: options.defaultVariant || null, description: options.description || '' };
}

function applyComponentOverrides(elements, component, overrides = {}, variantId = null) {
  const variant = (component.variants || []).find(item => item.id === variantId || item.name === variantId);
  const values = { ...(variant?.values || {}), ...(overrides || {}) };
  const propertyById = new Map((component.properties || []).map(property => [property.id, property]));
  for (const element of elements) {
    const property = propertyById.get(element.componentPropertyId);
    if (!property) continue;
    const value = values[property.id] ?? values[property.name];
    if (value == null) continue;
    if (property.type === 'text' && element.type === 'text') element.text = String(value);
    else if (property.type === 'image' && element.type === 'image') {
      if (typeof value === 'object') Object.assign(element, value);
      else if (String(value).startsWith('http') || String(value).startsWith('data:')) element.src = String(value);
      else element.assetId = String(value);
    } else if (property.type === 'boolean') element.hidden = !value;
    else if (property.type === 'enum') element.componentVariant = String(value);
  }
  return elements;
}

export function instantiateComponent(component, x = 120, y = 120, { linked = false, overrides = {}, variant = null } = {}) {
  const instanceId = uuid();
  const elements = cloneElementTree(component.elements || [], { offsetX: x, offsetY: y, componentId: component.id, componentInstanceId: instanceId, componentLinked: linked || component.linked });
  return applyComponentOverrides(elements, component, overrides, variant || component.defaultVariant);
}

export function replaceColors(document, colors) {
  const doc = normalizeDocument(document), palette = (colors || []).filter(Boolean);
  if (!palette.length) return doc;
  const map = new Map(); let next = 0;
  const replacement = color => { if (typeof color !== 'string' || !color.startsWith('#')) return color; if (!map.has(color)) map.set(color, palette[next++ % palette.length]); return map.get(color); };
  const recolorPaint = paint => { const value = normalizePaint(paint); if (value.type === 'solid') value.color = replacement(value.color); else if (value.type === 'pattern') { value.foreground = replacement(value.foreground); value.background = replacement(value.background); } else if (value.stops) value.stops = value.stops.map(stop => ({ ...stop, color: replacement(stop.color) })); return value; };
  for (const page of doc.pages) {
    page.backgroundPaint = recolorPaint(page.backgroundPaint ?? page.background); page.background = paintPrimaryColor(page.backgroundPaint, page.background);
    for (const element of page.elements) {
      for (const key of ['fill', 'stroke', 'foreground', 'background']) if (typeof element[key] === 'string' && element[key].startsWith('#')) element[key] = replacement(element[key]);
      element.appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
      element.appearance.fills = element.appearance.fills.map(layer => ({ ...layer, paint: recolorPaint(layer.paint) }));
      element.appearance.strokes = element.appearance.strokes.map(layer => ({ ...layer, color: replacement(layer.color) }));
      element.appearance.shadows = element.appearance.shadows.map(layer => ({ ...layer, color: replacement(layer.color) }));
      element.appearance.fill = element.appearance.fills[0]?.paint || element.appearance.fill;
      element.appearance.stroke = element.appearance.strokes[0] || element.appearance.stroke;
      element.appearance.shadow = element.appearance.shadows[0] || element.appearance.shadow;
      if (element.effect?.stroke) element.effect.stroke = replacement(element.effect.stroke);
    }
  }
  return doc;
}
export function replaceFonts(document, fonts) { const doc = normalizeDocument(document), list = (fonts || []).filter(Boolean); if (!list.length) return doc; let next = 0; const map = new Map(); for (const page of doc.pages) for (const element of page.elements) if (element.type === 'text' || element.type === 'chart' || element.type === 'table') { const current = element.fontFamily || element.options?.fontFamily || 'Arial'; if (!map.has(current)) map.set(current, list[next++ % list.length]); if (element.type === 'text') element.fontFamily = map.get(current); else element.options = { ...(element.options || {}), fontFamily: map.get(current) }; } return doc; }
export function assetUsage(document, assetId) { let count = 0; for (const page of document?.pages || []) for (const element of page.elements || []) if (element.assetId === assetId) count++; return count; }
export const clampNumber = clamp;

import {
  FabricObject, Rect, Ellipse, Circle, Textbox, Text, FabricImage, Line, Polyline,
  Polygon, Group, Shadow, Path, Triangle, Gradient, Pattern, filters, loadSVGFromString, util
} from 'fabric';
import QRCode from 'qrcode';
import { svgDataUrl } from './svg.js';
import {
  colorWithOpacity, normalizeAppearance, normalizePaint, paintPrimaryColor,
  strokeDashArray
} from './appearance.js';

FabricObject.customProperties = ['elementId', 'elementType', 'name', 'groupId', 'parentId', 'isGuide', 'guideAxis', 'guideIndex', 'maintainAspectRatio', 'canvasforgeFrameOffsetY', 'canvasforgeTextFit', 'canvasforgeNominalWidth', 'canvasforgeNominalHeight'];
const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));

function makePatternSource(paint) {
  const size = Math.max(8, Math.round(paint.scale || 24));
  const canvas = globalThis.document?.createElement?.('canvas');
  if (!canvas) return null;
  canvas.width = size;
  canvas.height = size;
  const context = canvas.getContext('2d');
  if (!context) return null;
  context.fillStyle = colorWithOpacity(paint.background, paint.backgroundOpacity);
  context.fillRect(0, 0, size, size);
  context.strokeStyle = colorWithOpacity(paint.foreground, paint.foregroundOpacity);
  context.fillStyle = colorWithOpacity(paint.foreground, paint.foregroundOpacity);
  context.lineWidth = Math.max(1, paint.lineWidth || 4);
  context.lineCap = 'round';
  const spacing = Math.max(2, paint.spacing || size / 2);
  if (paint.pattern === 'dots') {
    context.beginPath();
    context.arc(size / 2, size / 2, Math.max(1, paint.lineWidth || 3), 0, Math.PI * 2);
    context.fill();
  } else if (paint.pattern === 'grid') {
    context.beginPath();
    context.moveTo(0, 0); context.lineTo(size, 0);
    context.moveTo(0, 0); context.lineTo(0, size);
    context.stroke();
  } else if (paint.pattern === 'checker') {
    context.fillRect(0, 0, size / 2, size / 2);
    context.fillRect(size / 2, size / 2, size / 2, size / 2);
  } else {
    context.save();
    context.translate(size / 2, size / 2);
    context.rotate((paint.angle || 0) * Math.PI / 180);
    context.translate(-size / 2, -size / 2);
    const drawLines = offset => {
      context.beginPath();
      for (let x = -size * 2 + offset; x <= size * 3; x += spacing) {
        if (paint.pattern === 'zigzag') {
          context.moveTo(x, -size);
          for (let y = -size; y <= size * 2; y += spacing) {
            context.lineTo(x + spacing / 2, y + spacing / 2);
            context.lineTo(x, y + spacing);
          }
        } else {
          context.moveTo(x, -size);
          context.lineTo(x, size * 2);
        }
      }
      context.stroke();
    };
    drawLines(0);
    if (paint.pattern === 'crosshatch') {
      context.rotate(Math.PI / 2);
      drawLines(0);
    }
    context.restore();
  }
  return canvas;
}

export function paintToFabric(paint, width = 1, height = 1, fallback = '#4f46e5') {
  const value = normalizePaint(paint, fallback);
  if (value.type === 'none') return 'transparent';
  if (value.type === 'solid') return colorWithOpacity(value.color, value.opacity);
  if (value.type === 'pattern') {
    const source = makePatternSource(value);
    return source ? new Pattern({ source, repeat: 'repeat' }) : colorWithOpacity(value.foreground, value.foregroundOpacity);
  }
  const colorStops = value.stops.map(stop => ({ offset: stop.offset, color: colorWithOpacity(stop.color, stop.opacity) }));
  if (value.type === 'radial') {
    const x = width * value.centerX;
    const y = height * value.centerY;
    return new Gradient({
      type: 'radial', gradientUnits: 'pixels',
      coords: { x1: x, y1: y, r1: 0, x2: x, y2: y, r2: Math.max(width, height) * value.radius },
      colorStops
    });
  }
  const radians = (value.angle || 0) * Math.PI / 180;
  const cosine = Math.cos(radians), sine = Math.sin(radians);
  const length = Math.abs(width * cosine) + Math.abs(height * sine);
  const centerX = width / 2, centerY = height / 2;
  return new Gradient({
    type: 'linear', gradientUnits: 'pixels',
    coords: {
      x1: centerX - cosine * length / 2, y1: centerY - sine * length / 2,
      x2: centerX + cosine * length / 2, y2: centerY + sine * length / 2
    },
    colorStops
  });
}

function paintWithLayerOpacity(paint, opacity = 1) {
  const value = structuredClone(paint || { type: 'none' });
  const alpha = clamp(Number(opacity ?? 1), 0, 1);
  if (value.type === 'solid') value.opacity = clamp(Number(value.opacity ?? 1) * alpha, 0, 1);
  else if (value.type === 'pattern') {
    value.foregroundOpacity = clamp(Number(value.foregroundOpacity ?? 1) * alpha, 0, 1);
    value.backgroundOpacity = clamp(Number(value.backgroundOpacity ?? 1) * alpha, 0, 1);
  } else if (Array.isArray(value.stops)) value.stops = value.stops.map(stop => ({ ...stop, opacity: clamp(Number(stop.opacity ?? 1) * alpha, 0, 1) }));
  return value;
}

function appearanceOptions(element, width = element.width || 1, height = element.height || 1, { includeFill = true, fillLayer = null, strokeLayer = null, shadowLayer = null } = {}) {
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  const activeFill = fillLayer || appearance.fills?.find(layer => layer.enabled) || { paint: appearance.fill, opacity: 1, blendMode: appearance.blendMode };
  const stroke = strokeLayer || appearance.strokes?.find(layer => layer.enabled) || appearance.stroke;
  const shadow = shadowLayer || appearance.shadows?.find(layer => layer.enabled && layer.type !== 'inner') || { enabled: false, color: '#000000', opacity: 0, blur: 0, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 };
  return {
    ...(includeFill ? { fill: paintToFabric(paintWithLayerOpacity(activeFill.paint || appearance.fill, activeFill.opacity), width, height, element.fill || '#4f46e5') } : {}),
    stroke: stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : 'transparent',
    strokeWidth: stroke.enabled ? stroke.width : 0,
    strokeDashArray: strokeDashArray(stroke),
    strokeLineCap: stroke.lineCap,
    strokeLineJoin: stroke.lineJoin,
    strokeUniform: true,
    shadow: shadow.enabled ? new Shadow({
      color: colorWithOpacity(shadow.color, shadow.opacity), blur: shadow.blur,
      offsetX: shadow.offsetX, offsetY: shadow.offsetY
    }) : null,
    globalCompositeOperation: activeFill.blendMode || stroke?.blendMode || appearance.blendMode || 'source-over'
  };
}

export function commonOptions(element) {
  return {
    left: element.x, top: element.y, angle: element.rotation || 0, opacity: element.opacity ?? 1,
    visible: !element.hidden, selectable: !element.locked, evented: !element.locked,
    lockMovementX: !!element.locked, lockMovementY: !!element.locked, lockRotation: !!element.locked,
    lockScalingX: !!element.locked, lockScalingY: !!element.locked,
    maintainAspectRatio: !!element.constraints?.maintainAspectRatio,
    flipX: !!element.flipX, flipY: !!element.flipY, originX: 'left', originY: 'top',
    transparentCorners: false, cornerColor: '#4f46e5', cornerStrokeColor: '#ffffff',
    cornerStyle: 'circle', borderColor: '#4f46e5', cornerSize: 10, padding: 2,
    elementId: element.id, elementType: element.type, groupId: element.groupId || null, parentId: element.parentId || null, name: element.name,
    canvasforgeNominalWidth: element.width || 1, canvasforgeNominalHeight: element.height || 1,
    objectCaching: element.type !== 'text',
    ...appearanceOptions(element, element.width || 1, element.height || 1)
  };
}

function curvePath(width, curve) {
  if (!curve) return null;
  const amount = clamp(curve, -100, 100), rise = Math.abs(amount) * 2.2;
  return new Path(amount > 0 ? `M 0 ${rise} Q ${width / 2} 0 ${width} ${rise}` : `M 0 0 Q ${width / 2} ${rise} ${width} 0`, { visible: false, fill: '', stroke: '' });
}
const childText = (text, options = {}) => new Text(String(text ?? ''), { fontFamily: 'Arial', fontSize: 16, fill: '#111827', selectable: false, evented: false, originX: 'left', originY: 'top', ...options });

function regularPolygonPoints(width, height, sides, rotation = -Math.PI / 2) {
  const cx = width / 2, cy = height / 2, rx = width / 2, ry = height / 2;
  return Array.from({ length: sides }, (_, index) => {
    const angle = rotation + index * Math.PI * 2 / sides;
    return { x: cx + Math.cos(angle) * rx, y: cy + Math.sin(angle) * ry };
  });
}
function starPoints(width, height, points = 5, innerRatio = .46) {
  const cx = width / 2, cy = height / 2, rx = width / 2, ry = height / 2;
  return Array.from({ length: points * 2 }, (_, index) => {
    const radius = index % 2 ? innerRatio : 1;
    const angle = -Math.PI / 2 + index * Math.PI / points;
    return { x: cx + Math.cos(angle) * rx * radius, y: cy + Math.sin(angle) * ry * radius };
  });
}
function scaledPath(pathData, element) {
  const path = new Path(pathData, { ...commonOptions(element) });
  path.set({ scaleX: element.width / Math.max(1, path.width), scaleY: element.height / Math.max(1, path.height) });
  return path;
}
function shapeObject(element) {
  const width = Math.max(1, element.width), height = Math.max(1, element.height), options = element.shapeOptions || {};
  const base = { ...commonOptions(element), ...appearanceOptions(element, width, height) };
  if (element.shapeKind === 'triangle') return new Triangle({ ...base, width, height });
  if (element.shapeKind === 'diamond') return new Polygon([{ x: width / 2, y: 0 }, { x: width, y: height / 2 }, { x: width / 2, y: height }, { x: 0, y: height / 2 }], base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'pentagon') return new Polygon(regularPolygonPoints(width, height, 5), base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'hexagon') return new Polygon(regularPolygonPoints(width, height, 6), base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'star') return new Polygon(starPoints(width, height, options.points || 5, options.innerRatio || .46), base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'burst') return new Polygon(starPoints(width, height, options.points || 12, options.innerRatio || .68), base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'arrow') return new Polygon([
    { x: 0, y: height * .28 }, { x: width * .58, y: height * .28 }, { x: width * .58, y: 0 },
    { x: width, y: height / 2 }, { x: width * .58, y: height }, { x: width * .58, y: height * .72 }, { x: 0, y: height * .72 }
  ], base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'chevron') return new Polygon([
    { x: 0, y: 0 }, { x: width * .62, y: 0 }, { x: width, y: height / 2 },
    { x: width * .62, y: height }, { x: 0, y: height }, { x: width * .38, y: height / 2 }
  ], base);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'heart') return scaledPath('M 50 92 C 42 82 4 57 4 28 C 4 10 26 2 40 16 L 50 27 L 60 16 C 74 2 96 10 96 28 C 96 57 58 82 50 92 Z', element);
  if (element.shapeKind === 'speech') return scaledPath('M 8 4 H 92 Q 98 4 98 12 V 68 Q 98 76 90 76 H 42 L 20 96 L 25 76 H 8 Q 2 76 2 68 V 12 Q 2 4 8 4 Z', element);
  return new Rect({ ...base, width, height, rx: element.radius || 0, ry: element.radius || 0 });
}

function pathObject(element) {
  const object = new Path(element.pathData || [], { ...commonOptions(element), fill: 'transparent' });
  const nativeWidth = Math.max(1, object.width || element.width || 1);
  const nativeHeight = Math.max(1, object.height || element.height || 1);
  object.set({
    scaleX: Math.max(.0001, Number(element.width || nativeWidth) / nativeWidth),
    scaleY: Math.max(.0001, Number(element.height || nativeHeight) / nativeHeight),
    strokeUniform: true,
    objectCaching: false
  });
  return object;
}

function stackableElement(element) {
  return ['rect', 'frame', 'ellipse', 'shape', 'line', 'path'].includes(element.type);
}

async function cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, options = {}) {
  const copy = await base.clone();
  const stroke = options.stroke || null;
  const fill = options.fill || null;
  const shadow = options.shadow || null;
  copy.set({
    left: 0, top: 0, angle: 0, opacity: options.opacity ?? 1,
    selectable: false, evented: false, elementId: null, elementType: null, parentId: null, groupId: null,
    fill: fill ? paintToFabric(paintWithLayerOpacity(fill.paint, fill.opacity), element.width, element.height, element.fill || '#4f46e5') : 'transparent',
    stroke: stroke?.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : 'transparent',
    strokeWidth: stroke?.enabled ? stroke.width : 0,
    strokeDashArray: stroke?.enabled ? strokeDashArray(stroke) : null,
    strokeLineCap: stroke?.lineCap || 'round', strokeLineJoin: stroke?.lineJoin || 'round',
    shadow: shadow?.enabled && shadow.type !== 'inner' ? new Shadow({ color: colorWithOpacity(shadow.color, shadow.opacity), blur: shadow.blur, offsetX: shadow.offsetX, offsetY: shadow.offsetY }) : null,
    globalCompositeOperation: options.blendMode || fill?.blendMode || stroke?.blendMode || 'source-over',
    objectCaching: false
  });
  if (stroke?.enabled && stroke.alignment !== 'center') {
    const deltaX = stroke.width / Math.max(1, element.width);
    const deltaY = stroke.width / Math.max(1, element.height);
    const factor = stroke.alignment === 'inside' ? -1 : 1;
    copy.set({ scaleX: Math.max(.05, (copy.scaleX || 1) + factor * deltaX), scaleY: Math.max(.05, (copy.scaleY || 1) + factor * deltaY) });
  }
  copy.setCoords();
  return copy;
}

async function applyAppearanceStack(base, element) {
  if (!stackableElement(element)) return base;
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element);
  const fills = (appearance.fills || []).filter(layer => layer.enabled);
  const strokes = (appearance.strokes || []).filter(layer => layer.enabled && layer.width > 0);
  const shadows = (appearance.shadows || []).filter(layer => layer.enabled && layer.type !== 'inner');
  const innerShadows = (appearance.shadows || []).filter(layer => layer.enabled && layer.type === 'inner');
  const effects = (appearance.effects || []).filter(effect => effect.enabled && effect.amount > 0);
  const needsStack = fills.length > 1 || strokes.length > 1 || shadows.length > 1 || innerShadows.length > 0 || effects.length > 0 || strokes.some(stroke => stroke.alignment !== 'center');
  if (!needsStack) return base;
  const children = [];
  const primaryFill = fills[0] || { paint: { type: 'none' }, opacity: 1 };
  for (const effect of effects.filter(item => item.type === 'layer-blur').reverse()) {
    const glow = await cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, {
      fill: primaryFill,
      shadow: { enabled: true, type: 'drop', color: paintPrimaryColor(primaryFill.paint, element.fill || '#4f46e5'), opacity: Math.min(.7, Math.max(.15, primaryFill.opacity ?? 1)), blur: effect.amount, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 },
      opacity: Math.min(.42, primaryFill.opacity ?? 1)
    });
    children.push(glow);
  }
  for (const shadow of [...shadows].reverse()) children.push(await cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, { fill: primaryFill, shadow }));
  for (const fill of [...fills].reverse()) children.push(await cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, { fill, blendMode: fill.blendMode }));
  for (const inner of [...innerShadows].reverse()) {
    const inset = await cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, { stroke: { enabled: true, color: inner.color, opacity: inner.opacity, width: Math.max(1, inner.blur / 2 + Math.max(0, inner.spread)), alignment: 'inside', style: 'solid', lineCap: 'round', lineJoin: 'round' }, blendMode: inner.blendMode });
    inset.set({ left: inner.offsetX || 0, top: inner.offsetY || 0, opacity: Math.min(1, inner.opacity * 1.5) });
    const clip = await base.clone();
    clip.set({ left: 0, top: 0, angle: 0, selectable: false, evented: false, shadow: null });
    inset.clipPath = clip;
    children.push(inset);
  }
  for (const stroke of [...strokes].reverse()) children.push(await cloneForAppearanceLayer(base, element, { stroke, blendMode: stroke.blendMode }));
  const group = new Group(children, {
    ...commonOptions(element), fill: undefined, stroke: undefined, strokeWidth: 0, shadow: null,
    subTargetCheck: false, interactive: false, objectCaching: false
  });
  group.set({ canvasforgeNominalWidth: element.width, canvasforgeNominalHeight: element.height });
  return group;
}

export function frameClipPath(frame) {
  return new Rect({
    left: frame.x, top: frame.y, width: Math.max(1, frame.width), height: Math.max(1, frame.height),
    angle: frame.rotation || 0, rx: frame.radius || 0, ry: frame.radius || 0,
    originX: 'left', originY: 'top', absolutePositioned: true, selectable: false, evented: false
  });
}

function chartGroup(element) {
  const w = Math.max(120, element.width), h = Math.max(100, element.height), opts = element.options || {}, colors = opts.colors?.length ? opts.colors : ['#4f46e5', '#f59e0b', '#10b981', '#ec4899'];
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element), objects = [];
  objects.push(new Rect({ left: 0, top: 0, width: w, height: h, ...appearanceOptions(element, w, h), selectable: false, evented: false, shadow: null, globalCompositeOperation: 'source-over' }));
  const labels = element.data?.labels || [], series = element.data?.series || [];
  const all = series.flatMap(item => item.values || []).map(Number).filter(Number.isFinite);
  const max = Math.max(1, ...all), plot = { x: 48, y: 24, w: w - 72, h: h - (opts.showLegend ? 70 : 48) };
  if (opts.grid !== false) for (let index = 0; index <= 4; index++) {
    const y = plot.y + plot.h * index / 4;
    objects.push(new Line([plot.x, y, plot.x + plot.w, y], { stroke: '#e5e7eb', strokeWidth: 1, selectable: false, evented: false }));
  }
  if (element.chartType === 'pie' || element.chartType === 'donut') {
    const values = series[0]?.values || [], total = Math.max(1, values.reduce((sum, value) => sum + Number(value || 0), 0));
    let angle = -Math.PI / 2;
    const cx = w / 2, cy = (h - (opts.showLegend ? 42 : 0)) / 2, radius = Math.min(w, h - (opts.showLegend ? 42 : 0)) * .34;
    values.forEach((raw, index) => {
      const value = Number(raw || 0), sweep = value / total * Math.PI * 2, start = angle, end = angle + sweep, large = sweep > Math.PI ? 1 : 0;
      const x1 = cx + radius * Math.cos(start), y1 = cy + radius * Math.sin(start), x2 = cx + radius * Math.cos(end), y2 = cy + radius * Math.sin(end);
      objects.push(new Path(`M ${cx} ${cy} L ${x1} ${y1} A ${radius} ${radius} 0 ${large} 1 ${x2} ${y2} Z`, { fill: colors[index % colors.length], stroke: '#fff', strokeWidth: 1, selectable: false, evented: false }));
      angle = end;
    });
    if (element.chartType === 'donut') objects.push(new Circle({ left: cx - radius * .52, top: cy - radius * .52, radius: radius * .52, fill: paintPrimaryColor(appearance.fill, '#ffffff'), selectable: false, evented: false }));
  } else if (element.chartType === 'line' || element.chartType === 'area') {
    series.forEach((seriesItem, seriesIndex) => {
      const points = (seriesItem.values || []).map((value, index) => ({ x: plot.x + (labels.length <= 1 ? 0 : index / (labels.length - 1)) * plot.w, y: plot.y + plot.h - Number(value || 0) / max * plot.h }));
      if (element.chartType === 'area' && points.length > 1) objects.push(new Polygon([{ x: points[0].x, y: plot.y + plot.h }, ...points, { x: points.at(-1).x, y: plot.y + plot.h }], { fill: `${colors[seriesIndex % colors.length]}33`, stroke: 'transparent', selectable: false, evented: false }));
      objects.push(new Polyline(points, { fill: 'transparent', stroke: colors[seriesIndex % colors.length], strokeWidth: 4, selectable: false, evented: false }));
      points.forEach(point => objects.push(new Circle({ left: point.x - 4, top: point.y - 4, radius: 4, fill: colors[seriesIndex % colors.length], selectable: false, evented: false })));
    });
  } else if (element.chartType === 'kpi') {
    const value = series[0]?.values?.[0] ?? 0;
    objects.push(childText(value, { left: w / 2, top: h / 2 - 34, originX: 'center', originY: 'center', fontFamily: opts.fontFamily || 'Arial', fontSize: 64, fontWeight: 700, fill: colors[0] }));
    objects.push(childText(labels[0] || series[0]?.name || 'Metric', { left: w / 2, top: h / 2 + 30, originX: 'center', fontFamily: opts.fontFamily || 'Arial', fontSize: 22, fill: '#6b7280' }));
  } else {
    const groupCount = Math.max(1, labels.length), seriesCount = Math.max(1, series.length), slot = plot.w / groupCount, barWidth = Math.max(3, slot * .72 / seriesCount);
    series.forEach((seriesItem, seriesIndex) => (seriesItem.values || []).forEach((value, index) => {
      const barHeight = Number(value || 0) / max * plot.h;
      objects.push(new Rect({ left: plot.x + index * slot + slot * .14 + seriesIndex * barWidth, top: plot.y + plot.h - barHeight, width: barWidth - 2, height: barHeight, fill: colors[seriesIndex % colors.length], rx: 2, ry: 2, selectable: false, evented: false }));
    }));
  }
  if (opts.showLabels !== false && labels.length && !['pie', 'donut', 'kpi'].includes(element.chartType)) labels.forEach((label, index) => objects.push(childText(label, { left: plot.x + (index + .5) * plot.w / labels.length, top: plot.y + plot.h + 8, originX: 'center', fontFamily: opts.fontFamily || 'Arial', fontSize: Math.min(15, plot.w / Math.max(4, labels.length) / 5), fill: '#6b7280' })));
  if (opts.showLegend !== false && series.length && element.chartType !== 'kpi') series.forEach((seriesItem, index) => {
    const x = 18 + index * Math.max(110, w / series.length);
    objects.push(new Rect({ left: x, top: h - 25, width: 12, height: 12, fill: colors[index % colors.length], selectable: false, evented: false }));
    objects.push(childText(seriesItem.name || `Series ${index + 1}`, { left: x + 18, top: h - 28, fontFamily: opts.fontFamily || 'Arial', fontSize: 15, fill: '#374151' }));
  });
  const group = new Group(objects, { ...commonOptions(element), fill: undefined, stroke: undefined, strokeWidth: 0, subTargetCheck: false, objectCaching: false });
  group.set({ scaleX: 1, scaleY: 1 });
  return group;
}

function tableGroup(element) {
  const rows = Math.max(1, element.rows || element.cells?.length || 1), columns = Math.max(1, element.columns || element.cells?.[0]?.length || 1), width = Math.max(120, element.width), height = Math.max(80, element.height), cellWidth = width / columns, rowHeight = height / rows, options = element.options || {}, objects = [];
  objects.push(new Rect({ left: 0, top: 0, width, height, ...appearanceOptions(element, width, height), selectable: false, evented: false, shadow: null, globalCompositeOperation: 'source-over' }));
  for (let row = 0; row < rows; row++) for (let column = 0; column < columns; column++) {
    const header = row < (options.headerRows ?? 1), fill = header ? (options.headerFill || '#111827') : (row % 2 && options.alternateFill ? options.alternateFill : (options.cellFill || '#fff'));
    objects.push(new Rect({ left: column * cellWidth, top: row * rowHeight, width: cellWidth, height: rowHeight, fill, stroke: options.borderColor || '#d1d5db', strokeWidth: options.borderWidth ?? 1, selectable: false, evented: false }));
    objects.push(new Textbox(String(element.cells?.[row]?.[column] ?? ''), { left: column * cellWidth + (options.padding || 10), top: row * rowHeight + (options.padding || 10), width: Math.max(10, cellWidth - 2 * (options.padding || 10)), height: Math.max(10, rowHeight - 2 * (options.padding || 10)), fontFamily: options.fontFamily || 'Arial', fontSize: options.fontSize || 22, fontWeight: header ? 700 : 400, fill: header ? (options.headerText || '#fff') : (options.textColor || '#111827'), textAlign: options.textAlign || 'left', selectable: false, evented: false, splitByGrapheme: false }));
  }
  return new Group(objects, { ...commonOptions(element), fill: undefined, stroke: undefined, strokeWidth: 0, subTargetCheck: false, objectCaching: false });
}

async function rasterSvgFallback(element) {
  const image = await FabricImage.fromURL(svgDataUrl(element.svg), { crossOrigin: 'anonymous' });
  const nativeWidth = Math.max(1, image.width || element.width || 1);
  const nativeHeight = Math.max(1, image.height || element.height || 1);
  const scaleX = element.width / nativeWidth;
  const scaleY = element.height / nativeHeight;
  const scale = element.preserveAspectRatio !== false ? Math.min(scaleX, scaleY) : null;
  const renderedWidth = nativeWidth * (scale ?? scaleX);
  const renderedHeight = nativeHeight * (scale ?? scaleY);
  image.set({ left: (element.width - renderedWidth) / 2, top: (element.height - renderedHeight) / 2, scaleX: scale ?? scaleX, scaleY: scale ?? scaleY, selectable: false, evented: false, objectCaching: false });
  return image;
}

async function svgObject(element) {
  const frame = new Rect({ left: 0, top: 0, width: element.width, height: element.height, fill: 'transparent', stroke: 'transparent', selectable: false, evented: false });
  try {
    const parsed = await loadSVGFromString(element.svg);
    const objects = (parsed?.objects || []).filter(Boolean);
    if (!objects.length) throw new Error('The SVG did not contain any renderable objects.');
    const vector = typeof util.groupSVGElements === 'function'
      ? util.groupSVGElements(objects, parsed.options || {})
      : new Group(objects, { subTargetCheck: false, objectCaching: false });
    const nativeWidth = Math.max(1, vector.width || parsed.options?.width || element.width || 1);
    const nativeHeight = Math.max(1, vector.height || parsed.options?.height || element.height || 1);
    const scaleX = element.width / nativeWidth;
    const scaleY = element.height / nativeHeight;
    const scale = element.preserveAspectRatio !== false ? Math.min(scaleX, scaleY) : null;
    const renderedWidth = nativeWidth * (scale ?? scaleX);
    const renderedHeight = nativeHeight * (scale ?? scaleY);
    vector.set({
      left: (element.width - renderedWidth) / 2,
      top: (element.height - renderedHeight) / 2,
      scaleX: scale ?? scaleX,
      scaleY: scale ?? scaleY,
      selectable: false,
      evented: false,
      objectCaching: false
    });
    return new Group([frame, vector], { ...commonOptions(element), fill: undefined, stroke: undefined, strokeWidth: 0, subTargetCheck: false, objectCaching: false });
  } catch (error) {
    console.warn('Design Commons SVG vector parsing failed; using raster fallback.', error);
    const fallback = await rasterSvgFallback(element);
    return new Group([frame, fallback], { ...commonOptions(element), fill: undefined, stroke: undefined, strokeWidth: 0, subTargetCheck: false, objectCaching: false });
  }
}

async function qrObject(element) {
  const dataUrl = await QRCode.toDataURL(element.value || '', { errorCorrectionLevel: element.errorCorrection || 'M', margin: element.margin ?? 2, color: { dark: element.foreground || '#111827', light: element.background || '#ffffff' }, width: Math.max(128, Math.round(Math.max(element.width, element.height) * 2)) });
  const image = await FabricImage.fromURL(dataUrl, {}, commonOptions(element));
  image.set({ width: image.width, height: image.height, scaleX: element.width / image.width, scaleY: element.height / image.height, objectCaching: false });
  return image;
}


function textFitsFrame(object, frameHeight, maxLines = 0) {
  object.initDimensions?.();
  const lines = object._textLines?.length || String(object.text || '').split('\n').length;
  return object.height <= frameHeight + .5 && (!maxLines || lines <= maxLines);
}

function fitTextboxToFrame(object, element) {
  const frameWidth = Math.max(1, Number(element.width || object.width || 1));
  const frameHeight = Math.max(1, Number(element.height || object.height || 1));
  const requested = Math.max(4, Number(element.fontSize || object.fontSize || 48));
  const minimum = Math.max(4, Math.min(requested, Number(element.minFontSize || 8)));
  const maxLines = Math.max(0, Number(element.maxLines || 0));

  if (element.autoFit && element.height > 0) {
    let low = minimum, high = requested, best = minimum;
    object.set({ fontSize: minimum });
    object.initDimensions?.();
    if (!textFitsFrame(object, frameHeight, maxLines)) {
      object.set({ fontSize: minimum });
    } else {
      while (high - low > .25) {
        const mid = (low + high) / 2;
        object.set({ fontSize: mid });
        object.initDimensions?.();
        if (textFitsFrame(object, frameHeight, maxLines)) { best = mid; low = mid; }
        else high = mid;
      }
      object.set({ fontSize: Math.floor(best * 10) / 10 });
    }
  }

  object.initDimensions?.();
  const overflow = !textFitsFrame(object, frameHeight, maxLines);
  object.canvasforgeTextFit = {
    requestedFontSize: requested,
    fittedFontSize: object.fontSize,
    frameHeight,
    overflow,
    lines: object._textLines?.length || 1,
    maxLines
  };

  const freeHeight = Math.max(0, frameHeight - Number(object.height || 0));
  const offsetY = element.verticalAlign === 'bottom' ? freeHeight : element.verticalAlign === 'middle' ? freeHeight / 2 : 0;
  object.set({ top: Number(element.y || 0) + offsetY });
  object.canvasforgeFrameOffsetY = offsetY;

  const shouldClip =
    element.overflowBehavior === 'clip' ||
    element.overflowBehavior === 'ellipsis' ||
    overflow;

  if (shouldClip) {
    // Fabric positions relative clip paths from the object's centre.
    // A left/top clip at (0, 0) therefore starts in the middle of the
    // text object and hides its upper-left portion. Centre the clipping
    // frame and offset it back to the element's nominal text box.
    object.clipPath = new Rect({
      left: 0,
      top: (frameHeight - Number(object.height || 0)) / 2 - offsetY,
      width: frameWidth,
      height: frameHeight,
      originX: 'center',
      originY: 'center',
      absolutePositioned: false,
      selectable: false,
      evented: false
    });
  } else {
    object.clipPath = null;
  }

  return object;
}

export async function elementToObject(element) {
  let object;
  const appearance = normalizeAppearance(element), stroke = appearance.stroke;
  const style = appearanceOptions(element, element.width, element.height);
  if (element.type === 'rect' || element.type === 'frame') object = new Rect({ ...commonOptions(element), ...style, width: element.width, height: element.height, rx: element.radius || 0, ry: element.radius || 0 });
  else if (element.type === 'ellipse') object = new Ellipse({ ...commonOptions(element), ...style, rx: element.width / 2, ry: element.height / 2 });
  else if (element.type === 'shape') object = shapeObject(element);
  else if (element.type === 'text') {
    const effect = element.effect || {}, hollow = !!effect.hollow;
    const fill = hollow ? 'transparent' : paintToFabric(appearance.fill, element.width, element.height, element.fill || '#111827');
    const outlineColor = stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : (hollow ? colorWithOpacity(paintPrimaryColor(appearance.fill, element.fill || '#111827'), 1) : 'transparent');
    const outlineWidth = stroke.enabled ? stroke.width : (hollow ? Math.max(1, effect.strokeWidth || 2) : 0);
    object = new Textbox(element.text || '', {
      ...commonOptions(element), width: Math.max(20, element.width), fontFamily: element.fontFamily || 'Arial',
      fontSize: element.fontSize || 48, fontWeight: element.fontWeight || 400, fontStyle: element.fontStyle || 'normal',
      underline: !!element.underline, linethrough: !!element.linethrough, fill,
      stroke: outlineColor, strokeWidth: outlineWidth, strokeDashArray: strokeDashArray(stroke),
      paintFirst: 'stroke', textAlign: element.textAlign || 'left', lineHeight: element.lineHeight || 1.16,
      charSpacing: element.charSpacing || 0, textBackgroundColor: element.textBackgroundColor || '',
      styles: element.styles || {}, splitByGrapheme: false, path: curvePath(element.width, effect.curve),
      pathSide: effect.curve < 0 ? 'right' : 'left', pathAlign: 'center', pathStartOffset: 0
    });
    object.set({ scaleX: 1, scaleY: 1 });
    fitTextboxToFrame(object, element);
  } else if (element.type === 'image') object = await imageElementToObject(element);
  else if (element.type === 'svg') object = await svgObject(element);
  else if (element.type === 'line') object = new Line([0, 0, element.width, element.height], { ...commonOptions(element), ...style, fill: undefined, stroke: stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : (element.stroke || '#111827'), strokeWidth: stroke.enabled ? stroke.width : (element.strokeWidth || 4) });
  else if (element.type === 'path') object = pathObject(element);
  else if (element.type === 'chart') object = chartGroup(element);
  else if (element.type === 'table') object = tableGroup(element);
  else if (element.type === 'qrcode') object = await qrObject(element);
  else object = new Rect({ ...commonOptions(element), width: element.width, height: element.height, fill: '#d1d5db' });
  object = await applyAppearanceStack(object, element);
  object.setCoords();
  return object;
}

export function cropGeometry(element) {
  const nativeWidth = Math.max(1, Number(element.nativeWidth || 1)), nativeHeight = Math.max(1, Number(element.nativeHeight || 1)), frameWidth = Math.max(1, Number(element.width || 1)), frameHeight = Math.max(1, Number(element.height || 1)), zoom = Math.max(1, Number(element.cropZoom || 1)), scale = Math.max(frameWidth / nativeWidth, frameHeight / nativeHeight) * zoom, cropWidth = Math.min(nativeWidth, frameWidth / scale), cropHeight = Math.min(nativeHeight, frameHeight / scale), maxX = Math.max(0, nativeWidth - cropWidth), maxY = Math.max(0, nativeHeight - cropHeight);
  let cropX = Number.isFinite(element.cropX) ? element.cropX : maxX * (element.cropAnchorX ?? .5), cropY = Number.isFinite(element.cropY) ? element.cropY : maxY * (element.cropAnchorY ?? .5);
  cropX = clamp(cropX, 0, maxX); cropY = clamp(cropY, 0, maxY);
  return { nw: nativeWidth, nh: nativeHeight, frameW: frameWidth, frameH: frameHeight, scale, cropW: cropWidth, cropH: cropHeight, cropX, cropY, maxX, maxY };
}
function clipPathFromSvg(pathData, cropWidth, cropHeight) {
  const path = new Path(pathData, { originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  path.set({ scaleX: cropWidth / Math.max(1, path.width), scaleY: cropHeight / Math.max(1, path.height) });
  return path;
}
function imageClipPath(mask, cropWidth, cropHeight, radius = 24) {
  if (mask === 'circle') return new Ellipse({ rx: cropWidth / 2, ry: cropHeight / 2, originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  if (mask === 'triangle') return new Triangle({ width: cropWidth, height: cropHeight, originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  if (mask === 'rounded') return new Rect({ width: cropWidth, height: cropHeight, rx: radius, ry: radius, originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  if (mask === 'hexagon') return new Polygon(regularPolygonPoints(cropWidth, cropHeight, 6), { originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  if (mask === 'star') return new Polygon(starPoints(cropWidth, cropHeight, 5, .46), { originX: 'center', originY: 'center' });
  if (mask === 'heart') return clipPathFromSvg('M 50 92 C 42 82 4 57 4 28 C 4 10 26 2 40 16 L 50 27 L 60 16 C 74 2 96 10 96 28 C 96 57 58 82 50 92 Z', cropWidth, cropHeight);
  if (mask === 'arch') return clipPathFromSvg('M 4 96 V 50 C 4 22 24 4 50 4 C 76 4 96 22 96 50 V 96 Z', cropWidth, cropHeight);
  if (mask === 'blob') return clipPathFromSvg('M 72 8 C 91 18 100 39 91 57 C 82 75 65 96 43 92 C 21 88 2 72 6 49 C 10 26 25 8 47 5 C 56 4 64 4 72 8 Z', cropWidth, cropHeight);
  return null;
}

export function buildImageFilters(values = {}, effects = []) {
  const list = [];
  if (values.brightness) list.push(new filters.Brightness({ brightness: Number(values.brightness) }));
  if (values.contrast) list.push(new filters.Contrast({ contrast: Number(values.contrast) }));
  if (values.saturation) list.push(new filters.Saturation({ saturation: Number(values.saturation) }));
  if (values.vibrance && filters.Vibrance) list.push(new filters.Vibrance({ vibrance: Number(values.vibrance) }));
  if (values.hue) list.push(new filters.HueRotation({ rotation: Number(values.hue) }));
  if (values.gamma && Number(values.gamma) !== 1 && filters.Gamma) list.push(new filters.Gamma({ gamma: [Number(values.gamma), Number(values.gamma), Number(values.gamma)] }));
  if (values.tintOpacity && filters.BlendColor) list.push(new filters.BlendColor({ color: values.tint || '#ffffff', mode: 'tint', alpha: Number(values.tintOpacity) }));
  const layerBlur = (effects || []).filter(effect => effect.enabled && effect.type === 'layer-blur').reduce((max, effect) => Math.max(max, Number(effect.amount || 0)), 0);
  if (values.blur || layerBlur) list.push(new filters.Blur({ blur: Math.min(1, Math.max(Number(values.blur || 0), layerBlur / 160)) }));
  if (values.noise && filters.Noise) list.push(new filters.Noise({ noise: Math.round(Number(values.noise)) }));
  if (values.pixelate && filters.Pixelate) list.push(new filters.Pixelate({ blocksize: Math.max(2, Math.round(Number(values.pixelate))) }));
  if (values.grayscale) list.push(new filters.Grayscale());
  if (values.sepia) list.push(new filters.Sepia());
  return list;
}

export async function imageElementToObject(element) {
  const object = await FabricImage.fromURL(element.src, { crossOrigin: 'anonymous' }, commonOptions(element));
  const nativeWidth = object.getElement()?.naturalWidth || object.width || element.nativeWidth || 1, nativeHeight = object.getElement()?.naturalHeight || object.height || element.nativeHeight || 1;
  element.nativeWidth = nativeWidth; element.nativeHeight = nativeHeight;
  const geometry = cropGeometry(element), appearance = normalizeAppearance(element), stroke = appearance.stroke;
  object.set({
    ...commonOptions(element), width: geometry.cropW, height: geometry.cropH, cropX: geometry.cropX, cropY: geometry.cropY,
    scaleX: geometry.scale, scaleY: geometry.scale,
    clipPath: imageClipPath(element.mask, geometry.cropW, geometry.cropH, (element.radius || 24) / geometry.scale),
    filters: buildImageFilters(element.filters, appearance.effects), imageSmoothing: true, objectCaching: false,
    stroke: stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : 'transparent',
    strokeWidth: stroke.enabled ? stroke.width / geometry.scale : 0,
    strokeDashArray: strokeDashArray(stroke)?.map(value => value / geometry.scale) || null
  });
  object.applyFilters(); object.setCoords(); return object;
}
export function updateImageObject(object, element) {
  const geometry = cropGeometry(element), options = commonOptions(element), appearance = normalizeAppearance(element), stroke = appearance.stroke;
  object.set({
    ...options, width: geometry.cropW, height: geometry.cropH, cropX: geometry.cropX, cropY: geometry.cropY,
    scaleX: geometry.scale, scaleY: geometry.scale,
    clipPath: imageClipPath(element.mask, geometry.cropW, geometry.cropH, (element.radius || 24) / geometry.scale),
    filters: buildImageFilters(element.filters, appearance.effects),
    stroke: stroke.enabled ? colorWithOpacity(stroke.color, stroke.opacity) : 'transparent',
    strokeWidth: stroke.enabled ? stroke.width / geometry.scale : 0,
    strokeDashArray: strokeDashArray(stroke)?.map(value => value / geometry.scale) || null
  });
  object.applyFilters(); object.setCoords();
}
export function objectTransformToPatch(object, element) {
  const scaleX = Math.abs(object.scaleX || 1), scaleY = Math.abs(object.scaleY || 1), patch = { x: object.left || 0, y: (object.top || 0) - Number(object.canvasforgeFrameOffsetY || 0), rotation: object.angle || 0, opacity: object.opacity ?? 1, flipX: !!object.flipX, flipY: !!object.flipY };
  if (element.type === 'text') {
    patch.width = Math.max(20, (object.width || element.width || 20) * scaleX);
    patch.height = Math.max(1, (object.height || element.height || 1) * scaleY);
    patch.fontSize = Math.max(4, (object.fontSize || element.fontSize || 48) * scaleY);
  } else {
    const nominalWidth = Number(object.canvasforgeNominalWidth || object.width || element.width || 1);
    const nominalHeight = Number(object.canvasforgeNominalHeight || object.height || element.height || 1);
    patch.width = Math.max(1, nominalWidth * scaleX); patch.height = Math.max(1, nominalHeight * scaleY);
  }
  return patch;
}
export function textObjectToPatch(object, element) {
  const transform = objectTransformToPatch(object, element);
  const fill = typeof object.fill === 'string' && object.fill !== 'transparent' ? object.fill : element.fill;
  return { ...transform, text: object.text, styles: object.styles || {}, fontFamily: object.fontFamily, fontSize: transform.fontSize, fontWeight: object.fontWeight, fontStyle: object.fontStyle, underline: object.underline, linethrough: object.linethrough, fill: element.effect?.hollow ? element.fill : fill, textAlign: object.textAlign, lineHeight: object.lineHeight, charSpacing: object.charSpacing, textBackgroundColor: object.textBackgroundColor || '' };
}
export function createGuide(axis, value, pageSize, index, locked) {
  const vertical = axis === 'vertical';
  return new Line(vertical ? [0, 0, 0, pageSize.height] : [0, 0, pageSize.width, 0], { left: vertical ? value : 0, top: vertical ? 0 : value, stroke: '#06b6d4', strokeWidth: 1, strokeDashArray: [5, 5], selectable: !locked, evented: !locked, hasControls: false, hasBorders: false, lockMovementX: !vertical, lockMovementY: vertical, hoverCursor: vertical ? 'ew-resize' : 'ns-resize', isGuide: true, guideAxis: axis, guideIndex: index, excludeFromExport: true, originX: 'left', originY: 'top' });
}

// FILE: src/lib/fabricReconciler.js

import { frameClipPath } from './fabricAdapter.js';


export function elementRenderSignature(element) {
  return JSON.stringify(element);
}

function clippingFrames(page, element) {
  const byId = new Map((page?.elements || []).map(item => [item.id, item]));
  const frames = [];
  let parent = element?.parentId ? byId.get(element.parentId) : null;
  while (parent) {
    if (parent.type === 'frame' && parent.clipChildren) frames.push(parent);
    parent = parent.parentId ? byId.get(parent.parentId) : null;
  }
  return frames;
}

export function applyHierarchyClip(object, page, element) {
  const frames = clippingFrames(page, element);
  if (!frames.length || !object) return object;
  let tail = object.clipPath || null;
  for (const frame of frames) {
    const clip = frameClipPath(frame);
    if (tail) tail.clipPath = clip;
    else object.clipPath = clip;
    tail = clip;
  }
  object.dirty = true;
  return object;
}

export async function reconcileFabricElements({ canvas, page, renderState, createObject, selectedIds = new Set(), readOnly = false, renderMode = false, full = false }) {
  if (!canvas || !page) return;
  const state = renderState.current || { pageId: null, signatures: new Map(), objects: new Map() };
  if (full || state.pageId !== page.id) {
    state.pageId = page.id;
    state.signatures = new Map();
    state.objects = new Map();
  } else {
    state.objects = new Map(canvas.getObjects().filter(object => object.elementId).map(object => [object.elementId, object]));
  }

  const nextIds = new Set(page.elements.map(element => element.id));
  for (const [id, object] of state.objects) {
    if (!nextIds.has(id)) {
      canvas.remove(object);
      state.objects.delete(id);
      state.signatures.delete(id);
    }
  }

  const sorted = [...page.elements].sort((a, b) => (a.zIndex || 0) - (b.zIndex || 0));
  for (const element of sorted) {
    const signature = elementRenderSignature(element);
    const current = state.objects.get(element.id);
    if (!current || state.signatures.get(element.id) !== signature) {
      if (current) canvas.remove(current);
      const object = applyHierarchyClip(await createObject(element), page, element);
      if (readOnly || renderMode) { object.selectable = false; object.evented = false; }
      canvas.add(object);
      state.objects.set(element.id, object);
      state.signatures.set(element.id, signature);
    }
  }

  const backgroundOffset = canvas.getObjects().some(object => object.isPageBackground) ? 1 : 0;
  sorted.forEach((element, index) => {
    const object = state.objects.get(element.id);
    if (!object) return;
    if (typeof canvas.moveObjectTo === 'function') canvas.moveObjectTo(object, index + backgroundOffset);
  });

  const active = sorted.map(element => state.objects.get(element.id)).filter(object => object && selectedIds.has(object.elementId));
  renderState.current = state;
  return { active, objects: state.objects };
}

const SYSTEM_FONTS = new Set([
  'Arial', 'Georgia', 'Verdana', 'Trebuchet MS', 'Courier New', 'Times New Roman',
  'Comic Sans MS', 'Impact', 'Palatino Linotype', 'Lucida Console', 'Brush Script MT',
  'Monaco', 'Copperplate', 'Garamond', 'Cambria', 'Calibri'
]);
const pending = new Map();
const reports = new Map();

const quoteFont = value => `"${String(value).replaceAll('"', '\\"')}"`;
const googleFamily = value => encodeURIComponent(String(value).trim()).replaceAll('%20', '+');
const fontCssId = value => `canvasforge-font-${String(value).toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')}`;
const timeout = (promise, milliseconds) => Promise.race([
  promise,
  new Promise((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`Font load timed out after ${milliseconds}ms.`)), milliseconds))
]);

function setReport(fontFamily, status, source, error = '') {
  const report = { fontFamily, status, source, error: error ? String(error) : '', checkedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  reports.set(fontFamily, report);
  return report;
}

function ensureGoogleFontLink(fontFamily) {
  const document = globalThis.document;
  if (!document?.head || SYSTEM_FONTS.has(fontFamily)) return null;
  const id = fontCssId(fontFamily);
  const existing = document.getElementById(id);
  if (existing) return existing;
  const link = document.createElement('link');
  link.id = id;
  link.rel = 'stylesheet';
  link.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
  link.href = `https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=${googleFamily(fontFamily)}&display=swap`;
  document.head.appendChild(link);
  return link;
}

async function waitForStylesheet(link, timeoutMs) {
  if (!link || link.sheet) return;
  await timeout(new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const done = () => { cleanup(); resolve(); };
    const fail = () => { cleanup(); reject(new Error('The font stylesheet could not be loaded.')); };
    const cleanup = () => { link.removeEventListener('load', done); link.removeEventListener('error', fail); };
    link.addEventListener('load', done, { once: true });
    link.addEventListener('error', fail, { once: true });
  }), timeoutMs);
}

export function isFontAvailable(fontFamily) {
  if (!fontFamily) return false;
  const fonts = globalThis.document?.fonts;
  if (!fonts?.check) return SYSTEM_FONTS.has(fontFamily);
  try { return fonts.check(`16px ${quoteFont(fontFamily)}`); } catch { return false; }
}

export async function ensureFontLoaded(fontFamily, { timeoutMs = 7000 } = {}) {
  const name = String(fontFamily || '').trim();
  if (!name) return setReport(name, 'skipped', 'none');
  const existingReport = reports.get(name);
  if (existingReport?.status === 'loaded') return existingReport;
  if (SYSTEM_FONTS.has(name) && isFontAvailable(name)) return setReport(name, 'loaded', 'system');
  if (pending.has(name)) return pending.get(name);
  const task = (async () => {
    const document = globalThis.document;
    if (!document?.fonts) return setReport(name, 'unavailable', 'no-font-api', 'The Font Loading API is unavailable.');
    try {
      const link = ensureGoogleFontLink(name);
      if (link) await waitForStylesheet(link, timeoutMs).catch(() => {});
      await timeout(document.fonts.load(`16px ${quoteFont(name)}`), timeoutMs);
      await timeout(document.fonts.ready, timeoutMs).catch(() => {});
      if (isFontAvailable(name)) return setReport(name, 'loaded', link ? 'google-fonts' : 'document');
      try {
        const localFace = new FontFace(name, `local(${quoteFont(name)})`, { style: 'normal', weight: '400' });
        await timeout(localFace.load(), Math.min(timeoutMs, 3000));
        document.fonts.add(localFace);
      } catch {}
      return isFontAvailable(name)
        ? setReport(name, 'loaded', 'local')
        : setReport(name, 'fallback', link ? 'google-fonts' : 'local', 'The requested font was not available and the browser will use a fallback.');
    } catch (error) {
      return setReport(name, 'fallback', SYSTEM_FONTS.has(name) ? 'system' : 'google-fonts', error?.message || error);
    } finally {
      pending.delete(name);
    }
  })();
  pending.set(name, task);
  return task;
}

export async function ensureFontsLoaded(fontFamilies = [], options = {}) {
  const unique = [...new Set(fontFamilies.map(value => String(value || '').trim()).filter(Boolean))];
  const results = await Promise.all(unique.map(font => ensureFontLoaded(font, options)));
  return {
    results,
    loaded: results.filter(item => item.status === 'loaded'),
    failed: results.filter(item => !['loaded', 'skipped'].includes(item.status))
  };
}

export function getFontLoadReport(fontFamilies = null) {
  const names = fontFamilies ? [...new Set(fontFamilies)] : [...reports.keys()];
  return names.map(name => reports.get(name) || {
    fontFamily: name,
    status: isFontAvailable(name) ? 'loaded' : 'unknown',
    source: isFontAvailable(name) ? 'document' : 'unchecked',
    error: '',
    checkedAt: null
  });
}
