import { clamp01, normalizeAppearance, normalizePaint, paintPrimaryColor, solidPaint } from './appearance.js';

const stroke = (color = '#111827', width = 0, opacity = 1, style = 'solid') => ({
  enabled: width > 0,
  color,
  opacity,
  width,
  style,
  dash: 10,
  gap: 8,
  lineCap: 'round',
  lineJoin: 'round'
});
const shadow = (color = '#000000', opacity = 0, blur = 0, offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0) => ({
  enabled: opacity > 0,
  color,
  opacity,
  blur,
  offsetX,
  offsetY
});
const linear = (angle, ...colors) => ({
  type: 'linear',
  angle,
  stops: colors.map((color, index) => ({ offset: colors.length === 1 ? 0 : index / (colors.length - 1), color, opacity: 1 }))
});
const radial = (...colors) => ({
  type: 'radial', centerX: .5, centerY: .45, radius: .78,
  stops: colors.map((color, index) => ({ offset: colors.length === 1 ? 0 : index / (colors.length - 1), color, opacity: 1 }))
});
const appearance = (fill, border = stroke(), dropShadow = shadow(), blendMode = 'source-over') => ({ fill, stroke: border, shadow: dropShadow, blendMode });
const preset = (id, name, category, fill, border, dropShadow, blendMode = 'source-over', tags = []) => ({
  id, name, category, tags: [category.toLowerCase(), ...tags], compatibleTypes: ['*'], appearance: appearance(fill, border, dropShadow, blendMode)
});

const GRADIENT_DEFINITIONS = [

const hex8ToStop = color => {
  if (/^#[0-9a-f]{8}$/i.test(color)) {
    return { color: color.slice(0, 7), opacity: parseInt(color.slice(7), 16) / 255 };
  }
  return { color, opacity: 1 };
};

export const GRADIENT_PRESETS = GRADIENT_DEFINITIONS.map(([id, name, category, angle, colors]) => {
  const stops = colors.map((raw, index) => ({ offset: index / (colors.length - 1), ...hex8ToStop(raw) }));
  const paint = angle === 'radial'
    ? { type: 'radial', centerX: .5, centerY: .45, radius: .75, stops }
    : { type: 'linear', angle, stops };
  return { id: `gradient-${id}`, name, category, tags: ['gradient', category.toLowerCase()], paint };
});

const gradientBy = id => GRADIENT_PRESETS.find(item => item.id === `gradient-${id}`)?.paint || linear(45, '#4f46e5', '#ec4899');

const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
const scalePaintOpacity = (paint, factor) => {
  const value = normalizePaint(paint);
  if (value.type === 'solid') return { ...value, opacity: clamp01(value.opacity * factor) };
  if (value.type === 'pattern') return { ...value, foregroundOpacity: clamp01(value.foregroundOpacity * factor), backgroundOpacity: clamp01(value.backgroundOpacity * Math.min(1, .7 + factor * .3)) };
  if (value.type === 'linear' || value.type === 'radial') return { ...value, stops: value.stops.map(stop => ({ ...stop, opacity: clamp01(stop.opacity * factor) })) };
  return value;
};

export function scaleAppearancePreset(input, intensity = 1) {
  const value = normalizeAppearance({ appearance: input });
  const factor = clamp(Number(intensity) || 1, .25, 2);
  const fills = value.fills.map(layer => ({ ...layer, paint: scalePaintOpacity(layer.paint, Math.min(1.35, .65 + factor * .35)), opacity: clamp01(layer.opacity * Math.min(1.35, .65 + factor * .35)) }));
  const strokes = value.strokes.map(layer => ({
    ...layer,
    opacity: clamp01(layer.opacity * Math.min(1.5, factor)),
    width: layer.enabled ? Math.max(.5, layer.width * (.6 + factor * .4)) : layer.width
  }));
  const shadows = value.shadows.map(layer => ({
    ...layer,
    opacity: clamp01(layer.opacity * factor),
    blur: layer.blur * (.55 + factor * .45),
    spread: layer.spread * factor,
    offsetX: layer.offsetX * factor,
    offsetY: layer.offsetY * factor
  }));
  return {
    ...value,
    fills,
    strokes,
    shadows,
    fill: fills.find(layer => layer.enabled)?.paint || fills[0]?.paint || value.fill,
    stroke: strokes.find(layer => layer.enabled) || strokes[0] || value.stroke,
    shadow: shadows.find(layer => layer.enabled) || shadows[0] || value.shadow
  };
}

const neutralFilterValue = key => key === 'gamma' ? 1 : key === 'tint' ? '#ffffff' : key === 'grayscale' || key === 'sepia' ? false : 0;
export function scaleImageFilters(filters, intensity = 1) {
  const factor = clamp(Number(intensity) || 1, 0, 2);
  const result = { ...neutralImage };
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries({ ...neutralImage, ...filters })) {
    const neutral = neutralFilterValue(key);
    if (typeof value === 'number' && typeof neutral === 'number') result[key] = neutral + (value - neutral) * factor;
    else if (typeof value === 'boolean') result[key] = factor >= .45 ? value : false;
    else result[key] = value;
  }
  return result;
}

const paintColors = paint => {
  const value = normalizePaint(paint);
  if (value.type === 'solid') return [value.color];
  if (value.type === 'pattern') return [value.foreground, value.background];
  return value.stops?.map(stop => stop.color) || [paintPrimaryColor(value)];
};
export function recolorPaint(targetPaint, sourcePaint) {
  const target = normalizePaint(targetPaint);
  const colors = paintColors(sourcePaint);
  if (target.type === 'solid') return { ...target, color: colors[0] };
  if (target.type === 'pattern') return { ...target, foreground: colors[0], background: colors[1] || '#ffffff' };
  if (target.type === 'linear' || target.type === 'radial') return { ...target, stops: target.stops.map((stop, index) => ({ ...stop, color: colors[index % colors.length] })) };
  return target;
}

export function mergeAppearancePreset(currentInput, presetInput, options = {}) {
  const current = normalizeAppearance({ appearance: currentInput });
  let incoming = scaleAppearancePreset(presetInput, options.intensity ?? 1);
  if (options.preserveColors) {
    const fills = incoming.fills.map((layer, index) => ({ ...layer, paint: recolorPaint(layer.paint, current.fills[index % current.fills.length]?.paint || current.fill) }));
    const strokes = incoming.strokes.map((layer, index) => ({ ...layer, color: current.strokes[index % current.strokes.length]?.color || current.stroke.color }));
    const shadows = incoming.shadows.map((layer, index) => ({ ...layer, color: current.shadows[index % current.shadows.length]?.color || current.shadow.color }));
    incoming = { ...incoming, fills, strokes, shadows, fill: fills[0]?.paint || incoming.fill, stroke: strokes[0] || incoming.stroke, shadow: shadows[0] || incoming.shadow };
  }
  if (options.mode !== 'merge') return incoming;
  const sections = options.sections || { fill: true, stroke: true, shadow: true, blendMode: true };
  const fills = sections.fill ? incoming.fills : current.fills;
  const strokes = sections.stroke ? incoming.strokes : current.strokes;
  const shadows = sections.shadow ? incoming.shadows : current.shadows;
  return {
    fills,
    strokes,
    shadows,
    effects: incoming.effects?.length ? incoming.effects : current.effects,
    fill: fills.find(layer => layer.enabled)?.paint || fills[0]?.paint || current.fill,
    stroke: strokes.find(layer => layer.enabled) || strokes[0] || current.stroke,
    shadow: shadows.find(layer => layer.enabled) || shadows[0] || current.shadow,
    blendMode: sections.blendMode ? incoming.blendMode : current.blendMode
  };
}

const DB_NAME='canvasforge-recovery';const STORE='documents';
function openDb(){return new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{const req=indexedDB.open(DB_NAME,1);req.onupgradeneeded=()=>req.result.createObjectStore(STORE,{keyPath:'designId'});req.onsuccess=()=>resolve(req.result);req.onerror=()=>reject(req.error);});}
export async function saveRecovery(designId,document){if(!designId)return;const db=await openDb();await new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{const tx=db.transaction(STORE,'readwrite');tx.objectStore(STORE).put({designId,document,updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()});tx.oncomplete=resolve;tx.onerror=()=>reject(tx.error);});db.close();}
export async function loadRecovery(designId){const db=await openDb();const value=await new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{const req=db.transaction(STORE).objectStore(STORE).get(designId);req.onsuccess=()=>resolve(req.result||null);req.onerror=()=>reject(req.error);});db.close();return value;}
export async function clearRecovery(designId){if(!designId)return;const db=await openDb();await new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{const tx=db.transaction(STORE,'readwrite');tx.objectStore(STORE).delete(designId);tx.oncomplete=resolve;tx.onerror=()=>reject(tx.error);});db.close();}

// FILE: src/lib/svg.js

const SVG_NAMESPACE = 'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg';

export const DEFAULT_SVG_MARKUP = `<svg xmlns="${SVG_NAMESPACE}" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><circle cx="50" cy="50" r="45" fill="#4f46e5"/></svg>`;

function removeScripts(markup) {
  return markup.replace(/<script\b[\s\S]*?<\/script\s*>/gi, '');
}
function removeEventHandlers(markup) {
  return markup.replace(/\s+on\w+\s*=\s*(?:"[^"]*"|'[^']*'|[^\s>]+)/gi, '');
}
function removeForbiddenElements(markup) {
  return markup
    .replace(/<foreignObject\b[\s\S]*?<\/foreignObject\s*>/gi, '')
    .replace(/<(?:iframe|object|embed|audio|video|canvas)\b[\s\S]*?<\/(?:iframe|object|embed|audio|video|canvas)\s*>/gi, '')
    .replace(/<(?:iframe|object|embed|audio|video|canvas)\b[^>]*\/?\s*>/gi, '');
}
function removeExternalReferences(markup) {
  return markup
    .replace(/\b(?:xlink:)?href\s*=\s*"(?!\#)(?!data:image\/)[^"]*"/gi, 'href="#"')
    .replace(/\b(?:xlink:)?href\s*=\s*'(?!\#)(?!data:image\/)[^']*'/gi, "href='#'")
    .replace(/url\(\s*['"]?(?!#|data:image\/)[^)]+\)/gi, 'none');
}
function normalizeRoot(markup) {
  let next = markup;
  if (!/\bxmlns\s*=/.test(next)) next = next.replace(/<svg\b/i, `<svg xmlns="${SVG_NAMESPACE}"`);
  if (!/\bviewBox\s*=/.test(next)) {
    const width = Number(next.match(/\bwidth\s*=\s*["']([\d.]+)/i)?.[1]) || 100;
    const height = Number(next.match(/\bheight\s*=\s*["']([\d.]+)/i)?.[1]) || 100;
    next = next.replace(/<svg\b/i, `<svg viewBox="0 0 ${width} ${height}"`);
  }
  return next;
}

export function inspectSvgMarkup(input) {
  const original = String(input || '').trim();
  const issues = [];
  if (!original) return { valid: false, issues: ['SVG content is empty.'], markup: '', viewBox: null };
  if (original.length > 200000) issues.push('SVG exceeds the maximum allowed size.');
  if (/<script\b/i.test(original)) issues.push('Script elements were removed.');
  if (/\son\w+\s*=/i.test(original)) issues.push('Inline event handlers were removed.');
  if (/<foreignObject\b/i.test(original)) issues.push('foreignObject content was removed.');
  if (/\b(?:xlink:)?href\s*=\s*["'](?!#|data:image\/)/i.test(original)) issues.push('External references were removed.');
  let markup = original;
  if (/^\s*[Mm]\s*[\d\s,\-.]+/.test(markup)) markup = `<svg xmlns="${SVG_NAMESPACE}" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><path d="${markup}"/></svg>`;
  if (!/<svg\b/i.test(markup)) return { valid: false, issues: [...issues, 'SVG content must contain a root <svg> element.'], markup: '', viewBox: null };
  markup = normalizeRoot(removeExternalReferences(removeEventHandlers(removeForbiddenElements(removeScripts(markup)))));
  const viewBoxMatch = markup.match(/\bviewBox\s*=\s*["']\s*([\d+\-.eE]+)[,\s]+([\d+\-.eE]+)[,\s]+([\d+\-.eE]+)[,\s]+([\d+\-.eE]+)\s*["']/i);
  const viewBox = viewBoxMatch ? viewBoxMatch.slice(1).map(Number) : null;
  if (viewBox && (!(viewBox[2] > 0) || !(viewBox[3] > 0))) issues.push('The SVG viewBox width and height must be positive.');
  if (typeof DOMParser !== 'undefined') {
    try {
      const parsed = new DOMParser().parseFromString(markup, 'image/svg+xml');
      const parserError = parsed.querySelector('parsererror');
      if (parserError) issues.push(`SVG parse error: ${parserError.textContent?.trim().slice(0, 240) || 'invalid markup'}`);
      if (parsed.documentElement?.localName !== 'svg') issues.push('The root element must be <svg>.');
    } catch (error) {
      issues.push(`SVG parse error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }
  const fatal = issues.some(issue => /exceeds|must contain|parse error|must be positive|root element/i.test(issue));
  return { valid: !fatal && !!markup, issues, markup, viewBox };
}

export function sanitizeSvgMarkup(input) {
  const result = inspectSvgMarkup(input);
  if (!result.valid) throw new Error(result.issues.join(' '));
  return result.markup;
}

export function svgDataUrl(svg) {
  const markup = typeof svg === 'string' ? svg : DEFAULT_SVG_MARKUP;
  const encoded = globalThis.btoa ? globalThis.btoa(unescapePercent(encodeURIComponent(markup))) : Buffer.from(markup).toString('base64');
  return `data:image/svg+xml;base64,${encoded}`;
}

function unescapePercent(str) {
  return str.replace(/%([0-9A-F]{2})/gi, (_, hex) => String.fromCharCode(parseInt(hex, 16)));
}

// FILE: src/lib/theme.js
================================================================================
const THEME_KEY = 'canvasforge-theme';
const THEMES = new Set(['light', 'dark', 'system']);

export function getThemePreference() {
  try {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(THEME_KEY);
    return THEMES.has(saved) ? saved : 'system';
  } catch {
    return 'system';
  }
}

export function resolveTheme(preference = getThemePreference()) {
  if (preference === 'system') {
    return globalThis.matchMedia?.('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light';
  }
  return preference;
}

export function applyTheme(preference = getThemePreference()) {
  const resolved = resolveTheme(preference);
  const root = globalThis.document?.documentElement;
  if (root) {
    root.dataset.theme = resolved;
    root.dataset.themePreference = preference;
    root.style.colorScheme = resolved;
    const meta = globalThis.document?.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]');
    if (meta) meta.setAttribute('content', resolved === 'dark' ? '#111319' : '#f4f6fa');
  }
  return resolved;
}

export function saveThemePreference(preference) {
  const safe = THEMES.has(preference) ? preference : 'system';
  try { localStorage.setItem(THEME_KEY, safe); } catch {}
  applyTheme(safe);
  globalThis.dispatchEvent?.(new CustomEvent('canvasforge:theme', { detail: { preference: safe } }));
  return safe;
}

export function subscribeToSystemTheme(listener) {
  const query = globalThis.matchMedia?.('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
  if (!query) return () => {};
  const handle = () => {
    if (getThemePreference() === 'system') listener(applyTheme('system'));
  };
  query.addEventListener?.('change', handle);
  return () => query.removeEventListener?.('change', handle);
}
