export const useEditorStore = create((set, get) => ({
  session: readMigratedStorage('session') || '',
  user: null,
  workspaces: [],
  currentWorkspaceId: readMigratedStorage('organization') || localStorage.getItem(workspaceIdKey) || localStorage.getItem(legacyWorkspaceIdKey) || localStorage.getItem(legacyOrgKey) || '',
  organizations: [],
  currentOrganizationId: readMigratedStorage('organization') || localStorage.getItem(workspaceIdKey) || localStorage.getItem(legacyWorkspaceIdKey) || localStorage.getItem(legacyOrgKey) || '',
  role: 'viewer',
  aiMode: loadAIProviderSettings().activeMode,
  billingSummary: null,
  creditLedger: [],
  aiUsage: null,
  marketplaceListings: [],
  marketplacePurchases: [],
  marketplaceEarnings: null,
  commercialBusy: false,

  design: null,
  document: null,
  pageIndex: 0,
  selection: [],
  history: [],
  future: [],
  historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
  historyTransactionRevision: null,

  status: 'idle',
  lastError: '',
  online: navigator.onLine,
  tabConflict: false,
  recoveryPending: false,
  documentRevision: 0,
  savedRevision: 0,
  savingRevision: null,
  saveQueued: false,
  lastSavedAt: null,
  lastAutoVersionAt: 0,

  ...workspacePreferences,
  toasts: [],

  aiPanelOpen: false,
  aiBusy: false,
  aiError: '',
  aiPlan: null,
  aiPreview: null,
  aiRuns: [],
  aiRender: null,
  aiRenders: [],
  aiAnnotation: null,
  aiCandidates: [],
  aiRefinementLimit: 3,
  aiTheme: null,
  aiAssetRequests: [],
  aiAssetResults: [],
  aiAssetLoop: null,
  aiAgent: null,

  assets: [],
  assetFolders: [],
  templateFolders: [],
  templates: [],
  components: [],
  brands: [],
  versions: [],
  exports: [],
  comments: [],
  shares: [],
  members: [],
  notifications: [],

  notify(message, type = 'info', timeout = 4500) {
    const id = uuid();
    set(state => ({ toasts: [...state.toasts, { id, message, type }] }));
    if (timeout) setTimeout(() => get().dismissToast(id), timeout);
    return id;
  },
  dismissToast(id) {
    set(state => ({ toasts: state.toasts.filter(item => item.id !== id) }));
  },
  toggleAIPanel(value) { set({ aiPanelOpen: typeof value === 'boolean' ? value : !get().aiPanelOpen }); },
  clearAIPlan() { set({ aiPlan: null, aiPreview: null, aiError: '', aiTheme: null, aiAssetRequests: [], aiAssetResults: [], aiAssetLoop: null }); },
  resetAIAgent() {
    agentRunToken++;
    set({ aiAgent: null, aiBusy: false, aiError: '', aiPlan: null, aiPreview: null });
  },
  async startAIAgent(instruction, options = {}) {
    const state = get();
    const context = state.getAIContext();
    if (!context) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    if (!String(instruction || '').trim()) throw new Error('Describe what you want the design agent to create or revise.');
    const session = createAgentSession(instruction, context, options);
    const shouldClarify = session.questions.length > 0 && options.askQuestions !== false;
    set({
      aiAgent: { ...session, status: shouldClarify ? AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_CLARIFICATION : AGENT_STATES.PLANNING },
      aiError: '', aiPlan: null, aiPreview: null
    });
    if (shouldClarify) return get().aiAgent;
    return get().generateAIAgentConcepts();
  },
  async answerAIAgent(answer) {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    const content = String(answer || '').trim();
    if (!content) throw new Error('Add an answer or choose the recommended assumptions.');
    set({
      aiAgent: {
        ...session,
        brief: appendBriefAnswer(session.brief, content),
        questions: [],
        status: AGENT_STATES.PLANNING,
        messages: [...session.messages, { id: uuid(), role: 'user', content, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      }
    });
    return get().generateAIAgentConcepts();
  },
  async generateAIAgentConcepts({ refinement = '', parentConceptId = null } = {}) {
    const state = get();
    const session = state.aiAgent;
    const context = state.getAIContext();
    if (!session || !context) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    if (session.status === AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED) throw new Error('This agent session was cancelled.');
    const token = ++agentRunToken;
    const status = parentConceptId ? AGENT_STATES.REFINING_CONCEPT : AGENT_STATES.GENERATING_CONCEPTS;
    set({
      aiBusy: true,
      aiError: '',
      aiAgent: {
        ...session,
        paused: false,
        status,
        tasks: updateAgentTask(session.tasks, 'concepts', { status: 'in_progress', progress: 20, details: refinement || 'Creating three low-quality variants' }),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      }
    });
    try {
      let concepts = [];
      const current = get().aiAgent;
      if (current.options?.provider !== 'local') {
        try {
          const payload = await api.aiAgentConcepts(state.design.id, {
            instruction: current.instruction,
            context,
            brief: current.brief,
            count: 3,
            quality: 'low',
            refinement,
            parentConceptId,
            steering: current.steering
          });
          concepts = normalizeAgentConcepts(payload, context, current.brief);
        } catch (error) {
          if (current.options?.provider === 'server' && ![404, 405, 501].includes(error.status)) throw error;
        }
      }
      const localConcepts = createLocalConceptVariants(context, current.brief, { refinement, parentConceptId });
      if (!concepts.length) {
        concepts = localConcepts;
        if (current.options?.provider !== 'local') {
          const width = Number(context.design?.width || 1080);
          const height = Number(context.design?.height || 1080);
          const draftScale = Math.min(1, 512 / Math.max(width, height));
          const generated = await Promise.all(localConcepts.map(async concept => {
            try {
              const image = await api.aiGenerateImage({
                prompt: concept.prompt,
                negativePrompt: concept.negativePrompt,
                width: Math.max(256, Math.round(width * draftScale)),
                height: Math.max(256, Math.round(height * draftScale)),
                quality: 'draft',
                count: 1,
                seed: concept.seed,
                referenceAssetIds: current.brief.mustUseAssetIds || [],
                sessionId: current.id,
                conceptId: concept.id
              });
              const previewUrl = image?.url || image?.previewUrl || image?.images?.[0]?.url || null;
              return previewUrl ? { ...concept, previewUrl, previewMode: 'image', generatedAssetId: image?.assetId || image?.images?.[0]?.assetId || null } : concept;
            } catch {
              return concept;
            }
          }));
          concepts = generated;
        }
      } else concepts = concepts.map((concept, index) => ({ ...localConcepts[index], ...concept, commandBatch: concept.commandBatch || localConcepts[index]?.commandBatch }));

      const previewed = concepts.map(concept => {
        if (!concept.commandBatch) return concept;
        const batch = { ...concept.commandBatch, baseRevision: state.documentRevision };
        try {
          const result = applyCommandBatch(state.document, batch, {
            pageIndex: state.pageIndex, selection: state.selection, assets: state.assets, brands: state.brands,
            components: state.components, revision: state.documentRevision
          });
          const lint = lintDocument(result.document);
          return {
            ...concept,
            commandBatch: batch,
            document: result.document,
            pageIndex: Math.max(0, result.document.pages.length - 1),
            diff: diffDocuments(state.document, result.document),
            lint,
            blockingIssues: lint.issues.filter(issue => issue.severity === 'critical')
          };
        } catch (error) {
          return { ...concept, commandBatch: batch, previewError: error.message };
        }
      });
      if (token !== agentRunToken || get().aiAgent?.paused || get().aiAgent?.status === AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED) return get().aiAgent;
      const latest = get().aiAgent;
      const assistantMessage = refinement
        ? `I created three refinements based on: ${refinement}`
        : `I created three low-quality concept directions for ${latest.classification.intent.replaceAll('_', ' ')}.`;
      const next = {
        ...latest,
        concepts: previewed,
        selectedConceptId: null,
        status: AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_CONCEPT_SELECTION,
        messages: [...latest.messages, { id: uuid(), role: 'assistant', content: assistantMessage, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
        tasks: updateAgentTask(updateAgentTask(latest.tasks, 'concepts', { status: 'completed', progress: 100 }), 'selection', { status: 'in_progress', progress: 10 }),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };
      set({ aiAgent: next });
      return next;
    } catch (error) {
      if (token === agentRunToken) set(currentState => ({
        aiError: error.message || 'Concept generation failed.',
        aiAgent: currentState.aiAgent ? { ...currentState.aiAgent, status: AGENT_STATES.FAILED, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : null
      }));
      throw error;
    } finally {
      if (token === agentRunToken) set({ aiBusy: false });
    }
  },
  selectAIAgentConcept(conceptId) {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    const concept = session.concepts.find(item => item.id === conceptId);
    if (!concept) throw new Error('The selected concept no longer exists.');
    set({
      aiAgent: {
        ...session,
        selectedConceptId: conceptId,
        status: AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_CONCEPT_APPROVAL,
        tasks: updateAgentTask(session.tasks, 'selection', { status: 'completed', progress: 100, details: concept.title }),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      }
    });
    return concept;
  },
  async refineAIAgentConcept(conceptId, feedback) {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    const concept = session.concepts.find(item => item.id === conceptId);
    if (!concept) throw new Error('Select a concept to refine.');
    const content = String(feedback || '').trim();
    if (!content) throw new Error('Describe what should change in the next variants.');
    set({
      aiAgent: {
        ...session,
        selectedConceptId: conceptId,
        steering: [...session.steering, { id: uuid(), content, conceptId, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
        messages: [...session.messages, { id: uuid(), role: 'user', content, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      }
    });
    return get().generateAIAgentConcepts({ refinement: content, parentConceptId: conceptId });
  },
  async approveAIAgentConcept(conceptId) {
    const state = get();
    const session = state.aiAgent;
    if (!session) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    const concept = session.concepts.find(item => item.id === conceptId);
    if (!concept) throw new Error('Select a concept to approve.');
    set({ aiBusy: true, aiError: '', aiAgent: { ...session, selectedConceptId: conceptId, status: AGENT_STATES.COMPILING_DESIGN, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } });
    try {
      let batch = concept.commandBatch;
      if (!batch) {
        const payload = await api.aiAgentCompile(state.design.id, {
          context: state.getAIContext(),
          brief: session.brief,
          concept,
          steering: session.steering
        });
        batch = payload?.commandBatch || payload?.batch || payload;
      }
      if (!batch?.commands) throw new Error('The approved concept did not include an editable command bundle. Configure the agent compile endpoint or regenerate the concepts.');
      batch = { ...batch, schemaVersion: Number(batch.schemaVersion || 1), baseRevision: state.documentRevision };
      const preview = get().previewAICommands(batch);
      const latest = get().aiAgent || session;
      set({
        aiAgent: {
          ...latest,
          selectedConceptId: conceptId,
          status: AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_FINAL_APPROVAL,
          tasks: updateAgentTask(updateAgentTask(updateAgentTask(latest.tasks, 'compile', { status: 'completed', progress: 100 }), 'quality', { status: 'completed', progress: 100, details: `${preview.lint?.issues?.length || 0} design checks` }), 'approval', { status: 'in_progress', progress: 20 }),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }
      });
      return preview;
    } catch (error) {
      set(current => ({ aiError: error.message, aiAgent: current.aiAgent ? { ...current.aiAgent, status: AGENT_STATES.FAILED } : null }));
      throw error;
    } finally {
      set({ aiBusy: false });
    }
  },
  async steerAIAgent(message) {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session) throw new Error('Start an agent session first.');
    const content = String(message || '').trim();
    if (!content) return session;
    agentRunToken++;
    const steering = { id: uuid(), content, conceptId: session.selectedConceptId || null, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
    const next = {
      ...session,
      paused: true,
      previousStatus: session.status,
      status: AGENT_STATES.PAUSED,
      steering: [...session.steering, steering],
      messages: [...session.messages, { id: uuid(), role: 'user', content, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    set({ aiAgent: next, aiBusy: false });
    return next;
  },
  pauseAIAgent() {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session || [AGENT_STATES.COMPLETED, AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED].includes(session.status)) return;
    agentRunToken++;
    set({ aiBusy: false, aiAgent: { ...session, paused: true, previousStatus: session.status, status: AGENT_STATES.PAUSED, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } });
  },
  async resumeAIAgent() {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session || !session.paused) return session;
    const feedback = session.steering.at(-1)?.content || '';
    const selected = session.selectedConceptId;
    set({ aiAgent: { ...session, paused: false, status: session.previousStatus || AGENT_STATES.PLANNING, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } });
    if (selected && feedback) return get().generateAIAgentConcepts({ refinement: feedback, parentConceptId: selected });
    if (!session.concepts.length) return get().generateAIAgentConcepts();
    return get().aiAgent;
  },
  cancelAIAgent() {
    const session = get().aiAgent;
    if (!session) return;
    agentRunToken++;
    set({ aiBusy: false, aiAgent: { ...session, paused: false, status: AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } });
  },

  setWorkspacePreference(key, value) {
    set({ [key]: value });
    persistWorkspace(get());
  },
  toggleLeftPanel() {
    const open = !get().leftPanelOpen;
    set({ leftPanelOpen: open, ...(open && window.innerWidth <= 900 ? { rightPanelOpen: false } : {}) });
    persistWorkspace(get());
  },
  toggleRightPanel() {
    const open = !get().rightPanelOpen;
    set({ rightPanelOpen: open, ...(open && window.innerWidth <= 900 ? { leftPanelOpen: false } : {}) });
    persistWorkspace(get());
  },

  async login(email, password) {
    const result = await api.login(email, password);
    get().applyAuth(result);
    return result;
  },
  async register(input) {
    const result = await api.register(input);
    get().applyAuth(result);
    return result;
  },
  async tokenLogin(token) {
    const result = await api.tokenLogin(token);
    get().applyAuth(result);
    return result;
  },
  applyAuth(result) {
    writeStorage('session', result.token);
    const rawWorkspaces = result.workspaces || result.organizations || [];
    const workspaces = rawWorkspaces.map(item => ({
      ...item,
      id: item.id || item.workspace_id || item.organization_id,
      workspace_id: item.workspace_id || item.id || item.organization_id,
      organization_id: item.organization_id || item.workspace_id || item.id,
      type: item.type || 'organization'
    }));
    const workspaceId = result.currentWorkspaceId || result.currentOrganizationId || workspaces[0]?.id || '';
    if (workspaceId) {
      writeStorage('organization', workspaceId);
      localStorage.setItem(workspaceIdKey, workspaceId);
      localStorage.setItem(legacyWorkspaceIdKey, workspaceId);
      localStorage.setItem(legacyOrgKey, workspaceId);
    }
    const role = workspaces.find(item => item.id === workspaceId)?.role || 'viewer';
    set({
      session: result.token,
      user: result.user,
      workspaces,
      organizations: workspaces,
      currentWorkspaceId: workspaceId,
      currentOrganizationId: workspaceId,
      role
    });
  },
  async hydrateAuth() {
    if (!get().session) return false;
    try {
      const result = await api.me();
      get().applyAuth({ ...result, token: get().session });
      await get().refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {});
      return true;
    } catch {
      get().logout();
      return false;
    }
  },
  async logout() {
    try { await api.logout(); } catch {}
    removeStorage('session');
    localStorage.removeItem(workspaceIdKey);
    localStorage.removeItem(legacyWorkspaceIdKey);
    localStorage.removeItem(legacyOrgKey);
    removeStorage('organization');
    set({ session: '', user: null, workspaces: [], organizations: [], currentWorkspaceId: '', currentOrganizationId: '', role: 'viewer', design: null, document: null, billingSummary: null, creditLedger: [], aiUsage: null });
  },
  setWorkspace(id) {
    writeStorage('organization', id);
    localStorage.setItem(workspaceIdKey, id);
    localStorage.setItem(legacyWorkspaceIdKey, id);
    localStorage.setItem(legacyOrgKey, id);
    const workspace = get().workspaces.find(item => item.id === id || item.workspace_id === id || item.organization_id === id);
    set({
      currentWorkspaceId: id,
      currentOrganizationId: id,
      role: workspace?.role || 'viewer',
      design: null,
      document: null,
      assets: [],
      assetFolders: [],
      templateFolders: [],
      templates: [],
      components: [],
      brands: [],
      billingSummary: null,
      creditLedger: [],
      aiUsage: null
    });
    get().refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {});
  },
  setOrganization(id) { get().setWorkspace(id); },
  async createWorkspace(input) {
    const workspace = await api.createWorkspace(typeof input === 'string' ? { name: input, type: 'organization' } : input);
    const result = await api.me();
    get().applyAuth({ ...result, token: get().session, currentWorkspaceId: workspace.id });
    return workspace;
  },
  async createOrganization(name) { return get().createWorkspace({ name, type: 'organization' }); },
  async changePassword(currentPassword, newPassword) {
    await api.changePassword(currentPassword, newPassword);
    await get().logout();
  },

  setOnline(online) {
    const state = get();
    const hasUnsaved = state.documentRevision > state.savedRevision;
    const status = !online ? 'offline' : state.tabConflict ? 'conflict' : state.recoveryPending ? 'recovered' : hasUnsaved ? 'dirty' : (state.status === 'offline' ? 'saved' : state.status);
    set({ online, status });
    if (online && state.document && hasUnsaved && !state.tabConflict && !state.recoveryPending) get().save().catch(() => {});
  },
  setSelection: selection => set({ selection }),
  setPageIndex: pageIndex => set({ pageIndex, selection: [] }),
  closeDesign: () => set({
    design: null,
    document: null,
    pageIndex: 0,
    selection: [],
    history: [],
    future: [],
    historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
    historyTransactionRevision: null,
    tabConflict: false,
    recoveryPending: false,
    documentRevision: 0,
    savedRevision: 0,
    aiPlan: null,
    aiPreview: null,
    aiRender: null,
    aiRenders: [],
    aiAnnotation: null,
    aiCandidates: [],
    aiRefinementLimit: 3,
    aiTheme: null,
    aiAssetRequests: [],
    aiAssetResults: [],
    aiAssetLoop: null,
    aiAgent: null,
    aiError: ''
  }),

  async loadDesign(id, { ignoreRecovery = false } = {}) {
    set({ status: 'loading', lastError: '', tabConflict: false, recoveryPending: false });
    channel?.postMessage({ type: 'open', designId: id, tabId });
    const design = await api.getDesign(id);
    const serverDocument = normalizeDocument(design.document);
    const recovery = ignoreRecovery ? null : await loadRecovery(id).catch(() => null);
    const useRecovery = recovery?.updatedAt > design.updated_at && recovery?.document;
    const document = useRecovery ? normalizeDocument(recovery.document) : serverDocument;
    set({
      design,
      document,
      pageIndex: 0,
      selection: [],
      history: [],
      future: [],
      historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
      historyTransactionRevision: null,
      status: useRecovery ? 'recovered' : 'saved',
      recoveryPending: !!useRecovery,
      documentRevision: useRecovery ? 1 : 0,
      savedRevision: 0,
      savingRevision: null,
      saveQueued: false,
      lastSavedAt: design.updated_at ? new Date(design.updated_at).getTime() : Date.now(),
      aiPlan: null,
      aiPreview: null,
      aiRender: null,
      aiRenders: [],
      aiAnnotation: null,
      aiCandidates: [],
      aiRefinementLimit: 3,
      aiTheme: null,
      aiAssetRequests: [],
      aiAssetResults: [],
      aiAssetLoop: null,
      aiError: ''
    });
    await get().refreshResources();
  },
  async createDesign(input = {}) {
    const design = await api.createDesign(input);
    await get().loadDesign(design.id);
    return design;
  },
  async refreshResources() {
    const design = get().design;
    const tasks = [api.listAssets(), api.listAssetFolders(), api.listTemplateFolders().catch(() => []), api.listTemplateFolderItems().catch(() => []), api.listTemplates(), api.listComponents(), api.listBrandKits(), api.listNotifications()];
    if (design) tasks.push(api.listVersions(design.id), api.listExports(design.id), api.listComments(design.id), api.listShares(design.id));
    const [assets, assetFolders, templateFolders, templateFolderItems, rawTemplates, components, brands, notifications, versions = [], exports = [], comments = [], shares = []] = await Promise.all(tasks);
    const folderByTemplate = new Map(templateFolderItems.map(item => [item.templateId || item.template_id, item.folderId || item.folder_id || null]));
    const templates = rawTemplates.map(item => ({ ...item, folder_id: item.folder_id || item.folderId || folderByTemplate.get(item.id) || null }));
    set({ assets, assetFolders, templateFolders, templates, components, brands, notifications, versions, exports, comments, shares });
  },
  setAIMode(mode) {
    const settings = saveAIProviderSettings({ activeMode: mode });
    set({ aiMode: settings.activeMode });
  },
  async refreshCommercialData() {
    if (!get().session) return null;
    set({ commercialBusy: true });
    try {
      const [billingSummary, creditLedger, aiUsage] = await Promise.all([
        api.billingSummary().catch(() => null),
        api.creditLedger(50).catch(() => []),
        api.aiUsage().catch(() => null)
      ]);
      set({ billingSummary, creditLedger: creditLedger?.entries || creditLedger || [], aiUsage });
      return { billingSummary, creditLedger, aiUsage };
    } finally { set({ commercialBusy: false }); }
  },
  async loadMarketplace(params = {}) {
    set({ commercialBusy: true });
    try {
      const [marketplaceListings, marketplacePurchases, marketplaceEarnings] = await Promise.all([
        api.marketplaceListings(params),
        api.marketplacePurchases().catch(() => []),
        api.marketplaceEarnings().catch(() => null)
      ]);
      set({ marketplaceListings: marketplaceListings?.items || marketplaceListings || [], marketplacePurchases: marketplacePurchases?.items || marketplacePurchases || [], marketplaceEarnings });
      return marketplaceListings;
    } finally { set({ commercialBusy: false }); }
  },
  async publishAsset(assetId, input = {}) {
    if (!input?.rightsDeclaration?.ownsRights || !input?.rightsDeclaration?.allowsRedistribution) throw new Error('A complete rights declaration is required before an asset can be submitted to the Commons.');
    const listing = await api.publishMarketplaceListing({ listingType: 'asset', sourceAssetId: assetId, commons: true, ...input });
    await get().loadMarketplace().catch(() => {});
    return listing;
  },
  async publishTemplate(templateId, input = {}) {
    const listing = await api.publishMarketplaceListing({ listingType: 'template', sourceTemplateId: templateId, ...input });
    await get().loadMarketplace().catch(() => {});
    return listing;
  },
  async acquireMarketplaceListing(id) {
    const listing = get().marketplaceListings.find(item => item.id === id);
    if (listing?.priceType === 'credits' && Number(listing.priceCredits) > 0) await api.purchaseMarketplaceListing(id);
    const result = await api.installMarketplaceListing(id, get().currentWorkspaceId);
    await Promise.all([get().refreshResources(), get().refreshCommercialData()]);
    return result;
  },

  beginHistoryTransaction() {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.document || state.historyTransactionSnapshot) return;
    set({ historyTransactionSnapshot: clone(state.document), historyTransactionRevision: state.documentRevision });
  },
  commitHistoryTransaction() {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.historyTransactionSnapshot) return;
    const before = state.historyTransactionSnapshot;
    const changed = state.documentRevision !== state.historyTransactionRevision;
    set(current => ({
      historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
      historyTransactionRevision: null,
      history: changed ? [...current.history.slice(-79), before] : current.history,
      future: changed ? [] : current.future
    }));
  },
  cancelHistoryTransaction() {
    set({ historyTransactionSnapshot: null, historyTransactionRevision: null });
  },
  commitDocument(nextDocument, { recordHistory = true, status = 'dirty' } = {}) {
    const current = get().document;
    if (!current) return;
    const next = normalizeDocument(nextDocument);
    set(state => ({
      document: next,
      documentRevision: state.documentRevision + 1,
      history: recordHistory && !state.historyTransactionSnapshot ? [...state.history.slice(-79), clone(current)] : state.history,
      future: recordHistory && !state.historyTransactionSnapshot ? [] : state.future,
      status: state.online ? status : 'offline'
    }));
    clearTimeout(recoveryTimer);
    recoveryTimer = setTimeout(() => saveRecovery(get().design?.id, next).catch(() => {}), 250);
  },
  updatePage(mutator, options = {}) {
    const doc = clone(get().document);
    if (!doc) return;
    const page = doc.pages[get().pageIndex];
    mutator(page, doc);
    applyAllFrameLayouts(page);
    get().commitDocument(doc, options);
  },
  updateElements(ids, patch, options = {}) {
    const targetIds = new Set(ids || []);
    get().updatePage(page => {
      const before = new Map(page.elements.map(element => [element.id, clone(element)]));
      page.elements = page.elements.map(element => targetIds.has(element.id)
        ? { ...element, ...(typeof patch === 'function' ? patch(element) : patch) }
        : element);
      const selectedFrames = page.elements.filter(element => targetIds.has(element.id) && element.type === 'frame');
      const rootFrames = selectedFrames.filter(frame => {
        let parentId = before.get(frame.id)?.parentId;
        while (parentId) {
          if (targetIds.has(parentId)) return false;
          parentId = before.get(parentId)?.parentId;
        }
        return true;
      });
      for (const frame of rootFrames) {
        const previous = before.get(frame.id);
        if (previous && ['x', 'y', 'width', 'height', 'rotation'].some(key => Number(previous[key] || 0) !== Number(frame[key] || 0))) {
          transformFrameDescendants(page, frame.id, previous, frame);
        }
      }
    }, options);
  },
  addElement(element) {
    get().updatePage(page => {
      element.zIndex = page.elements.length;
      page.elements.push(element);
    });
    set({ selection: [element.id] });
  },
  addElements(elements) {
    get().updatePage(page => {
      const start = page.elements.length;
      page.elements.push(...elements.map((element, index) => ({ ...element, zIndex: start + index })));
    });
    set({ selection: elements.map(element => element.id) });
  },
  removeSelection() {
    const ids = get().selection;
    if (!ids.length) return;
    get().updatePage((page, doc) => {
      const removed = new Set([...ids, ...collectDescendantIds(page, ids)]);
      page.elements = page.elements.filter(element => !removed.has(element.id)).map((element, index) => ({ ...element, zIndex: index }));
      doc.layoutGroups = (doc.layoutGroups || [])
        .map(group => ({ ...group, elementIds: group.elementIds.filter(id => !removed.has(id)) }))
        .filter(group => group.elementIds.length > 1);
    });
    set({ selection: [] });
  },
  reparentSelection(parentId = null) {
    const ids = get().selection;
    if (!ids.length) return;
    get().updatePage(page => reparentElements(page, ids, parentId));
  },
  groupSelection() {
    const ids = get().selection;
    if (ids.length < 2) throw new Error('Select at least two objects to group.');
    const groupId = uuid();
    get().updatePage(page => {
      page.elements = page.elements.map(element => ids.includes(element.id) ? { ...element, groupId } : element);
    });
    set({ selection: ids });
    return groupId;
  },
  ungroupSelection() {
    const { selection, document, pageIndex } = get();
    const page = document?.pages?.[pageIndex];
    const groupIds = new Set((page?.elements || []).filter(element => selection.includes(element.id)).map(element => element.groupId).filter(Boolean));
    if (!groupIds.size) throw new Error('The current selection is not grouped.');
    get().updatePage(currentPage => {
      currentPage.elements = currentPage.elements.map(element => groupIds.has(element.groupId) ? { ...element, groupId: null } : element);
    });
    return [...groupIds];
  },
  pushHistorySnapshot(snapshot) {
    if (!snapshot) return;
    set(state => ({ history: [...state.history.slice(-79), clone(snapshot)], future: [] }));
  },
  undo() {
    const { history, document, future } = get();
    if (!history.length) return;
    set(state => ({
      document: clone(history.at(-1)),
      history: history.slice(0, -1),
      future: [clone(document), ...future].slice(0, 80),
      status: state.online ? 'dirty' : 'offline',
      selection: [],
      historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
      historyTransactionRevision: null,
      documentRevision: state.documentRevision + 1
    }));
  },
  redo() {
    const { history, document, future } = get();
    if (!future.length) return;
    set(state => ({
      document: clone(future[0]),
      history: [...history, clone(document)].slice(-80),
      future: future.slice(1),
      status: state.online ? 'dirty' : 'offline',
      selection: [],
      historyTransactionSnapshot: null,
      historyTransactionRevision: null,
      documentRevision: state.documentRevision + 1
    }));
  },

  async save({ createVersion = false, versionLabel = null, retry = 0, forceOverwrite = false, allowRecovered = false } = {}) {
    const initial = get();
    if (!initial.design || !initial.document) return initial.design;
    if (initial.tabConflict && !forceOverwrite) {
      const error = new Error('This design is open in another tab. Resolve the editing conflict before saving.');
      set({ status: 'conflict', lastError: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
    if (initial.recoveryPending && !allowRecovered) {
      const error = new Error('Choose whether to continue with or discard the recovered version before saving.');
      set({ status: 'recovered', lastError: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
    if (!initial.online) {
      set({ status: 'offline' });
      return initial.design;
    }
    if (activeSavePromise) {
      const designId = initial.design.id;
      set({ saveQueued: true });
      await activeSavePromise.catch(() => {});
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
      const latest = get();
      if (latest.design?.id === designId && latest.documentRevision > latest.savedRevision && !latest.tabConflict && !latest.recoveryPending) {
        return get().save({ createVersion, versionLabel, retry, forceOverwrite, allowRecovered });
      }
      return latest.design;
    }

    const snapshot = clone(initial.document);
    const revision = initial.documentRevision;
    const designId = initial.design.id;
    const autoVersion = !createVersion && Date.now() - initial.lastAutoVersionAt > 5 * 60 * 1000;
    clearTimeout(saveRetryTimer);
    set({ status: 'saving', lastError: '', savingRevision: revision, saveQueued: false });

    activeSavePromise = (async () => {
      try {
        const saved = await api.saveDesign(designId, {
          title: snapshot.title || initial.design.title,
          document: snapshot,
          createVersion: createVersion || autoVersion,
          versionLabel: versionLabel || (autoVersion ? 'Automatic recovery version' : null)
        });
        if (get().design?.id !== designId) return saved;
        await clearRecovery(designId).catch(() => {});
        const current = get();
        const pending = current.documentRevision > revision;
        if (pending) saveRecovery(designId, current.document).catch(() => {});
        set({
          design: saved,
          savedRevision: Math.max(current.savedRevision, revision),
          status: current.tabConflict ? 'conflict' : (pending ? 'dirty' : 'saved'),
          savingRevision: null,
          lastSavedAt: Date.now(),
          lastAutoVersionAt: autoVersion ? Date.now() : current.lastAutoVersionAt,
          recoveryPending: false
        });
        if (createVersion || autoVersion) set({ versions: await api.listVersions(designId) });
        return saved;
      } catch (error) {
        const current = get();
        if (current.design?.id !== designId) throw error;
        set({ status: current.tabConflict ? 'conflict' : (current.online ? 'save-failed' : 'offline'), lastError: error.message, savingRevision: null });
        if (retry < 4 && current.online && !current.tabConflict) {
          clearTimeout(saveRetryTimer);
          saveRetryTimer = setTimeout(() => {
            get().save({ createVersion, versionLabel, retry: retry + 1, forceOverwrite, allowRecovered }).catch(() => {});
          }, Math.min(30000, 1500 * 2 ** retry));
        }
        throw error;
      }
    })();

    try {
      return await activeSavePromise;
    } finally {
      activeSavePromise = null;
      const current = get();
      if ((current.saveQueued || current.documentRevision > current.savedRevision) && current.online && !current.tabConflict && !current.recoveryPending) {
        set({ saveQueued: false });
        queueMicrotask(() => get().save().catch(() => {}));
      }
    }
  },

  continueRecovery() {
    set({ recoveryPending: false, status: get().online ? 'dirty' : 'offline', lastError: '' });
  },
  async discardRecovery() {
    const id = get().design?.id;
    if (!id) return;
    await clearRecovery(id).catch(() => {});
    await get().loadDesign(id, { ignoreRecovery: true });
  },
  async reloadConflict() {
    const id = get().design?.id;
    if (!id) return;
    await get().loadDesign(id, { ignoreRecovery: true });
  },
  async takeOverConflict() {
    const id = get().design?.id;
    if (!id) return;
    set({ tabConflict: false, status: get().online ? 'dirty' : 'offline', lastError: '' });
    channel?.postMessage({ type: 'takeover', designId: id, tabId });
    return get().save({ forceOverwrite: true, allowRecovered: true });
  },

  async ensureAssetFolder(name) {
    let folder = get().assetFolders.find(item => String(item.name).toLowerCase() === String(name).toLowerCase());
    if (!folder) {
      folder = await api.createAssetFolder(name);
      set(state => ({ assetFolders: [...state.assetFolders, folder] }));
    }
    return folder;
  },
  async upload(file, opts = {}) {
    const options = { ...opts };
    if (!options.folderId) {
      const folder = await get().ensureAssetFolder(options.sourceType === 'ai_generation' ? 'AI generated' : 'Uploads').catch(() => null);
      if (folder) options.folderId = folder.id;
    }
    const asset = await api.uploadAsset(file, options);
    set(state => ({ assets: [asset, ...state.assets] }));
    return asset;
  },
  async uploadMany(files, opts = {}) {
    const options = { ...opts };
    if (!options.folderId) {
      const folder = await get().ensureAssetFolder(options.sourceType === 'ai_generation' ? 'AI generated' : 'Uploads').catch(() => null);
      if (folder) options.folderId = folder.id;
    }
    const result = await api.uploadAssets(files, options);
    const list = Array.isArray(result) ? result : [result];
    set(state => ({ assets: [...list, ...state.assets] }));
    return list;
  },
  async applyTemplate(id) {
    const item = await api.getTemplate(id);
    const doc = normalizeDocument(item.document);
    for (const page of doc.pages) for (const element of page.elements) {
      element.templateLocked = item.lockedElementIds?.includes(element.id) || false;
      if (element.templateLocked) element.locked = true;
    }
    get().commitDocument(doc);
    set({ pageIndex: 0, selection: [] });
  },
  async saveCurrentAsTemplate(input) {
    const lockedElementIds = get().document.pages.flatMap(page => page.elements.filter(element => element.locked || element.templateLocked).map(element => element.id));
    const item = await api.saveTemplate({
      ...input,
      lockedElementIds,
      thumbnailUrl: get().design?.thumbnail_url || null,
      document: get().document,
      sourceDesignId: get().design?.id
    });
    if (input.folderId) await api.assignTemplateFolder(item.id, input.folderId).catch(() => {});
    const nextItem = { ...item, folder_id: input.folderId || item.folder_id || null };
    set(state => ({ templates: [nextItem, ...state.templates] }));
    return nextItem;
  },
  async saveSelectionAsComponent(input = {}) {
    const page = get().document.pages[get().pageIndex];
    const roots = new Set(get().selection);
    const included = new Set([...roots, ...collectDescendantIds(page, roots)]);
    const selected = page.elements.filter(element => included.has(element.id));
    if (!selected.length) throw new Error('Select at least one element.');
    const data = componentFromElements(selected, input.title || 'Component');
    const item = await api.saveComponent({ ...data, ...input });
    set(state => ({ components: [item, ...state.components] }));
    return item;
  },
  insertComponent(component) {
    const elements = instantiateComponent(component, 120, 120, { linked: component.linked });
    get().addElements(elements);
  },
  async updateComponentFromSelection(component) {
    const page = get().document.pages[get().pageIndex];
    const roots = new Set(get().selection);
    const included = new Set([...roots, ...collectDescendantIds(page, roots)]);
    const selected = page.elements.filter(element => included.has(element.id));
    if (!selected.length) throw new Error('Select replacement elements first.');
    const data = componentFromElements(selected, component.title);
    const item = await api.updateComponent(component.id, {
      ...data,
      title: component.title,
      category: component.category,
      tags: component.tags,
      linked: component.linked,
      syncLinked: true
    });
    set(state => ({ components: state.components.map(componentItem => componentItem.id === item.id ? item : componentItem) }));
    return item;
  },
  createAutoLayout(options) {
    const { document, pageIndex, selection } = get();
    if (selection.length < 2) return;
    get().commitDocument(createLayoutGroup(document, document.pages[pageIndex].id, selection, options));
  },
  detachAutoLayout(groupId) {
    get().commitDocument(detachLayoutGroup(get().document, groupId));
  },
  magicResize(width, height) {
    get().commitDocument(resizeDocument(get().document, width, height));
  },
  async applyBrand(brand, { colors = true, fonts = true } = {}) {
    let doc = get().document;
    if (colors) doc = replaceColors(doc, brand.colors);
    if (fonts) doc = replaceFonts(doc, brand.fonts);
    get().commitDocument(doc);
  },
  async createBrand(input) {
    const item = await api.saveBrandKit(input);
    set(state => ({ brands: [...state.brands, item] }));
    return item;
  },
  async updateBrand(id, input) {
    const item = await api.updateBrandKit(id, input);
    set(state => ({ brands: state.brands.map(brand => brand.id === id ? item : brand) }));
    return item;
  },
  updatePrintSettings(patch) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    next.print = normalizePrintSettings({ ...(next.print || {}), ...(patch || {}) }, next.width, next.height);
    get().commitDocument(next);
  },
  createDesignStyle(kind, style) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    const created = upsertDesignStyle(next, kind, style);
    get().commitDocument(next);
    return created;
  },
  updateDesignStyle(kind, styleId, patch) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    const current = next.designSystem?.styles?.[kind]?.find(style => style.id === styleId);
    if (!current) throw new Error('Design style not found.');
    const updated = upsertDesignStyle(next, kind, { ...current, ...patch, value: { ...(current.value || {}), ...(patch?.value || {}) } });
    get().commitDocument(next);
    return updated;
  },
  deleteDesignStyle(kind, styleId) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    deleteDesignStyle(next, kind, styleId, { detach: true });
    get().commitDocument(next);
  },
  attachDesignStyle(kind, styleId, elementIds = get().selection) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    const page = next.pages[get().pageIndex];
    attachDesignStyle(next, page.elements.filter(element => elementIds.includes(element.id)), kind, styleId);
    get().commitDocument(next);
  },
  deduplicateDesignStyles() {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    const result = mergeDuplicateDesignStyles(next);
    get().commitDocument(result.document);
    return result.groups;
  },
  addDataSource(input) {
    const next = clone(get().document);
    const source = createDataSource(next, input);
    get().commitDocument(next);
    return source;
  },
  getAIVisuals() {
    const state = get();
    const renders = state.aiRenders?.length ? state.aiRenders : (state.aiRender?.url ? [state.aiRender] : []);
    const pageIndices = renders.length ? [...new Set(renders.map(item => item.pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex))] : [state.pageIndex];
    const pageVisuals = [];
    for (const pageIndex of pageIndices) {
      const render = renders.find(item => (item.pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex) === pageIndex);
      if (render?.url) pageVisuals.push({ source: render.url, url: render.url, label: `Clean render · ${state.document?.pages?.[pageIndex]?.name || `page ${pageIndex + 1}`}`, pageIndex, kind: 'page-render' });
      const svg = createInspectionSvg(state.document, pageIndex, { includeGrid: true, includeLabels: true });
      if (svg) pageVisuals.push({ source: svgToDataUrl(svg), dataUrl: svgToDataUrl(svg), label: `Structural inspection · ${state.document?.pages?.[pageIndex]?.name || `page ${pageIndex + 1}`}`, pageIndex, kind: 'inspection-render' });
    }
    if (!state.aiAnnotation?.dataUrl || state.aiAnnotation.revision !== state.documentRevision) return pageVisuals;
    return [{ source: state.aiAnnotation.dataUrl, dataUrl: state.aiAnnotation.dataUrl, label: 'User-annotated screenshot', pageIndex: state.aiAnnotation.pageIndex, kind: 'annotation' }, ...pageVisuals];
  },
  setAIAnnotation(annotation) {
    set({ aiAnnotation: annotation || null });
  },
  getAIContext() {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.document) return null;
    return createAIContext({
      document: state.document, design: state.design, pageIndex: state.pageIndex, selection: state.selection,
      assets: state.assets, brands: state.brands, components: state.components, revision: state.documentRevision,
      renderUrl: state.aiRender?.url || null, renders: state.aiRenders, annotation: state.aiAnnotation?.revision === state.documentRevision ? state.aiAnnotation : null
    });
  },
  getAIHandoffPackage(request = '', options = {}) {
    const context = get().getAIContext();
    if (!context) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    const origin = globalThis.location?.origin || 'http://localhost';
    const base = apiOrigin ? new URL(apiOrigin, origin).href.replace(/\/$/, '') : origin;
    const skillsUrl = new URL('skills.md', globalThis.document?.baseURI || `${base}/`).href;
    const visuals = options.visuals ?? get().getAIVisuals();
    return createLLMHandoffPackage({ context, request, scope: options.scope || 'page', skillsUrl, apiBase: base, visuals });
  },
  previewLLMText(text, options = {}) {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.document) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    const batch = normalizeLLMCommandBatch(text, { revision: state.documentRevision, instruction: options.instruction || '' });
    return get().previewAICommands(batch);
  },
  previewAICommands(batch) {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.document) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    const validation = validateCommandBatch(batch, { revision: state.documentRevision });
    if (!validation.valid) throw new Error(validation.errors.join(' '));
    const result = applyCommandBatch(state.document, batch, {
      pageIndex: state.pageIndex, selection: state.selection, assets: state.assets, brands: state.brands,
      components: state.components, revision: state.documentRevision
    });
    const lint = lintDocument(result.document);
    const preview = {
      ...result,
      baseRevision: state.documentRevision,
      diff: diffDocuments(state.document, result.document),
      lint,
      blockingIssues: lint.issues.filter(issue => issue.severity === 'critical'),
      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    set(state => ({ aiPlan: batch, aiPreview: preview, aiError: '', aiCandidates: [{ id: uuid(), score: preview.lint?.score?.overall ?? 0, generatedAt: preview.generatedAt, preview, plan: batch }, ...state.aiCandidates].slice(0, 12) }));
    return preview;
  },
  selectAICandidate(candidateId) {
    const candidate = get().aiCandidates.find(item => item.id === candidateId);
    if (!candidate) throw new Error('AI candidate not found.');
    set({ aiPreview: clone(candidate.preview), aiPlan: clone(candidate.plan || get().aiPlan), aiError: '' });
    return candidate;
  },
  applyAISafeFixes() {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.aiPreview) throw new Error('Generate a preview first.');
    const commands = [];
    const seen = new Set();
    for (const issue of state.aiPreview.lint?.issues || []) for (const command of issue.suggestedCommands || (issue.suggestedFix ? [issue.suggestedFix] : [])) {
      const key = JSON.stringify(command);
      if (!seen.has(key)) { seen.add(key); commands.push(command); }
    }
    if (!commands.length) throw new Error('No safe automatic fixes are available.');
    const batch = { schemaVersion: 1, instruction: 'Apply safe design-check fixes', commands };
    const result = applyCommandBatch(state.aiPreview.document, batch, {
      pageIndex: state.pageIndex, selection: state.selection, assets: state.assets, brands: state.brands,
      components: state.components, revision: null
    });
    const lint = lintDocument(result.document);
    const preview = {
      ...state.aiPreview,
      ...result,
      diff: diffDocuments(state.document, result.document),
      lint,
      blockingIssues: lint.issues.filter(issue => issue.severity === 'critical'),
      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    set(current => ({
      aiPreview: preview,
      aiPlan: { ...(current.aiPlan || batch), commands: [...(current.aiPlan?.commands || []), ...commands], instruction: current.aiPlan?.instruction || batch.instruction },
      aiCandidates: [{ id: uuid(), score: lint.score?.overall ?? 0, generatedAt: preview.generatedAt, preview, plan: current.aiPlan || batch }, ...current.aiCandidates].slice(0, 12)
    }));
    return preview;
  },
  async prepareAIPlan(instruction, options = {}) {
    const state = get();
    const context = state.getAIContext();
    if (!context) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    set({ aiBusy: true, aiError: '' });
    try {
      const visuals = options.useVisuals === false ? [] : await Promise.all(state.getAIVisuals().map(async item => ({
        label: item.label,
        pageIndex: item.pageIndex,
        kind: item.kind,
        dataUrl: await sourceToDataUrl(item.source || item.url)
      })));
      const plan = await api.aiPlan(state.design.id, {
        instruction,
        context,
        visuals,
        options: { ...options, mode: options.mode || state.aiMode, provider: undefined }
      });
      if (plan.commands && !plan.schemaVersion) plan.schemaVersion = 1;
      if (!Array.isArray(plan.commands)) plan.commands = [];
      if (!Number.isInteger(plan.baseRevision)) plan.baseRevision = state.documentRevision;
      const currentPlanningState = get();
      const theme = normalizeAITheme(plan.theme || currentPlanningState.aiTheme || { name: options.themeHint || 'Page theme' });
      const plannedRequests = normalizeAIAssetRequests(plan.assetRequests || []);
      const assetRequests = plannedRequests.length || options.assetPlanning !== false ? plannedRequests : currentPlanningState.aiAssetRequests;
      plan.theme = theme;
      plan.assetRequests = assetRequests;
      set({ aiTheme: theme, aiAssetRequests: assetRequests, aiPlan: plan });
      const preview = options.preview === false ? null : get().previewAICommands(plan);
      get().refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {});
      return { plan, preview, theme, assetRequests };
    } catch (error) {
      set({ aiError: error.message || 'AI planning failed.' });
      throw error;
    } finally { set({ aiBusy: false }); }
  },
  getAIAssetPromptList() {
    return assetRequestPromptList(get().aiAssetRequests, get().aiTheme || {});
  },
  async resolveAIAssetRequests(requests = null, { preferExisting = true, maxAssets = 8 } = {}) {
    const list = normalizeAIAssetRequests(requests || get().aiAssetRequests).slice(0, Math.max(1, Math.min(16, Number(maxAssets) || 8)));
    const theme = normalizeAITheme(get().aiTheme || {});
    const results = [];
    set({ aiAssetLoop: { status: 'resolving', total: list.length, completed: 0 }, aiAssetResults: [] });
    for (const [index, request] of list.entries()) {
      let match = request.reuseAssetId ? get().assets.find(asset => asset.id === request.reuseAssetId) : null;
      let resolution = match ? 'reused-exact' : '';
      if (!match && preferExisting) {
        const found = findReusableAsset(get().assets, request);
        if (found) { match = found.asset; resolution = 'reused-search'; }
      }
      if (!match) {
        const prompt = buildThemedAssetPrompt(request, theme);
        const generated = await get().generateAIAsset({
          kind: request.kind,
          mode: get().aiMode,
          prompt,
          aspectRatio: request.aspectRatio,
          transparent: request.transparent,
          tags: [...request.tags, 'ai-theme-asset', request.role, theme.name].filter(Boolean),
          requestKey: request.key
        });
        match = generated.asset;
        resolution = 'generated';
      }
      const item = { request, asset: match, resolution };
      results.push(item);
      set({ aiAssetResults: [...results], aiAssetLoop: { status: 'resolving', total: list.length, completed: index + 1 } });
    }
    set({ aiAssetResults: results, aiAssetLoop: { status: 'complete', total: list.length, completed: list.length } });
    return results;
  },
  async prepareAIPlanWithAssets(instruction, options = {}) {
    const assetMode = options.assetMode || 'reuse-only';
    const passes = Math.max(1, Math.min(3, Number(options.assetRounds || 1)));
    if (assetMode === 'reuse-only') return get().prepareAIPlan(assetPlanningInstruction(instruction, { themeHint: options.themeHint, assetMode }), { ...options, assetPlanning: true, preview: true });

    let resolved = [];
    let planning = null;
    for (let pass = 1; pass <= passes; pass++) {
      planning = await get().prepareAIPlan(assetPlanningInstruction(instruction, { themeHint: options.themeHint, assetMode, pass, priorAssets: summarizeResolvedAssets(resolved) }), { ...options, assetPlanning: true, preview: false, useAssets: true });
      if (assetMode === 'prompts') return planning;
      const unresolved = normalizeAIAssetRequests(planning.assetRequests).filter(request => !resolved.some(item => item.request.key === request.key));
      if (!unresolved.length) break;
      const passResults = await get().resolveAIAssetRequests(unresolved, { preferExisting: true, maxAssets: options.maxGeneratedAssets || 8 });
      resolved = [...resolved, ...passResults];
    }

    const manifest = summarizeResolvedAssets(resolved);
    const finalInstruction = `${instruction}

FINAL ASSET MANIFEST
${JSON.stringify(manifest, null, 2)}
Use these exact asset IDs in the final design. Preserve one coherent theme: ${JSON.stringify(get().aiTheme || {})}. Return the complete final command bundle. Do not request any asset already listed in the manifest.`;
    const result = await get().prepareAIPlan(finalInstruction, { ...options, assetPlanning: false, preview: true, useAssets: true, generatedAssets: manifest });
    set({ aiAssetResults: resolved, aiAssetLoop: { status: 'complete', total: resolved.length, completed: resolved.length } });
    return result;
  },
  applyAIPlan({ approved = false, keepAgentOpen = false } = {}) {
    const state = get();
    if (!approved) throw new Error('AI changes require explicit approval.');
    if (!state.aiPreview || !state.aiPlan) throw new Error('Generate and preview an AI plan first.');
    if (state.aiPreview.baseRevision !== state.documentRevision) throw new Error('The design changed after this preview was generated. Generate the preview again.');
    if (state.aiPreview.blockingIssues?.length) throw new Error(`Fix the ${state.aiPreview.blockingIssues.length} blocking design issue${state.aiPreview.blockingIssues.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} before applying these commands.`);
    const runId = uuid();
    const next = clone(state.aiPreview.document);
    next.ai = { ...(next.ai || {}), lastRunId: runId, lastRenderUrl: state.aiRender?.url || null };
    get().commitDocument(next, { recordHistory: true });
    set(current => ({
      selection: state.aiPreview.createdIds || [],
      aiRuns: [{ id: runId, instruction: state.aiPlan.instruction || '', commandCount: state.aiPlan.commands.length, diff: state.aiPreview.diff, warnings: state.aiPreview.warnings, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }, ...current.aiRuns].slice(0, 50),
      aiPlan: null,
      aiPreview: null,
      aiError: '',
      aiAgent: current.aiAgent ? {
        ...current.aiAgent,
        status: keepAgentOpen ? AGENT_STATES.ASSEMBLING_DESIGN : AGENT_STATES.COMPLETED,
        paused: false,
        tasks: keepAgentOpen
          ? updateAgentTask(current.aiAgent.tasks, 'quality', { status: 'in_progress', progress: 55, details: 'Rendering the reconstructed design for visual correction' })
          : updateAgentTask(current.aiAgent.tasks, 'approval', { status: 'completed', progress: 100 }),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      } : null
    }));
    return runId;
  },
  async applyAIPlanAndRefine({ multiplier = 1 } = {}) {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.aiPlan || !state.aiPreview) throw new Error('Generate and preview an AI plan first.');
    const session = state.aiAgent;
    if (session && session.correctionLoop >= session.maxCorrectionLoops) throw new Error(`The agent reached its ${session.maxCorrectionLoops}-loop safety limit. Review the current design or start another refinement.`);
    const originalInstruction = state.aiPlan.instruction || 'Improve the design';
    const pageIndex = state.pageIndex;
    get().applyAIPlan({ approved: true, keepAgentOpen: !!session });
    if (session) set(current => ({ aiAgent: current.aiAgent ? { ...current.aiAgent, status: AGENT_STATES.RENDERING, correctionLoop: current.aiAgent.correctionLoop + 1, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : null }));
    const render = await get().renderAIImage({ multiplier, pageIndex });
    if (get().aiAgent?.paused) return { render, paused: true };
    if (session) set(current => ({ aiAgent: current.aiAgent ? { ...current.aiAgent, status: AGENT_STATES.CRITIQUING, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : null }));
    const result = await get().prepareAIPlan(
      `Act as a visual QA agent. Review the latest rendered PNG at ${render.url}. Refine the editable design to better match the approved direction, improve hierarchy, spacing, typography, image treatment, and alignment, and resolve any lint issues. Preserve correct copy and exact prices. Return only a focused correction command bundle. Original request: ${originalInstruction}`,
      { provider: 'server', scope: 'document', useBrand: true, useAssets: true, iterationOf: originalInstruction }
    );
    if (session) set(current => ({
      aiAgent: current.aiAgent ? {
        ...current.aiAgent,
        status: AGENT_STATES.AWAITING_FINAL_APPROVAL,
        tasks: updateAgentTask(current.aiAgent.tasks, 'quality', { status: 'completed', progress: 100, details: `Visual correction loop ${current.aiAgent.correctionLoop} ready for review` }),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      } : null
    }));
    return result;
  },
  async autoRefineAIPlan({ rounds = null, multiplier = 1 } = {}) {
    const limit = Math.max(1, Math.min(5, Number(rounds || get().aiRefinementLimit || 3)));
    let previousScore = get().aiPreview?.lint?.score?.overall ?? 0;
    let completed = 0;
    for (let round = 0; round < limit; round++) {
      const state = get();
      if (!state.aiPlan || !state.aiPreview) break;
      if (state.aiPreview.blockingIssues?.length) throw new Error('Resolve blocking design issues before automatic refinement.');
      const originalInstruction = state.aiPlan.instruction || 'Improve the design';
      get().applyAIPlan({ approved: true });
      await get().renderAIImage({ multiplier, pageIndex: state.pageIndex });
      await get().prepareAIPlan(
        `Refinement round ${round + 1} of ${limit}. Inspect both the clean render and structural inspection image. Correct alignment, spacing rhythm, typography hierarchy, repeated-component consistency, print safety, and any design-check findings. Preserve all correct content. Original request: ${originalInstruction}`,
        { mode: get().aiMode, scope: 'page', useBrand: true, useAssets: true, useVisuals: true, iterationOf: originalInstruction }
      );
      completed++;
      const score = get().aiPreview?.lint?.score?.overall ?? 0;
      if (score <= previousScore && round > 0) break;
      previousScore = Math.max(previousScore, score);
    }
    return { completed, candidates: get().aiCandidates, preview: get().aiPreview };
  },
  async renderAIImages({ multiplier = 1, scope = 'page', pageIndex = null } = {}) {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.design || !state.document) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    const pageIndices = scope === 'document'
      ? state.document.pages.map((_, index) => index)
      : [pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex];
    set({ aiBusy: true, aiError: '', aiRender: { status: 'saving', progress: 0, url: state.aiRender?.url || null } });
    try {
      await get().save({ createVersion: false, allowRecovered: true });
      const completed = [];
      const exportJobs = [];
      for (const [position, targetPageIndex] of pageIndices.entries()) {
        let job = await api.createExport(state.design.id, 'png', { multiplier, pageIndex: targetPageIndex, purpose: 'ai-preview' });
        exportJobs.push(job);
        set({ aiRender: { status: job.status, progress: Math.round((position / pageIndices.length) * 100), jobId: job.id, url: null, pageIndex: targetPageIndex } });
        for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 240 && ['queued', 'processing'].includes(job.status); attempt++) {
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
          job = await api.getExport(job.id);
          const pageProgress = Number(job.progress || 0) / 100;
          set({ aiRender: { status: job.status, progress: Math.round(((position + pageProgress) / pageIndices.length) * 100), jobId: job.id, url: job.output_url || null, pageIndex: targetPageIndex } });
        }
        if (job.status !== 'completed' || !job.output_url) throw new Error(job.error || `The AI preview for page ${targetPageIndex + 1} did not complete.`);
        const url = new URL(job.output_url, globalThis.location?.origin || 'http://localhost').href;
        completed.push({ status: 'completed', progress: 100, jobId: job.id, url, pageIndex: targetPageIndex, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() });
        exportJobs[exportJobs.length - 1] = job;
      }
      const currentRender = completed.find(item => item.pageIndex === (pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex)) || completed[0];
      set(current => ({
        aiRender: currentRender,
        aiRenders: completed,
        exports: [...exportJobs, ...current.exports.filter(item => !exportJobs.some(job => job.id === item.id))]
      }));
      return completed;
    } catch (error) {
      set(current => ({ aiError: error.message || 'Could not render the AI preview image.', aiRender: { ...(current.aiRender || {}), status: 'failed', error: error.message } }));
      throw error;
    } finally {
      set({ aiBusy: false });
    }
  },
  async renderAIImage({ multiplier = 1, pageIndex = null } = {}) {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.design || !state.document) throw new Error('No design is open.');
    set({ aiBusy: true, aiError: '', aiRender: { status: 'saving', progress: 0, url: state.aiRender?.url || null } });
    try {
      await get().save({ createVersion: false, allowRecovered: true });
      let job = await api.createExport(state.design.id, 'png', { multiplier, pageIndex: pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex, purpose: 'ai-preview' });
      set({ aiRender: { status: job.status, progress: job.progress || 0, jobId: job.id, url: null } });
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 240 && ['queued', 'processing'].includes(job.status); attempt++) {
        const agent = get().aiAgent;
        if (agent?.paused || agent?.status === AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED) throw new Error(agent.status === AGENT_STATES.CANCELLED ? 'The agent session was stopped.' : 'The agent was paused. The server export may finish, but no further loop steps will run.');
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
        job = await api.getExport(job.id);
        set({ aiRender: { status: job.status, progress: job.progress || 0, jobId: job.id, url: job.output_url || null } });
      }
      if (job.status !== 'completed' || !job.output_url) throw new Error(job.error || 'The AI preview image did not complete.');
      const url = new URL(job.output_url, globalThis.location?.origin || 'http://localhost').href;
      const render = { status: 'completed', progress: 100, jobId: job.id, url, pageIndex: pageIndex ?? state.pageIndex, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
      set(current => ({ aiRender: render, exports: current.exports.some(item => item.id === job.id) ? current.exports.map(item => item.id === job.id ? job : item) : [job, ...current.exports] }));
      return render;
    } catch (error) {
      set(current => ({ aiError: error.message || 'Could not render the AI preview image.', aiRender: { ...(current.aiRender || {}), status: 'failed', error: error.message } }));
      throw error;
    } finally {
      set({ aiBusy: false });
    }
  },
  async generateAIAsset(input) {
    set({ aiBusy: true, aiError: '' });
    try {
      const references = await Promise.all((input.references || []).slice(0, 6).map(async file => ({
        name: file.name || 'Reference image',
        dataUrl: await sourceToDataUrl(file)
      })));
      const generated = await api.aiGenerateAsset({
        kind: input.kind,
        mode: input.mode || get().aiMode,
        prompt: input.prompt,
        references,
        aspectRatio: input.aspectRatio,
        transparent: !!input.transparent
      });
      if (generated.kind === 'svg') generated.svg = sanitizeSvgMarkup(generated.svg);
      const safeBase = String(input.prompt || 'ai-asset').slice(0, 48).replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/gi, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '').toLowerCase() || 'ai-asset';
      const extension = generated.kind === 'svg' ? 'svg' : (generated.mimeType?.includes('jpeg') ? 'jpg' : generated.mimeType?.includes('webp') ? 'webp' : 'png');
      const source = generated.kind === 'svg' ? `data:image/svg+xml;base64,${btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(generated.svg)))}` : generated.dataUrl;
      const file = await dataUrlToFile(source, `${safeBase}.${extension}`);
      const aiFolder = get().assetFolders.find(folder => String(folder.name).toLowerCase() === 'ai generated');
      const asset = await get().upload(file, { folderId: aiFolder?.id || '', tags: [...new Set(['ai-generated', input.mode || get().aiMode, ...(input.tags || [])].filter(Boolean))], sourceType: 'ai_generation', sourceJobId: generated.jobId || input.requestKey || '' });
      await get().refreshCommercialData().catch(() => {});
      return { ...generated, dataUrl: source, asset };
    } catch (error) {
      set({ aiError: error.message || 'AI asset generation failed.' });
      throw error;
    } finally { set({ aiBusy: false }); }
  },

  async exportDesign(format, options = {}) {
    const { design } = get();
    await get().save({ createVersion: false, allowRecovered: true });
    const job = await api.createExport(design.id, format, options);
    set(state => ({ exports: [job, ...state.exports] }));
    return job;
  },
  async refreshExport(id) {
    const job = await api.getExport(id);
    set(state => ({ exports: state.exports.map(item => item.id === id ? job : item) }));
    return job;
  },
  async addComment(input) {
    const item = await api.addComment(get().design.id, input);
    set(state => ({ comments: [...state.comments, item] }));
    return item;
  },
  async resolveComment(id, resolved = true) {
    const item = await api.resolveComment(id, resolved);
    set(state => ({ comments: state.comments.map(comment => comment.id === id ? item : comment) }));
  },
  async markNotification(id, read = true) {
    const item = await api.markNotification(id, read);
    set(state => ({ notifications: state.notifications.map(notification => notification.id === id ? item : notification) }));
    return item;
  },
  async markAllNotifications() {
    const notifications = await api.markAllNotifications();
    set({ notifications });
  },
  async setStatus(status) {
    const design = await api.setDesignStatus(get().design.id, status);
    set({ design });
    return design;
  },
  async createShare(input) {
    const item = await api.createShare(get().design.id, input);
    set(state => ({ shares: [item, ...state.shares] }));
    return item;
  },
  async loadMembers() {
    const members = await api.listMembers();
    set({ members });
    return members;
  }
}));

window.addEventListener('online', () => useEditorStore.getState().setOnline(true));
window.addEventListener('offline', () => useEditorStore.getState().setOnline(false));

channel?.addEventListener('message', event => {
  const message = event.data;
  if (message?.tabId === tabId) return;
  const state = useEditorStore.getState();
  if (message?.type === 'open' && message.designId && state.design?.id === message.designId) {
    useEditorStore.setState({ tabConflict: true, status: 'conflict', lastError: 'This design is open in another tab.' });
    channel.postMessage({ type: 'conflict', designId: message.designId, tabId });
  }
  if (message?.type === 'conflict' && message.designId === state.design?.id) {
    useEditorStore.setState({ tabConflict: true, status: 'conflict', lastError: 'This design is open in another tab.' });
  }
  if (message?.type === 'takeover' && message.designId === state.design?.id) {
    useEditorStore.setState({ tabConflict: true, status: 'conflict', lastError: 'Another tab took over editing this design.' });
  }
  if (message?.type === 'close' && message.designId === state.design?.id && state.tabConflict) {
    const unsaved = state.documentRevision > state.savedRevision;
    useEditorStore.setState({ tabConflict: false, status: state.online ? (unsaved ? 'dirty' : 'saved') : 'offline', lastError: '' });
  }
});

window.addEventListener('pagehide', () => {
  const id = useEditorStore.getState().design?.id;
  if (id) channel?.postMessage({ type: 'close', designId: id, tabId });
});

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  window.DesignCommonsAI = {
    version: 2,
    appName: APP_NAME,
    capabilities: () => getAICapabilities(),
    context: () => useEditorStore.getState().getAIContext(),
    handoff: (request = '', options = {}) => useEditorStore.getState().getAIHandoffPackage(request, options),
    lint: () => lintDocument(useEditorStore.getState().document),
    validate: batch => validateCommandBatch(batch, { revision: useEditorStore.getState().documentRevision }),
    preview: batch => useEditorStore.getState().previewAICommands(batch),
    previewText: (text, options = {}) => useEditorStore.getState().previewLLMText(text, options),
    apply: (batch, options = {}) => {
      if (batch) useEditorStore.getState().previewAICommands(batch);
      return useEditorStore.getState().applyAIPlan(options);
    },
    plan: (instruction, options = {}) => useEditorStore.getState().prepareAIPlan(instruction, options),
    render: options => useEditorStore.getState().renderAIImage(options),
    refine: options => useEditorStore.getState().applyAIPlanAndRefine(options),
    agent: {
      start: (instruction, options = {}) => useEditorStore.getState().startAIAgent(instruction, options),
      answer: answer => useEditorStore.getState().answerAIAgent(answer),
      concepts: options => useEditorStore.getState().generateAIAgentConcepts(options),
      select: conceptId => useEditorStore.getState().selectAIAgentConcept(conceptId),
      refine: (conceptId, feedback) => useEditorStore.getState().refineAIAgentConcept(conceptId, feedback),
      approve: conceptId => useEditorStore.getState().approveAIAgentConcept(conceptId),
      steer: message => useEditorStore.getState().steerAIAgent(message),
      pause: () => useEditorStore.getState().pauseAIAgent(),
      resume: () => useEditorStore.getState().resumeAIAgent(),
      cancel: () => useEditorStore.getState().cancelAIAgent(),
      state: () => useEditorStore.getState().aiAgent
    },
    undo: () => useEditorStore.getState().undo()
  };
  window.CanvasForgeAI = window.DesignCommonsAI;
}

import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  base: process.env.VITE_BASE_PATH || '/design-commons/',
  server: {
    port: 3020,
    allowedHosts: true,
    proxy: {
      '/api': 'http://localhost:4300',
      '/storage': 'http://localhost:4300'
    }
  },
  preview: {
    port: 3020,
    proxy: {
      '/api': 'http://localhost:4300',
      '/storage': 'http://localhost:4300'
    }
  }
});

// FILE: index.html
================================================================================
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Design Commons</title>
    <meta name="theme-color" content="#f4f6fa" />
    <script>
      (() => {
        try {
          const saved = localStorage.getItem('design-commons-theme') || localStorage.getItem('canvasforge-theme') || 'system';
          if (localStorage.getItem('canvasforge-theme') && !localStorage.getItem('design-commons-theme')) {
            localStorage.setItem('design-commons-theme', localStorage.getItem('canvasforge-theme'));
            localStorage.removeItem('canvasforge-theme');
          }
          const resolved = saved === 'system'
            ? (matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light')
            : saved;
          document.documentElement.dataset.theme = resolved;
          document.documentElement.dataset.themePreference = saved;
          document.documentElement.style.colorScheme = resolved;
        } catch {}
      })();
    </script>
  </head>
  <body>
    <div id="root"></div>
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.jsx"></script>
  </body>
</html>
